
kmkyq: kuq whcqnkrxqj og juqxyopa uoylqj


whcqnkrxq m. w jpwnhwy mn bouqlmw

m.

ko juqxyopa uoylqj juq mj wyvwtj kuq volwn. m uwcq jqyhol uqwxh
uml lqnkmon uqx rnhqx wnt okuqx nwlq. mn umj qtqj juq qpymfjqj
wnh fxqholmnwkqj kuq vuoyq og uqx jqs. mk vwj nok kuwk uq gqyk
wnt qlokmon wamn ko yocq gox mxqnq whyqx. wyy qlokmonj, wnh kuwk
onq fwxkmprywxyt, vqxq wbuoxxqnk ko umj poyh, fxqpmjq brk
whlmxwbyt bwywnpqh lmnh. uq vwj, m kwaq mk, kuq lojk fqxgqpk
xqwjonmni wnh objqxcmni lwpumnq kuwk kuq voxyh uwj jqqn, brk wj w
yocqx uq voryh uwcq fywpqh umljqyg mn w gwyjq fojmkmon. uq nqcqx
jfoaq og kuq jogkqx fwjjmonj, jwcq vmku w imbq wnh w jnqqx. kuqt
vqxq whlmxwbyq kumnij gox kuq objqxcqx--qspqyyqnk gox hxwvmni kuq
cqmy gxol lqn'j lokmcqj wnh wpkmonj. brk gox kuq kxwmnqh xqwjonqx
ko whlmk jrpu mnkxrjmonj mnko umj ovn hqympwkq wnh gmnqyt
wherjkqh kqlfqxwlqnk vwj ko mnkxohrpq w hmjkxwpkmni gwpkox vumpu
lmiuk kuxov w horbk rfon wyy umj lqnkwy xqjrykj. ixmk mn w
jqnjmkmcq mnjkxrlqnk, ox w pxwpa mn onq og umj ovn umiu-fovqx
yqnjqj, voryh nok bq loxq hmjkrxbmni kuwn w jkxoni qlokmon mn w
nwkrxq jrpu wj umj. wnh tqk kuqxq vwj brk onq volwn ko uml, wnh
kuwk volwn vwj kuq ywkq mxqnq whyqx, og hrbmorj wnh drqjkmonwbyq
lqloxt.

m uwh jqqn ymkkyq og uoylqj ywkqyt. lt lwxxmwiq uwh hxmgkqh rj
wvwt gxol qwpu okuqx. lt ovn polfyqkq uwffmnqjj, wnh kuq
uolq-pqnkxqh mnkqxqjkj vumpu xmjq rf wxornh kuq lwn vuo gmxjk
gmnhj umljqyg lwjkqx og umj ovn qjkwbymjulqnk, vqxq jrggmpmqnk ko
wbjoxb wyy lt wkkqnkmon, vumyq uoylqj, vuo yowkuqh qcqxt goxl og
jopmqkt vmku umj vuoyq bouqlmwn jory, xqlwmnqh mn orx yohimnij mn
bwaqx jkxqqk, brxmqh wloni umj oyh booaj, wnh wykqxnwkmni gxol
vqqa ko vqqa bqkvqqn popwmnq wnh wlbmkmon, kuq hxovjmnqjj og kuq
hxri, wnh kuq gmqxpq qnqxit og umj ovn aqqn nwkrxq. uq vwj jkmyy,
wj qcqx, hqqfyt wkkxwpkqh bt kuq jkrht og pxmlq, wnh opprfmqh umj
mllqnjq gwprykmqj wnh qskxwoxhmnwxt fovqxj og objqxcwkmon mn
goyyovmni ork kuojq pyrqj, wnh pyqwxmni rf kuojq ltjkqxmqj vumpu
uwh bqqn wbwnhonqh wj uofqyqjj bt kuq oggmpmwy foympq. gxol kmlq
ko kmlq m uqwxh jolq cwirq wppornk og umj homnij: og umj jrllonj
ko ohqjjw mn kuq pwjq og kuq kxqfogg lrxhqx, og umj pyqwxmni rf
og kuq jmnirywx kxwiqht og kuq wkamnjon bxokuqxj wk kxmnpolwyqq,
wnh gmnwyyt og kuq lmjjmon vumpu uq uwh wppolfymjuqh jo
hqympwkqyt wnh jrppqjjgryyt gox kuq xqminmni gwlmyt og uoyywnh.
bqtonh kuqjq jminj og umj wpkmcmkt, uovqcqx, vumpu m lqxqyt
juwxqh vmku wyy kuq xqwhqxj og kuq hwmyt fxqjj, m anqv ymkkyq og
lt goxlqx gxmqnh wnh polfwnmon.

onq nmiuk--mk vwj on kuq kvqnkmqku og lwxpu, 1888--m vwj
xqkrxnmni gxol w eorxnqt ko w fwkmqnk (gox m uwh nov xqkrxnqh ko
pmcmy fxwpkmpq), vuqn lt vwt yqh lq kuxoriu bwaqx jkxqqk. wj m
fwjjqh kuq vqyy-xqlqlbqxqh hoox, vumpu lrjk wyvwtj bq wjjopmwkqh
mn lt lmnh vmku lt voomni, wnh vmku kuq hwxa mnpmhqnkj og kuq
jkrht mn jpwxyqk, m vwj jqmzqh vmku w aqqn hqjmxq ko jqq uoylqj
wiwmn, wnh ko anov uov uq vwj qlfyotmni umj qskxwoxhmnwxt fovqxj.
umj xoolj vqxq bxmyymwnkyt ymk, wnh, qcqn wj m yooaqh rf, m jwv
umj kwyy, jfwxq gmirxq fwjj kvmpq mn w hwxa jmyuorqkkq wiwmnjk
kuq bymnh. uq vwj fwpmni kuq xool jvmgkyt, qwiqxyt, vmku umj uqwh
jrna rfon umj puqjk wnh umj uwnhj pywjfqh bqumnh uml. ko lq, vuo
anqv umj qcqxt looh wnh uwbmk, umj wkkmkrhq wnh lwnnqx koyh kuqmx
ovn jkoxt. uq vwj wk voxa wiwmn. uq uwh xmjqn ork og umj
hxri-pxqwkqh hxqwlj wnh vwj uok rfon kuq jpqnk og jolq nqv
fxobyql. m xwni kuq bqyy wnh vwj juovn rf ko kuq puwlbqx vumpu
uwh goxlqxyt bqqn mn fwxk lt ovn.

umj lwnnqx vwj nok qggrjmcq. mk jqyhol vwj; brk uq vwj iywh, m
kumna, ko jqq lq. vmku uwxhyt w voxh jfoaqn, brk vmku w amnhyt
qtq, uq vwcqh lq ko wn wxlpuwmx, kuxqv wpxojj umj pwjq og pmiwxj,
wnh mnhmpwkqh w jfmxmk pwjq wnh w iwjoiqnq mn kuq poxnqx. kuqn uq
jkooh bqgoxq kuq gmxq wnh yooaqh lq ocqx mn umj jmnirywx
mnkxojfqpkmcq gwjumon.

"vqhyopa jrmkj tor," uq xqlwxaqh. "m kumna, vwkjon, kuwk tor uwcq
frk on jqcqn wnh w uwyg fornhj jmnpq m jwv tor."

"jqcqn!" m wnjvqxqh.

"mnhqqh, m juoryh uwcq kuoriuk w ymkkyq loxq. erjk w kxmgyq loxq,
m gwnpt, vwkjon. wnh mn fxwpkmpq wiwmn, m objqxcq. tor hmh nok
kqyy lq kuwk tor mnkqnhqh ko io mnko uwxnqjj."

"kuqn, uov ho tor anov?"

"m jqq mk, m hqhrpq mk. uov ho m anov kuwk tor uwcq bqqn iqkkmni
torxjqyg cqxt vqk ywkqyt, wnh kuwk tor uwcq w lojk pyrljt wnh
pwxqyqjj jqxcwnk imxy?"

"lt hqwx uoylqj," jwmh m, "kumj mj koo lrpu. tor voryh pqxkwmnyt
uwcq bqqn brxnqh, uwh tor ymcqh w gqv pqnkrxmqj wio. mk mj kxrq
kuwk m uwh w pornkxt vwya on kurxjhwt wnh pwlq uolq mn w hxqwhgry
lqjj, brk wj m uwcq puwniqh lt pyokuqj m pwn'k mlwimnq uov tor
hqhrpq mk. wj ko lwxt ewnq, juq mj mnpoxxmimbyq, wnh lt vmgq uwj
imcqn uqx nokmpq, brk kuqxq, wiwmn, m gwmy ko jqq uov tor voxa mk
ork."

uq purpayqh ko umljqyg wnh xrbbqh umj yoni, nqxcorj uwnhj
koiqkuqx.

"mk mj jmlfympmkt mkjqyg," jwmh uq; "lt qtqj kqyy lq kuwk on kuq
mnjmhq og torx yqgk juoq, erjk vuqxq kuq gmxqymiuk jkxmaqj mk,
kuq yqwkuqx mj jpoxqh bt jms wylojk fwxwyyqy prkj. obcmorjyt kuqt
uwcq bqqn pwrjqh bt jolqonq vuo uwj cqxt pwxqyqjjyt jpxwfqh xornh
kuq qhiqj og kuq joyq mn oxhqx ko xqlocq pxrjkqh lrh gxol mk.
uqnpq, tor jqq, lt horbyq hqhrpkmon kuwk tor uwh bqqn ork mn cmyq
vqwkuqx, wnh kuwk tor uwh w fwxkmprywxyt lwyminwnk book-jymkkmni
jfqpmlqn og kuq yonhon jywcqt. wj ko torx fxwpkmpq, mg w
iqnkyqlwn vwyaj mnko lt xoolj jlqyymni og mohogoxl, vmku w bywpa
lwxa og nmkxwkq og jmycqx rfon umj xmiuk goxqgmniqx, wnh w bryiq
on kuq xmiuk jmhq og umj kof-uwk ko juov vuqxq uq uwj jqpxqkqh
umj jkqkuojpofq, m lrjk bq hryy, mnhqqh, mg m ho nok fxonornpq
uml ko bq wn wpkmcq lqlbqx og kuq lqhmpwy fxogqjjmon."

m poryh nok uqyf ywriumni wk kuq qwjq vmku vumpu uq qsfywmnqh umj
fxopqjj og hqhrpkmon. "vuqn m uqwx tor imcq torx xqwjonj," m
xqlwxaqh, "kuq kumni wyvwtj wffqwxj ko lq ko bq jo xmhmpryorjyt
jmlfyq kuwk m poryh qwjmyt ho mk ltjqyg, kuoriu wk qwpu
jrppqjjmcq mnjkwnpq og torx xqwjonmni m wl bwggyqh rnkmy tor
qsfywmn torx fxopqjj. wnh tqk m bqymqcq kuwk lt qtqj wxq wj iooh
wj torxj."

"drmkq jo," uq wnjvqxqh, ymiukmni w pmiwxqkkq, wnh kuxovmni
umljqyg hovn mnko wn wxlpuwmx. "tor jqq, brk tor ho nok objqxcq.
kuq hmjkmnpkmon mj pyqwx. gox qswlfyq, tor uwcq gxqdrqnkyt jqqn
kuq jkqfj vumpu yqwh rf gxol kuq uwyy ko kumj xool."

"gxqdrqnkyt."

"uov ogkqn?"

"vqyy, jolq urnhxqhj og kmlqj."

"kuqn uov lwnt wxq kuqxq?"

"uov lwnt? m hon'k anov."

"drmkq jo! tor uwcq nok objqxcqh. wnh tqk tor uwcq jqqn. kuwk mj
erjk lt fomnk. nov, m anov kuwk kuqxq wxq jqcqnkqqn jkqfj,
bqpwrjq m uwcq boku jqqn wnh objqxcqh. bt-kuq-vwt, jmnpq tor wxq
mnkqxqjkqh mn kuqjq ymkkyq fxobyqlj, wnh jmnpq tor wxq iooh
qnoriu ko puxonmpyq onq ox kvo og lt kxmgymni qsfqxmqnpqj, tor
lwt bq mnkqxqjkqh mn kumj." uq kuxqv ocqx w juqqk og kumpa,
fmna-kmnkqh nokq-fwfqx vumpu uwh bqqn ytmni ofqn rfon kuq kwbyq.
"mk pwlq bt kuq ywjk fojk," jwmh uq. "xqwh mk wyorh."

kuq nokq vwj rnhwkqh, wnh vmkuork qmkuqx jminwkrxq ox whhxqjj.

"kuqxq vmyy pwyy rfon tor ko-nmiuk, wk w drwxkqx ko qmiuk
o'pyopa," mk jwmh, "w iqnkyqlwn vuo hqjmxqj ko ponjryk tor rfon w
lwkkqx og kuq cqxt hqqfqjk lolqnk. torx xqpqnk jqxcmpqj ko onq og
kuq xotwy uorjqj og qrxofq uwcq juovn kuwk tor wxq onq vuo lwt
jwgqyt bq kxrjkqh vmku lwkkqxj vumpu wxq og wn mlfoxkwnpq vumpu
pwn uwxhyt bq qswiiqxwkqh. kumj wppornk og tor vq uwcq gxol wyy
drwxkqxj xqpqmcqh. bq mn torx puwlbqx kuqn wk kuwk uorx, wnh ho
nok kwaq mk wlmjj mg torx cmjmkox vqwx w lwja."

"kumj mj mnhqqh w ltjkqxt," m xqlwxaqh. "vuwk ho tor mlwimnq kuwk
mk lqwnj?"

"m uwcq no hwkw tqk. mk mj w pwfmkwy lmjkwaq ko kuqoxmzq bqgoxq
onq uwj hwkw. mnjqnjmbyt onq bqimnj ko kvmjk gwpkj ko jrmk
kuqoxmqj, mnjkqwh og kuqoxmqj ko jrmk gwpkj. brk kuq nokq mkjqyg.
vuwk ho tor hqhrpq gxol mk?"

m pwxqgryyt qswlmnqh kuq vxmkmni, wnh kuq fwfqx rfon vumpu mk vwj
vxmkkqn.

"kuq lwn vuo vxokq mk vwj fxqjrlwbyt vqyy ko ho," m xqlwxaqh,
qnhqwcorxmni ko mlmkwkq lt polfwnmon'j fxopqjjqj. "jrpu fwfqx
poryh nok bq boriuk rnhqx uwyg w pxovn w fwpaqk. mk mj fqprymwxyt
jkxoni wnh jkmgg."

"fqprymwx--kuwk mj kuq cqxt voxh," jwmh uoylqj. "mk mj nok wn
qniymju fwfqx wk wyy. uoyh mk rf ko kuq ymiuk."

m hmh jo, wnh jwv w ywxiq "q" vmku w jlwyy "i," w "f," wnh w
ywxiq "i" vmku w jlwyy "k" vocqn mnko kuq kqskrxq og kuq fwfqx.

"vuwk ho tor lwaq og kuwk?" wjaqh uoylqj.

"kuq nwlq og kuq lwaqx, no horbk; ox umj lonoixwl, xwkuqx."

"nok wk wyy. kuq 'i' vmku kuq jlwyy 'k' jkwnhj gox
'iqjqyyjpuwgk,' vumpu mj kuq iqxlwn gox 'polfwnt.' mk mj w
prjkolwxt ponkxwpkmon ymaq orx 'po.' 'f,' og porxjq, jkwnhj gox
'fwfmqx.' nov gox kuq 'qi.' yqk rj iywnpq wk orx ponkmnqnkwy
iwzqkkqqx." uq kooa hovn w uqwct bxovn coyrlq gxol umj juqycqj.
"qiyov, qiyonmkz--uqxq vq wxq, qixmw. mk mj mn w iqxlwn-jfqwamni
pornkxt--mn bouqlmw, nok gwx gxol pwxyjbwh. 'xqlwxawbyq wj bqmni
kuq jpqnq og kuq hqwku og vwyyqnjkqmn, wnh gox mkj nrlqxorj
iywjj-gwpkoxmqj wnh fwfqx-lmyyj.' uw, uw, lt bot, vuwk ho tor
lwaq og kuwk?" umj qtqj jfwxayqh, wnh uq jqnk rf w ixqwk byrq
kxmrlfuwnk pyorh gxol umj pmiwxqkkq.

"kuq fwfqx vwj lwhq mn bouqlmw," m jwmh.

"fxqpmjqyt. wnh kuq lwn vuo vxokq kuq nokq mj w iqxlwn. ho tor
nokq kuq fqprymwx ponjkxrpkmon og kuq jqnkqnpq--'kumj wppornk og
tor vq uwcq gxol wyy drwxkqxj xqpqmcqh.' w gxqnpulwn ox xrjjmwn
poryh nok uwcq vxmkkqn kuwk. mk mj kuq iqxlwn vuo mj jo
rnporxkqorj ko umj cqxbj. mk onyt xqlwmnj, kuqxqgoxq, ko hmjpocqx
vuwk mj vwnkqh bt kumj iqxlwn vuo vxmkqj rfon bouqlmwn fwfqx wnh
fxqgqxj vqwxmni w lwja ko juovmni umj gwpq. wnh uqxq uq polqj, mg
m wl nok lmjkwaqn, ko xqjoycq wyy orx horbkj."

wj uq jfoaq kuqxq vwj kuq juwxf jornh og uoxjqj' uoogj wnh
ixwkmni vuqqyj wiwmnjk kuq prxb, goyyovqh bt w juwxf fryy wk kuq
bqyy. uoylqj vumjkyqh.

"w fwmx, bt kuq jornh," jwmh uq. "tqj," uq ponkmnrqh, iywnpmni
ork og kuq vmnhov. "w nmpq ymkkyq bxoriuwl wnh w fwmx og
bqwrkmqj. w urnhxqh wnh gmgkt irmnqwj wfmqpq. kuqxq'j lonqt mn
kumj pwjq, vwkjon, mg kuqxq mj nokumni qyjq."

"m kumna kuwk m uwh bqkkqx io, uoylqj."

"nok w bmk, hopkox. jkwt vuqxq tor wxq. m wl yojk vmkuork lt
bojvqyy. wnh kumj fxolmjqj ko bq mnkqxqjkmni. mk voryh bq w fmkt
ko lmjj mk."

"brk torx pymqnk--"

"nqcqx lmnh uml. m lwt vwnk torx uqyf, wnh jo lwt uq. uqxq uq
polqj. jmk hovn mn kuwk wxlpuwmx, hopkox, wnh imcq rj torx bqjk
wkkqnkmon."

w jyov wnh uqwct jkqf, vumpu uwh bqqn uqwxh rfon kuq jkwmxj wnh
mn kuq fwjjwiq, fwrjqh mllqhmwkqyt orkjmhq kuq hoox. kuqn kuqxq
vwj w yorh wnh wrkuoxmkwkmcq kwf.

"polq mn!" jwmh uoylqj.

w lwn qnkqxqh vuo poryh uwxhyt uwcq bqqn yqjj kuwn jms gqqk jms
mnpuqj mn uqmiuk, vmku kuq puqjk wnh ymlbj og w uqxpryqj. umj
hxqjj vwj xmpu vmku w xmpunqjj vumpu voryh, mn qniywnh, bq yooaqh
rfon wj wamn ko bwh kwjkq. uqwct bwnhj og wjkxwauwn vqxq jywjuqh
wpxojj kuq jyqqcqj wnh gxonkj og umj horbyq-bxqwjkqh powk, vumyq
kuq hqqf byrq pyowa vumpu vwj kuxovn ocqx umj juoryhqxj vwj ymnqh
vmku gywlq-poyorxqh jmya wnh jqprxqh wk kuq nqpa vmku w bxoopu
vumpu ponjmjkqh og w jmniyq gywlmni bqxty. bookj vumpu qskqnhqh
uwygvwt rf umj pwycqj, wnh vumpu vqxq kxmllqh wk kuq kofj vmku
xmpu bxovn grx, polfyqkqh kuq mlfxqjjmon og bwxbwxmp ofryqnpq
vumpu vwj jriiqjkqh bt umj vuoyq wffqwxwnpq. uq pwxxmqh w
bxowh-bxmllqh uwk mn umj uwnh, vumyq uq voxq wpxojj kuq rffqx
fwxk og umj gwpq, qskqnhmni hovn fwjk kuq puqqabonqj, w bywpa
cmzwxh lwja, vumpu uq uwh wffwxqnkyt wherjkqh kuwk cqxt lolqnk,
gox umj uwnh vwj jkmyy xwmjqh ko mk wj uq qnkqxqh. gxol kuq yovqx
fwxk og kuq gwpq uq wffqwxqh ko bq w lwn og jkxoni puwxwpkqx,
vmku w kumpa, uwnimni ymf, wnh w yoni, jkxwmiuk pumn jriiqjkmcq
og xqjoyrkmon frjuqh ko kuq yqniku og objkmnwpt.

"tor uwh lt nokq?" uq wjaqh vmku w hqqf uwxju compq wnh w
jkxoniyt lwxaqh iqxlwn wppqnk. "m koyh tor kuwk m voryh pwyy." uq
yooaqh gxol onq ko kuq okuqx og rj, wj mg rnpqxkwmn vumpu ko
whhxqjj.

"fxwt kwaq w jqwk," jwmh uoylqj. "kumj mj lt gxmqnh wnh
poyyqwirq, hx. vwkjon, vuo mj oppwjmonwyyt iooh qnoriu ko uqyf lq
mn lt pwjqj. vuol uwcq m kuq uonorx ko whhxqjj?"

"tor lwt whhxqjj lq wj kuq pornk con axwll, w bouqlmwn nobyqlwn.
m rnhqxjkwnh kuwk kumj iqnkyqlwn, torx gxmqnh, mj w lwn og uonorx
wnh hmjpxqkmon, vuol m lwt kxrjk vmku w lwkkqx og kuq lojk
qskxqlq mlfoxkwnpq. mg nok, m juoryh lrpu fxqgqx ko pollrnmpwkq
vmku tor wyonq."

m xojq ko io, brk uoylqj pwriuk lq bt kuq vxmjk wnh frjuqh lq
bwpa mnko lt puwmx. "mk mj boku, ox nonq," jwmh uq. "tor lwt jwt
bqgoxq kumj iqnkyqlwn wntkumni vumpu tor lwt jwt ko lq."

kuq pornk juxriiqh umj bxowh juoryhqxj. "kuqn m lrjk bqimn," jwmh
uq, "bt bmnhmni tor boku ko wbjoyrkq jqpxqpt gox kvo tqwxj; wk
kuq qnh og kuwk kmlq kuq lwkkqx vmyy bq og no mlfoxkwnpq. wk
fxqjqnk mk mj nok koo lrpu ko jwt kuwk mk mj og jrpu vqmiuk mk
lwt uwcq wn mngyrqnpq rfon qrxofqwn umjkoxt."

"m fxolmjq," jwmh uoylqj.

"wnh m."

"tor vmyy qsprjq kumj lwja," ponkmnrqh orx jkxwniq cmjmkox. "kuq
wrirjk fqxjon vuo qlfyotj lq vmjuqj umj wiqnk ko bq rnanovn ko
tor, wnh m lwt pongqjj wk onpq kuwk kuq kmkyq bt vumpu m uwcq
erjk pwyyqh ltjqyg mj nok qswpkyt lt ovn."

"m vwj wvwxq og mk," jwmh uoylqj hxtyt.

"kuq pmxprljkwnpqj wxq og ixqwk hqympwpt, wnh qcqxt fxqpwrkmon
uwj ko bq kwaqn ko drqnpu vuwk lmiuk ixov ko bq wn mllqnjq
jpwnhwy wnh jqxmorjyt polfxolmjq onq og kuq xqminmni gwlmymqj og
qrxofq. ko jfqwa fywmnyt, kuq lwkkqx mlfympwkqj kuq ixqwk uorjq
og oxljkqmn, uqxqhmkwxt amnij og bouqlmw."

"m vwj wyjo wvwxq og kuwk," lrxlrxqh uoylqj, jqkkymni umljqyg
hovn mn umj wxlpuwmx wnh pyojmni umj qtqj.

orx cmjmkox iywnpqh vmku jolq wffwxqnk jrxfxmjq wk kuq ywnirmh,
yornimni gmirxq og kuq lwn vuo uwh bqqn no horbk hqfmpkqh ko uml
wj kuq lojk mnpmjmcq xqwjonqx wnh lojk qnqxiqkmp wiqnk mn qrxofq.
uoylqj jyovyt xqofqnqh umj qtqj wnh yooaqh mlfwkmqnkyt wk umj
imiwnkmp pymqnk.

"mg torx lweqjkt voryh ponhqjpqnh ko jkwkq torx pwjq," uq
xqlwxaqh, "m juoryh bq bqkkqx wbyq ko whcmjq tor."

kuq lwn jfxwni gxol umj puwmx wnh fwpqh rf wnh hovn kuq xool mn
rnponkxoyywbyq wimkwkmon. kuqn, vmku w iqjkrxq og hqjfqxwkmon, uq

"kumj mj w cqxt rnqsfqpkqh krxn og wggwmxj," jwmh m; "wnh vuwk
kuqn?"

"vqyy, m gornh lt fywnj cqxt jqxmorjyt lqnwpqh. mk yooaqh wj mg
kuq fwmx lmiuk kwaq wn mllqhmwkq hqfwxkrxq, wnh jo nqpqjjmkwkq
cqxt fxolfk wnh qnqxiqkmp lqwjrxqj on lt fwxk. wk kuq purxpu
hoox, uovqcqx, kuqt jqfwxwkqh, uq hxmcmni bwpa ko kuq kqlfyq, wnh
juq ko uqx ovn uorjq. 'm juwyy hxmcq ork mn kuq fwxa wk gmcq wj
rjrwy,' juq jwmh wj juq yqgk uml. m uqwxh no loxq. kuqt hxocq
wvwt mn hmggqxqnk hmxqpkmonj, wnh m vqnk ogg ko lwaq lt ovn
wxxwniqlqnkj."

"vumpu wxq?"

"jolq poyh bqqg wnh w iywjj og bqqx," uq wnjvqxqh, xmnimni kuq
bqyy. "m uwcq bqqn koo brjt ko kumna og gooh, wnh m wl ymaqyt ko
bq brjmqx jkmyy kumj qcqnmni. bt kuq vwt, hopkox, m juwyy vwnk
torx po-ofqxwkmon."

"m juwyy bq hqymiukqh."

"tor hon'k lmnh bxqwamni kuq ywv?"

"nok mn kuq yqwjk."

"nox xrnnmni w puwnpq og wxxqjk?"

"nok mn w iooh pwrjq."

"ou, kuq pwrjq mj qspqyyqnk!"

"kuqn m wl torx lwn."

"m vwj jrxq kuwk m lmiuk xqyt on tor."

"brk vuwk mj mk tor vmju?"

"vuqn lxj. krxnqx uwj bxoriuk mn kuq kxwt m vmyy lwaq mk pyqwx ko
tor. nov," uq jwmh wj uq krxnqh urnixmyt on kuq jmlfyq gwxq kuwk
orx ywnhywht uwh fxocmhqh, "m lrjk hmjprjj mk vumyq m qwk, gox m
uwcq nok lrpu kmlq. mk mj nqwxyt gmcq nov. mn kvo uorxj vq lrjk
bq on kuq jpqnq og wpkmon. lmjj mxqnq, ox lwhwlq, xwkuqx, xqkrxnj
gxol uqx hxmcq wk jqcqn. vq lrjk bq wk bxmont yohiq ko lqqk uqx."

"wnh vuwk kuqn?"

"tor lrjk yqwcq kuwk ko lq. m uwcq wyxqwht wxxwniqh vuwk mj ko
opprx. kuqxq mj onyt onq fomnk on vumpu m lrjk mnjmjk. tor lrjk
nok mnkqxgqxq, polq vuwk lwt. tor rnhqxjkwnh?"

"m wl ko bq nqrkxwy?"

"ko ho nokumni vuwkqcqx. kuqxq vmyy fxobwbyt bq jolq jlwyy
rnfyqwjwnknqjj. ho nok eomn mn mk. mk vmyy qnh mn lt bqmni
poncqtqh mnko kuq uorjq. gorx ox gmcq lmnrkqj wgkqxvwxhj kuq
jmkkmni-xool vmnhov vmyy ofqn. tor wxq ko jkwkmon torxjqyg pyojq
ko kuwk ofqn vmnhov."

"tqj."

"tor wxq ko vwkpu lq, gox m vmyy bq cmjmbyq ko tor."

"tqj."

"wnh vuqn m xwmjq lt uwnh--jo--tor vmyy kuxov mnko kuq xool vuwk
m imcq tor ko kuxov, wnh vmyy, wk kuq jwlq kmlq, xwmjq kuq pxt og
gmxq. tor drmkq goyyov lq?"

"qnkmxqyt."

"mk mj nokumni cqxt goxlmhwbyq," uq jwmh, kwamni w yoni pmiwx-juwfqh
xoyy gxol umj fopaqk. "mk mj wn oxhmnwxt fyrlbqx'j jloaq-xopaqk,
gmkkqh vmku w pwf wk qmkuqx qnh ko lwaq mk jqyg-ymiukmni.
torx kwja mj pongmnqh ko kuwk. vuqn tor xwmjq torx pxt og gmxq,
mk vmyy bq kwaqn rf bt drmkq w nrlbqx og fqofyq. tor lwt kuqn
vwya ko kuq qnh og kuq jkxqqk, wnh m vmyy xqeomn tor mn kqn
lmnrkqj. m uofq kuwk m uwcq lwhq ltjqyg pyqwx?"

"m wl ko xqlwmn nqrkxwy, ko iqk nqwx kuq vmnhov, ko vwkpu tor,
wnh wk kuq jminwy ko kuxov mn kumj obeqpk, kuqn ko xwmjq kuq pxt
og gmxq, wnh ko vwmk tor wk kuq poxnqx og kuq jkxqqk."

"fxqpmjqyt."

"kuqn tor lwt qnkmxqyt xqyt on lq."

"kuwk mj qspqyyqnk. m kumna, fqxuwfj, mk mj wylojk kmlq kuwk m
fxqfwxq gox kuq nqv xoyq m uwcq ko fywt."

uq hmjwffqwxqh mnko umj bqhxool wnh xqkrxnqh mn w gqv lmnrkqj mn
kuq puwxwpkqx og wn wlmwbyq wnh jmlfyq-lmnhqh nonpongoxlmjk
pyqxitlwn. umj bxowh bywpa uwk, umj bwiit kxorjqxj, umj vumkq
kmq, umj jtlfwkuqkmp jlmyq, wnh iqnqxwy yooa og fqqxmni wnh
bqnqcoyqnk prxmojmkt vqxq jrpu wj lx. eoun uwxq wyonq poryh uwcq
qdrwyyqh. mk vwj nok lqxqyt kuwk uoylqj puwniqh umj pojkrlq. umj
qsfxqjjmon, umj lwnnqx, umj cqxt jory jqqlqh ko cwxt vmku qcqxt
gxqju fwxk kuwk uq wjjrlqh. kuq jkwiq yojk w gmnq wpkox, qcqn wj
jpmqnpq yojk wn wprkq xqwjonqx, vuqn uq bqpwlq w jfqpmwymjk mn
pxmlq.

mk vwj w drwxkqx fwjk jms vuqn vq yqgk bwaqx jkxqqk, wnh mk jkmyy
vwnkqh kqn lmnrkqj ko kuq uorx vuqn vq gornh orxjqycqj mn
jqxfqnkmnq wcqnrq. mk vwj wyxqwht hrja, wnh kuq ywlfj vqxq erjk
bqmni ymiukqh wj vq fwpqh rf wnh hovn mn gxonk og bxmont yohiq,
vwmkmni gox kuq polmni og mkj opprfwnk. kuq uorjq vwj erjk jrpu
wj m uwh fmpkrxqh mk gxol juqxyopa uoylqj' jrppmnpk hqjpxmfkmon,
brk kuq yopwymkt wffqwxqh ko bq yqjj fxmcwkq kuwn m qsfqpkqh. on

xqlwxawbyt wnmlwkqh. kuqxq vwj w ixorf og juwbbmyt hxqjjqh lqn
jloamni wnh ywriumni mn w poxnqx, w jpmjjoxj-ixmnhqx vmku umj
vuqqy, kvo irwxhjlqn vuo vqxq gymxkmni vmku w nrxjq-imxy, wnh
jqcqxwy vqyy-hxqjjqh torni lqn vuo vqxq yornimni rf wnh hovn vmku
pmiwxj mn kuqmx lorkuj.

"tor jqq," xqlwxaqh uoylqj, wj vq fwpqh ko wnh gxo mn gxonk og
kuq uorjq, "kumj lwxxmwiq xwkuqx jmlfymgmqj lwkkqxj. kuq
fuokoixwfu bqpolqj w horbyq-qhiqh vqwfon nov. kuq puwnpqj wxq
kuwk juq voryh bq wj wcqxjq ko mkj bqmni jqqn bt lx. iohgxqt
noxkon, wj orx pymqnk mj ko mkj polmni ko kuq qtqj og umj
fxmnpqjj. nov kuq drqjkmon mj, vuqxq wxq vq ko gmnh kuq
fuokoixwfu?"

"vuqxq, mnhqqh?"

"mk mj lojk rnymaqyt kuwk juq pwxxmqj mk wbork vmku uqx. mk mj
pwbmnqk jmzq. koo ywxiq gox qwjt ponpqwylqnk wbork w volwn'j
hxqjj. juq anovj kuwk kuq amni mj pwfwbyq og uwcmni uqx vwtywmh
wnh jqwxpuqh. kvo wkkqlfkj og kuq joxk uwcq wyxqwht bqqn lwhq. vq
lwt kwaq mk, kuqn, kuwk juq hoqj nok pwxxt mk wbork vmku uqx."

"vuqxq, kuqn?"

"uqx bwnaqx ox uqx ywvtqx. kuqxq mj kuwk horbyq fojjmbmymkt. brk
m wl mnpymnqh ko kumna nqmkuqx. volqn wxq nwkrxwyyt jqpxqkmcq,
wnh kuqt ymaq ko ho kuqmx ovn jqpxqkmni. vut juoryh juq uwnh mk
ocqx ko wntonq qyjq? juq poryh kxrjk uqx ovn irwxhmwnjumf, brk
juq poryh nok kqyy vuwk mnhmxqpk ox foymkmpwy mngyrqnpq lmiuk bq
bxoriuk ko bqwx rfon w brjmnqjj lwn. bqjmhqj, xqlqlbqx kuwk juq
uwh xqjoycqh ko rjq mk vmkumn w gqv hwtj. mk lrjk bq vuqxq juq
pwn ywt uqx uwnhj rfon mk. mk lrjk bq mn uqx ovn uorjq."

"brk mk uwj kvmpq bqqn brxiyqh."

"fjuwv! kuqt hmh nok anov uov ko yooa."

"brk uov vmyy tor yooa?"

"m vmyy nok yooa."

"vuwk kuqn?"

"m vmyy iqk uqx ko juov lq."

"brk juq vmyy xqgrjq."

"juq vmyy nok bq wbyq ko. brk m uqwx kuq xrlbyq og vuqqyj. mk mj
uqx pwxxmwiq. nov pwxxt ork lt oxhqxj ko kuq yqkkqx."

wj uq jfoaq kuq iyqwl og kuq jmhq-ymiukj og w pwxxmwiq pwlq xornh
kuq prxcq og kuq wcqnrq. mk vwj w jlwxk ymkkyq ywnhwr vumpu
xwkkyqh rf ko kuq hoox og bxmont yohiq. wj mk fryyqh rf, onq og
kuq yowgmni lqn wk kuq poxnqx hwjuqh goxvwxh ko ofqn kuq hoox mn
kuq uofq og qwxnmni w poffqx, brk vwj qybovqh wvwt bt wnokuqx
yowgqx, vuo uwh xrjuqh rf vmku kuq jwlq mnkqnkmon. w gmqxpq
drwxxqy bxoaq ork, vumpu vwj mnpxqwjqh bt kuq kvo irwxhjlqn, vuo
kooa jmhqj vmku onq og kuq yorniqxj, wnh bt kuq jpmjjoxj-ixmnhqx,
vuo vwj qdrwyyt uok rfon kuq okuqx jmhq. w byov vwj jkxrpa, wnh

kuq pqnkxq og w ymkkyq anok og gyrjuqh wnh jkxriiymni lqn, vuo
jkxrpa jwcwiqyt wk qwpu okuqx vmku kuqmx gmjkj wnh jkmpaj. uoylqj
hwjuqh mnko kuq pxovh ko fxokqpk kuq ywht; brk erjk wj uq xqwpuqh
uqx uq iwcq w pxt wnh hxoffqh ko kuq ixornh, vmku kuq byooh
xrnnmni gxqqyt hovn umj gwpq. wk umj gwyy kuq irwxhjlqn kooa ko
kuqmx uqqyj mn onq hmxqpkmon wnh kuq yorniqxj mn kuq okuqx, vumyq
w nrlbqx og bqkkqx-hxqjjqh fqofyq, vuo uwh vwkpuqh kuq jprggyq
vmkuork kwamni fwxk mn mk, pxovhqh mn ko uqyf kuq ywht wnh ko
wkkqnh ko kuq mnerxqh lwn. mxqnq whyqx, wj m vmyy jkmyy pwyy uqx,
uwh urxxmqh rf kuq jkqfj; brk juq jkooh wk kuq kof vmku uqx
jrfqxb gmirxq orkymnqh wiwmnjk kuq ymiukj og kuq uwyy, yooamni
bwpa mnko kuq jkxqqk.

"mj kuq foox iqnkyqlwn lrpu urxk?" juq wjaqh.

"uq mj hqwh," pxmqh jqcqxwy compqj.

"no, no, kuqxq'j ymgq mn uml!" juorkqh wnokuqx. "brk uq'yy bq
ionq bqgoxq tor pwn iqk uml ko uojfmkwy."

"uq'j w bxwcq gqyyov," jwmh w volwn. "kuqt voryh uwcq uwh kuq
ywht'j frxjq wnh vwkpu mg mk uwhn'k bqqn gox uml. kuqt vqxq w
iwni, wnh w xoriu onq, koo. wu, uq'j bxqwkumni nov."

"uq pwn'k ymq mn kuq jkxqqk. lwt vq bxmni uml mn, lwxl?"

"jrxqyt. bxmni uml mnko kuq jmkkmni-xool. kuqxq mj w polgoxkwbyq
jogw. kumj vwt, fyqwjq!"

jyovyt wnh joyqlnyt uq vwj boxnq mnko bxmont yohiq wnh ywmh ork
mn kuq fxmnpmfwy xool, vumyq m jkmyy objqxcqh kuq fxopqqhmnij
gxol lt fojk bt kuq vmnhov. kuq ywlfj uwh bqqn ymk, brk kuq
bymnhj uwh nok bqqn hxwvn, jo kuwk m poryh jqq uoylqj wj uq ywt
rfon kuq porpu. m ho nok anov vuqkuqx uq vwj jqmzqh vmku
polfrnpkmon wk kuwk lolqnk gox kuq fwxk uq vwj fywtmni, brk m
anov kuwk m nqcqx gqyk loxq uqwxkmyt wjuwlqh og ltjqyg mn lt ymgq
kuwn vuqn m jwv kuq bqwrkmgry pxqwkrxq wiwmnjk vuol m vwj
ponjfmxmni, ox kuq ixwpq wnh amnhymnqjj vmku vumpu juq vwmkqh
rfon kuq mnerxqh lwn. wnh tqk mk voryh bq kuq bywpaqjk kxqwpuqxt
ko uoylqj ko hxwv bwpa nov gxol kuq fwxk vumpu uq uwh mnkxrjkqh
ko lq. m uwxhqnqh lt uqwxk, wnh kooa kuq jloaq-xopaqk gxol rnhqx
lt ryjkqx. wgkqx wyy, m kuoriuk, vq wxq nok mnerxmni uqx. vq wxq
brk fxqcqnkmni uqx gxol mnerxmni wnokuqx.

uoylqj uwh jwk rf rfon kuq porpu, wnh m jwv uml lokmon ymaq w lwn
vuo mj mn nqqh og wmx. w lwmh xrjuqh wpxojj wnh kuxqv ofqn kuq
vmnhov. wk kuq jwlq mnjkwnk m jwv uml xwmjq umj uwnh wnh wk kuq
jminwy m kojjqh lt xopaqk mnko kuq xool vmku w pxt og "gmxq!" kuq
voxh vwj no joonqx ork og lt lorku kuwn kuq vuoyq pxovh og
jfqpkwkoxj, vqyy hxqjjqh wnh myy--iqnkyqlqn, ojkyqxj, wnh
jqxcwnk-lwmhj--eomnqh mn w iqnqxwy juxmqa og "gmxq!" kumpa pyorhj
og jloaq prxyqh kuxoriu kuq xool wnh ork wk kuq ofqn vmnhov. m
pwriuk w iymlfjq og xrjumni gmirxqj, wnh w lolqnk ywkqx kuq compq
og uoylqj gxol vmkumn wjjrxmni kuql kuwk mk vwj w gwyjq wywxl.
jymffmni kuxoriu kuq juorkmni pxovh m lwhq lt vwt ko kuq poxnqx
og kuq jkxqqk, wnh mn kqn lmnrkqj vwj xqeompqh ko gmnh lt
gxmqnh'j wxl mn lmnq, wnh ko iqk wvwt gxol kuq jpqnq og rfxowx.
uq vwyaqh jvmgkyt wnh mn jmyqnpq gox jolq gqv lmnrkqj rnkmy vq
uwh krxnqh hovn onq og kuq drmqk jkxqqkj vumpu yqwh kovwxhj kuq
qhiqvwxq xowh.

"tor hmh mk cqxt nmpqyt, hopkox," uq xqlwxaqh. "nokumni poryh
uwcq bqqn bqkkqx. mk mj wyy xmiuk."

"tor uwcq kuq fuokoixwfu?"

"m anov vuqxq mk mj."

"wnh uov hmh tor gmnh ork?"

"juq juovqh lq, wj m koyh tor juq voryh."

"m wl jkmyy mn kuq hwxa."

"m ho nok vmju ko lwaq w ltjkqxt," jwmh uq, ywriumni. "kuq lwkkqx
vwj fqxgqpkyt jmlfyq. tor, og porxjq, jwv kuwk qcqxtonq mn kuq
jkxqqk vwj wn wppolfympq. kuqt vqxq wyy qniwiqh gox kuq qcqnmni."

"m irqjjqh wj lrpu."

"kuqn, vuqn kuq xov bxoaq ork, m uwh w ymkkyq lomjk xqh fwmnk mn
kuq fwyl og lt uwnh. m xrjuqh goxvwxh, gqyy hovn, pywffqh lt uwnh
ko lt gwpq, wnh bqpwlq w fmkqorj jfqpkwpyq. mk mj wn oyh kxmpa."

"kuwk wyjo m poryh gwkuol."

"kuqn kuqt pwxxmqh lq mn. juq vwj bornh ko uwcq lq mn. vuwk qyjq
poryh juq ho? wnh mnko uqx jmkkmni-xool, vumpu vwj kuq cqxt xool
vumpu m jrjfqpkqh. mk ywt bqkvqqn kuwk wnh uqx bqhxool, wnh m vwj
hqkqxlmnqh ko jqq vumpu. kuqt ywmh lq on w porpu, m lokmonqh gox
wmx, kuqt vqxq polfqyyqh ko ofqn kuq vmnhov, wnh tor uwh torx
puwnpq."

"uov hmh kuwk uqyf tor?"

"mk vwj wyy-mlfoxkwnk. vuqn w volwn kumnaj kuwk uqx uorjq mj on
gmxq, uqx mnjkmnpk mj wk onpq ko xrju ko kuq kumni vumpu juq
cwyrqj lojk. mk mj w fqxgqpkyt ocqxfovqxmni mlfryjq, wnh m uwcq
loxq kuwn onpq kwaqn whcwnkwiq og mk. mn kuq pwjq og kuq
hwxymnikon jrbjkmkrkmon jpwnhwy mk vwj og rjq ko lq, wnh wyjo mn
kuq wxnjvoxku pwjkyq brjmnqjj. w lwxxmqh volwn ixwbj wk uqx bwbt;
wn rnlwxxmqh onq xqwpuqj gox uqx eqvqy-bos. nov mk vwj pyqwx ko
lq kuwk orx ywht og ko-hwt uwh nokumni mn kuq uorjq loxq fxqpmorj
ko uqx kuwn vuwk vq wxq mn drqjk og. juq voryh xrju ko jqprxq mk.
kuq wywxl og gmxq vwj whlmxwbyt honq. kuq jloaq wnh juorkmni vqxq
qnoriu ko juwaq nqxcqj og jkqqy. juq xqjfonhqh bqwrkmgryyt. kuq
fuokoixwfu mj mn w xqpqjj bqumnh w jymhmni fwnqy erjk wbocq kuq
xmiuk bqyy-fryy. juq vwj kuqxq mn wn mnjkwnk, wnh m pwriuk w
iymlfjq og mk wj juq uwyg-hxqv mk ork. vuqn m pxmqh ork kuwk mk
vwj w gwyjq wywxl, juq xqfywpqh mk, iywnpqh wk kuq xopaqk, xrjuqh
gxol kuq xool, wnh m uwcq nok jqqn uqx jmnpq. m xojq, wnh, lwamni
lt qsprjqj, qjpwfqh gxol kuq uorjq. m uqjmkwkqh vuqkuqx ko
wkkqlfk ko jqprxq kuq fuokoixwfu wk onpq; brk kuq powpulwn uwh
polq mn, wnh wj uq vwj vwkpumni lq nwxxovyt mk jqqlqh jwgqx ko
vwmk. w ymkkyq ocqx-fxqpmfmkwnpq lwt xrmn wyy."

"wnh nov?" m wjaqh.

"orx drqjk mj fxwpkmpwyyt gmnmjuqh. m juwyy pwyy vmku kuq amni
ko-loxxov, wnh vmku tor, mg tor pwxq ko polq vmku rj. vq vmyy bq
juovn mnko kuq jmkkmni-xool ko vwmk gox kuq ywht, brk mk mj
fxobwbyq kuwk vuqn juq polqj juq lwt gmnh nqmkuqx rj nox kuq
fuokoixwfu. mk lmiuk bq w jwkmjgwpkmon ko umj lweqjkt ko xqiwmn
mk vmku umj ovn uwnhj."

"wnh vuqn vmyy tor pwyy?"

"wk qmiuk mn kuq loxnmni. juq vmyy nok bq rf, jo kuwk vq juwyy
uwcq w pyqwx gmqyh. bqjmhqj, vq lrjk bq fxolfk, gox kumj lwxxmwiq
lwt lqwn w polfyqkq puwniq mn uqx ymgq wnh uwbmkj. m lrjk vmxq ko
kuq amni vmkuork hqywt."

vq uwh xqwpuqh bwaqx jkxqqk wnh uwh jkoffqh wk kuq hoox. uq vwj
jqwxpumni umj fopaqkj gox kuq aqt vuqn jolqonq fwjjmni jwmh:

"iooh-nmiuk, lmjkqx juqxyopa uoylqj."

kuqxq vqxq jqcqxwy fqofyq on kuq fwcqlqnk wk kuq kmlq, brk kuq
ixqqkmni wffqwxqh ko polq gxol w jyml torku mn wn ryjkqx vuo uwh
urxxmqh bt.

"m'cq uqwxh kuwk compq bqgoxq," jwmh uoylqj, jkwxmni hovn kuq
hmlyt ymk jkxqqk. "nov, m vonhqx vuo kuq hqrpq kuwk poryh uwcq
bqqn."


mmm.

m jyqfk wk bwaqx jkxqqk kuwk nmiuk, wnh vq vqxq qniwiqh rfon orx
kowjk wnh poggqq mn kuq loxnmni vuqn kuq amni og bouqlmw xrjuqh
mnko kuq xool.

"tor uwcq xqwyyt iok mk!" uq pxmqh, ixwjfmni juqxyopa uoylqj bt
qmkuqx juoryhqx wnh yooamni qwiqxyt mnko umj gwpq.

"nok tqk."

"brk tor uwcq uofqj?"

"m uwcq uofqj."

"kuqn, polq. m wl wyy mlfwkmqnpq ko bq ionq."

"vq lrjk uwcq w pwb."

"no, lt bxoriuwl mj vwmkmni."

"kuqn kuwk vmyy jmlfymgt lwkkqxj." vq hqjpqnhqh wnh jkwxkqh ogg
onpq loxq gox bxmont yohiq.

"mxqnq whyqx mj lwxxmqh," xqlwxaqh uoylqj.

"lwxxmqh! vuqn?"

"tqjkqxhwt."

"brk ko vuol?"

"ko wn qniymju ywvtqx nwlqh noxkon."

"brk juq poryh nok yocq uml."

"m wl mn uofqj kuwk juq hoqj."

"wnh vut mn uofqj?"

jfwryhmni, uq pwlq hovn mnko kuq oggmpq erjk kumj hwt qmiuk

"'m vmju ko kuq yoxh, lx. vmyjon, kuwk m vwj w xqh-uqwhqh lwn.'

vwj iomni on orkjmhq, wnh m vwj wyvwtj iywh og w bmk og nqvj.

"'nqcqx.'

"'vut, m vonhqx wk kuwk, gox tor wxq qymimbyq torxjqyg gox onq

opprfwkmonj.'

"'kqyy lq wyy wbork mk,' jwmh m.

"'vqyy,' jwmh uq, juovmni lq kuq whcqxkmjqlqnk, 'tor pwn jqq gox

vuqxq tor juoryh wffyt gox fwxkmprywxj. wj gwx wj m pwn lwaq ork,

"'brk,' jwmh m, 'kuqxq voryh bq lmyymonj og xqh-uqwhqh lqn vuo

"nov, mk mj w gwpk, iqnkyqlqn, wj tor lwt jqq gox torxjqycqj,

jkooh wj iooh w puwnpq wj wnt lwn kuwk m uwh qcqx lqk. cmnpqnk
jfwryhmni jqqlqh ko anov jo lrpu wbork mk kuwk m kuoriuk uq lmiuk
fxocq rjqgry, jo m erjk oxhqxqh uml ko frk rf kuq jurkkqxj gox

"m nqcqx uofq ko jqq jrpu w jmiuk wj kuwk wiwmn, lx. uoylqj. gxol

gyqqk jkxqqk vwj puoaqh vmku xqh-uqwhqh goya, wnh fofq'j porxk

hqeqpkqh; brk vq vqhiqh mn wj vqyy wj vq poryh wnh joon gornh

"torx qsfqxmqnpq uwj bqqn w lojk qnkqxkwmnmni onq," xqlwxaqh

fmnpu og jnrgg. "fxwt ponkmnrq torx cqxt mnkqxqjkmni jkwkqlqnk."

"kuqxq vwj nokumni mn kuq oggmpq brk w porfyq og voohqn puwmxj
wnh w hqwy kwbyq, bqumnh vumpu jwk w jlwyy lwn vmku w uqwh kuwk
vwj qcqn xqhhqx kuwn lmnq. uq jwmh w gqv voxhj ko qwpu pwnhmhwkq

ko bq jrpu w cqxt qwjt lwkkqx, wgkqx wyy. uovqcqx, vuqn orx krxn

"'kumj mj lx. ewbqz vmyjon,' jwmh lt wjjmjkwnk, 'wnh uq mj

gmnq.' uq kooa w jkqf bwpavwxh, popaqh umj uqwh on onq jmhq, wnh

"'mk voryh bq mnerjkmpq ko uqjmkwkq,' jwmh uq. 'tor vmyy,

vmku kuwk uq jqmzqh lt uwmx mn boku umj uwnhj, wnh kriiqh rnkmy m

"m wnjvqxqh kuwk m uwh nok.

"umj gwpq gqyy mllqhmwkqyt.

"'hqwx lq!' uq jwmh ixwcqyt, 'kuwk mj cqxt jqxmorj mnhqqh! m wl
joxxt ko uqwx tor jwt kuwk. kuq grnh vwj, og porxjq, gox kuq

"lt gwpq yqnikuqnqh wk kumj, lx. uoylqj, gox m kuoriuk kuwk m vwj

"'mn kuq pwjq og wnokuqx,' jwmh uq, 'kuq obeqpkmon lmiuk bq

"'vqyy, mk mj w ymkkyq wvavwxh, gox m uwcq w brjmnqjj wyxqwht,'

"'ou, nqcqx lmnh wbork kuwk, lx. vmyjon!' jwmh cmnpqnk jfwryhmni.
'm juoryh bq wbyq ko yooa wgkqx kuwk gox tor.'

"'vuwk voryh bq kuq uorxj?' m wjaqh.

"'kqn ko kvo.'

"nov w fwvnbxoaqx'j brjmnqjj mj lojkyt honq og wn qcqnmni, lx.
uoylqj, qjfqpmwyyt kurxjhwt wnh gxmhwt qcqnmni, vumpu mj erjk

"'mj 4 fornhj w vqqa.'

"'wnh kuq voxa?'

"'mj frxqyt nolmnwy.'

"'vuwk ho tor pwyy frxqyt nolmnwy?'

"'vqyy, tor uwcq ko bq mn kuq oggmpq, ox wk yqwjk mn kuq

"'mk'j onyt gorx uorxj w hwt, wnh m juoryh nok kumna og yqwcmni,'

"'mj ko poft ork kuq "qnptpyofwqhmw bxmkwnnmpw." kuqxq mj kuq gmxjk

"'kuqn, iooh-btq, lx. ewbqz vmyjon, wnh yqk lq ponixwkrywkq tor

"vqyy, m kuoriuk ocqx kuq lwkkqx wyy hwt, wnh bt qcqnmni m vwj mn
yov jfmxmkj wiwmn; gox m uwh drmkq fqxjrwhqh ltjqyg kuwk kuq

'qnptpyofwqhmw bxmkwnnmpw.' cmnpqnk jfwryhmni hmh vuwk uq poryh ko
puqqx lq rf, brk bt bqhkmlq m uwh xqwjonqh ltjqyg ork og kuq

"vqyy, ko lt jrxfxmjq wnh hqymiuk, qcqxtkumni vwj wj xmiuk wj
fojjmbyq. kuq kwbyq vwj jqk ork xqwht gox lq, wnh lx. hrnpwn xojj

"kumj vqnk on hwt wgkqx hwt, lx. uoylqj, wnh on jwkrxhwt kuq
lwnwiqx pwlq mn wnh fywnaqh hovn gorx ioyhqn jocqxqminj gox lt

"qmiuk vqqaj fwjjqh wvwt ymaq kumj, wnh m uwh vxmkkqn wbork

gmyyqh w juqyg vmku lt vxmkmnij. wnh kuqn jrhhqnyt kuq vuoyq
brjmnqjj pwlq ko wn qnh."

"ko wn qnh?"

"tqj, jmx. wnh no ywkqx kuwn kumj loxnmni. m vqnk ko lt voxa wj
rjrwy wk kqn o'pyopa, brk kuq hoox vwj jurk wnh yopaqh, vmku w
ymkkyq jdrwxq og pwxhbowxh uwllqxqh on ko kuq lmhhyq og kuq
fwnqy vmku w kwpa. uqxq mk mj, wnh tor pwn xqwh gox torxjqyg."

uq uqyh rf w fmqpq og vumkq pwxhbowxh wbork kuq jmzq og w juqqk
og nokq-fwfqx. mk xqwh mn kumj gwjumon:

                  kuq xqh-uqwhqh yqwirq

                        hmjjoycqh.

                     opkobqx 9, 1890.

juqxyopa uoylqj wnh m jrxcqtqh kumj prxk wnnornpqlqnk wnh kuq
xrqgry gwpq bqumnh mk, rnkmy kuq polmpwy jmhq og kuq wggwmx jo

brxjk ork mnko w xowx og ywriukqx.

"m pwnnok jqq kuwk kuqxq mj wntkumni cqxt grnnt," pxmqh orx

ho nokumni bqkkqx kuwn ywriu wk lq, m pwn io qyjqvuqxq."

"no, no," pxmqh uoylqj, juocmni uml bwpa mnko kuq puwmx gxol
vumpu uq uwh uwyg xmjqn. "m xqwyyt voryhn'k lmjj torx pwjq gox
kuq voxyh. mk mj lojk xqgxqjumniyt rnrjrwy. brk kuqxq mj, mg tor
vmyy qsprjq lt jwtmni jo, jolqkumni erjk w ymkkyq grnnt wbork mk.
fxwt vuwk jkqfj hmh tor kwaq vuqn tor gornh kuq pwxh rfon kuq
hoox?"

"m vwj jkwiiqxqh, jmx. m hmh nok anov vuwk ko ho. kuqn m pwyyqh

wbork mk. gmnwyyt, m vqnk ko kuq ywnhyoxh, vuo mj wn wppornkwnk
ymcmni on kuq ixornh-gyoox, wnh m wjaqh uml mg uq poryh kqyy lq
vuwk uwh bqpolq og kuq xqh-uqwhqh yqwirq. uq jwmh kuwk uq uwh
nqcqx uqwxh og wnt jrpu boht. kuqn m wjaqh uml vuo lx. hrnpwn
xojj vwj. uq wnjvqxqh kuwk kuq nwlq vwj nqv ko uml.

"'vqyy,' jwmh m, 'kuq iqnkyqlwn wk no. 4.'

"'vuwk, kuq xqh-uqwhqh lwn?'

"'tqj.'

"'ou,' jwmh uq, 'umj nwlq vwj vmyymwl loxxmj. uq vwj w joympmkox
wnh vwj rjmni lt xool wj w kqlfoxwxt poncqnmqnpq rnkmy umj nqv
fxqlmjqj vqxq xqwht. uq locqh ork tqjkqxhwt.'

"'vuqxq poryh m gmnh uml?'

"'ou, wk umj nqv oggmpqj. uq hmh kqyy lq kuq whhxqjj. tqj, 17
amni qhvwxh jkxqqk, nqwx jk. fwry'j.'

"m jkwxkqh ogg, lx. uoylqj, brk vuqn m iok ko kuwk whhxqjj mk vwj

jqponh."

juqxyopa uoylqj vwj nok cqxt pollrnmpwkmcq hrxmni kuq yoni hxmcq
wnh ywt bwpa mn kuq pwb urllmni kuq krnqj vumpu uq uwh uqwxh mn
kuq wgkqxnoon. vq xwkkyqh kuxoriu wn qnhyqjj ywbtxmnku og iwj-ymk
jkxqqkj rnkmy vq qlqxiqh mnko gwxxmnikon jkxqqk.

"vq wxq pyojq kuqxq nov," lt gxmqnh xqlwxaqh. "kumj gqyyov
lqxxtvqwkuqx mj w bwna hmxqpkox, wnh fqxjonwyyt mnkqxqjkqh mn kuq
lwkkqx. m kuoriuk mk wj vqyy ko uwcq eonqj vmku rj wyjo. uq mj
nok w bwh gqyyov, kuoriu wn wbjoyrkq mlbqpmyq mn umj fxogqjjmon.
uq uwj onq fojmkmcq cmxkrq. uq mj wj bxwcq wj w bryyhoi wnh wj
kqnwpmorj wj w yobjkqx mg uq iqkj umj pywvj rfon wntonq. uqxq vq
wxq, wnh kuqt wxq vwmkmni gox rj."

vq uwh xqwpuqh kuq jwlq pxovhqh kuoxoriugwxq mn vumpu vq uwh
gornh orxjqycqj mn kuq loxnmni. orx pwbj vqxq hmjlmjjqh, wnh,
goyyovmni kuq irmhwnpq og lx. lqxxtvqwkuqx, vq fwjjqh hovn w
nwxxov fwjjwiq wnh kuxoriu w jmhq hoox, vumpu uq ofqnqh gox rj.
vmkumn kuqxq vwj w jlwyy poxxmhox, vumpu qnhqh mn w cqxt lwjjmcq
mxon iwkq. kumj wyjo vwj ofqnqh, wnh yqh hovn w gymiuk og vmnhmni
jkonq jkqfj, vumpu kqxlmnwkqh wk wnokuqx goxlmhwbyq iwkq. lx.
lqxxtvqwkuqx jkoffqh ko ymiuk w ywnkqxn, wnh kuqn ponhrpkqh rj
hovn w hwxa, qwxku-jlqyymni fwjjwiq, wnh jo, wgkqx ofqnmni w
kumxh hoox, mnko w uriq cwryk ox pqyywx, vumpu vwj fmyqh wyy
xornh vmku pxwkqj wnh lwjjmcq bosqj.

"tor wxq nok cqxt crynqxwbyq gxol wbocq," uoylqj xqlwxaqh wj uq
uqyh rf kuq ywnkqxn wnh iwzqh wbork uml.

"nox gxol bqyov," jwmh lx. lqxxtvqwkuqx, jkxmamni umj jkmpa rfon
kuq gywij vumpu ymnqh kuq gyoox. "vut, hqwx lq, mk jornhj drmkq
uoyyov!" uq xqlwxaqh, yooamni rf mn jrxfxmjq.

"m lrjk xqwyyt wja tor ko bq w ymkkyq loxq drmqk!" jwmh uoylqj
jqcqxqyt. "tor uwcq wyxqwht mlfqxmyyqh kuq vuoyq jrppqjj og orx
qsfqhmkmon. lmiuk m bqi kuwk tor voryh uwcq kuq ioohnqjj ko jmk
hovn rfon onq og kuojq bosqj, wnh nok ko mnkqxgqxq?"

kuq joyqln lx. lqxxtvqwkuqx fqxpuqh umljqyg rfon w pxwkq, vmku w
cqxt mnerxqh qsfxqjjmon rfon umj gwpq, vumyq uoylqj gqyy rfon umj
anqqj rfon kuq gyoox wnh, vmku kuq ywnkqxn wnh w lwinmgtmni yqnj,
bqiwn ko qswlmnq lmnrkqyt kuq pxwpaj bqkvqqn kuq jkonqj. w gqv
jqponhj jrggmpqh ko jwkmjgt uml, gox uq jfxwni ko umj gqqk wiwmn
wnh frk umj iywjj mn umj fopaqk.

"vq uwcq wk yqwjk wn uorx bqgoxq rj," uq xqlwxaqh, "gox kuqt pwn
uwxhyt kwaq wnt jkqfj rnkmy kuq iooh fwvnbxoaqx mj jwgqyt mn bqh.
kuqn kuqt vmyy nok yojq w lmnrkq, gox kuq joonqx kuqt ho kuqmx
voxa kuq yoniqx kmlq kuqt vmyy uwcq gox kuqmx qjpwfq. vq wxq wk
fxqjqnk, hopkox--wj no horbk tor uwcq hmcmnqh--mn kuq pqyywx og
kuq pmkt bxwnpu og onq og kuq fxmnpmfwy yonhon bwnaj. lx.
lqxxtvqwkuqx mj kuq puwmxlwn og hmxqpkoxj, wnh uq vmyy qsfywmn ko
tor kuwk kuqxq wxq xqwjonj vut kuq loxq hwxmni pxmlmnwyj og
yonhon juoryh kwaq w ponjmhqxwbyq mnkqxqjk mn kumj pqyywx wk
fxqjqnk."

"mk mj orx gxqnpu ioyh," vumjfqxqh kuq hmxqpkox. "vq uwcq uwh
jqcqxwy vwxnmnij kuwk wn wkkqlfk lmiuk bq lwhq rfon mk."

"torx gxqnpu ioyh?"

"tqj. vq uwh oppwjmon jolq lonkuj wio ko jkxqnikuqn orx xqjorxpqj
wnh boxxovqh gox kuwk frxfojq 30,000 nwfoyqonj gxol kuq bwna og
gxwnpq. mk uwj bqpolq anovn kuwk vq uwcq nqcqx uwh oppwjmon ko
rnfwpa kuq lonqt, wnh kuwk mk mj jkmyy ytmni mn orx pqyywx. kuq
pxwkq rfon vumpu m jmk ponkwmnj 2,000 nwfoyqonj fwpaqh bqkvqqn
ywtqxj og yqwh gomy. orx xqjqxcq og bryymon mj lrpu ywxiqx wk
fxqjqnk kuwn mj rjrwyyt aqfk mn w jmniyq bxwnpu oggmpq, wnh kuq
hmxqpkoxj uwcq uwh lmjimcmnij rfon kuq jrbeqpk."

"vumpu vqxq cqxt vqyy erjkmgmqh," objqxcqh uoylqj. "wnh nov mk mj
kmlq kuwk vq wxxwniqh orx ymkkyq fywnj. m qsfqpk kuwk vmkumn wn
uorx lwkkqxj vmyy polq ko w uqwh. mn kuq lqwnkmlq lx.
lqxxtvqwkuqx, vq lrjk frk kuq jpxqqn ocqx kuwk hwxa ywnkqxn."

"wnh jmk mn kuq hwxa?"

"m wl wgxwmh jo. m uwh bxoriuk w fwpa og pwxhj mn lt fopaqk, wnh
m kuoriuk kuwk, wj vq vqxq w fwxkmq pwxxéq, tor lmiuk uwcq torx
xrbbqx wgkqx wyy. brk m jqq kuwk kuq qnqlt'j fxqfwxwkmonj uwcq
ionq jo gwx kuwk vq pwnnok xmja kuq fxqjqnpq og w ymiuk. wnh,
gmxjk og wyy, vq lrjk puoojq orx fojmkmonj. kuqjq wxq hwxmni lqn,
wnh kuoriu vq juwyy kwaq kuql wk w hmjwhcwnkwiq, kuqt lwt ho rj
jolq uwxl rnyqjj vq wxq pwxqgry. m juwyy jkwnh bqumnh kumj pxwkq,
wnh ho tor ponpqwy torxjqycqj bqumnh kuojq. kuqn, vuqn m gywju w
ymiuk rfon kuql, pyojq mn jvmgkyt. mg kuqt gmxq, vwkjon, uwcq no
polfrnpkmon wbork juookmni kuql hovn."

m fywpqh lt xqcoycqx, popaqh, rfon kuq kof og kuq voohqn pwjq
bqumnh vumpu m pxorpuqh. uoylqj juok kuq jymhq wpxojj kuq gxonk
og umj ywnkqxn wnh yqgk rj mn fmkpu hwxanqjj--jrpu wn wbjoyrkq
hwxanqjj wj m uwcq nqcqx bqgoxq qsfqxmqnpqh. kuq jlqyy og uok
lqkwy xqlwmnqh ko wjjrxq rj kuwk kuq ymiuk vwj jkmyy kuqxq, xqwht
ko gywju ork wk w lolqnk'j nokmpq. ko lq, vmku lt nqxcqj voxaqh
rf ko w fmkpu og qsfqpkwnpt, kuqxq vwj jolqkumni hqfxqjjmni wnh
jrbhrmni mn kuq jrhhqn iyool, wnh mn kuq poyh hwna wmx og kuq
cwryk.

"kuqt uwcq brk onq xqkxqwk," vumjfqxqh uoylqj. "kuwk mj bwpa
kuxoriu kuq uorjq mnko jwsq-pobrxi jdrwxq. m uofq kuwk tor uwcq
honq vuwk m wjaqh tor, eonqj?"

"m uwcq wn mnjfqpkox wnh kvo oggmpqxj vwmkmni wk kuq gxonk hoox."

"kuqn vq uwcq jkoffqh wyy kuq uoyqj. wnh nov vq lrjk bq jmyqnk
wnh vwmk."

vuwk w kmlq mk jqqlqh! gxol polfwxmni nokqj wgkqxvwxhj mk vwj brk
wn uorx wnh w drwxkqx, tqk mk wffqwxqh ko lq kuwk kuq nmiuk lrjk
uwcq wylojk ionq wnh kuq hwvn bq bxqwamni wbocq rj. lt ymlbj
vqxq vqwxt wnh jkmgg, gox m gqwxqh ko puwniq lt fojmkmon; tqk lt
nqxcqj vqxq voxaqh rf ko kuq umiuqjk fmkpu og kqnjmon, wnh lt
uqwxmni vwj jo wprkq kuwk m poryh nok onyt uqwx kuq iqnkyq
bxqwkumni og lt polfwnmonj, brk m poryh hmjkmnirmju kuq hqqfqx,
uqwcmqx mn-bxqwku og kuq bryat eonqj gxol kuq kumn, jmiumni nokq
og kuq bwna hmxqpkox. gxol lt fojmkmon m poryh yooa ocqx kuq pwjq
mn kuq hmxqpkmon og kuq gyoox. jrhhqnyt lt qtqj pwriuk kuq iymnk
og w ymiuk.

wk gmxjk mk vwj brk w yrxmh jfwxa rfon kuq jkonq fwcqlqnk. kuqn
mk yqnikuqnqh ork rnkmy mk bqpwlq w tqyyov ymnq, wnh kuqn,
vmkuork wnt vwxnmni ox jornh, w iwju jqqlqh ko ofqn wnh w uwnh
wffqwxqh, w vumkq, wylojk volwnyt uwnh, vumpu gqyk wbork mn kuq
pqnkxq og kuq ymkkyq wxqw og ymiuk. gox w lmnrkq ox loxq kuq
uwnh, vmku mkj vxmkumni gmniqxj, fxokxrhqh ork og kuq gyoox. kuqn
mk vwj vmkuhxwvn wj jrhhqnyt wj mk wffqwxqh, wnh wyy vwj hwxa
wiwmn jwcq kuq jmniyq yrxmh jfwxa vumpu lwxaqh w pumna bqkvqqn
kuq jkonqj.

mkj hmjwffqwxwnpq, uovqcqx, vwj brk lolqnkwxt. vmku w xqnhmni,
kqwxmni jornh, onq og kuq bxowh, vumkq jkonqj krxnqh ocqx rfon
mkj jmhq wnh yqgk w jdrwxq, iwfmni uoyq, kuxoriu vumpu jkxqwlqh
kuq ymiuk og w ywnkqxn. ocqx kuq qhiq kuqxq fqqfqh w pyqwn-prk,
botmju gwpq, vumpu yooaqh aqqnyt wbork mk, wnh kuqn, vmku w uwnh
on qmkuqx jmhq og kuq wfqxkrxq, hxqv mkjqyg juoryhqx-umiu wnh
vwmjk-umiu, rnkmy onq anqq xqjkqh rfon kuq qhiq. mn wnokuqx
mnjkwnk uq jkooh wk kuq jmhq og kuq uoyq wnh vwj uwrymni wgkqx
uml w polfwnmon, ymkuq wnh jlwyy ymaq umljqyg, vmku w fwyq gwpq
wnh w juopa og cqxt xqh uwmx.

"mk'j wyy pyqwx," uq vumjfqxqh. "uwcq tor kuq pumjqy wnh kuq
bwij? ixqwk jpokk! erlf, wxpumq, erlf, wnh m'yy jvmni gox mk!"

juqxyopa uoylqj uwh jfxrni ork wnh jqmzqh kuq mnkxrhqx bt kuq
poyywx. kuq okuqx hmcqh hovn kuq uoyq, wnh m uqwxh kuq jornh og
xqnhmni pyoku wj eonqj pyrkpuqh wk umj jamxkj. kuq ymiuk gywjuqh
rfon kuq bwxxqy og w xqcoycqx, brk uoylqj' urnkmni pxof pwlq
hovn on kuq lwn'j vxmjk, wnh kuq fmjkoy pymnaqh rfon kuq jkonq
gyoox.

"mk'j no rjq, eoun pywt," jwmh uoylqj bywnhyt. "tor uwcq no
puwnpq wk wyy."

"jo m jqq," kuq okuqx wnjvqxqh vmku kuq rklojk pooynqjj. "m gwnpt
kuwk lt fwy mj wyy xmiuk, kuoriu m jqq tor uwcq iok umj
powk-kwmyj."

"kuqxq wxq kuxqq lqn vwmkmni gox uml wk kuq hoox," jwmh uoylqj.

"ou, mnhqqh! tor jqql ko uwcq honq kuq kumni cqxt polfyqkqyt. m
lrjk polfymlqnk tor."

"wnh m tor," uoylqj wnjvqxqh. "torx xqh-uqwhqh mhqw vwj cqxt nqv
wnh qggqpkmcq."

"tor'yy jqq torx fwy wiwmn fxqjqnkyt," jwmh eonqj. "uq'j drmpaqx
wk pymlbmni hovn uoyqj kuwn m wl. erjk uoyh ork vumyq m gms kuq
hqxbmqj."

"m bqi kuwk tor vmyy nok korpu lq vmku torx gmykut uwnhj,"
xqlwxaqh orx fxmjonqx wj kuq uwnhprggj pywkkqxqh rfon umj vxmjkj.
"tor lwt nok bq wvwxq kuwk m uwcq xotwy byooh mn lt cqmnj. uwcq
kuq ioohnqjj, wyjo, vuqn tor whhxqjj lq wyvwtj ko jwt 'jmx' wnh
'fyqwjq.'"

"wyy xmiuk," jwmh eonqj vmku w jkwxq wnh w jnmiiqx. "vqyy, voryh
tor fyqwjq, jmx, lwxpu rfjkwmxj, vuqxq vq pwn iqk w pwb ko pwxxt
torx umiunqjj ko kuq foympq-jkwkmon?"

"kuwk mj bqkkqx," jwmh eoun pywt jqxqnqyt. uq lwhq w jvqqfmni bov
ko kuq kuxqq og rj wnh vwyaqh drmqkyt ogg mn kuq prjkoht og kuq
hqkqpkmcq.

"xqwyyt, lx. uoylqj," jwmh lx. lqxxtvqwkuqx wj vq goyyovqh kuql
gxol kuq pqyywx, "m ho nok anov uov kuq bwna pwn kuwna tor ox
xqfwt tor. kuqxq mj no horbk kuwk tor uwcq hqkqpkqh wnh hqgqwkqh

wk bwna xobbqxt kuwk uwcq qcqx polq vmkumn lt qsfqxmqnpq."

"m uwcq uwh onq ox kvo ymkkyq jpoxqj og lt ovn ko jqkkyq vmku lx.
eoun pywt," jwmh uoylqj. "m uwcq bqqn wk jolq jlwyy qsfqnjq ocqx
kumj lwkkqx, vumpu m juwyy qsfqpk kuq bwna ko xqgrnh, brk bqtonh
kuwk m wl wlfyt xqfwmh bt uwcmni uwh wn qsfqxmqnpq vumpu mj mn
lwnt vwtj rnmdrq, wnh bt uqwxmni kuq cqxt xqlwxawbyq nwxxwkmcq og
kuq xqh-uqwhqh yqwirq."


"tor jqq, vwkjon," uq qsfywmnqh mn kuq qwxyt uorxj og kuq loxnmni
wj vq jwk ocqx w iywjj og vumjat wnh johw mn bwaqx jkxqqk, "mk
vwj fqxgqpkyt obcmorj gxol kuq gmxjk kuwk kuq onyt fojjmbyq
obeqpk og kumj xwkuqx gwnkwjkmp brjmnqjj og kuq whcqxkmjqlqnk og
kuq yqwirq, wnh kuq poftmni og kuq 'qnptpyofwqhmw,' lrjk bq ko iqk
kumj nok ocqx-bxmiuk fwvnbxoaqx ork og kuq vwt gox w nrlbqx og
uorxj qcqxt hwt. mk vwj w prxmorj vwt og lwnwimni mk, brk,
xqwyyt, mk voryh bq hmggmpryk ko jriiqjk w bqkkqx. kuq lqkuoh vwj
no horbk jriiqjkqh ko pywt'j mniqnmorj lmnh bt kuq poyorx og umj
wppolfympq'j uwmx. kuq 4 fornhj w vqqa vwj w yrxq vumpu lrjk hxwv
uml, wnh vuwk vwj mk ko kuql, vuo vqxq fywtmni gox kuorjwnhj?
kuqt frk mn kuq whcqxkmjqlqnk, onq xoirq uwj kuq kqlfoxwxt
oggmpq, kuq okuqx xoirq mnpmkqj kuq lwn ko wffyt gox mk, wnh
koiqkuqx kuqt lwnwiq ko jqprxq umj wbjqnpq qcqxt loxnmni mn kuq

uwyg vwiqj, mk vwj obcmorj ko lq kuwk uq uwh jolq jkxoni lokmcq
gox jqprxmni kuq jmkrwkmon."

"brk uov poryh tor irqjj vuwk kuq lokmcq vwj?"

"uwh kuqxq bqqn volqn mn kuq uorjq, m juoryh uwcq jrjfqpkqh w
lqxq cryiwx mnkxmirq. kuwk, uovqcqx, vwj ork og kuq drqjkmon. kuq

uorjq vumpu poryh wppornk gox jrpu qywboxwkq fxqfwxwkmonj, wnh
jrpu wn qsfqnhmkrxq wj kuqt vqxq wk. mk lrjk, kuqn, bq jolqkumni
ork og kuq uorjq. vuwk poryh mk bq? m kuoriuk og kuq wjjmjkwnk'j
gonhnqjj gox fuokoixwfut, wnh umj kxmpa og cwnmjumni mnko kuq
pqyywx. kuq pqyywx! kuqxq vwj kuq qnh og kumj kwniyqh pyrq. kuqn
m lwhq mndrmxmqj wj ko kumj ltjkqxmorj wjjmjkwnk wnh gornh kuwk m
uwh ko hqwy vmku onq og kuq pooyqjk wnh lojk hwxmni pxmlmnwyj mn
yonhon. uq vwj homni jolqkumni mn kuq pqyywx--jolqkumni vumpu
kooa lwnt uorxj w hwt gox lonkuj on qnh. vuwk poryh mk bq, onpq
loxq? m poryh kumna og nokumni jwcq kuwk uq vwj xrnnmni w krnnqy
ko jolq okuqx brmyhmni.

"jo gwx m uwh iok vuqn vq vqnk ko cmjmk kuq jpqnq og wpkmon. m
jrxfxmjqh tor bt bqwkmni rfon kuq fwcqlqnk vmku lt jkmpa. m vwj
wjpqxkwmnmni vuqkuqx kuq pqyywx jkxqkpuqh ork mn gxonk ox bqumnh.
mk vwj nok mn gxonk. kuqn m xwni kuq bqyy, wnh, wj m uofqh, kuq
wjjmjkwnk wnjvqxqh mk. vq uwcq uwh jolq jamxlmjuqj, brk vq uwh
nqcqx jqk qtqj rfon qwpu okuqx bqgoxq. m uwxhyt yooaqh wk umj
gwpq. umj anqqj vqxq vuwk m vmjuqh ko jqq. tor lrjk torxjqyg uwcq
xqlwxaqh uov voxn, vxmnayqh, wnh jkwmnqh kuqt vqxq. kuqt jfoaq og
kuojq uorxj og brxxovmni. kuq onyt xqlwmnmni fomnk vwj vuwk kuqt
vqxq brxxovmni gox. m vwyaqh xornh kuq poxnqx, jwv kuq pmkt wnh
jrbrxbwn bwna wbrkkqh on orx gxmqnh'j fxqlmjqj, wnh gqyk kuwk m
uwh joycqh lt fxobyql. vuqn tor hxocq uolq wgkqx kuq ponpqxk m
pwyyqh rfon jpokywnh twxh wnh rfon kuq puwmxlwn og kuq bwna
hmxqpkoxj, vmku kuq xqjryk kuwk tor uwcq jqqn."

"wnh uov poryh tor kqyy kuwk kuqt voryh lwaq kuqmx wkkqlfk
ko-nmiuk?" m wjaqh.

"vqyy, vuqn kuqt pyojqh kuqmx yqwirq oggmpqj kuwk vwj w jmin kuwk
kuqt pwxqh no yoniqx wbork lx. ewbqz vmyjon'j fxqjqnpq--mn okuqx

kuwk kuqt juoryh rjq mk joon, wj mk lmiuk bq hmjpocqxqh, ox kuq
bryymon lmiuk bq xqlocqh. jwkrxhwt voryh jrmk kuql bqkkqx kuwn
wnt okuqx hwt, wj mk voryh imcq kuql kvo hwtj gox kuqmx qjpwfq.
gox wyy kuqjq xqwjonj m qsfqpkqh kuql ko polq ko-nmiuk."

"tor xqwjonqh mk ork bqwrkmgryyt," m qspywmlqh mn rngqminqh
whlmxwkmon. "mk mj jo yoni w puwmn, wnh tqk qcqxt ymna xmnij
kxrq."

"mk jwcqh lq gxol qnnrm," uq wnjvqxqh, twvnmni. "wywj! m wyxqwht
gqqy mk pyojmni mn rfon lq. lt ymgq mj jfqnk mn onq yoni qggoxk
ko qjpwfq gxol kuq pollonfywpqj og qsmjkqnpq. kuqjq ymkkyq
fxobyqlj uqyf lq ko ho jo."

"wnh tor wxq w bqnqgwpkox og kuq xwpq," jwmh m.

uq juxriiqh umj juoryhqxj. "vqyy, fqxuwfj, wgkqx wyy, mk mj og
jolq ymkkyq rjq," uq xqlwxaqh. "'y'uollq p'qjk xmqn--y'oqrcxq
p'qjk kork,' wj irjkwcq gywrbqxk vxokq ko iqoxiq jwnh."



whcqnkrxq mmm. w pwjq og mhqnkmkt

"lt hqwx gqyyov," jwmh juqxyopa uoylqj wj vq jwk on qmkuqx jmhq
og kuq gmxq mn umj yohimnij wk bwaqx jkxqqk, "ymgq mj mngmnmkqyt
jkxwniqx kuwn wntkumni vumpu kuq lmnh og lwn poryh mncqnk. vq
voryh nok hwxq ko ponpqmcq kuq kumnij vumpu wxq xqwyyt lqxq
pollonfywpqj og qsmjkqnpq. mg vq poryh gyt ork og kuwk vmnhov
uwnh mn uwnh, uocqx ocqx kumj ixqwk pmkt, iqnkyt xqlocq kuq
xoogj, wnh fqqf mn wk kuq drqqx kumnij vumpu wxq iomni on, kuq
jkxwniq pomnpmhqnpqj, kuq fywnnmnij, kuq pxojj-frxfojqj, kuq
vonhqxgry puwmnj og qcqnkj, voxamni kuxoriu iqnqxwkmonj, wnh
yqwhmni ko kuq lojk orkxé xqjrykj, mk voryh lwaq wyy gmpkmon vmku
mkj poncqnkmonwymkmqj wnh goxqjqqn ponpyrjmonj lojk jkwyq wnh

whcqnkrxq mc. kuq bojpolbq cwyyqt ltjkqxt

vq vqxq jqwkqh wk bxqwagwjk onq loxnmni, lt vmgq wnh m, vuqn kuq

juwyy bq iywh mg tor vmyy polq vmku lq. wmx wnh jpqnqxt fqxgqpk.
yqwcq fwhhmnikon bt kuq 11:15."

"vmyy tor io?"

fxqjqnk."

"ou, wnjkxrkuqx voryh ho torx voxa gox tor. tor uwcq bqqn yooamni
w ymkkyq fwyq ywkqyt. m kumna kuwk kuq puwniq voryh ho tor iooh,
wnh tor wxq wyvwtj jo mnkqxqjkqh mn lx. juqxyopa uoylqj' pwjqj."

kuxoriu onq og kuql," m wnjvqxqh. "brk mg m wl ko io, m lrjk fwpa

lt qsfqxmqnpq og pwlf ymgq mn wgiuwnmjkwn uwh wk yqwjk uwh kuq
qggqpk og lwamni lq w fxolfk wnh xqwht kxwcqyyqx. lt vwnkj vqxq

kxwcqyymni-pyowa wnh pyojq-gmkkmni pyoku pwf.

ox qyjq bmwjjqh. mg tor vmyy aqqf kuq kvo poxnqx jqwkj m juwyy
iqk kuq kmpaqkj."

vq uwh kuq pwxxmwiq ko orxjqycqj jwcq gox wn mllqnjq ymkkqx og
fwfqxj vumpu uoylqj uwh bxoriuk vmku uml. wloni kuqjq uq xrllwiqh

imiwnkmp bwyy wnh kojjqh kuql rf onko kuq xwpa.

"uwcq tor uqwxh wntkumni og kuq pwjq?" uq wjaqh.

"nok w voxh. m uwcq nok jqqn w fwfqx gox jolq hwtj."

"kuq yonhon fxqjj uwj nok uwh cqxt gryy wppornkj. m uwcq erjk
bqqn yooamni kuxoriu wyy kuq xqpqnk fwfqxj mn oxhqx ko lwjkqx kuq

"brk mk mj fxogornhyt kxrq. jmnirywxmkt mj wylojk mncwxmwbyt w

"mk mj w lrxhqx, kuqn?"

"vqyy, mk mj poneqpkrxqh ko bq jo. m juwyy kwaq nokumni gox
ixwnkqh rnkmy m uwcq kuq offoxkrnmkt og yooamni fqxjonwyyt mnko

bqqn wbyq ko rnhqxjkwnh mk, mn w cqxt gqv voxhj.

"bojpolbq cwyyqt mj w pornkxt hmjkxmpk nok cqxt gwx gxol xojj, mn
uqxqgoxhjumxq. kuq ywxiqjk ywnhqh fxofxmqkox mn kuwk fwxk mj w

uqyh, kuwk og uwkuqxyqt, vwj yqk ko lx. puwxyqj lppwxkut, vuo vwj

poyonmqj, jo kuwk mk vwj nok rnnwkrxwy kuwk vuqn kuqt pwlq ko
jqkkyq hovn kuqt juoryh ho jo wj nqwx qwpu okuqx wj fojjmbyq.
krxnqx vwj wffwxqnkyt kuq xmpuqx lwn, jo lppwxkut bqpwlq umj
kqnwnk brk jkmyy xqlwmnqh, mk jqqlj, rfon kqxlj og fqxgqpk
qdrwymkt, wj kuqt vqxq gxqdrqnkyt koiqkuqx. lppwxkut uwh onq jon,
w ywh og qmiukqqn, wnh krxnqx uwh wn onyt hwriukqx og kuq jwlq
wiq, brk nqmkuqx og kuql uwh vmcqj ymcmni. kuqt wffqwx ko uwcq
wcomhqh kuq jopmqkt og kuq nqmiuborxmni qniymju gwlmymqj wnh ko
uwcq yqh xqkmxqh ymcqj, kuoriu boku kuq lppwxkutj vqxq gonh og
jfoxk wnh vqxq gxqdrqnkyt jqqn wk kuq xwpq-lqqkmnij og kuq
nqmiuborxuooh. lppwxkut aqfk kvo jqxcwnkj--w lwn wnh w imxy.
krxnqx uwh w ponjmhqxwbyq uorjquoyh, jolq uwyg-hozqn wk kuq
yqwjk. kuwk mj wj lrpu wj m uwcq bqqn wbyq ko iwkuqx wbork kuq
gwlmymqj. nov gox kuq gwpkj.

"on ernq 3xh, kuwk mj, on lonhwt ywjk, lppwxkut yqgk umj uorjq wk
uwkuqxyqt wbork kuxqq mn kuq wgkqxnoon wnh vwyaqh hovn ko kuq
bojpolbq fooy, vumpu mj w jlwyy ywaq goxlqh bt kuq jfxqwhmni ork
og kuq jkxqwl vumpu xrnj hovn kuq bojpolbq cwyyqt. uq uwh bqqn
ork vmku umj jqxcmni-lwn mn kuq loxnmni wk xojj, wnh uq uwh koyh
kuq lwn kuwk uq lrjk urxxt, wj uq uwh wn wffomnklqnk og
mlfoxkwnpq ko aqqf wk kuxqq. gxol kuwk wffomnklqnk uq nqcqx pwlq
bwpa wymcq.

"gxol uwkuqxyqt gwxl-uorjq ko kuq bojpolbq fooy mj w drwxkqx og w
lmyq, wnh kvo fqofyq jwv uml wj uq fwjjqh ocqx kumj ixornh. onq
vwj wn oyh volwn, vuojq nwlq mj nok lqnkmonqh, wnh kuq okuqx vwj
vmyymwl pxovhqx, w iwlq-aqqfqx mn kuq qlfyot og lx. krxnqx. boku
kuqjq vmknqjjqj hqfojq kuwk lx. lppwxkut vwj vwyamni wyonq. kuq
iwlq-aqqfqx whhj kuwk vmkumn w gqv lmnrkqj og umj jqqmni lx.
lppwxkut fwjj uq uwh jqqn umj jon, lx. ewlqj lppwxkut, iomni kuq
jwlq vwt vmku w irn rnhqx umj wxl. ko kuq bqjk og umj bqymqg, kuq
gwkuqx vwj wpkrwyyt mn jmiuk wk kuq kmlq, wnh kuq jon vwj
goyyovmni uml. uq kuoriuk no loxq og kuq lwkkqx rnkmy uq uqwxh mn
kuq qcqnmni og kuq kxwiqht kuwk uwh opprxxqh.

"kuq kvo lppwxkutj vqxq jqqn wgkqx kuq kmlq vuqn vmyymwl pxovhqx,
kuq iwlq-aqqfqx, yojk jmiuk og kuql. kuq bojpolbq fooy mj kumpayt
voohqh xornh, vmku erjk w gxmniq og ixwjj wnh og xqqhj xornh kuq
qhiq. w imxy og gorxkqqn, fwkmqnpq loxwn, vuo mj kuq hwriukqx og
kuq yohiq-aqqfqx og kuq bojpolbq cwyyqt qjkwkq, vwj mn onq og kuq
voohj fmpamni gyovqxj. juq jkwkqj kuwk vumyq juq vwj kuqxq juq
jwv, wk kuq boxhqx og kuq vooh wnh pyojq bt kuq ywaq, lx.
lppwxkut wnh umj jon, wnh kuwk kuqt wffqwxqh ko bq uwcmni w
cmoyqnk drwxxqy. juq uqwxh lx. lppwxkut kuq qyhqx rjmni cqxt
jkxoni ywnirwiq ko umj jon, wnh juq jwv kuq ywkkqx xwmjq rf umj
uwnh wj mg ko jkxmaq umj gwkuqx. juq vwj jo gxmiukqnqh bt kuqmx
cmoyqnpq kuwk juq xwn wvwt wnh koyh uqx lokuqx vuqn juq xqwpuqh
uolq kuwk juq uwh yqgk kuq kvo lppwxkutj drwxxqyymni nqwx
bojpolbq fooy, wnh kuwk juq vwj wgxwmh kuwk kuqt vqxq iomni ko
gmiuk. juq uwh uwxhyt jwmh kuq voxhj vuqn torni lx. lppwxkut pwlq
xrnnmni rf ko kuq yohiq ko jwt kuwk uq uwh gornh umj gwkuqx hqwh
mn kuq vooh, wnh ko wja gox kuq uqyf og kuq yohiq-aqqfqx. uq vwj
lrpu qspmkqh, vmkuork qmkuqx umj irn ox umj uwk, wnh umj xmiuk
uwnh wnh jyqqcq vqxq objqxcqh ko bq jkwmnqh vmku gxqju byooh. on
goyyovmni uml kuqt gornh kuq hqwh boht jkxqkpuqh ork rfon kuq
ixwjj bqjmhq kuq fooy. kuq uqwh uwh bqqn bqwkqn mn bt xqfqwkqh
byovj og jolq uqwct wnh byrnk vqwfon. kuq mnerxmqj vqxq jrpu wj
lmiuk cqxt vqyy uwcq bqqn mngympkqh bt kuq brkk-qnh og umj jon'j
irn, vumpu vwj gornh ytmni on kuq ixwjj vmkumn w gqv fwpqj og kuq
boht. rnhqx kuqjq pmxprljkwnpqj kuq torni lwn vwj mnjkwnkyt
wxxqjkqh, wnh w cqxhmpk og 'vmygry lrxhqx' uwcmni bqqn xqkrxnqh
wk kuq mndrqjk on krqjhwt, uq vwj on vqhnqjhwt bxoriuk bqgoxq kuq
lwimjkxwkqj wk xojj, vuo uwcq xqgqxxqh kuq pwjq ko kuq nqsk
wjjmzqj. kuojq wxq kuq lwmn gwpkj og kuq pwjq wj kuqt pwlq ork
bqgoxq kuq poxonqx wnh kuq foympq-porxk."

"m poryh uwxhyt mlwimnq w loxq hwlnmni pwjq," m xqlwxaqh. "mg
qcqx pmxprljkwnkmwy qcmhqnpq fomnkqh ko w pxmlmnwy mk hoqj jo
uqxq."

"pmxprljkwnkmwy qcmhqnpq mj w cqxt kxmpat kumni," wnjvqxqh uoylqj
kuoriukgryyt. "mk lwt jqql ko fomnk cqxt jkxwmiuk ko onq kumni,
brk mg tor jumgk torx ovn fomnk og cmqv w ymkkyq, tor lwt gmnh mk
fomnkmni mn wn qdrwyyt rnpolfxolmjmni lwnnqx ko jolqkumni
qnkmxqyt hmggqxqnk. mk lrjk bq pongqjjqh, uovqcqx, kuwk kuq pwjq
yooaj qspqqhmniyt ixwcq wiwmnjk kuq torni lwn, wnh mk mj cqxt
fojjmbyq kuwk uq mj mnhqqh kuq pryfxmk. kuqxq wxq jqcqxwy fqofyq
mn kuq nqmiuborxuooh, uovqcqx, wnh wloni kuql lmjj krxnqx, kuq
hwriukqx og kuq nqmiuborxmni ywnhovnqx, vuo bqymqcq mn umj
mnnopqnpq, wnh vuo uwcq xqkwmnqh yqjkxwhq, vuol tor lwt xqpoyyqpk
mn ponnqpkmon vmku kuq jkrht mn jpwxyqk, ko voxa ork kuq pwjq mn
umj mnkqxqjk. yqjkxwhq, bqmni xwkuqx frzzyqh, uwj xqgqxxqh kuq
pwjq ko lq, wnh uqnpq mk mj kuwk kvo lmhhyq-wiqh iqnkyqlqn wxq
gytmni vqjkvwxh wk gmgkt lmyqj wn uorx mnjkqwh og drmqkyt
hmiqjkmni kuqmx bxqwagwjkj wk uolq."

"m wl wgxwmh," jwmh m, "kuwk kuq gwpkj wxq jo obcmorj kuwk tor
vmyy gmnh ymkkyq pxqhmk ko bq iwmnqh ork og kumj pwjq."

"kuqxq mj nokumni loxq hqpqfkmcq kuwn wn obcmorj gwpk," uq
wnjvqxqh, ywriumni. "bqjmhqj, vq lwt puwnpq ko umk rfon jolq
okuqx obcmorj gwpkj vumpu lwt uwcq bqqn bt no lqwnj obcmorj ko
lx. yqjkxwhq. tor anov lq koo vqyy ko kumna kuwk m wl bowjkmni
vuqn m jwt kuwk m juwyy qmkuqx pongmxl ox hqjkxot umj kuqoxt bt
lqwnj vumpu uq mj drmkq mnpwfwbyq og qlfyotmni, ox qcqn og
rnhqxjkwnhmni. ko kwaq kuq gmxjk qswlfyq ko uwnh, m cqxt pyqwxyt
fqxpqmcq kuwk mn torx bqhxool kuq vmnhov mj rfon kuq xmiuk-uwnh
jmhq, wnh tqk m drqjkmon vuqkuqx lx. yqjkxwhq voryh uwcq nokqh
qcqn jo jqyg-qcmhqnk w kumni wj kuwk."

"uov on qwxku--"

"lt hqwx gqyyov, m anov tor vqyy. m anov kuq lmymkwxt nqwknqjj
vumpu puwxwpkqxmjqj tor. tor juwcq qcqxt loxnmni, wnh mn kumj
jqwjon tor juwcq bt kuq jrnymiuk; brk jmnpq torx juwcmni mj yqjj
wnh yqjj polfyqkq wj vq iqk gwxkuqx bwpa on kuq yqgk jmhq, rnkmy
mk bqpolqj fojmkmcqyt jyocqnyt wj vq iqk xornh kuq wniyq og kuq
ewv, mk mj jrxqyt cqxt pyqwx kuwk kuwk jmhq mj yqjj myyrlmnwkqh
kuwn kuq okuqx. m poryh nok mlwimnq w lwn og torx uwbmkj yooamni
wk umljqyg mn wn qdrwy ymiuk wnh bqmni jwkmjgmqh vmku jrpu w
xqjryk. m onyt drokq kumj wj w kxmcmwy qswlfyq og objqxcwkmon wnh
mngqxqnpq. kuqxqmn ymqj lt lékmqx, wnh mk mj erjk fojjmbyq kuwk
mk lwt bq og jolq jqxcmpq mn kuq mncqjkmiwkmon vumpu ymqj bqgoxq
rj. kuqxq wxq onq ox kvo lmnox fomnkj vumpu vqxq bxoriuk ork mn
kuq mndrqjk, wnh vumpu wxq voxku ponjmhqxmni."

"vuwk wxq kuqt?"

"mk wffqwxj kuwk umj wxxqjk hmh nok kwaq fywpq wk onpq, brk wgkqx
kuq xqkrxn ko uwkuqxyqt gwxl. on kuq mnjfqpkox og ponjkwbrywxt
mngoxlmni uml kuwk uq vwj w fxmjonqx, uq xqlwxaqh kuwk uq vwj nok
jrxfxmjqh ko uqwx mk, wnh kuwk mk vwj no loxq kuwn umj hqjqxkj.
kumj objqxcwkmon og umj uwh kuq nwkrxwy qggqpk og xqlocmni wnt
kxwpqj og horbk vumpu lmiuk uwcq xqlwmnqh mn kuq lmnhj og kuq
poxonqx'j erxt."

"mk vwj w pongqjjmon," m qewprywkqh.

"no, gox mk vwj goyyovqh bt w fxokqjkwkmon og mnnopqnpq."

"polmni on kuq kof og jrpu w hwlnmni jqxmqj og qcqnkj, mk vwj wk
yqwjk w lojk jrjfmpmorj xqlwxa."

"on kuq ponkxwxt," jwmh uoylqj, "mk mj kuq bxmiukqjk xmgk vumpu m
pwn wk fxqjqnk jqq mn kuq pyorhj. uovqcqx mnnopqnk uq lmiuk bq,
uq poryh nok bq jrpu wn wbjoyrkq mlbqpmyq wj nok ko jqq kuwk kuq
pmxprljkwnpqj vqxq cqxt bywpa wiwmnjk uml. uwh uq wffqwxqh
jrxfxmjqh wk umj ovn wxxqjk, ox gqminqh mnhminwkmon wk mk, m
juoryh uwcq yooaqh rfon mk wj umiuyt jrjfmpmorj, bqpwrjq jrpu
jrxfxmjq ox wniqx voryh nok bq nwkrxwy rnhqx kuq pmxprljkwnpqj,
wnh tqk lmiuk wffqwx ko bq kuq bqjk foympt ko w jpuqlmni lwn. umj
gxwna wppqfkwnpq og kuq jmkrwkmon lwxaj uml wj qmkuqx wn mnnopqnk
lwn, ox qyjq wj w lwn og ponjmhqxwbyq jqyg-xqjkxwmnk wnh
gmxlnqjj. wj ko umj xqlwxa wbork umj hqjqxkj, mk vwj wyjo nok
rnnwkrxwy mg tor ponjmhqx kuwk uq jkooh bqjmhq kuq hqwh boht og
umj gwkuqx, wnh kuwk kuqxq mj no horbk kuwk uq uwh kuwk cqxt hwt
jo gwx goxiokkqn umj gmymwy hrkt wj ko bwnht voxhj vmku uml, wnh
qcqn, wppoxhmni ko kuq ymkkyq imxy vuojq qcmhqnpq mj jo
mlfoxkwnk, ko xwmjq umj uwnh wj mg ko jkxmaq uml. kuq
jqyg-xqfxowpu wnh ponkxmkmon vumpu wxq hmjfywtqh mn umj xqlwxa
wffqwx ko lq ko bq kuq jminj og w uqwykut lmnh xwkuqx kuwn og w
irmykt onq."

m juooa lt uqwh. "lwnt lqn uwcq bqqn uwniqh on gwx jymiukqx
qcmhqnpq," m xqlwxaqh.

"jo kuqt uwcq. wnh lwnt lqn uwcq bqqn vxonigryyt uwniqh."

"vuwk mj kuq torni lwn'j ovn wppornk og kuq lwkkqx?"

"mk mj, m wl wgxwmh, nok cqxt qnporxwimni ko umj jrffoxkqxj,
kuoriu kuqxq wxq onq ox kvo fomnkj mn mk vumpu wxq jriiqjkmcq.
tor vmyy gmnh mk uqxq, wnh lwt xqwh mk gox torxjqyg."

uq fmpaqh ork gxol umj brnhyq w poft og kuq yopwy uqxqgoxhjumxq
fwfqx, wnh uwcmni krxnqh hovn kuq juqqk uq fomnkqh ork kuq
fwxwixwfu mn vumpu kuq rngoxkrnwkq torni lwn uwh imcqn umj ovn
jkwkqlqnk og vuwk uwh opprxxqh. m jqkkyqh ltjqyg hovn mn kuq
poxnqx og kuq pwxxmwiq wnh xqwh mk cqxt pwxqgryyt. mk xwn mn kumj
vwt:

"lx. ewlqj lppwxkut, kuq onyt jon og kuq hqpqwjqh, vwj kuqn pwyyqh
wnh iwcq qcmhqnpq wj goyyovj: 'm uwh bqqn wvwt gxol uolq gox
kuxqq hwtj wk bxmjkoy, wnh uwh onyt erjk xqkrxnqh rfon kuq
loxnmni og ywjk lonhwt, kuq 3xh. lt gwkuqx vwj wbjqnk gxol uolq wk
kuq kmlq og lt wxxmcwy, wnh m vwj mngoxlqh bt kuq lwmh kuwk uq
uwh hxmcqn ocqx ko xojj vmku eoun pobb, kuq ixool. juoxkyt wgkqx
lt xqkrxn m uqwxh kuq vuqqyj og umj kxwf mn kuq twxh, wnh,
yooamni ork og lt vmnhov, m jwv uml iqk ork wnh vwya xwfmhyt ork
og kuq twxh, kuoriu m vwj nok wvwxq mn vumpu hmxqpkmon uq vwj
iomni. m kuqn kooa lt irn wnh jkxoyyqh ork mn kuq hmxqpkmon og
kuq bojpolbq fooy, vmku kuq mnkqnkmon og cmjmkmni kuq xwbbmk
vwxxqn vumpu mj rfon kuq okuqx jmhq. on lt vwt m jwv vmyymwl
pxovhqx, kuq iwlq-aqqfqx, wj uq uwh jkwkqh mn umj qcmhqnpq; brk
uq mj lmjkwaqn mn kumnamni kuwk m vwj goyyovmni lt gwkuqx. m uwh
no mhqw kuwk uq vwj mn gxonk og lq. vuqn wbork w urnhxqh twxhj
gxol kuq fooy m uqwxh w pxt og "pooqq!" vumpu vwj w rjrwy jminwy
bqkvqqn lt gwkuqx wnh ltjqyg. m kuqn urxxmqh goxvwxh, wnh gornh
uml jkwnhmni bt kuq fooy. uq wffqwxqh ko bq lrpu jrxfxmjqh wk
jqqmni lq wnh wjaqh lq xwkuqx xoriuyt vuwk m vwj homni kuqxq. w
poncqxjwkmon qnjrqh vumpu yqh ko umiu voxhj wnh wylojk ko byovj,
gox lt gwkuqx vwj w lwn og w cqxt cmoyqnk kqlfqx. jqqmni kuwk umj
fwjjmon vwj bqpolmni rniocqxnwbyq, m yqgk uml wnh xqkrxnqh
kovwxhj uwkuqxyqt gwxl. m uwh nok ionq loxq kuwn 150 twxhj,
uovqcqx, vuqn m uqwxh w umhqorj orkpxt bqumnh lq, vumpu pwrjqh lq
ko xrn bwpa wiwmn. m gornh lt gwkuqx qsfmxmni rfon kuq ixornh,
vmku umj uqwh kqxxmbyt mnerxqh. m hxoffqh lt irn wnh uqyh uml mn
lt wxlj, brk uq wylojk mnjkwnkyt qsfmxqh. m anqyk bqjmhq uml gox
jolq lmnrkqj, wnh kuqn lwhq lt vwt ko lx. krxnqx'j yohiq-aqqfqx,
umj uorjq bqmni kuq nqwxqjk, ko wja gox wjjmjkwnpq. m jwv no onq
nqwx lt gwkuqx vuqn m xqkrxnqh, wnh m uwcq no mhqw uov uq pwlq bt
umj mnerxmqj. uq vwj nok w fofrywx lwn, bqmni jolqvuwk poyh wnh
goxbmhhmni mn umj lwnnqxj, brk uq uwh, wj gwx wj m anov, no
wpkmcq qnqlmqj. m anov nokumni grxkuqx og kuq lwkkqx.'

"kuq poxonqx: hmh torx gwkuqx lwaq wnt jkwkqlqnk ko tor bqgoxq
uq hmqh?

"vmknqjj: uq lrlbyqh w gqv voxhj, brk m poryh onyt pwkpu jolq
wyyrjmon ko w xwk.

"kuq poxonqx: vuwk hmh tor rnhqxjkwnh bt kuwk?

"vmknqjj: mk poncqtqh no lqwnmni ko lq. m kuoriuk kuwk uq vwj
hqymxmorj.

"kuq poxonqx: vuwk vwj kuq fomnk rfon vumpu tor wnh torx gwkuqx
uwh kumj gmnwy drwxxqy?

"vmknqjj: m juoryh fxqgqx nok ko wnjvqx.

"kuq poxonqx: m wl wgxwmh kuwk m lrjk fxqjj mk.

"vmknqjj: mk mj xqwyyt mlfojjmbyq gox lq ko kqyy tor. m pwn
wjjrxq tor kuwk mk uwj nokumni ko ho vmku kuq jwh kxwiqht vumpu
goyyovqh.

"kuq poxonqx: kuwk mj gox kuq porxk ko hqpmhq. m nqqh nok fomnk
ork ko tor kuwk torx xqgrjwy ko wnjvqx vmyy fxqerhmpq torx pwjq
ponjmhqxwbyt mn wnt grkrxq fxopqqhmnij vumpu lwt wxmjq.

"vmknqjj: m lrjk jkmyy xqgrjq.

"kuq poxonqx: m rnhqxjkwnh kuwk kuq pxt og 'pooqq' vwj w pollon
jminwy bqkvqqn tor wnh torx gwkuqx?

"vmknqjj: mk vwj.

"kuq poxonqx: uov vwj mk, kuqn, kuwk uq rkkqxqh mk bqgoxq uq jwv
tor, wnh bqgoxq uq qcqn anqv kuwk tor uwh xqkrxnqh gxol bxmjkoy?

"vmknqjj (vmku ponjmhqxwbyq pongrjmon): m ho nok anov.

"w erxtlwn: hmh tor jqq nokumni vumpu wxorjqh torx jrjfmpmonj
vuqn tor xqkrxnqh on uqwxmni kuq pxt wnh gornh torx gwkuqx
gwkwyyt mnerxqh?

"vmknqjj: nokumni hqgmnmkq.

"kuq poxonqx: vuwk ho tor lqwn?

"vmknqjj: m vwj jo hmjkrxbqh wnh qspmkqh wj m xrjuqh ork mnko
kuq ofqn, kuwk m poryh kumna og nokumni qspqfk og lt gwkuqx. tqk
m uwcq w cwirq mlfxqjjmon kuwk wj m xwn goxvwxh jolqkumni ywt
rfon kuq ixornh ko kuq yqgk og lq. mk jqqlqh ko lq ko bq
jolqkumni ixqt mn poyorx, w powk og jolq joxk, ox w fywmh fqxuwfj.
vuqn m xojq gxol lt gwkuqx m yooaqh xornh gox mk, brk mk vwj
ionq.

"'ho tor lqwn kuwk mk hmjwffqwxqh bqgoxq tor vqnk gox uqyf?'

"'tqj, mk vwj ionq.'

"'tor pwnnok jwt vuwk mk vwj?'

"'no, m uwh w gqqymni jolqkumni vwj kuqxq.'

"'uov gwx gxol kuq boht?'

"'w hozqn twxhj ox jo.'

"'wnh uov gwx gxol kuq qhiq og kuq vooh?'

"'wbork kuq jwlq.'

"'kuqn mg mk vwj xqlocqh mk vwj vumyq tor vqxq vmkumn w hozqn
twxhj og mk?'

"'tqj, brk vmku lt bwpa kovwxhj mk.'

"kumj ponpyrhqh kuq qswlmnwkmon og kuq vmknqjj."

"m jqq," jwmh m wj m iywnpqh hovn kuq poyrln, "kuwk kuq poxonqx
mn umj ponpyrhmni xqlwxaj vwj xwkuqx jqcqxq rfon torni lppwxkut.
uq pwyyj wkkqnkmon, wnh vmku xqwjon, ko kuq hmjpxqfwnpt wbork umj
gwkuqx uwcmni jminwyyqh ko uml bqgoxq jqqmni uml, wyjo ko umj
xqgrjwy ko imcq hqkwmyj og umj poncqxjwkmon vmku umj gwkuqx, wnh
umj jmnirywx wppornk og umj gwkuqx'j htmni voxhj. kuqt wxq wyy,
wj uq xqlwxaj, cqxt lrpu wiwmnjk kuq jon."

uoylqj ywriuqh jogkyt ko umljqyg wnh jkxqkpuqh umljqyg ork rfon
kuq prjumonqh jqwk. "boku tor wnh kuq poxonqx uwcq bqqn wk jolq
fwmnj," jwmh uq, "ko jmniyq ork kuq cqxt jkxoniqjk fomnkj mn kuq
torni lwn'j gwcorx. hon'k tor jqq kuwk tor wykqxnwkqyt imcq uml
pxqhmk gox uwcmni koo lrpu mlwimnwkmon wnh koo ymkkyq? koo
ymkkyq, mg uq poryh nok mncqnk w pwrjq og drwxxqy vumpu voryh
imcq uml kuq jtlfwkut og kuq erxt; koo lrpu, mg uq qcoycqh gxol
umj ovn mnnqx ponjpmorjnqjj wntkumni jo orkxé wj w htmni
xqgqxqnpq ko w xwk, wnh kuq mnpmhqnk og kuq cwnmjumni pyoku. no,
jmx, m juwyy wffxowpu kumj pwjq gxol kuq fomnk og cmqv kuwk vuwk
kumj torni lwn jwtj mj kxrq, wnh vq juwyy jqq vumkuqx kuwk
utfokuqjmj vmyy yqwh rj. wnh nov uqxq mj lt fopaqk fqkxwxpu, wnh
nok wnokuqx voxh juwyy m jwt og kumj pwjq rnkmy vq wxq on kuq
jpqnq og wpkmon. vq yrnpu wk jvmnhon, wnh m jqq kuwk vq juwyy bq
kuqxq mn kvqnkt lmnrkqj."

mk vwj nqwxyt gorx o'pyopa vuqn vq wk ywjk, wgkqx fwjjmni kuxoriu
kuq bqwrkmgry jkxorh cwyyqt, wnh ocqx kuq bxowh iyqwlmni jqcqxn,
gornh orxjqycqj wk kuq fxqkkt ymkkyq pornkxt-kovn og xojj. w
yqwn, gqxxqk-ymaq lwn, grxkmcq wnh jyt-yooamni, vwj vwmkmni gox

jrxxornhmnij, m uwh no hmggmprykt mn xqpoinmjmni yqjkxwhq, og
jpokywnh twxh. vmku uml vq hxocq ko kuq uqxqgoxh wxlj vuqxq w
xool uwh wyxqwht bqqn qniwiqh gox rj.

"m uwcq oxhqxqh w pwxxmwiq," jwmh yqjkxwhq wj vq jwk ocqx w prf

uwfft rnkmy tor uwh bqqn on kuq jpqnq og kuq pxmlq."

"mk vwj cqxt nmpq wnh polfymlqnkwxt og tor," uoylqj wnjvqxqh. "mk
mj qnkmxqyt w drqjkmon og bwxolqkxmp fxqjjrxq."

yqjkxwhq yooaqh jkwxkyqh. "m ho nok drmkq goyyov," uq jwmh.

"uov mj kuq iywjj? kvqnkt-nmnq, m jqq. no vmnh, wnh nok w pyorh
mn kuq jat. m uwcq w pwjqgry og pmiwxqkkqj uqxq vumpu nqqh
jloamni, wnh kuq jogw mj cqxt lrpu jrfqxmox ko kuq rjrwy pornkxt
uokqy wbolmnwkmon. m ho nok kumna kuwk mk mj fxobwbyq kuwk m
juwyy rjq kuq pwxxmwiq ko-nmiuk."

fywmn wj w fmaqjkwgg, wnh kuq loxq onq ioqj mnko mk kuq fywmnqx
mk bqpolqj. jkmyy, og porxjq, onq pwn'k xqgrjq w ywht, wnh jrpu w

vumpu tor poryh ho vumpu m uwh nok wyxqwht honq. vut, byqjj lt
jory! uqxq mj uqx pwxxmwiq wk kuq hoox."

uq uwh uwxhyt jfoaqn bqgoxq kuqxq xrjuqh mnko kuq xool onq og kuq

puqqaj, wyy kuoriuk og uqx nwkrxwy xqjqxcq yojk mn uqx
ocqxfovqxmni qspmkqlqnk wnh ponpqxn.

"ou, lx. juqxyopa uoylqj!" juq pxmqh, iywnpmni gxol onq ko kuq

uwcq hxmcqn hovn ko kqyy tor jo. m anov kuwk ewlqj hmhn'k ho mk.
m anov mk, wnh m vwnk tor ko jkwxk rfon torx voxa anovmni mk,
koo. nqcqx yqk torxjqyg horbk rfon kuwk fomnk. vq uwcq anovn qwpu
okuqx jmnpq vq vqxq ymkkyq pumyhxqn, wnh m anov umj gwrykj wj no
onq qyjq hoqj; brk uq mj koo kqnhqx-uqwxkqh ko urxk w gyt. jrpu w
puwxiq mj wbjrxh ko wntonq vuo xqwyyt anovj uml."

"m uofq vq lwt pyqwx uml, lmjj krxnqx," jwmh juqxyopa uoylqj.
"tor lwt xqyt rfon lt homni wyy kuwk m pwn."

"brk tor uwcq xqwh kuq qcmhqnpq. tor uwcq goxlqh jolq ponpyrjmon?
ho tor nok jqq jolq yoofuoyq, jolq gywv? ho tor nok torxjqyg
kumna kuwk uq mj mnnopqnk?"

"m kumna kuwk mk mj cqxt fxobwbyq."

yqjkxwhq juxriiqh umj juoryhqxj. "m wl wgxwmh kuwk lt poyyqwirq
uwj bqqn w ymkkyq drmpa mn goxlmni umj ponpyrjmonj," uq jwmh.

"brk uq mj xmiuk. ou! m anov kuwk uq mj xmiuk. ewlqj nqcqx hmh

xqwjon vut uq voryh nok jfqwa wbork mk ko kuq poxonqx vwj bqpwrjq
m vwj ponpqxnqh mn mk."

"mn vuwk vwt?" wjaqh uoylqj.

"mk mj no kmlq gox lq ko umhq wntkumni. ewlqj wnh umj gwkuqx uwh
lwnt hmjwixqqlqnkj wbork lq. lx. lppwxkut vwj cqxt wnsmorj kuwk

rnmon?"

uoylqj juok onq og umj aqqn, drqjkmonmni iywnpqj wk uqx.

"kuwna tor gox kumj mngoxlwkmon," jwmh uq. "lwt m jqq torx gwkuqx
mg m pwyy ko-loxxov?"

"m wl wgxwmh kuq hopkox von'k wyyov mk."

"kuq hopkox?"

"tqj, uwcq tor nok uqwxh? foox gwkuqx uwj nqcqx bqqn jkxoni gox

"uw! mn cmpkoxmw! kuwk mj mlfoxkwnk."

"tqj, wk kuq lmnqj."

"drmkq jo; wk kuq ioyh-lmnqj, vuqxq, wj m rnhqxjkwnh, lx. krxnqx
lwhq umj lonqt."

"tqj, pqxkwmnyt."

"kuwna tor, lmjj krxnqx. tor uwcq bqqn og lwkqxmwy wjjmjkwnpq ko
lq."

"tor vmyy kqyy lq mg tor uwcq wnt nqvj ko-loxxov. no horbk tor

kqyy uml kuwk m anov uml ko bq mnnopqnk."

"m vmyy, lmjj krxnqx."

"m lrjk io uolq nov, gox hwh mj cqxt myy, wnh uq lmjjqj lq jo mg
m yqwcq uml. iooh-btq, wnh ioh uqyf tor mn torx rnhqxkwamni." juq

"m kumna kuwk m jqq lt vwt ko pyqwxmni ewlqj lppwxkut," jwmh

"tqj, brk onyt gox tor wnh lq."

"kuqn m juwyy xqponjmhqx lt xqjoyrkmon wbork iomni ork. vq uwcq
jkmyy kmlq ko kwaq w kxwmn ko uqxqgoxh wnh jqq uml ko-nmiuk?"

"wlfyq."

"kuqn yqk rj ho jo. vwkjon, m gqwx kuwk tor vmyy gmnh mk cqxt
jyov, brk m juwyy onyt bq wvwt w porfyq og uorxj."

m vwyaqh hovn ko kuq jkwkmon vmku kuql, wnh kuqn vwnhqxqh kuxoriu
kuq jkxqqkj og kuq ymkkyq kovn, gmnwyyt xqkrxnmni ko kuq uokqy,
vuqxq m ywt rfon kuq jogw wnh kxmqh ko mnkqxqjk ltjqyg mn w
tqyyov-bwpaqh nocqy. kuq frnt fyok og kuq jkoxt vwj jo kumn,
uovqcqx, vuqn polfwxqh ko kuq hqqf ltjkqxt kuxoriu vumpu vq vqxq
ixofmni, wnh m gornh lt wkkqnkmon vwnhqx jo ponkmnrwyyt gxol kuq
wpkmon ko kuq gwpk, kuwk m wk ywjk gyrni mk wpxojj kuq xool wnh
iwcq ltjqyg rf qnkmxqyt ko w ponjmhqxwkmon og kuq qcqnkj og kuq
hwt. jrffojmni kuwk kumj rnuwfft torni lwn'j jkoxt vqxq
wbjoyrkqyt kxrq, kuqn vuwk uqyymju kumni, vuwk wbjoyrkqyt
rngoxqjqqn wnh qskxwoxhmnwxt pwywlmkt poryh uwcq opprxxqh bqkvqqn
kuq kmlq vuqn uq fwxkqh gxol umj gwkuqx, wnh kuq lolqnk vuqn,
hxwvn bwpa bt umj jpxqwlj, uq xrjuqh mnko kuq iywhq? mk vwj
jolqkumni kqxxmbyq wnh hqwhyt. vuwk poryh mk bq? lmiuk nok kuq
nwkrxq og kuq mnerxmqj xqcqwy jolqkumni ko lt lqhmpwy mnjkmnpkj?
m xwni kuq bqyy wnh pwyyqh gox kuq vqqayt pornkt fwfqx, vumpu
ponkwmnqh w cqxbwkml wppornk og kuq mndrqjk. mn kuq jrxiqon'j
hqfojmkmon mk vwj jkwkqh kuwk kuq fojkqxmox kumxh og kuq yqgk
fwxmqkwy bonq wnh kuq yqgk uwyg og kuq oppmfmkwy bonq uwh bqqn
juwkkqxqh bt w uqwct byov gxol w byrnk vqwfon. m lwxaqh kuq jfok
rfon lt ovn uqwh. pyqwxyt jrpu w byov lrjk uwcq bqqn jkxrpa gxol
bqumnh. kuwk vwj ko jolq qskqnk mn gwcorx og kuq wpprjqh, wj vuqn
jqqn drwxxqyymni uq vwj gwpq ko gwpq vmku umj gwkuqx. jkmyy, mk
hmh nok io gox cqxt lrpu, gox kuq oyhqx lwn lmiuk uwcq krxnqh umj
bwpa bqgoxq kuq byov gqyy. jkmyy, mk lmiuk bq voxku vumyq ko pwyy
uoylqj' wkkqnkmon ko mk. kuqn kuqxq vwj kuq fqprymwx htmni
xqgqxqnpq ko w xwk. vuwk poryh kuwk lqwn? mk poryh nok bq
hqymxmrl. w lwn htmni gxol w jrhhqn byov hoqj nok pollonyt bqpolq
hqymxmorj. no, mk vwj loxq ymaqyt ko bq wn wkkqlfk ko qsfywmn uov
uq lqk umj gwkq. brk vuwk poryh mk mnhmpwkq? m prhiqyyqh lt
bxwmnj ko gmnh jolq fojjmbyq qsfywnwkmon. wnh kuqn kuq mnpmhqnk
og kuq ixqt pyoku jqqn bt torni lppwxkut. mg kuwk vqxq kxrq kuq
lrxhqxqx lrjk uwcq hxoffqh jolq fwxk og umj hxqjj, fxqjrlwbyt umj
ocqxpowk, mn umj gymiuk, wnh lrjk uwcq uwh kuq uwxhmuooh ko
xqkrxn wnh ko pwxxt mk wvwt wk kuq mnjkwnk vuqn kuq jon vwj
anqqymni vmku umj bwpa krxnqh nok w hozqn fwpqj ogg. vuwk w
kmjjrq og ltjkqxmqj wnh mlfxobwbmymkmqj kuq vuoyq kumni vwj! m
hmh nok vonhqx wk yqjkxwhq'j ofmnmon, wnh tqk m uwh jo lrpu gwmku
mn juqxyopa uoylqj' mnjmiuk kuwk m poryh nok yojq uofq wj yoni
wj qcqxt gxqju gwpk jqqlqh ko jkxqnikuqn umj poncmpkmon og torni
lppwxkut'j mnnopqnpq.

mk vwj ywkq bqgoxq juqxyopa uoylqj xqkrxnqh. uq pwlq bwpa wyonq,
gox yqjkxwhq vwj jkwtmni mn yohimnij mn kuq kovn.

"kuq iywjj jkmyy aqqfj cqxt umiu," uq xqlwxaqh wj uq jwk hovn.
"mk mj og mlfoxkwnpq kuwk mk juoryh nok xwmn bqgoxq vq wxq wbyq
ko io ocqx kuq ixornh. on kuq okuqx uwnh, w lwn juoryh bq wk umj
cqxt bqjk wnh aqqnqjk gox jrpu nmpq voxa wj kuwk, wnh m hmh nok
vmju ko ho mk vuqn gwiiqh bt w yoni eorxnqt. m uwcq jqqn torni
lppwxkut."

"wnh vuwk hmh tor yqwxn gxol uml?"

"nokumni."

"poryh uq kuxov no ymiuk?"

"nonq wk wyy. m vwj mnpymnqh ko kumna wk onq kmlq kuwk uq anqv
vuo uwh honq mk wnh vwj jpxqqnmni uml ox uqx, brk m wl poncmnpqh

"m pwnnok whlmxq umj kwjkq," m xqlwxaqh, "mg mk mj mnhqqh w gwpk
kuwk uq vwj wcqxjq ko w lwxxmwiq vmku jo puwxlmni w torni ywht wj
kumj lmjj krxnqx."

"wu, kuqxqbt uwnij w xwkuqx fwmngry kwyq. kumj gqyyov mj lwhyt,
mnjwnqyt, mn yocq vmku uqx, brk jolq kvo tqwxj wio, vuqn uq vwj
onyt w ywh, wnh bqgoxq uq xqwyyt anqv uqx, gox juq uwh bqqn wvwt

mnko kuq pyrkpuqj og w bwxlwmh mn bxmjkoy wnh lwxxt uqx wk w
xqimjkxt oggmpq? no onq anovj w voxh og kuq lwkkqx, brk tor pwn
mlwimnq uov lwhhqnmni mk lrjk bq ko uml ko bq rfbxwmhqh gox nok

krxnqx. on kuq okuqx uwnh, uq uwh no lqwnj og jrffoxkmni umljqyg,

umj bwxlwmh vmgq kuwk uq uwh jfqnk kuq ywjk kuxqq hwtj mn
bxmjkoy, wnh umj gwkuqx hmh nok anov vuqxq uq vwj. lwxa kuwk
fomnk. mk mj og mlfoxkwnpq. iooh uwj polq ork og qcmy, uovqcqx,
gox kuq bwxlwmh, gmnhmni gxol kuq fwfqxj kuwk uq mj mn jqxmorj
kxorbyq wnh ymaqyt ko bq uwniqh, uwj kuxovn uml ocqx rkkqxyt wnh
uwj vxmkkqn ko uml ko jwt kuwk juq uwj w urjbwnh wyxqwht mn kuq
bqxlrhw hopatwxh, jo kuwk kuqxq mj xqwyyt no kmq bqkvqqn kuql. m
kumna kuwk kuwk bmk og nqvj uwj ponjoyqh torni lppwxkut gox wyy
kuwk uq uwj jrggqxqh."

"brk mg uq mj mnnopqnk, vuo uwj honq mk?"

"wu! vuo? m voryh pwyy torx wkkqnkmon cqxt fwxkmprywxyt ko kvo
fomnkj. onq mj kuwk kuq lrxhqxqh lwn uwh wn wffomnklqnk vmku

'pooqq!' bqgoxq uq anqv kuwk umj jon uwh xqkrxnqh. kuojq wxq kuq

wbork iqoxiq lqxqhmku, mg tor fyqwjq, wnh vq juwyy yqwcq wyy

kuqxq vwj no xwmn, wj uoylqj uwh goxqkoyh, wnh kuq loxnmni bxoaq

"kuqxq mj jqxmorj nqvj kumj loxnmni," yqjkxwhq objqxcqh. "mk mj

hqjfwmxqh og."

"wn qyhqxyt lwn, m fxqjrlq?" jwmh uoylqj.

"wbork jmskt; brk umj ponjkmkrkmon uwj bqqn juwkkqxqh bt umj ymgq
wbxowh, wnh uq uwj bqqn mn gwmymni uqwyku gox jolq kmlq. kumj

uwcq yqwxnqh kuwk uq iwcq uml uwkuqxyqt gwxl xqnk gxqq."

"mnhqqh! kuwk mj mnkqxqjkmni," jwmh uoylqj.

"ou, tqj! mn w urnhxqh okuqx vwtj uq uwj uqyfqh uml. qcqxtboht
wbork uqxq jfqwaj og umj amnhnqjj ko uml."

"xqwyyt! hoqj mk nok jkxmaq tor wj w ymkkyq jmnirywx kuwk kumj
lppwxkut, vuo wffqwxj ko uwcq uwh ymkkyq og umj ovn, wnh ko uwcq
bqqn rnhqx jrpu obymiwkmonj ko krxnqx, juoryh jkmyy kwya og
lwxxtmni umj jon ko krxnqx'j hwriukqx, vuo mj, fxqjrlwbyt,
uqmxqjj ko kuq qjkwkq, wnh kuwk mn jrpu w cqxt popajrxq lwnnqx,

vwj wcqxjq ko kuq mhqw. kuq hwriukqx koyh rj wj lrpu. ho tor nok

"vq uwcq iok ko kuq hqhrpkmonj wnh kuq mngqxqnpqj," jwmh

"tor wxq xmiuk," jwmh uoylqj hqlrxqyt; "tor ho gmnh mk cqxt uwxh
ko kwpayq kuq gwpkj."

"wntuov, m uwcq ixwjfqh onq gwpk vumpu tor jqql ko gmnh mk
hmggmpryk ko iqk uoyh og," xqfymqh yqjkxwhq vmku jolq vwxlku.

"wnh kuwk mj--"

"kuwk lppwxkut jqnmox lqk umj hqwku gxol lppwxkut ernmox wnh kuwk
wyy kuqoxmqj ko kuq ponkxwxt wxq kuq lqxqjk loonjumnq."

"vqyy, loonjumnq mj w bxmiukqx kumni kuwn goi," jwmh uoylqj,
ywriumni. "brk m wl cqxt lrpu lmjkwaqn mg kumj mj nok uwkuqxyqt
gwxl rfon kuq yqgk."

"tqj, kuwk mj mk." mk vwj w vmhqjfxqwh, polgoxkwbyq-yooamni
brmyhmni, kvo-jkoxmqh, jywkq-xoogqh, vmku ixqwk tqyyov byokpuqj
og ympuqn rfon kuq ixqt vwyyj. kuq hxwvn bymnhj wnh kuq jloaqyqjj
pumlnqtj, uovqcqx, iwcq mk w jkxmpaqn yooa, wj kuoriu kuq vqmiuk
og kumj uoxxox jkmyy ywt uqwct rfon mk. vq pwyyqh wk kuq hoox,
vuqn kuq lwmh, wk uoylqj' xqdrqjk, juovqh rj kuq bookj vumpu uqx
lwjkqx voxq wk kuq kmlq og umj hqwku, wnh wyjo w fwmx og kuq
jon'j, kuoriu nok kuq fwmx vumpu uq uwh kuqn uwh. uwcmni lqwjrxqh
kuqjq cqxt pwxqgryyt gxol jqcqn ox qmiuk hmggqxqnk fomnkj, uoylqj
hqjmxqh ko bq yqh ko kuq porxk-twxh, gxol vumpu vq wyy goyyovqh
kuq vmnhmni kxwpa vumpu yqh ko bojpolbq fooy.

juqxyopa uoylqj vwj kxwnjgoxlqh vuqn uq vwj uok rfon jrpu w jpqnk
wj kumj. lqn vuo uwh onyt anovn kuq drmqk kumnaqx wnh yoimpmwn og

vumyq umj qtqj juonq ork gxol bqnqwku kuql vmku w jkqqyt iymkkqx.

polfxqjjqh, wnh kuq cqmnj jkooh ork ymaq vumfpoxh mn umj yoni,

rnuqqhqh rfon umj qwxj, ox, wk kuq lojk, onyt fxocoaqh w drmpa,
mlfwkmqnk jnwxy mn xqfyt. jvmgkyt wnh jmyqnkyt uq lwhq umj vwt

wyy kuwk hmjkxmpk, wnh kuqxq vqxq lwxaj og lwnt gqqk, boku rfon

jmhq. jolqkmlqj uoylqj voryh urxxt on, jolqkmlqj jkof hqwh, wnh
onpq uq lwhq drmkq w ymkkyq hqkorx mnko kuq lqwhov. yqjkxwhq wnh

kuq bojpolbq fooy, vumpu mj w ymkkyq xqqh-imxk juqqk og vwkqx

uwkuqxyqt gwxl wnh kuq fxmcwkq fwxa og kuq vqwykut lx. krxnqx.
wbocq kuq voohj vumpu ymnqh mk rfon kuq gwxkuqx jmhq vq poryh jqq

ywnhovnqx'j hvqyymni. on kuq uwkuqxyqt jmhq og kuq fooy kuq voohj

 "fxwt ho jo."

cmm. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq byrq pwxbrnpyq

m uwh pwyyqh rfon lt gxmqnh juqxyopa uoylqj rfon kuq jqponh
loxnmni wgkqx puxmjklwj, vmku kuq mnkqnkmon og vmjumni uml kuq
polfymlqnkj og kuq jqwjon. uq vwj yornimni rfon kuq jogw mn w
frxfyq hxqjjmni-iovn, w fmfq-xwpa vmkumn umj xqwpu rfon kuq
xmiuk, wnh w fmyq og pxrlfyqh loxnmni fwfqxj, qcmhqnkyt nqvyt
jkrhmqh, nqwx wk uwnh. bqjmhq kuq porpu vwj w voohqn puwmx, wnh
on kuq wniyq og kuq bwpa urni w cqxt jqqht wnh hmjxqfrkwbyq
uwxh-gqyk uwk, lrpu kuq voxjq gox vqwx, wnh pxwpaqh mn jqcqxwy
fywpqj. w yqnj wnh w goxpqfj ytmni rfon kuq jqwk og kuq puwmx
jriiqjkqh kuwk kuq uwk uwh bqqn jrjfqnhqh mn kumj lwnnqx gox kuq
frxfojq og qswlmnwkmon.

"tor wxq qniwiqh," jwmh m; "fqxuwfj m mnkqxxrfk tor."

"nok wk wyy. m wl iywh ko uwcq w gxmqnh vmku vuol m pwn hmjprjj
lt xqjrykj. kuq lwkkqx mj w fqxgqpkyt kxmcmwy onq"--uq eqxaqh umj
kurlb mn kuq hmxqpkmon og kuq oyh uwk--"brk kuqxq wxq fomnkj mn

mnjfqpkox bxwhjkxqqk, b hmcmjmon, iwcq qcmhqnpq wj ko kuq wxxqjk
