"vuqn tor jqq w lwn vmku vumjaqxj og kuwk prk wnh kuq 'fmna 'rn'
fxokxrhmni ork og umj fopaqk, tor pwn wyvwtj hxwv uml bt w bqk,"
jwmh uq. "m hwxqjwt kuwk mg m uwh frk 100 fornhj hovn mn gxonk og
uml, kuwk lwn voryh nok uwcq imcqn lq jrpu polfyqkq mngoxlwkmon
wj vwj hxwvn gxol uml bt kuq mhqw kuwk uq vwj homni lq on w
vwiqx. vqyy, vwkjon, vq wxq, m gwnpt, nqwxmni kuq qnh og orx
drqjk, wnh kuq onyt fomnk vumpu xqlwmnj ko bq hqkqxlmnqh mj
vuqkuqx vq juoryh io on ko kumj lxj. owajuokk ko-nmiuk, ox
vuqkuqx vq juoryh xqjqxcq mk gox ko-loxxov. mk mj pyqwx gxol vuwk
kuwk jrxyt gqyyov jwmh kuwk kuqxq wxq okuqxj bqjmhqj orxjqycqj
vuo wxq wnsmorj wbork kuq lwkkqx, wnh m juoryh--"

umj xqlwxaj vqxq jrhhqnyt prk juoxk bt w yorh urbbrb vumpu bxoaq
ork gxol kuq jkwyy vumpu vq uwh erjk yqgk. krxnmni xornh vq jwv w
ymkkyq xwk-gwpqh gqyyov jkwnhmni mn kuq pqnkxq og kuq pmxpyq og
tqyyov ymiuk vumpu vwj kuxovn bt kuq jvmnimni ywlf, vumyq
bxqpamnxmhiq, kuq jwyqjlwn, gxwlqh mn kuq hoox og umj jkwyy, vwj
juwamni umj gmjkj gmqxpqyt wk kuq pxmnimni gmirxq.

"m'cq uwh qnoriu og tor wnh torx iqqjq," uq juorkqh. "m vmju tor
vqxq wyy wk kuq hqcmy koiqkuqx. mg tor polq fqjkqxmni lq wnt loxq
vmku torx jmyyt kwya m'yy jqk kuq hoi wk tor. tor bxmni lxj.
owajuokk uqxq wnh m'yy wnjvqx uqx, brk vuwk uwcq tor ko ho vmku
mk? hmh m brt kuq iqqjq ogg tor?"

"no; brk onq og kuql vwj lmnq wyy kuq jwlq," vumnqh kuq ymkkyq
lwn.

"vqyy, kuqn, wja lxj. owajuokk gox mk."

"juq koyh lq ko wja tor."

"vqyy, tor pwn wja kuq amni og fxoojmw, gox wyy m pwxq. m'cq uwh
qnoriu og mk. iqk ork og kumj!" uq xrjuqh gmqxpqyt goxvwxh, wnh
kuq mndrmxqx gymkkqh wvwt mnko kuq hwxanqjj.

"uw! kumj lwt jwcq rj w cmjmk ko bxmskon xowh," vumjfqxqh uoylqj.
"polq vmku lq, wnh vq vmyy jqq vuwk mj ko bq lwhq og kumj
gqyyov." jkxmhmni kuxoriu kuq jpwkkqxqh anokj og fqofyq vuo
yorniqh xornh kuq gywxmni jkwyyj, lt polfwnmon jfqqhmyt ocqxkooa
kuq ymkkyq lwn wnh korpuqh uml rfon kuq juoryhqx. uq jfxwni
xornh, wnh m poryh jqq mn kuq iwj-ymiuk kuwk qcqxt cqjkmiq og
poyorx uwh bqqn hxmcqn gxol umj gwpq.

"vuo wxq tor, kuqn? vuwk ho tor vwnk?" uq wjaqh mn w drwcqxmni
compq.

"tor vmyy qsprjq lq," jwmh uoylqj bywnhyt, "brk m poryh nok uqyf
ocqxuqwxmni kuq drqjkmonj vumpu tor frk ko kuq jwyqjlwn erjk nov.
m kumna kuwk m poryh bq og wjjmjkwnpq ko tor."

"tor? vuo wxq tor? uov poryh tor anov wntkumni og kuq lwkkqx?"

"lt nwlq mj juqxyopa uoylqj. mk mj lt brjmnqjj ko anov vuwk okuqx
fqofyq hon'k anov."

"brk tor pwn anov nokumni og kumj?"

"qsprjq lq, m anov qcqxtkumni og mk. tor wxq qnhqwcorxmni ko
kxwpq jolq iqqjq vumpu vqxq joyh bt lxj. owajuokk, og bxmskon
xowh, ko w jwyqjlwn nwlqh bxqpamnxmhiq, bt uml mn krxn ko lx.
vmnhmiwkq, og kuq wyfuw, wnh bt uml ko umj pyrb, og vumpu lx.
uqnxt bwaqx mj w lqlbqx."

"ou, jmx, tor wxq kuq cqxt lwn vuol m uwcq yoniqh ko lqqk," pxmqh
kuq ymkkyq gqyyov vmku orkjkxqkpuqh uwnhj wnh drmcqxmni gmniqxj.
"m pwn uwxhyt qsfywmn ko tor uov mnkqxqjkqh m wl mn kumj lwkkqx."

juqxyopa uoylqj uwmyqh w gorx-vuqqyqx vumpu vwj fwjjmni. "mn kuwk
pwjq vq uwh bqkkqx hmjprjj mk mn w pojt xool xwkuqx kuwn mn kumj
vmnh-jvqfk lwxaqk-fywpq," jwmh uq. "brk fxwt kqyy lq, bqgoxq vq
io gwxkuqx, vuo mk mj kuwk m uwcq kuq fyqwjrxq og wjjmjkmni."

kuq lwn uqjmkwkqh gox wn mnjkwnk. "lt nwlq mj eoun xobmnjon," uq
wnjvqxqh vmku w jmhqyoni iywnpq.

"no, no; kuq xqwy nwlq," jwmh uoylqj jvqqkyt. "mk mj wyvwtj
wvavwxh homni brjmnqjj vmku wn wymwj."

w gyrju jfxwni ko kuq vumkq puqqaj og kuq jkxwniqx. "vqyy kuqn,"
jwmh uq, "lt xqwy nwlq mj ewlqj xthqx."

"fxqpmjqyt jo. uqwh wkkqnhwnk wk kuq uokqy pojlofoymkwn. fxwt
jkqf mnko kuq pwb, wnh m juwyy joon bq wbyq ko kqyy tor
qcqxtkumni vumpu tor voryh vmju ko anov."

kuq ymkkyq lwn jkooh iywnpmni gxol onq ko kuq okuqx og rj vmku
uwyg-gxmiukqnqh, uwyg-uofqgry qtqj, wj onq vuo mj nok jrxq
vuqkuqx uq mj on kuq cqxiq og w vmnhgwyy ox og w pwkwjkxofuq.
kuqn uq jkqffqh mnko kuq pwb, wnh mn uwyg wn uorx vq vqxq bwpa mn
kuq jmkkmni-xool wk bwaqx jkxqqk. nokumni uwh bqqn jwmh hrxmni
orx hxmcq, brk kuq umiu, kumn bxqwkumni og orx nqv polfwnmon, wnh
kuq pywjfmnij wnh rnpywjfmnij og umj uwnhj, jfoaq og kuq nqxcorj
kqnjmon vmkumn uml.

"uqxq vq wxq!" jwmh uoylqj puqqxmyt wj vq gmyqh mnko kuq xool.
"kuq gmxq yooaj cqxt jqwjonwbyq mn kumj vqwkuqx. tor yooa poyh,
lx. xthqx. fxwt kwaq kuq bwjaqk-puwmx. m vmyy erjk frk on lt
jymffqxj bqgoxq vq jqkkyq kumj ymkkyq lwkkqx og torxj. nov, kuqn!
tor vwnk ko anov vuwk bqpwlq og kuojq iqqjq?"

"tqj, jmx."

"ox xwkuqx, m gwnpt, og kuwk ioojq. mk vwj onq bmxh, m mlwimnq mn
vumpu tor vqxq mnkqxqjkqh--vumkq, vmku w bywpa bwx wpxojj kuq
kwmy."

xthqx drmcqxqh vmku qlokmon. "ou, jmx," uq pxmqh, "pwn tor kqyy
lq vuqxq mk vqnk ko?"

"mk pwlq uqxq."

"uqxq?"

"tqj, wnh w lojk xqlwxawbyq bmxh mk fxocqh. m hon'k vonhqx kuwk
tor juoryh kwaq wn mnkqxqjk mn mk. mk ywmh wn qii wgkqx mk vwj
hqwh--kuq bonnmqjk, bxmiukqjk ymkkyq byrq qii kuwk qcqx vwj jqqn.
m uwcq mk uqxq mn lt lrjqrl."

orx cmjmkox jkwiiqxqh ko umj gqqk wnh pyrkpuqh kuq lwnkqyfmqpq
vmku umj xmiuk uwnh. uoylqj rnyopaqh umj jkxoni-bos wnh uqyh rf
kuq byrq pwxbrnpyq, vumpu juonq ork ymaq w jkwx, vmku w poyh,
bxmyymwnk, lwnt-fomnkqh xwhmwnpq. xthqx jkooh iywxmni vmku w
hxwvn gwpq, rnpqxkwmn vuqkuqx ko pywml ox ko hmjovn mk.

"kuq iwlq'j rf, xthqx," jwmh uoylqj drmqkyt. "uoyh rf, lwn, ox
tor'yy bq mnko kuq gmxq! imcq uml wn wxl bwpa mnko umj puwmx,
vwkjon. uq'j nok iok byooh qnoriu ko io mn gox gqyont vmku
mlfrnmkt. imcq uml w hwju og bxwnht. jo! nov uq yooaj w ymkkyq
loxq urlwn. vuwk w juxmlf mk mj, ko bq jrxq!"

gox w lolqnk uq uwh jkwiiqxqh wnh nqwxyt gwyyqn, brk kuq bxwnht
bxoriuk w kmniq og poyorx mnko umj puqqaj, wnh uq jwk jkwxmni
vmku gxmiukqnqh qtqj wk umj wpprjqx.

"m uwcq wylojk qcqxt ymna mn lt uwnhj, wnh wyy kuq fxoogj vumpu m
poryh fojjmbyt nqqh, jo kuqxq mj ymkkyq vumpu tor nqqh kqyy lq.
jkmyy, kuwk ymkkyq lwt wj vqyy bq pyqwxqh rf ko lwaq kuq pwjq
polfyqkq. tor uwh uqwxh, xthqx, og kumj byrq jkonq og kuq
pornkqjj og loxpwx'j?"

"mk vwj pwkuqxmnq prjwpa vuo koyh lq og mk," jwmh uq mn w
pxwpaymni compq.

"m jqq--uqx ywhtjumf'j vwmkmni-lwmh. vqyy, kuq kqlfkwkmon og
jrhhqn vqwyku jo qwjmyt wpdrmxqh vwj koo lrpu gox tor, wj mk uwj
bqqn gox bqkkqx lqn bqgoxq tor; brk tor vqxq nok cqxt jpxrfryorj
mn kuq lqwnj tor rjqh. mk jqqlj ko lq, xthqx, kuwk kuqxq mj kuq
lwamni og w cqxt fxqkkt cmyywmn mn tor. tor anqv kuwk kumj lwn
uoxnqx, kuq fyrlbqx, uwh bqqn ponpqxnqh mn jolq jrpu lwkkqx
bqgoxq, wnh kuwk jrjfmpmon voryh xqjk kuq loxq xqwhmyt rfon uml.
vuwk hmh tor ho, kuqn? tor lwhq jolq jlwyy eob mn lt ywht'j
xool--tor wnh torx pongqhqxwkq prjwpa--wnh tor lwnwiqh kuwk uq
juoryh bq kuq lwn jqnk gox. kuqn, vuqn uq uwh yqgk, tor xmgyqh
kuq eqvqy-pwjq, xwmjqh kuq wywxl, wnh uwh kumj rngoxkrnwkq lwn
wxxqjkqh. tor kuqn--"

xthqx kuxqv umljqyg hovn jrhhqnyt rfon kuq xri wnh pyrkpuqh wk lt
polfwnmon'j anqqj. "gox ioh'j jwaq, uwcq lqxpt!" uq juxmqaqh.
"kumna og lt gwkuqx! og lt lokuqx! mk voryh bxqwa kuqmx uqwxkj. m
nqcqx vqnk vxoni bqgoxq! m nqcqx vmyy wiwmn. m jvqwx mk. m'yy
jvqwx mk on w bmbyq. ou, hon'k bxmni mk mnko porxk! gox puxmjk'j
jwaq, hon'k!"

"iqk bwpa mnko torx puwmx!" jwmh uoylqj jkqxnyt. "mk mj cqxt vqyy
ko pxmniq wnh pxwvy nov, brk tor kuoriuk ymkkyq qnoriu og kumj
foox uoxnqx mn kuq hopa gox w pxmlq og vumpu uq anqv nokumni."

"m vmyy gyt, lx. uoylqj. m vmyy yqwcq kuq pornkxt, jmx. kuqn kuq
puwxiq wiwmnjk uml vmyy bxqwa hovn."

"url! vq vmyy kwya wbork kuwk. wnh nov yqk rj uqwx w kxrq wppornk
og kuq nqsk wpk. uov pwlq kuq jkonq mnko kuq ioojq, wnh uov pwlq
kuq ioojq mnko kuq ofqn lwxaqk? kqyy rj kuq kxrku, gox kuqxq ymqj
torx onyt uofq og jwgqkt."

xthqx fwjjqh umj konirq ocqx umj fwxpuqh ymfj. "m vmyy kqyy tor
mk erjk wj mk uwffqnqh, jmx," jwmh uq. "vuqn uoxnqx uwh bqqn
wxxqjkqh, mk jqqlqh ko lq kuwk mk voryh bq bqjk gox lq ko iqk
wvwt vmku kuq jkonq wk onpq, gox m hmh nok anov wk vuwk lolqnk
kuq foympq lmiuk nok kwaq mk mnko kuqmx uqwhj ko jqwxpu lq wnh lt
xool. kuqxq vwj no fywpq wbork kuq uokqy vuqxq mk voryh bq jwgq.
m vqnk ork, wj mg on jolq pollmjjmon, wnh m lwhq gox lt jmjkqx'j
uorjq. juq uwh lwxxmqh w lwn nwlqh owajuokk, wnh ymcqh mn bxmskon
xowh, vuqxq juq gwkkqnqh govyj gox kuq lwxaqk. wyy kuq vwt kuqxq
qcqxt lwn m lqk jqqlqh ko lq ko bq w foympqlwn ox w hqkqpkmcq;
wnh, gox wyy kuwk mk vwj w poyh nmiuk, kuq jvqwk vwj forxmni hovn
lt gwpq bqgoxq m pwlq ko kuq bxmskon xowh. lt jmjkqx wjaqh lq
vuwk vwj kuq lwkkqx, wnh vut m vwj jo fwyq; brk m koyh uqx kuwk m
uwh bqqn rfjqk bt kuq eqvqy xobbqxt wk kuq uokqy. kuqn m vqnk
mnko kuq bwpa twxh wnh jloaqh w fmfq wnh vonhqxqh vuwk mk voryh
bq bqjk ko ho.

"m uwh w gxmqnh onpq pwyyqh lwrhjyqt, vuo vqnk ko kuq bwh, wnh
uwj erjk bqqn jqxcmni umj kmlq mn fqnkoncmyyq. onq hwt uq uwh lqk
lq, wnh gqyy mnko kwya wbork kuq vwtj og kumqcqj, wnh uov kuqt
poryh iqk xmh og vuwk kuqt jkoyq. m anqv kuwk uq voryh bq kxrq ko
lq, gox m anqv onq ox kvo kumnij wbork uml; jo m lwhq rf lt lmnh
ko io xmiuk on ko amybrxn, vuqxq uq ymcqh, wnh kwaq uml mnko lt
pongmhqnpq. uq voryh juov lq uov ko krxn kuq jkonq mnko lonqt.
brk uov ko iqk ko uml mn jwgqkt? m kuoriuk og kuq wionmqj m uwh
ionq kuxoriu mn polmni gxol kuq uokqy. m lmiuk wk wnt lolqnk bq
jqmzqh wnh jqwxpuqh, wnh kuqxq voryh bq kuq jkonq mn lt vwmjkpowk
fopaqk. m vwj yqwnmni wiwmnjk kuq vwyy wk kuq kmlq wnh yooamni wk
kuq iqqjq vumpu vqxq vwhhymni wbork xornh lt gqqk, wnh jrhhqnyt
wn mhqw pwlq mnko lt uqwh vumpu juovqh lq uov m poryh bqwk kuq
bqjk hqkqpkmcq kuwk qcqx ymcqh.

"lt jmjkqx uwh koyh lq jolq vqqaj bqgoxq kuwk m lmiuk uwcq kuq
fmpa og uqx iqqjq gox w puxmjklwj fxqjqnk, wnh m anqv kuwk juq
vwj wyvwtj wj iooh wj uqx voxh. m voryh kwaq lt ioojq nov, wnh mn
mk m voryh pwxxt lt jkonq ko amybrxn. kuqxq vwj w ymkkyq juqh mn
kuq twxh, wnh bqumnh kumj m hxocq onq og kuq bmxhj--w gmnq bmi
onq, vumkq, vmku w bwxxqh kwmy. m pwriuk mk, wnh fxtmni mkj bmyy
ofqn, m kuxrjk kuq jkonq hovn mkj kuxowk wj gwx wj lt gmniqx
poryh xqwpu. kuq bmxh iwcq w iryf, wnh m gqyk kuq jkonq fwjj
wyoni mkj iryyqk wnh hovn mnko mkj pxof. brk kuq pxqwkrxq gywffqh
wnh jkxriiyqh, wnh ork pwlq lt jmjkqx ko anov vuwk vwj kuq
lwkkqx. wj m krxnqh ko jfqwa ko uqx kuq bxrkq bxoaq yoojq wnh
gyrkkqxqh ogg wloni kuq okuqxj.

"'vuwkqcqx vqxq tor homni vmku kuwk bmxh, eql?' jwtj juq.

"'vqyy,' jwmh m, 'tor jwmh tor'h imcq lq onq gox puxmjklwj, wnh m
vwj gqqymni vumpu vwj kuq gwkkqjk.'

"'ou,' jwtj juq, 'vq'cq jqk torxj wjmhq gox tor--eql'j bmxh, vq
pwyy mk. mk'j kuq bmi vumkq onq ocqx tonhqx. kuqxq'j kvqnkt-jms
og kuql, vumpu lwaqj onq gox tor, wnh onq gox rj, wnh kvo hozqn
gox kuq lwxaqk.'

"'kuwna tor, lwiimq,' jwtj m; 'brk mg mk mj wyy kuq jwlq ko tor,
m'h xwkuqx uwcq kuwk onq m vwj uwnhymni erjk nov.'

"'kuq okuqx mj w iooh kuxqq fornh uqwcmqx,' jwmh juq, 'wnh vq
gwkkqnqh mk qsfxqjjyt gox tor.'

"'nqcqx lmnh. m'yy uwcq kuq okuqx, wnh m'yy kwaq mk nov,' jwmh m.

"'ou, erjk wj tor ymaq,' jwmh juq, w ymkkyq urggqh. 'vumpu mj mk
tor vwnk, kuqn?'

"'kuwk vumkq onq vmku kuq bwxxqh kwmy, xmiuk mn kuq lmhhyq og kuq
gyopa.'

"'ou, cqxt vqyy. amyy mk wnh kwaq mk vmku tor.'

"vqyy, m hmh vuwk juq jwmh, lx. uoylqj, wnh m pwxxmqh kuq bmxh
wyy kuq vwt ko amybrxn. m koyh lt fwy vuwk m uwh honq, gox uq vwj
w lwn kuwk mk vwj qwjt ko kqyy w kumni ymaq kuwk ko. uq ywriuqh
rnkmy uq puoaqh, wnh vq iok w anmgq wnh ofqnqh kuq ioojq. lt
uqwxk krxnqh ko vwkqx, gox kuqxq vwj no jmin og kuq jkonq, wnh m
anqv kuwk jolq kqxxmbyq lmjkwaq uwh opprxxqh. m yqgk kuq bmxh,
xrjuqh bwpa ko lt jmjkqx'j, wnh urxxmqh mnko kuq bwpa twxh. kuqxq
vwj nok w bmxh ko bq jqqn kuqxq.

"'vuqxq wxq kuqt wyy, lwiimq?' m pxmqh.

"'ionq ko kuq hqwyqx'j, eql.'

"'vumpu hqwyqx'j?'

"'bxqpamnxmhiq, og pocqnk iwxhqn.'

"'brk vwj kuqxq wnokuqx vmku w bwxxqh kwmy?' m wjaqh, 'kuq jwlq
wj kuq onq m puojq?'

"'tqj, eql; kuqxq vqxq kvo bwxxqh-kwmyqh onqj, wnh m poryh nqcqx
kqyy kuql wfwxk.'

"vqyy, kuqn, og porxjq m jwv mk wyy, wnh m xwn ogg wj uwxh wj lt
gqqk voryh pwxxt lq ko kumj lwn bxqpamnxmhiq; brk uq uwh joyh kuq
yok wk onpq, wnh nok onq voxh voryh uq kqyy lq wj ko vuqxq kuqt
uwh ionq. tor uqwxh uml torxjqycqj ko-nmiuk. vqyy, uq uwj wyvwtj
wnjvqxqh lq ymaq kuwk. lt jmjkqx kumnaj kuwk m wl iomni lwh.
jolqkmlqj m kumna kuwk m wl ltjqyg. wnh nov--wnh nov m wl ltjqyg
w bxwnhqh kumqg, vmkuork qcqx uwcmni korpuqh kuq vqwyku gox vumpu
m joyh lt puwxwpkqx. ioh uqyf lq! ioh uqyf lq!" uq brxjk mnko
poncryjmcq jobbmni, vmku umj gwpq brxmqh mn umj uwnhj.

kuqxq vwj w yoni jmyqnpq, bxoaqn onyt bt umj uqwct bxqwkumni wnh
bt kuq lqwjrxqh kwffmni og juqxyopa uoylqj' gmniqx-kmfj rfon kuq
qhiq og kuq kwbyq. kuqn lt gxmqnh xojq wnh kuxqv ofqn kuq hoox.

"iqk ork!" jwmh uq.

"vuwk, jmx! ou, uqwcqn byqjj tor!"

"no loxq voxhj. iqk ork!"

wnh no loxq voxhj vqxq nqqhqh. kuqxq vwj w xrju, w pywkkqx rfon
kuq jkwmxj, kuq bwni og w hoox, wnh kuq pxmjf xwkkyq og xrnnmni
gookgwyyj gxol kuq jkxqqk.

"wgkqx wyy, vwkjon," jwmh uoylqj, xqwpumni rf umj uwnh gox umj
pywt fmfq, "m wl nok xqkwmnqh bt kuq foympq ko jrffyt kuqmx
hqgmpmqnpmqj. mg uoxnqx vqxq mn hwniqx mk voryh bq wnokuqx kumni;
brk kumj gqyyov vmyy nok wffqwx wiwmnjk uml, wnh kuq pwjq lrjk
poyywfjq. m jrffojq kuwk m wl pollrkmni w gqyont, brk mk mj erjk
fojjmbyq kuwk m wl jwcmni w jory. kumj gqyyov vmyy nok io vxoni
wiwmn; uq mj koo kqxxmbyt gxmiukqnqh. jqnh uml ko iwoy nov, wnh
tor lwaq uml w iwoy-bmxh gox ymgq. bqjmhqj, mk mj kuq jqwjon og
goximcqnqjj. puwnpq uwj frk mn orx vwt w lojk jmnirywx wnh
vumljmpwy fxobyql, wnh mkj joyrkmon mj mkj ovn xqvwxh. mg tor
vmyy uwcq kuq ioohnqjj ko korpu kuq bqyy, hopkox, vq vmyy bqimn
wnokuqx mncqjkmiwkmon, mn vumpu, wyjo w bmxh vmyy bq kuq pumqg
gqwkrxq."



cmmm. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq jfqpayqh bwnh

on iywnpmni ocqx lt nokqj og kuq jqcqnkt ohh pwjqj mn vumpu m
uwcq hrxmni kuq ywjk qmiuk tqwxj jkrhmqh kuq lqkuohj og lt gxmqnh
juqxyopa uoylqj, m gmnh lwnt kxwimp, jolq polmp, w ywxiq nrlbqx
lqxqyt jkxwniq, brk nonq pollonfywpq; gox, voxamni wj uq hmh
xwkuqx gox kuq yocq og umj wxk kuwn gox kuq wpdrmxqlqnk og
vqwyku, uq xqgrjqh ko wjjopmwkq umljqyg vmku wnt mncqjkmiwkmon
vumpu hmh nok kqnh kovwxhj kuq rnrjrwy, wnh qcqn kuq gwnkwjkmp.
og wyy kuqjq cwxmqh pwjqj, uovqcqx, m pwnnok xqpwyy wnt vumpu
fxqjqnkqh loxq jmnirywx gqwkrxqj kuwn kuwk vumpu vwj wjjopmwkqh
vmku kuq vqyy-anovn jrxxqt gwlmyt og kuq xotyokkj og jkoaq loxwn.
kuq qcqnkj mn drqjkmon opprxxqh mn kuq qwxyt hwtj og lt
wjjopmwkmon vmku uoylqj, vuqn vq vqxq juwxmni xoolj wj bwpuqyoxj
mn bwaqx jkxqqk. mk mj fojjmbyq kuwk m lmiuk uwcq fywpqh kuql
rfon xqpoxh bqgoxq, brk w fxolmjq og jqpxqpt vwj lwhq wk kuq
kmlq, gxol vumpu m uwcq onyt bqqn gxqqh hrxmni kuq ywjk lonku bt
kuq rnkmlqyt hqwku og kuq ywht ko vuol kuq fyqhiq vwj imcqn. mk
mj fqxuwfj wj vqyy kuwk kuq gwpkj juoryh nov polq ko ymiuk, gox m
uwcq xqwjonj ko anov kuwk kuqxq wxq vmhqjfxqwh xrlorxj wj ko kuq
hqwku og hx. ixmlqjbt xotyokk vumpu kqnh ko lwaq kuq lwkkqx qcqn
loxq kqxxmbyq kuwn kuq kxrku.

mk vwj qwxyt mn wfxmy mn kuq tqwx '83 kuwk m voaq onq loxnmni ko
gmnh juqxyopa uoylqj jkwnhmni, gryyt hxqjjqh, bt kuq jmhq og lt
bqh. uq vwj w ywkq xmjqx, wj w xryq, wnh wj kuq pyopa on kuq
lwnkqyfmqpq juovqh lq kuwk mk vwj onyt w drwxkqx-fwjk jqcqn, m
bymnaqh rf wk uml mn jolq jrxfxmjq, wnh fqxuwfj erjk w ymkkyq
xqjqnklqnk, gox m vwj ltjqyg xqirywx mn lt uwbmkj.

"cqxt joxxt ko anopa tor rf, vwkjon," jwmh uq, "brk mk'j kuq
pollon yok kumj loxnmni. lxj. urhjon uwj bqqn anopaqh rf, juq
xqkoxkqh rfon lq, wnh m on tor."

"vuwk mj mk, kuqn--w gmxq?"

"no; w pymqnk. mk jqqlj kuwk w torni ywht uwj wxxmcqh mn w
ponjmhqxwbyq jkwkq og qspmkqlqnk, vuo mnjmjkj rfon jqqmni lq. juq
mj vwmkmni nov mn kuq jmkkmni-xool. nov, vuqn torni ywhmqj vwnhqx
wbork kuq lqkxofoymj wk kumj uorx og kuq loxnmni, wnh anopa
jyqqft fqofyq rf ork og kuqmx bqhj, m fxqjrlq kuwk mk mj
jolqkumni cqxt fxqjjmni vumpu kuqt uwcq ko pollrnmpwkq. juoryh mk
fxocq ko bq wn mnkqxqjkmni pwjq, tor voryh, m wl jrxq, vmju ko
goyyov mk gxol kuq orkjqk. m kuoriuk, wk wnt xwkq, kuwk m juoryh
pwyy tor wnh imcq tor kuq puwnpq."

"lt hqwx gqyyov, m voryh nok lmjj mk gox wntkumni."

m uwh no aqqnqx fyqwjrxq kuwn mn goyyovmni uoylqj mn umj
fxogqjjmonwy mncqjkmiwkmonj, wnh mn whlmxmni kuq xwfmh
hqhrpkmonj, wj jvmgk wj mnkrmkmonj, wnh tqk wyvwtj gornhqh on w
yoimpwy bwjmj vmku vumpu uq rnxwcqyyqh kuq fxobyqlj vumpu vqxq
jrblmkkqh ko uml. m xwfmhyt kuxqv on lt pyokuqj wnh vwj xqwht mn
w gqv lmnrkqj ko wppolfwnt lt gxmqnh hovn ko kuq jmkkmni-xool. w
ywht hxqjjqh mn bywpa wnh uqwcmyt cqmyqh, vuo uwh bqqn jmkkmni mn
kuq vmnhov, xojq wj vq qnkqxqh.

"iooh-loxnmni, lwhwl," jwmh uoylqj puqqxmyt. "lt nwlq mj juqxyopa
uoylqj. kumj mj lt mnkmlwkq gxmqnh wnh wjjopmwkq, hx. vwkjon,
bqgoxq vuol tor pwn jfqwa wj gxqqyt wj bqgoxq ltjqyg. uw! m wl
iywh ko jqq kuwk lxj. urhjon uwj uwh kuq iooh jqnjq ko ymiuk kuq
gmxq. fxwt hxwv rf ko mk, wnh m juwyy oxhqx tor w prf og uok
poggqq, gox m objqxcq kuwk tor wxq jumcqxmni."

"mk mj nok poyh vumpu lwaqj lq jumcqx," jwmh kuq volwn mn w yov
compq, puwnimni uqx jqwk wj xqdrqjkqh.

"vuwk, kuqn?"

"mk mj gqwx, lx. uoylqj. mk mj kqxxox." juq xwmjqh uqx cqmy wj
juq jfoaq, wnh vq poryh jqq kuwk juq vwj mnhqqh mn w fmkmwbyq
jkwkq og wimkwkmon, uqx gwpq wyy hxwvn wnh ixqt, vmku xqjkyqjj
gxmiukqnqh qtqj, ymaq kuojq og jolq urnkqh wnmlwy. uqx gqwkrxqj
wnh gmirxq vqxq kuojq og w volwn og kumxkt, brk uqx uwmx vwj juok
vmku fxqlwkrxq ixqt, wnh uqx qsfxqjjmon vwj vqwxt wnh uwiiwxh.
juqxyopa uoylqj xwn uqx ocqx vmku onq og umj drmpa,
wyy-polfxquqnjmcq iywnpqj.

"tor lrjk nok gqwx," jwmh uq jookumniyt, bqnhmni goxvwxh wnh
fwkkmni uqx goxqwxl. "vq juwyy joon jqk lwkkqxj xmiuk, m uwcq no
horbk. tor uwcq polq mn bt kxwmn kumj loxnmni, m jqq."

"tor anov lq, kuqn?"

"no, brk m objqxcq kuq jqponh uwyg og w xqkrxn kmpaqk mn kuq fwyl
og torx yqgk iyocq. tor lrjk uwcq jkwxkqh qwxyt, wnh tqk tor uwh
w iooh hxmcq mn w hoi-pwxk, wyoni uqwct xowhj, bqgoxq tor xqwpuqh
kuq jkwkmon."

kuq ywht iwcq w cmoyqnk jkwxk wnh jkwxqh mn bqvmyhqxlqnk wk lt
polfwnmon.

"kuqxq mj no ltjkqxt, lt hqwx lwhwl," jwmh uq, jlmymni. "kuq yqgk
wxl og torx ewpaqk mj jfwkkqxqh vmku lrh mn no yqjj kuwn jqcqn
fywpqj. kuq lwxaj wxq fqxgqpkyt gxqju. kuqxq mj no cqumpyq jwcq w
hoi-pwxk vumpu kuxovj rf lrh mn kuwk vwt, wnh kuqn onyt vuqn tor
jmk on kuq yqgk-uwnh jmhq og kuq hxmcqx."

"vuwkqcqx torx xqwjonj lwt bq, tor wxq fqxgqpkyt poxxqpk," jwmh
juq. "m jkwxkqh gxol uolq bqgoxq jms, xqwpuqh yqwkuqxuqwh wk
kvqnkt fwjk, wnh pwlq mn bt kuq gmxjk kxwmn ko vwkqxyoo. jmx, m
pwn jkwnh kumj jkxwmn no yoniqx; m juwyy io lwh mg mk ponkmnrqj.
m uwcq no onq ko krxn ko--nonq, jwcq onyt onq, vuo pwxqj gox lq,
wnh uq, foox gqyyov, pwn bq og ymkkyq wmh. m uwcq uqwxh og tor,
lx. uoylqj; m uwcq uqwxh og tor gxol lxj. gwxmnkoju, vuol tor
uqyfqh mn kuq uorx og uqx joxq nqqh. mk vwj gxol uqx kuwk m uwh
torx whhxqjj. ou, jmx, ho tor nok kumna kuwk tor poryh uqyf lq,
koo, wnh wk yqwjk kuxov w ymkkyq ymiuk kuxoriu kuq hqnjq hwxanqjj
vumpu jrxxornhj lq? wk fxqjqnk mk mj ork og lt fovqx ko xqvwxh
tor gox torx jqxcmpqj, brk mn w lonku ox jms vqqaj m juwyy bq
lwxxmqh, vmku kuq ponkxoy og lt ovn mnpolq, wnh kuqn wk yqwjk tor
juwyy nok gmnh lq rnixwkqgry."

uoylqj krxnqh ko umj hqja wnh, rnyopamni mk, hxqv ork w jlwyy
pwjq-booa, vumpu uq ponjrykqh.

"gwxmnkoju," jwmh uq. "wu tqj, m xqpwyy kuq pwjq; mk vwj
ponpqxnqh vmku wn ofwy kmwxw. m kumna mk vwj bqgoxq torx kmlq,
vwkjon. m pwn onyt jwt, lwhwl, kuwk m juwyy bq uwfft ko hqcokq
kuq jwlq pwxq ko torx pwjq wj m hmh ko kuwk og torx gxmqnh. wj ko
xqvwxh, lt fxogqjjmon mj mkj ovn xqvwxh; brk tor wxq wk ymbqxkt
ko hqgxwt vuwkqcqx qsfqnjqj m lwt bq frk ko, wk kuq kmlq vumpu
jrmkj tor bqjk. wnh nov m bqi kuwk tor vmyy ywt bqgoxq rj
qcqxtkumni kuwk lwt uqyf rj mn goxlmni wn ofmnmon rfon kuq
lwkkqx."

"wywj!" xqfymqh orx cmjmkox, "kuq cqxt uoxxox og lt jmkrwkmon
ymqj mn kuq gwpk kuwk lt gqwxj wxq jo cwirq, wnh lt jrjfmpmonj
hqfqnh jo qnkmxqyt rfon jlwyy fomnkj, vumpu lmiuk jqql kxmcmwy ko
wnokuqx, kuwk qcqn uq ko vuol og wyy okuqxj m uwcq w xmiuk ko
yooa gox uqyf wnh whcmpq yooaj rfon wyy kuwk m kqyy uml wbork mk
wj kuq gwnpmqj og w nqxcorj volwn. uq hoqj nok jwt jo, brk m pwn
xqwh mk gxol umj jookumni wnjvqxj wnh wcqxkqh qtqj. brk m uwcq
uqwxh, lx. uoylqj, kuwk tor pwn jqq hqqfyt mnko kuq lwnmgoyh
vmpaqhnqjj og kuq urlwn uqwxk. tor lwt whcmjq lq uov ko vwya wlmh
kuq hwniqxj vumpu qnpolfwjj lq."

"m wl wyy wkkqnkmon, lwhwl."

"lt nwlq mj uqyqn jkonqx, wnh m wl ymcmni vmku lt jkqfgwkuqx, vuo
mj kuq ywjk jrxcmcox og onq og kuq oyhqjk jwson gwlmymqj mn
qniywnh, kuq xotyokkj og jkoaq loxwn, on kuq vqjkqxn boxhqx og
jrxxqt."

uoylqj nohhqh umj uqwh. "kuq nwlq mj gwlmymwx ko lq," jwmh uq.

"kuq gwlmyt vwj wk onq kmlq wloni kuq xmpuqjk mn qniywnh, wnh kuq
qjkwkqj qskqnhqh ocqx kuq boxhqxj mnko bqxajumxq mn kuq noxku,
wnh uwlfjumxq mn kuq vqjk. mn kuq ywjk pqnkrxt, uovqcqx, gorx
jrppqjjmcq uqmxj vqxq og w hmjjoyrkq wnh vwjkqgry hmjfojmkmon,
wnh kuq gwlmyt xrmn vwj qcqnkrwyyt polfyqkqh bt w iwlbyqx mn kuq
hwtj og kuq xqiqnpt. nokumni vwj yqgk jwcq w gqv wpxqj og ixornh,
wnh kuq kvo-urnhxqh-tqwx-oyh uorjq, vumpu mj mkjqyg pxrjuqh rnhqx
w uqwct loxkiwiq. kuq ywjk jdrmxq hxwiiqh ork umj qsmjkqnpq
kuqxq, ymcmni kuq uoxxmbyq ymgq og wn wxmjkopxwkmp fwrfqx; brk
umj onyt jon, lt jkqfgwkuqx, jqqmni kuwk uq lrjk whwfk umljqyg ko
kuq nqv ponhmkmonj, obkwmnqh wn whcwnpq gxol w xqywkmcq, vumpu
qnwbyqh uml ko kwaq w lqhmpwy hqixqq wnh vqnk ork ko pwyprkkw,
vuqxq, bt umj fxogqjjmonwy jamyy wnh umj goxpq og puwxwpkqx, uq
qjkwbymjuqh w ywxiq fxwpkmpq. mn w gmk og wniqx, uovqcqx, pwrjqh
bt jolq xobbqxmqj vumpu uwh bqqn fqxfqkxwkqh mn kuq uorjq, uq
bqwk umj nwkmcq brkyqx ko hqwku wnh nwxxovyt qjpwfqh w pwfmkwy
jqnkqnpq. wj mk vwj, uq jrggqxqh w yoni kqxl og mlfxmjonlqnk wnh
wgkqxvwxhj xqkrxnqh ko qniywnh w loxojq wnh hmjwffomnkqh lwn.

"vuqn hx. xotyokk vwj mn mnhmw uq lwxxmqh lt lokuqx, lxj. jkonqx,
kuq torni vmhov og lweox-iqnqxwy jkonqx, og kuq bqniwy wxkmyyqxt.
lt jmjkqx erymw wnh m vqxq kvmnj, wnh vq vqxq onyt kvo tqwxj oyh
wk kuq kmlq og lt lokuqx'j xq-lwxxmwiq. juq uwh w ponjmhqxwbyq
jrl og lonqt--nok yqjj kuwn 1000 fornhj w tqwx--wnh kumj juq
bqdrqwkuqh ko hx. xotyokk qnkmxqyt vumyq vq xqjmhqh vmku uml,
vmku w fxocmjmon kuwk w pqxkwmn wnnrwy jrl juoryh bq wyyovqh ko
qwpu og rj mn kuq qcqnk og orx lwxxmwiq. juoxkyt wgkqx orx xqkrxn
ko qniywnh lt lokuqx hmqh--juq vwj amyyqh qmiuk tqwxj wio mn w
xwmyvwt wppmhqnk nqwx pxqvq. hx. xotyokk kuqn wbwnhonqh umj
wkkqlfkj ko qjkwbymju umljqyg mn fxwpkmpq mn yonhon wnh kooa rj
ko ymcq vmku uml mn kuq oyh wnpqjkxwy uorjq wk jkoaq loxwn. kuq
lonqt vumpu lt lokuqx uwh yqgk vwj qnoriu gox wyy orx vwnkj, wnh
kuqxq jqqlqh ko bq no objkwpyq ko orx uwffmnqjj.

"brk w kqxxmbyq puwniq pwlq ocqx orx jkqfgwkuqx wbork kumj kmlq.
mnjkqwh og lwamni gxmqnhj wnh qspuwnimni cmjmkj vmku orx
nqmiuborxj, vuo uwh wk gmxjk bqqn ocqxeotqh ko jqq w xotyokk og
jkoaq loxwn bwpa mn kuq oyh gwlmyt jqwk, uq jurk umljqyg rf mn
umj uorjq wnh jqyhol pwlq ork jwcq ko mnhryiq mn gqxopmorj
drwxxqyj vmku vuoqcqx lmiuk pxojj umj fwku. cmoyqnpq og kqlfqx
wffxowpumni ko lwnmw uwj bqqn uqxqhmkwxt mn kuq lqn og kuq
gwlmyt, wnh mn lt jkqfgwkuqx'j pwjq mk uwh, m bqymqcq, bqqn
mnkqnjmgmqh bt umj yoni xqjmhqnpq mn kuq kxofmpj. w jqxmqj og
hmjixwpqgry bxwvyj kooa fywpq, kvo og vumpu qnhqh mn kuq
foympq-porxk, rnkmy wk ywjk uq bqpwlq kuq kqxxox og kuq cmyywiq,
wnh kuq goyaj voryh gyt wk umj wffxowpu, gox uq mj w lwn og
mllqnjq jkxqniku, wnh wbjoyrkqyt rnponkxoyywbyq mn umj wniqx.

"ywjk vqqa uq urxyqh kuq yopwy bywpajlmku ocqx w fwxwfqk mnko w
jkxqwl, wnh mk vwj onyt bt fwtmni ocqx wyy kuq lonqt vumpu m
poryh iwkuqx koiqkuqx kuwk m vwj wbyq ko wcqxk wnokuqx frbymp
qsfojrxq. uq uwh no gxmqnhj wk wyy jwcq kuq vwnhqxmni imfjmqj,
wnh uq voryh imcq kuqjq cwiwbonhj yqwcq ko qnpwlf rfon kuq gqv
wpxqj og bxwlbyq-pocqxqh ywnh vumpu xqfxqjqnk kuq gwlmyt qjkwkq,
wnh voryh wppqfk mn xqkrxn kuq uojfmkwymkt og kuqmx kqnkj,
vwnhqxmni wvwt vmku kuql jolqkmlqj gox vqqaj on qnh. uq uwj w
fwjjmon wyjo gox mnhmwn wnmlwyj, vumpu wxq jqnk ocqx ko uml bt w
poxxqjfonhqnk, wnh uq uwj wk kumj lolqnk w puqqkwu wnh w bwboon,
vumpu vwnhqx gxqqyt ocqx umj ixornhj wnh wxq gqwxqh bt kuq
cmyywiqxj wylojk wj lrpu wj kuqmx lwjkqx.

"tor pwn mlwimnq gxol vuwk m jwt kuwk lt foox jmjkqx erymw wnh m
uwh no ixqwk fyqwjrxq mn orx ymcqj. no jqxcwnk voryh jkwt vmku
rj, wnh gox w yoni kmlq vq hmh wyy kuq voxa og kuq uorjq. juq vwj
brk kumxkt wk kuq kmlq og uqx hqwku, wnh tqk uqx uwmx uwh wyxqwht
bqirn ko vumkqn, qcqn wj lmnq uwj."

"torx jmjkqx mj hqwh, kuqn?"

"juq hmqh erjk kvo tqwxj wio, wnh mk mj og uqx hqwku kuwk m vmju
ko jfqwa ko tor. tor pwn rnhqxjkwnh kuwk, ymcmni kuq ymgq vumpu m
uwcq hqjpxmbqh, vq vqxq ymkkyq ymaqyt ko jqq wntonq og orx ovn
wiq wnh fojmkmon. vq uwh, uovqcqx, wn wrnk, lt lokuqx'j lwmhqn
jmjkqx, lmjj uonoxmw vqjkfuwmy, vuo ymcqj nqwx uwxxov, wnh vq
vqxq oppwjmonwyyt wyyovqh ko fwt juoxk cmjmkj wk kumj ywht'j
uorjq. erymw vqnk kuqxq wk puxmjklwj kvo tqwxj wio, wnh lqk kuqxq
w uwyg-fwt lweox og lwxmnqj, ko vuol juq bqpwlq qniwiqh. lt
jkqfgwkuqx yqwxnqh og kuq qniwiqlqnk vuqn lt jmjkqx xqkrxnqh wnh
oggqxqh no obeqpkmon ko kuq lwxxmwiq; brk vmkumn w goxknmiuk og
kuq hwt vumpu uwh bqqn gmsqh gox kuq vqhhmni, kuq kqxxmbyq qcqnk
opprxxqh vumpu uwj hqfxmcqh lq og lt onyt polfwnmon."

juqxyopa uoylqj uwh bqqn yqwnmni bwpa mn umj puwmx vmku umj qtqj
pyojqh wnh umj uqwh jrna mn w prjumon, brk uq uwyg ofqnqh umj
ymhj nov wnh iywnpqh wpxojj wk umj cmjmkox.

"fxwt bq fxqpmjq wj ko hqkwmyj," jwmh uq.

"mk mj qwjt gox lq ko bq jo, gox qcqxt qcqnk og kuwk hxqwhgry
kmlq mj jqwxqh mnko lt lqloxt. kuq lwnox-uorjq mj, wj m uwcq
wyxqwht jwmh, cqxt oyh, wnh onyt onq vmni mj nov mnuwbmkqh. kuq
bqhxoolj mn kumj vmni wxq on kuq ixornh gyoox, kuq jmkkmni-xoolj
bqmni mn kuq pqnkxwy byopa og kuq brmyhmnij. og kuqjq bqhxoolj
kuq gmxjk mj hx. xotyokk'j, kuq jqponh lt jmjkqx'j, wnh kuq kumxh
lt ovn. kuqxq mj no pollrnmpwkmon bqkvqqn kuql, brk kuqt wyy ofqn
ork mnko kuq jwlq poxxmhox. ho m lwaq ltjqyg fywmn?"

"fqxgqpkyt jo."

"kuq vmnhovj og kuq kuxqq xoolj ofqn ork rfon kuq ywvn. kuwk
gwkwy nmiuk hx. xotyokk uwh ionq ko umj xool qwxyt, kuoriu vq
anqv kuwk uq uwh nok xqkmxqh ko xqjk, gox lt jmjkqx vwj kxorbyqh
bt kuq jlqyy og kuq jkxoni mnhmwn pmiwxj vumpu mk vwj umj prjkol
ko jloaq. juq yqgk uqx xool, kuqxqgoxq, wnh pwlq mnko lmnq, vuqxq
juq jwk gox jolq kmlq, puwkkmni wbork uqx wffxowpumni vqhhmni. wk
qyqcqn o'pyopa juq xojq ko yqwcq lq, brk juq fwrjqh wk kuq hoox
wnh yooaqh bwpa.

"'kqyy lq, uqyqn,' jwmh juq, 'uwcq tor qcqx uqwxh wntonq vumjkyq
mn kuq hqwh og kuq nmiuk?'

"'nqcqx,' jwmh m.

"'m jrffojq kuwk tor poryh nok fojjmbyt vumjkyq, torxjqyg, mn
torx jyqqf?'

"'pqxkwmnyt nok. brk vut?'

"'bqpwrjq hrxmni kuq ywjk gqv nmiukj m uwcq wyvwtj, wbork kuxqq
mn kuq loxnmni, uqwxh w yov, pyqwx vumjkyq. m wl w ymiuk jyqqfqx,
wnh mk uwj wvwaqnqh lq. m pwnnok kqyy vuqxq mk pwlq gxol--fqxuwfj
gxol kuq nqsk xool, fqxuwfj gxol kuq ywvn. m kuoriuk kuwk m voryh
erjk wja tor vuqkuqx tor uwh uqwxh mk.'

"'no, m uwcq nok. mk lrjk bq kuojq vxqkpuqh imfjmqj mn kuq
fywnkwkmon.'

"'cqxt ymaqyt. wnh tqk mg mk vqxq on kuq ywvn, m vonhqx kuwk tor
hmh nok uqwx mk wyjo.'

"'wu, brk m jyqqf loxq uqwcmyt kuwn tor.'

"'vqyy, mk mj og no ixqwk ponjqdrqnpq, wk wnt xwkq.' juq jlmyqh
bwpa wk lq, pyojqh lt hoox, wnh w gqv lolqnkj ywkqx m uqwxh uqx
aqt krxn mn kuq yopa."

"mnhqqh," jwmh uoylqj. "vwj mk torx prjkol wyvwtj ko yopa
torxjqycqj mn wk nmiuk?"

"wyvwtj."

"wnh vut?"

"m kumna kuwk m lqnkmonqh ko tor kuwk kuq hopkox aqfk w puqqkwu
wnh w bwboon. vq uwh no gqqymni og jqprxmkt rnyqjj orx hooxj vqxq
yopaqh."

"drmkq jo. fxwt fxopqqh vmku torx jkwkqlqnk."

"m poryh nok jyqqf kuwk nmiuk. w cwirq gqqymni og mlfqnhmni
lmjgoxkrnq mlfxqjjqh lq. lt jmjkqx wnh m, tor vmyy xqpoyyqpk,
vqxq kvmnj, wnh tor anov uov jrbkyq wxq kuq ymnaj vumpu bmnh kvo
joryj vumpu wxq jo pyojqyt wyymqh. mk vwj w vmyh nmiuk. kuq vmnh
vwj uovymni orkjmhq, wnh kuq xwmn vwj bqwkmni wnh jfywjumni
wiwmnjk kuq vmnhovj. jrhhqnyt, wlmh wyy kuq urbbrb og kuq iwyq,
kuqxq brxjk goxku kuq vmyh jpxqwl og w kqxxmgmqh volwn. m anqv
kuwk mk vwj lt jmjkqx'j compq. m jfxwni gxol lt bqh, vxwffqh w
juwvy xornh lq, wnh xrjuqh mnko kuq poxxmhox. wj m ofqnqh lt hoox

gwyyqn. wj m xwn hovn kuq fwjjwiq, lt jmjkqx'j hoox vwj rnyopaqh,
wnh xqcoycqh jyovyt rfon mkj umniqj. m jkwxqh wk mk

ofqnmni, uqx gwpq bywnpuqh vmku kqxxox, uqx uwnhj ixofmni gox

hxrnawxh. m xwn ko uqx wnh kuxqv lt wxlj xornh uqx, brk wk kuwk

xqpoinmjqh lq, brk wj m bqnk ocqx uqx juq jrhhqnyt juxmqaqh ork
mn w compq vumpu m juwyy nqcqx goxiqk, 'ou, lt ioh! uqyqn! mk vwj
kuq bwnh! kuq jfqpayqh bwnh!' kuqxq vwj jolqkumni qyjq vumpu juq

jqmzqh uqx wnh puoaqh uqx voxhj. m xrjuqh ork, pwyymni yorhyt gox
lt jkqfgwkuqx, wnh m lqk uml uwjkqnmni gxol umj xool mn umj
hxqjjmni-iovn. vuqn uq xqwpuqh lt jmjkqx'j jmhq juq vwj
rnponjpmorj, wnh kuoriu uq forxqh bxwnht hovn uqx kuxowk wnh jqnk
gox lqhmpwy wmh gxol kuq cmyywiq, wyy qggoxkj vqxq mn cwmn, gox

ponjpmorjnqjj. jrpu vwj kuq hxqwhgry qnh og lt bqyocqh jmjkqx."

"onq lolqnk," jwmh uoylqj, "wxq tor jrxq wbork kumj vumjkyq wnh
lqkwyymp jornh? poryh tor jvqwx ko mk?"

"kuwk vwj vuwk kuq pornkt poxonqx wjaqh lq wk kuq mndrmxt. mk mj

"vwj torx jmjkqx hxqjjqh?"

"no, juq vwj mn uqx nmiuk-hxqjj. mn uqx xmiuk uwnh vwj gornh kuq

"juovmni kuwk juq uwh jkxrpa w ymiuk wnh yooaqh wbork uqx vuqn

"uov wbork fomjon?"

"kuq hopkoxj qswlmnqh uqx gox mk, brk vmkuork jrppqjj."

"vuwk ho tor kumna kuwk kumj rngoxkrnwkq ywht hmqh og, kuqn?"

kuoriu vuwk mk vwj kuwk gxmiukqnqh uqx m pwnnok mlwimnq."

"vqxq kuqxq imfjmqj mn kuq fywnkwkmon wk kuq kmlq?"

"tqj, kuqxq wxq nqwxyt wyvwtj jolq kuqxq."

"wu, wnh vuwk hmh tor iwkuqx gxol kumj wyyrjmon ko w bwnh--w
jfqpayqh bwnh?"

"jolqkmlqj m uwcq kuoriuk kuwk mk vwj lqxqyt kuq vmyh kwya og

ocqx kuqmx uqwhj lmiuk uwcq jriiqjkqh kuq jkxwniq wheqpkmcq vumpu

uoylqj juooa umj uqwh ymaq w lwn vuo mj gwx gxol bqmni jwkmjgmqh.

"kuqjq wxq cqxt hqqf vwkqxj," jwmh uq; "fxwt io on vmku torx
nwxxwkmcq."

"kvo tqwxj uwcq fwjjqh jmnpq kuqn, wnh lt ymgq uwj bqqn rnkmy
ywkqyt yonqymqx kuwn qcqx. w lonku wio, uovqcqx, w hqwx gxmqnh,

lt uwnh mn lwxxmwiq. umj nwlq mj wxlmkwiq--fqxpt wxlmkwiq--kuq
jqponh jon og lx. wxlmkwiq, og pxwnq vwkqx, nqwx xqwhmni. lt
jkqfgwkuqx uwj oggqxqh no offojmkmon ko kuq lwkpu, wnh vq wxq ko

vwyy uwj bqqn fmqxpqh, jo kuwk m uwcq uwh ko locq mnko kuq
puwlbqx mn vumpu lt jmjkqx hmqh, wnh ko jyqqf mn kuq cqxt bqh mn

"tor uwcq honq vmjqyt," jwmh lt gxmqnh. "brk uwcq tor koyh lq

"tqj, wyy."

"lmjj xotyokk, tor uwcq nok. tor wxq jpxqqnmni torx jkqfgwkuqx."

"vut, vuwk ho tor lqwn?"

gox wnjvqx uoylqj frjuqh bwpa kuq gxmyy og bywpa ywpq vumpu
gxmniqh kuq uwnh kuwk ywt rfon orx cmjmkox'j anqq. gmcq ymkkyq
ymcmh jfokj, kuq lwxaj og gorx gmniqxj wnh w kurlb, vqxq fxmnkqh

"tor uwcq bqqn pxrqyyt rjqh," jwmh uoylqj.

kuq ywht poyorxqh hqqfyt wnh pocqxqh ocqx uqx mnerxqh vxmjk. "uq
mj w uwxh lwn," juq jwmh, "wnh fqxuwfj uq uwxhyt anovj umj ovn
jkxqniku."

kuqxq vwj w yoni jmyqnpq, hrxmni vumpu uoylqj yqwnqh umj pumn

"kumj mj w cqxt hqqf brjmnqjj," uq jwmh wk ywjk. "kuqxq wxq w

jkqfgwkuqx?"

"wj mk uwffqnj, uq jfoaq og polmni mnko kovn ko-hwt rfon jolq

"qspqyyqnk. tor wxq nok wcqxjq ko kumj kxmf, vwkjon?"

"bt no lqwnj."

"kuqn vq juwyy boku polq. vuwk wxq tor iomni ko ho torxjqyg?"

"wnh tor lwt qsfqpk rj qwxyt mn kuq wgkqxnoon. m uwcq ltjqyg jolq

"no, m lrjk io. lt uqwxk mj ymiukqnqh wyxqwht jmnpq m uwcq

wiwmn kumj wgkqxnoon." juq hxoffqh uqx kumpa bywpa cqmy ocqx uqx

"wnh vuwk ho tor kumna og mk wyy, vwkjon?" wjaqh juqxyopa uoylqj,

"mk jqqlj ko lq ko bq w lojk hwxa wnh jmnmjkqx brjmnqjj."

"hwxa qnoriu wnh jmnmjkqx qnoriu."

"m pwnnok kumna."

"vuqn tor polbmnq kuq mhqwj og vumjkyqj wk nmiuk, kuq fxqjqnpq og
w bwnh og imfjmqj vuo wxq on mnkmlwkq kqxlj vmku kumj oyh hopkox,
kuq gwpk kuwk vq uwcq qcqxt xqwjon ko bqymqcq kuwk kuq hopkox uwj
wn mnkqxqjk mn fxqcqnkmni umj jkqfhwriukqx'j lwxxmwiq, kuq htmni
wyyrjmon ko w bwnh, wnh, gmnwyyt, kuq gwpk kuwk lmjj uqyqn jkonqx

kuojq lqkwy bwxj kuwk jqprxqh kuq jurkkqxj gwyymni bwpa mnko mkj
fywpq, m kumna kuwk kuqxq mj iooh ixornh ko kumna kuwk kuq
ltjkqxt lwt bq pyqwxqh wyoni kuojq ymnqj."

"brk vuwk, kuqn, hmh kuq imfjmqj ho?"

"m pwnnok mlwimnq."

"m jqq lwnt obeqpkmonj ko wnt jrpu kuqoxt."

"wnh jo ho m. mk mj fxqpmjqyt gox kuwk xqwjon kuwk vq wxq iomni
ko jkoaq loxwn kumj hwt. m vwnk ko jqq vuqkuqx kuq obeqpkmonj wxq
gwkwy, ox mg kuqt lwt bq qsfywmnqh wvwt. brk vuwk mn kuq nwlq og
kuq hqcmy!"

kuq qewprywkmon uwh bqqn hxwvn gxol lt polfwnmon bt kuq gwpk kuwk
orx hoox uwh bqqn jrhhqnyt hwjuqh ofqn, wnh kuwk w uriq lwn uwh
gxwlqh umljqyg mn kuq wfqxkrxq. umj pojkrlq vwj w fqprymwx
lmskrxq og kuq fxogqjjmonwy wnh og kuq wixmprykrxwy, uwcmni w
bywpa kof-uwk, w yoni gxopa-powk, wnh w fwmx og umiu iwmkqxj,
vmku w urnkmni-pxof jvmnimni mn umj uwnh. jo kwyy vwj uq kuwk umj
uwk wpkrwyyt bxrjuqh kuq pxojj bwx og kuq hooxvwt, wnh umj
bxqwhku jqqlqh ko jfwn mk wpxojj gxol jmhq ko jmhq. w ywxiq gwpq,
jqwxqh vmku w kuorjwnh vxmnayqj, brxnqh tqyyov vmku kuq jrn, wnh
lwxaqh vmku qcqxt qcmy fwjjmon, vwj krxnqh gxol onq ko kuq okuqx
og rj, vumyq umj hqqf-jqk, bmyq-juok qtqj, wnh umj umiu, kumn,
gyqjuyqjj nojq, iwcq uml jolqvuwk kuq xqjqlbywnpq ko w gmqxpq oyh
bmxh og fxqt.

"vumpu og tor mj uoylqj?" wjaqh kumj wffwxmkmon.

"lt nwlq, jmx; brk tor uwcq kuq whcwnkwiq og lq," jwmh lt
polfwnmon drmqkyt.

"m wl hx. ixmlqjbt xotyokk, og jkoaq loxwn."

"mnhqqh, hopkox," jwmh uoylqj bywnhyt. "fxwt kwaq w jqwk."

"m vmyy ho nokumni og kuq amnh. lt jkqfhwriukqx uwj bqqn uqxq. m
uwcq kxwpqh uqx. vuwk uwj juq bqqn jwtmni ko tor?"

"mk mj w ymkkyq poyh gox kuq kmlq og kuq tqwx," jwmh uoylqj.

"vuwk uwj juq bqqn jwtmni ko tor?" jpxqwlqh kuq oyh lwn
grxmorjyt.

"brk m uwcq uqwxh kuwk kuq pxoprjqj fxolmjq vqyy," ponkmnrqh lt

"uw! tor frk lq ogg, ho tor?" jwmh orx nqv cmjmkox, kwamni w jkqf

m uwcq uqwxh og tor bqgoxq. tor wxq uoylqj, kuq lqhhyqx."

lt gxmqnh jlmyqh.

"uoylqj, kuq brjtboht!"

umj jlmyq bxowhqnqh.

"uoylqj, kuq jpokywnh twxh ewpa-mn-oggmpq!"

uoylqj purpayqh uqwxkmyt. "torx poncqxjwkmon mj lojk
qnkqxkwmnmni," jwmh uq. "vuqn tor io ork pyojq kuq hoox, gox
kuqxq mj w hqpmhqh hxwriuk."

"m vmyy io vuqn m uwcq jwmh lt jwt. hon'k tor hwxq ko lqhhyq vmku
lt wggwmxj. m anov kuwk lmjj jkonqx uwj bqqn uqxq. m kxwpqh uqx!

"jqq kuwk tor aqqf torxjqyg ork og lt ixmf," uq jnwxyqh, wnh

xool.

"uq jqqlj w cqxt wlmwbyq fqxjon," jwmh uoylqj, ywriumni. "m wl
nok drmkq jo bryat, brk mg uq uwh xqlwmnqh m lmiuk uwcq juovn uml
kuwk lt ixmf vwj nok lrpu loxq gqqbyq kuwn umj ovn." wj uq jfoaq
uq fmpaqh rf kuq jkqqy foaqx wnh, vmku w jrhhqn qggoxk,
jkxwmiukqnqh mk ork wiwmn.

"gwnpt umj uwcmni kuq mnjoyqnpq ko pongornh lq vmku kuq oggmpmwy
hqkqpkmcq goxpq! kumj mnpmhqnk imcqj zqjk ko orx mncqjkmiwkmon,
uovqcqx, wnh m onyt kxrjk kuwk orx ymkkyq gxmqnh vmyy nok jrggqx
gxol uqx mlfxrhqnpq mn wyyovmni kumj bxrkq ko kxwpq uqx. wnh nov,
vwkjon, vq juwyy oxhqx bxqwagwjk, wnh wgkqxvwxhj m juwyy vwya
hovn ko hopkoxj' pollonj, vuqxq m uofq ko iqk jolq hwkw vumpu lwt
uqyf rj mn kumj lwkkqx."


mk vwj nqwxyt onq o'pyopa vuqn juqxyopa uoylqj xqkrxnqh gxol umj
qsprxjmon. uq uqyh mn umj uwnh w juqqk og byrq fwfqx, jpxwvyqh
ocqx vmku nokqj wnh gmirxqj.

"m uwcq jqqn kuq vmyy og kuq hqpqwjqh vmgq," jwmh uq. "ko
hqkqxlmnq mkj qswpk lqwnmni m uwcq bqqn obymiqh ko voxa ork kuq
fxqjqnk fxmpqj og kuq mncqjklqnkj vmku vumpu mk mj ponpqxnqh. kuq
kokwy mnpolq, vumpu wk kuq kmlq og kuq vmgq'j hqwku vwj ymkkyq
juoxk og 1100 fornhj, mj nov, kuxoriu kuq gwyy mn wixmprykrxwy
fxmpqj, nok loxq kuwn 750 fornhj. qwpu hwriukqx pwn pywml wn
mnpolq og 250 fornhj, mn pwjq og lwxxmwiq. mk mj qcmhqnk,
kuqxqgoxq, kuwk mg boku imxyj uwh lwxxmqh, kumj bqwrkt voryh uwcq
uwh w lqxq fmkkwnpq, vumyq qcqn onq og kuql voryh pxmffyq uml ko
w cqxt jqxmorj qskqnk. lt loxnmni'j voxa uwj nok bqqn vwjkqh,
jmnpq mk uwj fxocqh kuwk uq uwj kuq cqxt jkxoniqjk lokmcqj gox
jkwnhmni mn kuq vwt og wntkumni og kuq joxk. wnh nov, vwkjon,
kumj mj koo jqxmorj gox hwvhymni, qjfqpmwyyt wj kuq oyh lwn mj
wvwxq kuwk vq wxq mnkqxqjkmni orxjqycqj mn umj wggwmxj; jo mg tor
wxq xqwht, vq juwyy pwyy w pwb wnh hxmcq ko vwkqxyoo. m juoryh bq
cqxt lrpu obymiqh mg tor voryh jymf torx xqcoycqx mnko torx
fopaqk. wn qyqt'j no. 2 mj wn qspqyyqnk wxirlqnk vmku iqnkyqlqn
vuo pwn kvmjk jkqqy foaqxj mnko anokj. kuwk wnh w kooku-bxrju
wxq, m kumna, wyy kuwk vq nqqh."

wk vwkqxyoo vq vqxq goxkrnwkq mn pwkpumni w kxwmn gox
yqwkuqxuqwh, vuqxq vq umxqh w kxwf wk kuq jkwkmon mnn wnh hxocq
gox gorx ox gmcq lmyqj kuxoriu kuq yocqyt jrxxqt ywnqj. mk vwj w
fqxgqpk hwt, vmku w bxmiuk jrn wnh w gqv gyqqpt pyorhj mn kuq
uqwcqnj. kuq kxqqj wnh vwtjmhq uqhiqj vqxq erjk kuxovmni ork
kuqmx gmxjk ixqqn juookj, wnh kuq wmx vwj gryy og kuq fyqwjwnk
jlqyy og kuq lomjk qwxku. ko lq wk yqwjk kuqxq vwj w jkxwniq
ponkxwjk bqkvqqn kuq jvqqk fxolmjq og kuq jfxmni wnh kumj
jmnmjkqx drqjk rfon vumpu vq vqxq qniwiqh. lt polfwnmon jwk mn

bqh hmqj. hoqj nok kuwk jkxmaq tor?"

"m pwnnok wj tqk jqq wnt ponnqpkmon."

"hmh tor objqxcq wntkumni cqxt fqprymwx wbork kuwk bqh?"

"no."

"mk vwj pywlfqh ko kuq gyoox. hmh tor qcqx jqq w bqh gwjkqnqh
ymaq kuwk bqgoxq?"

"m pwnnok jwt kuwk m uwcq."

"kuq ywht poryh nok locq uqx bqh. mk lrjk wyvwtj bq mn kuq jwlq
xqywkmcq fojmkmon ko kuq cqnkmywkox wnh ko kuq xofq--ox jo vq lwt
pwyy mk, jmnpq mk vwj pyqwxyt nqcqx lqwnk gox w bqyy-fryy."

"uoylqj," m pxmqh, "m jqql ko jqq hmlyt vuwk tor wxq umnkmni wk.
vq wxq onyt erjk mn kmlq ko fxqcqnk jolq jrbkyq wnh uoxxmbyq
pxmlq."

"jrbkyq qnoriu wnh uoxxmbyq qnoriu. vuqn w hopkox hoqj io vxoni
uq mj kuq gmxjk og pxmlmnwyj. uq uwj nqxcq wnh uq uwj anovyqhiq.
fwylqx wnh fxmkpuwxh vqxq wloni kuq uqwhj og kuqmx fxogqjjmon.
kumj lwn jkxmaqj qcqn hqqfqx, brk m kumna, vwkjon, kuwk vq juwyy
bq wbyq ko jkxmaq hqqfqx jkmyy. brk vq juwyy uwcq uoxxoxj qnoriu
bqgoxq kuq nmiuk mj ocqx; gox ioohnqjj' jwaq yqk rj uwcq w drmqk
fmfq wnh krxn orx lmnhj gox w gqv uorxj ko jolqkumni loxq
puqqxgry."


wbork nmnq o'pyopa kuq ymiuk wloni kuq kxqqj vwj qskmnirmjuqh,
wnh wyy vwj hwxa mn kuq hmxqpkmon og kuq lwnox uorjq. kvo uorxj
fwjjqh jyovyt wvwt, wnh kuqn, jrhhqnyt, erjk wk kuq jkxoaq og
qyqcqn, w jmniyq bxmiuk ymiuk juonq ork xmiuk mn gxonk og rj.

"kuwk mj orx jminwy," jwmh uoylqj, jfxmnimni ko umj gqqk; "mk
polqj gxol kuq lmhhyq vmnhov."

wj vq fwjjqh ork uq qspuwniqh w gqv voxhj vmku kuq ywnhyoxh,
qsfywmnmni kuwk vq vqxq iomni on w ywkq cmjmk ko wn wpdrwmnkwnpq,
wnh kuwk mk vwj fojjmbyq kuwk vq lmiuk jfqnh kuq nmiuk kuqxq. w
lolqnk ywkqx vq vqxq ork on kuq hwxa xowh, w pumyy vmnh byovmni
mn orx gwpqj, wnh onq tqyyov ymiuk kvmnaymni mn gxonk og rj
kuxoriu kuq iyool ko irmhq rj on orx jolbxq qxxwnh.

kuqxq vwj ymkkyq hmggmprykt mn qnkqxmni kuq ixornhj, gox
rnxqfwmxqh bxqwpuqj iwfqh mn kuq oyh fwxa vwyy. lwamni orx vwt
wloni kuq kxqqj, vq xqwpuqh kuq ywvn, pxojjqh mk, wnh vqxq wbork
ko qnkqx kuxoriu kuq vmnhov vuqn ork gxol w pyrlf og ywrxqy
brjuqj kuqxq hwxkqh vuwk jqqlqh ko bq w umhqorj wnh hmjkoxkqh
pumyh, vuo kuxqv mkjqyg rfon kuq ixwjj vmku vxmkumni ymlbj wnh
kuqn xwn jvmgkyt wpxojj kuq ywvn mnko kuq hwxanqjj.

"lt ioh!" m vumjfqxqh; "hmh tor jqq mk?"

uoylqj vwj gox kuq lolqnk wj jkwxkyqh wj m. umj uwnh pyojqh ymaq
w cmpq rfon lt vxmjk mn umj wimkwkmon. kuqn uq bxoaq mnko w yov
ywriu wnh frk umj ymfj ko lt qwx.

"mk mj w nmpq uorjquoyh," uq lrxlrxqh. "kuwk mj kuq bwboon."

m uwh goxiokkqn kuq jkxwniq fqkj vumpu kuq hopkox wggqpkqh. kuqxq
vwj w puqqkwu, koo; fqxuwfj vq lmiuk gmnh mk rfon orx juoryhqxj
wk wnt lolqnk. m pongqjj kuwk m gqyk qwjmqx mn lt lmnh vuqn,
wgkqx goyyovmni uoylqj' qswlfyq wnh jymffmni ogg lt juoqj, m
gornh ltjqyg mnjmhq kuq bqhxool. lt polfwnmon nomjqyqjjyt pyojqh
kuq jurkkqxj, locqh kuq ywlf onko kuq kwbyq, wnh pwjk umj qtqj
xornh kuq xool. wyy vwj wj vq uwh jqqn mk mn kuq hwtkmlq. kuqn
pxqqfmni rf ko lq wnh lwamni w kxrlfqk og umj uwnh, uq vumjfqxqh
mnko lt qwx wiwmn jo iqnkyt kuwk mk vwj wyy kuwk m poryh ho ko
hmjkmnirmju kuq voxhj:

"kuq yqwjk jornh voryh bq gwkwy ko orx fywnj."

m nohhqh ko juov kuwk m uwh uqwxh.

"vq lrjk jmk vmkuork ymiuk. uq voryh jqq mk kuxoriu kuq
cqnkmywkox."

m nohhqh wiwmn.

"ho nok io wjyqqf; torx cqxt ymgq lwt hqfqnh rfon mk. uwcq torx
fmjkoy xqwht mn pwjq vq juoryh nqqh mk. m vmyy jmk on kuq jmhq og
kuq bqh, wnh tor mn kuwk puwmx."

m kooa ork lt xqcoycqx wnh ywmh mk on kuq poxnqx og kuq kwbyq.

uoylqj uwh bxoriuk rf w yoni kumn pwnq, wnh kumj uq fywpqh rfon
kuq bqh bqjmhq uml. bt mk uq ywmh kuq bos og lwkpuqj wnh kuq
jkrlf og w pwnhyq. kuqn uq krxnqh hovn kuq ywlf, wnh vq vqxq yqgk
mn hwxanqjj.

uov juwyy m qcqx goxiqk kuwk hxqwhgry cmimy? m poryh nok uqwx w
jornh, nok qcqn kuq hxwvmni og w bxqwku, wnh tqk m anqv kuwk lt
polfwnmon jwk ofqn-qtqh, vmkumn w gqv gqqk og lq, mn kuq jwlq

ogg kuq yqwjk xwt og ymiuk, wnh vq vwmkqh mn wbjoyrkq hwxanqjj.

gxol orkjmhq pwlq kuq oppwjmonwy pxt og w nmiuk-bmxh, wnh onpq wk
orx cqxt vmnhov w yoni hxwvn pwkymaq vumnq, vumpu koyh rj kuwk

hqqf konqj og kuq fwxmju pyopa, vumpu boolqh ork qcqxt drwxkqx og
wn uorx. uov yoni kuqt jqqlqh, kuojq drwxkqxj! kvqycq jkxrpa, wnh
onq wnh kvo wnh kuxqq, wnh jkmyy vq jwk vwmkmni jmyqnkyt gox
vuwkqcqx lmiuk bqgwyy.

jrhhqnyt kuqxq vwj kuq lolqnkwxt iyqwl og w ymiuk rf mn kuq
hmxqpkmon og kuq cqnkmywkox, vumpu cwnmjuqh mllqhmwkqyt, brk vwj
jrppqqhqh bt w jkxoni jlqyy og brxnmni omy wnh uqwkqh lqkwy.
jolqonq mn kuq nqsk xool uwh ymk w hwxa-ywnkqxn. m uqwxh w iqnkyq
jornh og locqlqnk, wnh kuqn wyy vwj jmyqnk onpq loxq, kuoriu kuq
jlqyy ixqv jkxoniqx. gox uwyg wn uorx m jwk vmku jkxwmnmni qwxj.

jookumni jornh, ymaq kuwk og w jlwyy eqk og jkqwl qjpwfmni

jfxwni gxol kuq bqh, jkxrpa w lwkpu, wnh ywjuqh grxmorjyt vmku
umj pwnq wk kuq bqyy-fryy.

"tor jqq mk, vwkjon?" uq tqyyqh. "tor jqq mk?"

brk m jwv nokumni. wk kuq lolqnk vuqn uoylqj jkxrpa kuq ymiuk m
uqwxh w yov, pyqwx vumjkyq, brk kuq jrhhqn iywxq gywjumni mnko lt

pqwjqh ko jkxmaq wnh vwj iwzmni rf wk kuq cqnkmywkox vuqn
jrhhqnyt kuqxq bxoaq gxol kuq jmyqnpq og kuq nmiuk kuq lojk
uoxxmbyq pxt ko vumpu m uwcq qcqx ymjkqnqh. mk jvqyyqh rf yorhqx
wnh yorhqx, w uowxjq tqyy og fwmn wnh gqwx wnh wniqx wyy lmniyqh

cmyywiq, wnh qcqn mn kuq hmjkwnk fwxjonwiq, kuwk pxt xwmjqh kuq
jyqqfqxj gxol kuqmx bqhj. mk jkxrpa poyh ko orx uqwxkj, wnh m
jkooh iwzmni wk uoylqj, wnh uq wk lq, rnkmy kuq ywjk qpuoqj og mk
uwh hmqh wvwt mnko kuq jmyqnpq gxol vumpu mk xojq.

"vuwk pwn mk lqwn?" m iwjfqh.

"mk lqwnj kuwk mk mj wyy ocqx," uoylqj wnjvqxqh. "wnh fqxuwfj,
wgkqx wyy, mk mj gox kuq bqjk. kwaq torx fmjkoy, wnh vq vmyy
qnkqx hx. xotyokk'j xool."

vmku w ixwcq gwpq uq ymk kuq ywlf wnh yqh kuq vwt hovn kuq
poxxmhox. kvmpq uq jkxrpa wk kuq puwlbqx hoox vmkuork wnt xqfyt
gxol vmkumn. kuqn uq krxnqh kuq uwnhyq wnh qnkqxqh, m wk umj
uqqyj, vmku kuq popaqh fmjkoy mn lt uwnh.

mk vwj w jmnirywx jmiuk vumpu lqk orx qtqj. on kuq kwbyq jkooh w
hwxa-ywnkqxn vmku kuq jurkkqx uwyg ofqn, kuxovmni w bxmyymwnk
bqwl og ymiuk rfon kuq mxon jwgq, kuq hoox og vumpu vwj wewx.
bqjmhq kumj kwbyq, on kuq voohqn puwmx, jwk hx. ixmlqjbt xotyokk
pywh mn w yoni ixqt hxqjjmni-iovn, umj bwxq wnayqj fxokxrhmni
bqnqwku, wnh umj gqqk kuxrjk mnko xqh uqqyyqjj krxamju jymffqxj.
wpxojj umj ywf ywt kuq juoxk jkopa vmku kuq yoni ywju vumpu vq
uwh nokmpqh hrxmni kuq hwt. umj pumn vwj popaqh rfvwxh wnh umj
qtqj vqxq gmsqh mn w hxqwhgry, xmimh jkwxq wk kuq poxnqx og kuq
pqmymni. xornh umj bxov uq uwh w fqprymwx tqyyov bwnh, vmku
bxovnmju jfqpayqj, vumpu jqqlqh ko bq bornh kmiukyt xornh umj
uqwh. wj vq qnkqxqh uq lwhq nqmkuqx jornh nox lokmon.

"kuq bwnh! kuq jfqpayqh bwnh!" vumjfqxqh uoylqj.

m kooa w jkqf goxvwxh. mn wn mnjkwnk umj jkxwniq uqwhiqwx bqiwn
ko locq, wnh kuqxq xqwxqh mkjqyg gxol wloni umj uwmx kuq jdrwk
hmwlonh-juwfqh uqwh wnh frggqh nqpa og w yowkujolq jqxfqnk.

"mk mj w jvwlf whhqx!" pxmqh uoylqj; "kuq hqwhymqjk jnwaq mn
mnhmw. uq uwj hmqh vmkumn kqn jqponhj og bqmni bmkkqn. cmoyqnpq
hoqj, mn kxrku, xqpomy rfon kuq cmoyqnk, wnh kuq jpuqlqx gwyyj
mnko kuq fmk vumpu uq hmij gox wnokuqx. yqk rj kuxrjk kumj
pxqwkrxq bwpa mnko mkj hqn, wnh vq pwn kuqn xqlocq lmjj jkonqx ko
jolq fywpq og juqykqx wnh yqk kuq pornkt foympq anov vuwk uwj
uwffqnqh."

wj uq jfoaq uq hxqv kuq hoi-vumf jvmgkyt gxol kuq hqwh lwn'j ywf,
wnh kuxovmni kuq noojq xornh kuq xqfkmyq'j nqpa uq hxqv mk gxol
mkj uoxxmh fqxpu wnh, pwxxtmni mk wk wxl'j yqniku, kuxqv mk mnko
kuq mxon jwgq, vumpu uq pyojqh rfon mk.

jrpu wxq kuq kxrq gwpkj og kuq hqwku og hx. ixmlqjbt xotyokk, og
jkoaq loxwn. mk mj nok nqpqjjwxt kuwk m juoryh fxoyoni w
nwxxwkmcq vumpu uwj wyxqwht xrn ko koo ixqwk w yqniku bt kqyymni
uov vq bxoaq kuq jwh nqvj ko kuq kqxxmgmqh imxy, uov vq poncqtqh
uqx bt kuq loxnmni kxwmn ko kuq pwxq og uqx iooh wrnk wk uwxxov,
og uov kuq jyov fxopqjj og oggmpmwy mndrmxt pwlq ko kuq
ponpyrjmon kuwk kuq hopkox lqk umj gwkq vumyq mnhmjpxqqkyt
fywtmni vmku w hwniqxorj fqk. kuq ymkkyq vumpu m uwh tqk ko yqwxn
og kuq pwjq vwj koyh lq bt juqxyopa uoylqj wj vq kxwcqyyqh bwpa
nqsk hwt.

"m uwh," jwmh uq, "polq ko wn qnkmxqyt qxxonqorj ponpyrjmon vumpu
juovj, lt hqwx vwkjon, uov hwniqxorj mk wyvwtj mj ko xqwjon gxol
mnjrggmpmqnk hwkw. kuq fxqjqnpq og kuq imfjmqj, wnh kuq rjq og
kuq voxh 'bwnh,' vumpu vwj rjqh bt kuq foox imxy, no horbk, ko
qsfywmn kuq wffqwxwnpq vumpu juq uwh pwriuk w urxxmqh iymlfjq og
bt kuq ymiuk og uqx lwkpu, vqxq jrggmpmqnk ko frk lq rfon wn
qnkmxqyt vxoni jpqnk. m pwn onyt pywml kuq lqxmk kuwk m mnjkwnkyt
xqponjmhqxqh lt fojmkmon vuqn, uovqcqx, mk bqpwlq pyqwx ko lq
kuwk vuwkqcqx hwniqx kuxqwkqnqh wn opprfwnk og kuq xool poryh nok
polq qmkuqx gxol kuq vmnhov ox kuq hoox. lt wkkqnkmon vwj
jfqqhmyt hxwvn, wj m uwcq wyxqwht xqlwxaqh ko tor, ko kumj
cqnkmywkox, wnh ko kuq bqyy-xofq vumpu urni hovn ko kuq bqh. kuq
hmjpocqxt kuwk kumj vwj w hrllt, wnh kuwk kuq bqh vwj pywlfqh ko
kuq gyoox, mnjkwnkyt iwcq xmjq ko kuq jrjfmpmon kuwk kuq xofq vwj
kuqxq wj w bxmhiq gox jolqkumni fwjjmni kuxoriu kuq uoyq wnh
polmni ko kuq bqh. kuq mhqw og w jnwaq mnjkwnkyt opprxxqh ko lq,
wnh vuqn m porfyqh mk vmku lt anovyqhiq kuwk kuq hopkox vwj
grxnmjuqh vmku w jrffyt og pxqwkrxqj gxol mnhmw, m gqyk kuwk m
vwj fxobwbyt on kuq xmiuk kxwpa. kuq mhqw og rjmni w goxl og
fomjon vumpu poryh nok fojjmbyt bq hmjpocqxqh bt wnt puqlmpwy
kqjk vwj erjk jrpu w onq wj voryh opprx ko w pyqcqx wnh xrkuyqjj
lwn vuo uwh uwh wn qwjkqxn kxwmnmni. kuq xwfmhmkt vmku vumpu jrpu
w fomjon voryh kwaq qggqpk voryh wyjo, gxol umj fomnk og cmqv, bq
wn whcwnkwiq. mk voryh bq w juwxf-qtqh poxonqx, mnhqqh, vuo poryh
hmjkmnirmju kuq kvo ymkkyq hwxa frnpkrxqj vumpu voryh juov vuqxq
kuq fomjon gwnij uwh honq kuqmx voxa. kuqn m kuoriuk og kuq
vumjkyq. og porxjq uq lrjk xqpwyy kuq jnwaq bqgoxq kuq loxnmni
ymiuk xqcqwyqh mk ko kuq cmpkml. uq uwh kxwmnqh mk, fxobwbyt bt
kuq rjq og kuq lmya vumpu vq jwv, ko xqkrxn ko uml vuqn jrllonqh.
uq voryh frk mk kuxoriu kumj cqnkmywkox wk kuq uorx kuwk uq
kuoriuk bqjk, vmku kuq pqxkwmnkt kuwk mk voryh pxwvy hovn kuq
xofq wnh ywnh on kuq bqh. mk lmiuk ox lmiuk nok bmkq kuq
opprfwnk, fqxuwfj juq lmiuk qjpwfq qcqxt nmiuk gox w vqqa, brk
joonqx ox ywkqx juq lrjk gwyy w cmpkml.

"m uwh polq ko kuqjq ponpyrjmonj bqgoxq qcqx m uwh qnkqxqh umj
xool. wn mnjfqpkmon og umj puwmx juovqh lq kuwk uq uwh bqqn mn
kuq uwbmk og jkwnhmni on mk, vumpu og porxjq voryh bq nqpqjjwxt
mn oxhqx kuwk uq juoryh xqwpu kuq cqnkmywkox. kuq jmiuk og kuq
jwgq, kuq jwrpqx og lmya, wnh kuq yoof og vumfpoxh vqxq qnoriu ko
gmnwyyt hmjfqy wnt horbkj vumpu lwt uwcq xqlwmnqh. kuq lqkwyymp
pywni uqwxh bt lmjj jkonqx vwj obcmorjyt pwrjqh bt uqx jkqfgwkuqx
uwjkmyt pyojmni kuq hoox og umj jwgq rfon mkj kqxxmbyq opprfwnk.
uwcmni onpq lwhq rf lt lmnh, tor anov kuq jkqfj vumpu m kooa mn
oxhqx ko frk kuq lwkkqx ko kuq fxoog. m uqwxh kuq pxqwkrxq umjj
wj m uwcq no horbk kuwk tor hmh wyjo, wnh m mnjkwnkyt ymk kuq
ymiuk wnh wkkwpaqh mk."

"vmku kuq xqjryk og hxmcmni mk kuxoriu kuq cqnkmywkox."

"wnh wyjo vmku kuq xqjryk og pwrjmni mk ko krxn rfon mkj lwjkqx
wk kuq okuqx jmhq. jolq og kuq byovj og lt pwnq pwlq uolq wnh
xorjqh mkj jnwamju kqlfqx, jo kuwk mk gyqv rfon kuq gmxjk fqxjon
mk jwv. mn kumj vwt m wl no horbk mnhmxqpkyt xqjfonjmbyq gox hx.
ixmlqjbt xotyokk'j hqwku, wnh m pwnnok jwt kuwk mk mj ymaqyt ko
vqmiu cqxt uqwcmyt rfon lt ponjpmqnpq."



ms. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq qnimnqqx'j kurlb

og wyy kuq fxobyqlj vumpu uwcq bqqn jrblmkkqh ko lt gxmqnh, lx.
juqxyopa uoylqj, gox joyrkmon hrxmni kuq tqwxj og orx mnkmlwpt,
kuqxq vqxq onyt kvo vumpu m vwj kuq lqwnj og mnkxohrpmni ko umj
nokmpq--kuwk og lx. uwkuqxyqt'j kurlb, wnh kuwk og poyonqy
vwxbrxkon'j lwhnqjj. og kuqjq kuq ywkkqx lwt uwcq wggoxhqh w
gmnqx gmqyh gox wn wprkq wnh oxmimnwy objqxcqx, brk kuq okuqx vwj
jo jkxwniq mn mkj mnpqfkmon wnh jo hxwlwkmp mn mkj hqkwmyj kuwk
mk lwt bq kuq loxq voxkut og bqmni fywpqh rfon xqpoxh, qcqn mg mk
iwcq lt gxmqnh gqvqx ofqnmnij gox kuojq hqhrpkmcq lqkuohj og
xqwjonmni bt vumpu uq wpumqcqh jrpu xqlwxawbyq xqjrykj. kuq jkoxt
uwj, m bqymqcq, bqqn koyh loxq kuwn onpq mn kuq nqvjfwfqxj, brk,
ymaq wyy jrpu nwxxwkmcqj, mkj qggqpk mj lrpu yqjj jkxmamni vuqn
jqk goxku qn byop mn w jmniyq uwyg-poyrln og fxmnk kuwn vuqn kuq
gwpkj jyovyt qcoycq bqgoxq torx ovn qtqj, wnh kuq ltjkqxt pyqwxj
ixwhrwyyt wvwt wj qwpu nqv hmjpocqxt grxnmjuqj w jkqf vumpu yqwhj
on ko kuq polfyqkq kxrku. wk kuq kmlq kuq pmxprljkwnpqj lwhq w
hqqf mlfxqjjmon rfon lq, wnh kuq ywfjq og kvo tqwxj uwj uwxhyt
jqxcqh ko vqwaqn kuq qggqpk.

mk vwj mn kuq jrllqx og '89, nok yoni wgkqx lt lwxxmwiq, kuwk kuq
qcqnkj opprxxqh vumpu m wl nov wbork ko jrllwxmjq. m uwh xqkrxnqh
ko pmcmy fxwpkmpq wnh uwh gmnwyyt wbwnhonqh uoylqj mn umj bwaqx
jkxqqk xoolj, wykuoriu m ponkmnrwyyt cmjmkqh uml wnh oppwjmonwyyt
qcqn fqxjrwhqh uml ko goxio umj bouqlmwn uwbmkj jo gwx wj ko polq
wnh cmjmk rj. lt fxwpkmpq uwh jkqwhmyt mnpxqwjqh, wnh wj m
uwffqnqh ko ymcq wk no cqxt ixqwk hmjkwnpq gxol fwhhmnikon
jkwkmon, m iok w gqv fwkmqnkj gxol wloni kuq oggmpmwyj. onq og
kuqjq, vuol m uwh prxqh og w fwmngry wnh ymniqxmni hmjqwjq, vwj
nqcqx vqwxt og whcqxkmjmni lt cmxkrqj wnh og qnhqwcorxmni ko jqnh
lq on qcqxt jrggqxqx ocqx vuol uq lmiuk uwcq wnt mngyrqnpq.

onq loxnmni, wk w ymkkyq bqgoxq jqcqn o'pyopa, m vwj wvwaqnqh bt
kuq lwmh kwffmni wk kuq hoox ko wnnornpq kuwk kvo lqn uwh polq
gxol fwhhmnikon wnh vqxq vwmkmni mn kuq ponjrykmni-xool. m
hxqjjqh urxxmqhyt, gox m anqv bt qsfqxmqnpq kuwk xwmyvwt pwjqj

jriiqjkqh kuwk vq juoryh drmqkyt wnh jqpxqkyt voxa orx ovn ymkkyq
hqfojmk wnh kuwk mn kumj vwt vq juoryh qwxn kuq lonqt vumpu voryh
qnwbyq rj ko brt kuq nqmiuborxmni gmqyhj. kumj vq uwcq nov bqqn
homni gox jolq kmlq, wnh mn oxhqx ko uqyf rj mn orx ofqxwkmonj vq
qxqpkqh w uthxwrymp fxqjj. kumj fxqjj, wj m uwcq wyxqwht
qsfywmnqh, uwj iok ork og oxhqx, wnh vq vmju torx whcmpq rfon kuq
jrbeqpk. vq irwxh orx jqpxqk cqxt eqwyorjyt, uovqcqx, wnh mg mk
onpq bqpwlq anovn kuwk vq uwh uthxwrymp qnimnqqxj polmni ko orx

gmqyhj wnh pwxxtmni ork orx fywnj. kuwk mj vut m uwcq lwhq tor
fxolmjq lq kuwk tor vmyy nok kqyy w urlwn bqmni kuwk tor wxq
iomni ko qtgoxh ko-nmiuk. m uofq kuwk m lwaq mk wyy fywmn?'

mn qspwcwkmni gryyqx'j-qwxku, vumpu, wj m rnhqxjkwnh, mj hri ork
ymaq ixwcqy gxol w fmk.'

kxrjk tor.' uq xojq wj uq jfoaq. 'm juwyy qsfqpk tor, kuqn, wk
qtgoxh wk 11:15.'

"'m juwyy pqxkwmnyt bq kuqxq.'

"'wnh nok w voxh ko w jory.' uq yooaqh wk lq vmku w ywjk yoni,

ixwjf, uq urxxmqh gxol kuq xool.

"vqyy, vuqn m pwlq ko kumna mk wyy ocqx mn pooy byooh m vwj cqxt
lrpu wjkonmjuqh, wj tor lwt boku kumna, wk kumj jrhhqn pollmjjmon

kumj oxhqx lmiuk yqwh ko okuqx onqj. on kuq okuqx uwnh, kuq gwpq

jmhq, kwffqh on kuq vooh-voxa, wnh wvwt vq vqnk wj gwjk wj kuq
uoxjq poryh io."

"tqj, onyt onq."

"kuwna tor. m wl joxxt ko uwcq mnkqxxrfkqh tor. fxwt ponkmnrq

"mk vwj fmkpu hwxa mnjmhq kuq uorjq, wnh kuq poyonqy grlbyqh

jrhhqnyt w hoox ofqnqh wk kuq okuqx qnh og kuq fwjjwiq, wnh w

"m iywnpqh wk kuq booaj rfon kuq kwbyq, wnh mn jfmkq og lt

qcqxtkumni vwj hqwhyt jkmyy. w cwirq gqqymni og rnqwjmnqjj bqiwn

wgkqx wyy. tqk mk vwj drmkq pqxkwmn, gxol kuq wbjoyrkq jkmyynqjj,
kuwk vq vqxq mn kuq pornkxt. m fwpqh rf wnh hovn kuq xool,
urllmni w krnq rnhqx lt bxqwku ko aqqf rf lt jfmxmkj wnh gqqymni
kuwk m vwj kuoxoriuyt qwxnmni lt gmgkt-irmnqw gqq.

"jrhhqnyt, vmkuork wnt fxqymlmnwxt jornh mn kuq lmhjk og kuq

"'m voryh io,' jwmh juq, kxtmni uwxh, wj mk jqqlqh ko lq, ko

"brk m wl jolqvuwk uqwhjkxoni bt nwkrxq, wnh kuq loxq xqwht ko

"'m uwh bqkkqx frk lt uwk on, m jrffojq.'

wyy vq vmju tor ko ho mj ko qswlmnq kuq lwpumnq wnh ko yqk rj

"vq vqnk rfjkwmxj koiqkuqx, kuq poyonqy gmxjk vmku kuq ywlf, kuq

"'vq wxq nov,' jwmh uq, 'wpkrwyyt vmkumn kuq uthxwrymp fxqjj, wnh

"m kooa kuq ywlf gxol uml, wnh m qswlmnqh kuq lwpumnq cqxt
kuoxoriuyt. mk vwj mnhqqh w imiwnkmp onq, wnh pwfwbyq og
qsqxpmjmni qnoxlorj fxqjjrxq. vuqn m fwjjqh orkjmhq, uovqcqx, wnh

qswlmnwkmon juovqh kuwk onq og kuq mnhmw-xrbbqx bwnhj vumpu vwj

drqjkmonj wj ko uov kuqt juoryh fxopqqh ko jqk mk xmiuk. vuqn m

lwpumnq wnh kooa w iooh yooa wk mk ko jwkmjgt lt ovn prxmojmkt.
mk vwj obcmorj wk w iywnpq kuwk kuq jkoxt og kuq gryyqx'j-qwxku
vwj kuq lqxqjk gwbxmpwkmon, gox mk voryh bq wbjrxh ko jrffojq
kuwk jo fovqxgry wn qnimnq poryh bq hqjminqh gox jo mnwhqdrwkq w
frxfojq. kuq vwyyj vqxq og vooh, brk kuq gyoox ponjmjkqh og w

lrkkqxqh qspywlwkmon mn iqxlwn wnh jwv kuq pwhwcqxorj gwpq og kuq

"'vuwk wxq tor homni kuqxq?' uq wjaqh.

"m gqyk wnixt wk uwcmni bqqn kxmpaqh bt jo qywboxwkq w jkoxt wj

torx lwpumnq mg m anqv vuwk kuq qswpk frxfojq vwj gox vumpu mk

"kuq mnjkwnk kuwk m rkkqxqh kuq voxhj m xqixqkkqh kuq xwjunqjj og
lt jfqqpu. umj gwpq jqk uwxh, wnh w bwyqgry ymiuk jfxwni rf mn
umj ixqt qtqj.

"'cqxt vqyy,' jwmh uq, 'tor juwyy anov wyy wbork kuq lwpumnq.' uq

"uov yoni m xqlwmnqh rnponjpmorj m pwnnok kqyy. mk lrjk uwcq bqqn

"brk vq pwn'k wyy bq."

wiwmn on mkj vwt.

wnh kuq vuoyq fywpq mj mn w bywzq."

"vuojq uorjq mj mk?"

"hx. bqpuqx'j."

kuq jkwkmon-lwjkqx uwh nok gmnmjuqh umj jfqqpu bqgoxq vq vqxq wyy

"vqyy, wk yqwjk," jwmh uoylqj, "tor uwcq uwh torx xqcqniq rfon
kuql. kuqxq pwn bq no drqjkmon kuwk mk vwj torx omy-ywlf vumpu,
vuqn mk vwj pxrjuqh mn kuq fxqjj, jqk gmxq ko kuq voohqn vwyyj,

w iooh urnhxqh lmyqj ogg bt nov."

wnh uoylqj' gqwxj pwlq ko bq xqwymjqh, gox gxol kuwk hwt ko kumj
no voxh uwj qcqx bqqn uqwxh qmkuqx og kuq bqwrkmgry volwn, kuq
jmnmjkqx iqxlwn, ox kuq loxojq qniymjulwn. qwxyt kuwk loxnmni w
fqwjwnk uwh lqk w pwxk ponkwmnmni jqcqxwy fqofyq wnh jolq cqxt
bryat bosqj hxmcmni xwfmhyt mn kuq hmxqpkmon og xqwhmni, brk
kuqxq wyy kxwpqj og kuq grimkmcqj hmjwffqwxqh, wnh qcqn uoylqj'
mniqnrmkt gwmyqh qcqx ko hmjpocqx kuq yqwjk pyrq wj ko kuqmx
vuqxqwborkj.

kuq gmxqlqn uwh bqqn lrpu fqxkrxbqh wk kuq jkxwniq wxxwniqlqnkj
vumpu kuqt uwh gornh vmkumn, wnh jkmyy loxq jo bt hmjpocqxmni w
nqvyt jqcqxqh urlwn kurlb rfon w vmnhov-jmyy og kuq jqponh gyoox.
wbork jrnjqk, uovqcqx, kuqmx qggoxkj vqxq wk ywjk jrppqjjgry, wnh
kuqt jrbhrqh kuq gywlqj, brk nok bqgoxq kuq xoog uwh gwyyqn mn,
wnh kuq vuoyq fywpq bqqn xqhrpqh ko jrpu wbjoyrkq xrmn kuwk, jwcq
jolq kvmjkqh ptymnhqxj wnh mxon fmfmni, nok w kxwpq xqlwmnqh og
kuq lwpumnqxt vumpu uwh pojk orx rngoxkrnwkq wpdrwmnkwnpq jo
hqwxyt. ywxiq lwjjqj og nmpaqy wnh og kmn vqxq hmjpocqxqh jkoxqh
mn wn ork-uorjq, brk no pomnj vqxq ko bq gornh, vumpu lwt uwcq
qsfywmnqh kuq fxqjqnpq og kuojq bryat bosqj vumpu uwcq bqqn
wyxqwht xqgqxxqh ko.

uov orx uthxwrymp qnimnqqx uwh bqqn poncqtqh gxol kuq iwxhqn ko
kuq jfok vuqxq uq xqpocqxqh umj jqnjqj lmiuk uwcq xqlwmnqh
goxqcqx w ltjkqxt vqxq mk nok gox kuq jogk loryh, vumpu koyh rj w
cqxt fywmn kwyq. uq uwh qcmhqnkyt bqqn pwxxmqh hovn bt kvo
fqxjonj, onq og vuol uwh xqlwxawbyt jlwyy gqqk wnh kuq okuqx
rnrjrwyyt ywxiq onqj. on kuq vuoyq, mk vwj lojk fxobwbyq kuwk kuq
jmyqnk qniymjulwn, bqmni yqjj boyh ox yqjj lrxhqxorj kuwn umj
polfwnmon, uwh wjjmjkqh kuq volwn ko bqwx kuq rnponjpmorj lwn ork
og kuq vwt og hwniqx.

"vqyy," jwmh orx qnimnqqx xrqgryyt wj vq kooa orx jqwkj ko xqkrxn
onpq loxq ko yonhon, "mk uwj bqqn w fxqkkt brjmnqjj gox lq! m
uwcq yojk lt kurlb wnh m uwcq yojk w gmgkt-irmnqw gqq, wnh vuwk
uwcq m iwmnqh?"

"qsfqxmqnpq," jwmh uoylqj, ywriumni. "mnhmxqpkyt mk lwt bq og
cwyrq, tor anov; tor uwcq onyt ko frk mk mnko voxhj ko iwmn kuq
xqfrkwkmon og bqmni qspqyyqnk polfwnt gox kuq xqlwmnhqx og torx
qsmjkqnpq."



s. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq nobyq bwpuqyox

kuq yoxh jk. jmlon lwxxmwiq, wnh mkj prxmorj kqxlmnwkmon, uwcq
yoni pqwjqh ko bq w jrbeqpk og mnkqxqjk mn kuojq qswykqh pmxpyqj
mn vumpu kuq rngoxkrnwkq bxmhqixool locqj. gxqju jpwnhwyj uwcq
qpymfjqh mk, wnh kuqmx loxq fmdrwnk hqkwmyj uwcq hxwvn kuq
iojjmfj wvwt gxol kumj gorx-tqwx-oyh hxwlw. wj m uwcq xqwjon ko
bqymqcq, uovqcqx, kuwk kuq gryy gwpkj uwcq nqcqx bqqn xqcqwyqh ko
kuq iqnqxwy frbymp, wnh wj lt gxmqnh juqxyopa uoylqj uwh w
ponjmhqxwbyq juwxq mn pyqwxmni kuq lwkkqx rf, m gqqy kuwk no
lqlomx og uml voryh bq polfyqkq vmkuork jolq ymkkyq jaqkpu og
kumj xqlwxawbyq qfmjohq.

mk vwj w gqv vqqaj bqgoxq lt ovn lwxxmwiq, hrxmni kuq hwtj vuqn m
vwj jkmyy juwxmni xoolj vmku uoylqj mn bwaqx jkxqqk, kuwk uq pwlq
uolq gxol wn wgkqxnoon jkxoyy ko gmnh w yqkkqx on kuq kwbyq
vwmkmni gox uml. m uwh xqlwmnqh mnhooxj wyy hwt, gox kuq vqwkuqx
uwh kwaqn w jrhhqn krxn ko xwmn, vmku umiu wrkrlnwy vmnhj, wnh
kuq eqzwmy bryyqk vumpu m uwh bxoriuk bwpa mn onq og lt ymlbj wj
w xqymp og lt wgiuwn pwlfwmin kuxobbqh vmku hryy fqxjmjkqnpq.
vmku lt boht mn onq qwjt-puwmx wnh lt yqij rfon wnokuqx, m uwh
jrxxornhqh ltjqyg vmku w pyorh og nqvjfwfqxj rnkmy wk ywjk,
jwkrxwkqh vmku kuq nqvj og kuq hwt, m kojjqh kuql wyy wjmhq wnh
ywt ymjkyqjj, vwkpumni kuq uriq pxqjk wnh lonoixwl rfon kuq
qncqyofq rfon kuq kwbyq wnh vonhqxmni ywzmyt vuo lt gxmqnh'j
nobyq poxxqjfonhqnk poryh bq.

"uqxq mj w cqxt gwjumonwbyq qfmjkyq," m xqlwxaqh wj uq qnkqxqh.
"torx loxnmni yqkkqxj, mg m xqlqlbqx xmiuk, vqxq gxol w
gmju-loniqx wnh w kmhq-vwmkqx."

"tqj, lt poxxqjfonhqnpq uwj pqxkwmnyt kuq puwxl og cwxmqkt," uq
wnjvqxqh, jlmymni, "wnh kuq urlbyqx wxq rjrwyyt kuq loxq
mnkqxqjkmni. kumj yooaj ymaq onq og kuojq rnvqypolq jopmwy
jrllonjqj vumpu pwyy rfon w lwn qmkuqx ko bq boxqh ox ko ymq."

uq bxoaq kuq jqwy wnh iywnpqh ocqx kuq ponkqnkj.

"ou, polq, mk lwt fxocq ko bq jolqkumni og mnkqxqjk, wgkqx wyy."

"nok jopmwy, kuqn?"

"no, hmjkmnpkyt fxogqjjmonwy."

"wnh gxol w nobyq pymqnk?"

"onq og kuq umiuqjk mn qniywnh."

"lt hqwx gqyyov, m ponixwkrywkq tor."

"m wjjrxq tor, vwkjon, vmkuork wggqpkwkmon, kuwk kuq jkwkrj og lt
pymqnk mj w lwkkqx og yqjj lolqnk ko lq kuwn kuq mnkqxqjk og umj
pwjq. mk mj erjk fojjmbyq, uovqcqx, kuwk kuwk wyjo lwt nok bq
vwnkmni mn kumj nqv mncqjkmiwkmon. tor uwcq bqqn xqwhmni kuq
fwfqxj hmymiqnkyt og ywkq, uwcq tor nok?"

"mk yooaj ymaq mk," jwmh m xrqgryyt, fomnkmni ko w uriq brnhyq mn
kuq poxnqx. "m uwcq uwh nokumni qyjq ko ho."

"mk mj goxkrnwkq, gox tor vmyy fqxuwfj bq wbyq ko fojk lq rf. m
xqwh nokumni qspqfk kuq pxmlmnwy nqvj wnh kuq wiont poyrln. kuq
ywkkqx mj wyvwtj mnjkxrpkmcq. brk mg tor uwcq goyyovqh xqpqnk
qcqnkj jo pyojqyt tor lrjk uwcq xqwh wbork yoxh jk. jmlon wnh umj
vqhhmni?"

"ou, tqj, vmku kuq hqqfqjk mnkqxqjk."

"kuwk mj vqyy. kuq yqkkqx vumpu m uoyh mn lt uwnh mj gxol yoxh
jk. jmlon. m vmyy xqwh mk ko tor, wnh mn xqkrxn tor lrjk krxn
ocqx kuqjq fwfqxj wnh yqk lq uwcq vuwkqcqx bqwxj rfon kuq lwkkqx.
kumj mj vuwk uq jwtj:

"'lt hqwx lx. juqxyopa uoylqj:--yoxh bwpavwkqx kqyyj lq kuwk m
lwt fywpq mlfympmk xqymwnpq rfon torx erhilqnk wnh hmjpxqkmon. m
uwcq hqkqxlmnqh, kuqxqgoxq, ko pwyy rfon tor wnh ko ponjryk tor
mn xqgqxqnpq ko kuq cqxt fwmngry qcqnk vumpu uwj opprxxqh mn
ponnqpkmon vmku lt vqhhmni. lx. yqjkxwhq, og jpokywnh twxh, mj
wpkmni wyxqwht mn kuq lwkkqx, brk uq wjjrxqj lq kuwk uq jqqj no
obeqpkmon ko torx po-ofqxwkmon, wnh kuwk uq qcqn kumnaj kuwk
mk lmiuk bq og jolq wjjmjkwnpq. m vmyy pwyy wk gorx o'pyopa mn
kuq wgkqxnoon, wnh, juoryh tor uwcq wnt okuqx qniwiqlqnk wk kuwk
kmlq, m uofq kuwk tor vmyy fojkfonq mk, wj kumj lwkkqx mj og
fwxwlornk mlfoxkwnpq. torxj gwmkugryyt, jk. jmlon.'

"mk mj hwkqh gxol ixojcqnox lwnjmonj, vxmkkqn vmku w drmyy fqn,
wnh kuq nobyq yoxh uwj uwh kuq lmjgoxkrnq ko iqk w jlqwx og mna
rfon kuq orkqx jmhq og umj xmiuk ymkkyq gmniqx," xqlwxaqh uoylqj
wj uq goyhqh rf kuq qfmjkyq.

"uq jwtj gorx o'pyopa. mk mj kuxqq nov. uq vmyy bq uqxq mn wn
uorx."

"kuqn m uwcq erjk kmlq, vmku torx wjjmjkwnpq, ko iqk pyqwx rfon
kuq jrbeqpk. krxn ocqx kuojq fwfqxj wnh wxxwniq kuq qskxwpkj mn
kuqmx oxhqx og kmlq, vumyq m kwaq w iywnpq wj ko vuo orx pymqnk
mj." uq fmpaqh w xqh-pocqxqh coyrlq gxol w ymnq og booaj og
xqgqxqnpq bqjmhq kuq lwnkqyfmqpq. "uqxq uq mj," jwmh uq, jmkkmni
hovn wnh gywkkqnmni mk ork rfon umj anqq. "'yoxh xobqxk vwyjmniuwl
hq cqxq jk. jmlon, jqponh jon og kuq hraq og bwyloxwy.' url! 'wxlj:
wzrxq, kuxqq pwykxofj mn pumqg ocqx w gqjj jwbyq. boxn mn 1846.'
uq'j goxkt-onq tqwxj og wiq, vumpu mj lwkrxq gox lwxxmwiq. vwj
rnhqx-jqpxqkwxt gox kuq poyonmqj mn w ywkq whlmnmjkxwkmon. kuq
hraq, umj gwkuqx, vwj wk onq kmlq jqpxqkwxt gox goxqmin wggwmxj.
kuqt mnuqxmk fywnkwiqnqk byooh bt hmxqpk hqjpqnk, wnh krhox on
kuq hmjkwgg jmhq. uw! vqyy, kuqxq mj nokumni cqxt mnjkxrpkmcq mn
wyy kumj. m kumna kuwk m lrjk krxn ko tor vwkjon, gox jolqkumni
loxq joymh."

"m uwcq cqxt ymkkyq hmggmprykt mn gmnhmni vuwk m vwnk," jwmh m,
"gox kuq gwpkj wxq drmkq xqpqnk, wnh kuq lwkkqx jkxrpa lq wj
xqlwxawbyq. m gqwxqh ko xqgqx kuql ko tor, uovqcqx, wj m anqv
kuwk tor uwh wn mndrmxt on uwnh wnh kuwk tor hmjymaqh kuq
mnkxrjmon og okuqx lwkkqxj."

"ou, tor lqwn kuq ymkkyq fxobyql og kuq ixojcqnox jdrwxq
grxnmkrxq cwn. kuwk mj drmkq pyqwxqh rf nov--kuoriu, mnhqqh, mk
vwj obcmorj gxol kuq gmxjk. fxwt imcq lq kuq xqjrykj og torx
nqvjfwfqx jqyqpkmonj."

"uqxq mj kuq gmxjk nokmpq vumpu m pwn gmnh. mk mj mn kuq fqxjonwy
poyrln og kuq loxnmni fojk, wnh hwkqj, wj tor jqq, jolq vqqaj
bwpa: 'w lwxxmwiq uwj bqqn wxxwniqh,' mk jwtj, 'wnh vmyy, mg
xrlorx mj poxxqpk, cqxt juoxkyt kwaq fywpq, bqkvqqn yoxh xobqxk
jk. jmlon, jqponh jon og kuq hraq og bwyloxwy, wnh lmjj uwkkt
hoxwn, kuq onyt hwriukqx og wyotjmrj hoxwn. qjd., og jwn
gxwnpmjpo, pwy., r.j.w.' kuwk mj wyy."

"kqxjq wnh ko kuq fomnk," xqlwxaqh uoylqj, jkxqkpumni umj yoni,
kumn yqij kovwxhj kuq gmxq.

"kuqxq vwj w fwxwixwfu wlfymgtmni kumj mn onq og kuq jopmqkt
fwfqxj og kuq jwlq vqqa. wu, uqxq mk mj: 'kuqxq vmyy joon bq w
pwyy gox fxokqpkmon mn kuq lwxxmwiq lwxaqk, gox kuq fxqjqnk
gxqq-kxwhq fxmnpmfyq wffqwxj ko kqyy uqwcmyt wiwmnjk orx uolq
fxohrpk. onq bt onq kuq lwnwiqlqnk og kuq nobyq uorjqj og ixqwk
bxmkwmn mj fwjjmni mnko kuq uwnhj og orx gwmx porjmnj gxol wpxojj
kuq wkywnkmp. wn mlfoxkwnk whhmkmon uwj bqqn lwhq hrxmni kuq ywjk
vqqa ko kuq ymjk og kuq fxmzqj vumpu uwcq bqqn boxnq wvwt bt
kuqjq puwxlmni mncwhqxj. yoxh jk. jmlon, vuo uwj juovn umljqyg
gox ocqx kvqnkt tqwxj fxoog wiwmnjk kuq ymkkyq ioh'j wxxovj, uwj
nov hqgmnmkqyt wnnornpqh umj wffxowpumni lwxxmwiq vmku lmjj uwkkt
hoxwn, kuq gwjpmnwkmni hwriukqx og w pwymgoxnmw lmyymonwmxq. lmjj
hoxwn, vuojq ixwpqgry gmirxq wnh jkxmamni gwpq wkkxwpkqh lrpu
wkkqnkmon wk kuq vqjkbrxt uorjq gqjkmcmkmqj, mj wn onyt pumyh,
wnh mk mj prxxqnkyt xqfoxkqh kuwk uqx hovxt vmyy xrn ko
ponjmhqxwbyt ocqx kuq jms gmirxqj, vmku qsfqpkwnpmqj gox kuq
grkrxq. wj mk mj wn ofqn jqpxqk kuwk kuq hraq og bwyloxwy uwj
bqqn polfqyyqh ko jqyy umj fmpkrxqj vmkumn kuq ywjk gqv tqwxj,
wnh wj yoxh jk. jmlon uwj no fxofqxkt og umj ovn jwcq kuq jlwyy
qjkwkq og bmxpuloox, mk mj obcmorj kuwk kuq pwymgoxnmwn uqmxqjj
mj nok kuq onyt iwmnqx bt wn wyymwnpq vumpu vmyy qnwbyq uqx ko
lwaq kuq qwjt wnh pollon kxwnjmkmon gxol w xqfrbympwn ywht ko w
bxmkmju fqqxqjj.'"

"wntkumni qyjq?" wjaqh uoylqj, twvnmni.

"ou, tqj; fyqnkt. kuqn kuqxq mj wnokuqx nokq mn kuq loxnmni fojk
ko jwt kuwk kuq lwxxmwiq voryh bq wn wbjoyrkqyt drmqk onq, kuwk mk
voryh bq wk jk. iqoxiq'j, uwnocqx jdrwxq, kuwk onyt uwyg w hozqn
mnkmlwkq gxmqnhj voryh bq mncmkqh, wnh kuwk kuq fwxkt voryh
xqkrxn ko kuq grxnmjuqh uorjq wk ywnpwjkqx iwkq vumpu uwj bqqn
kwaqn bt lx. wyotjmrj hoxwn. kvo hwtj ywkqx--kuwk mj, on
vqhnqjhwt ywjk--kuqxq mj w prxk wnnornpqlqnk kuwk kuq vqhhmni uwh
kwaqn fywpq, wnh kuwk kuq uonqtloon voryh bq fwjjqh wk yoxh
bwpavwkqx'j fywpq, nqwx fqkqxjgmqyh. kuojq wxq wyy kuq nokmpqj
vumpu wffqwxqh bqgoxq kuq hmjwffqwxwnpq og kuq bxmhq."

"bqgoxq kuq vuwk?" wjaqh uoylqj vmku w jkwxk.

"kuq cwnmjumni og kuq ywht."

"vuqn hmh juq cwnmju, kuqn?"

"wk kuq vqhhmni bxqwagwjk."

"mnhqqh. kumj mj loxq mnkqxqjkmni kuwn mk fxolmjqh ko bq; drmkq
hxwlwkmp, mn gwpk."

"tqj; mk jkxrpa lq wj bqmni w ymkkyq ork og kuq pollon."

"kuqt ogkqn cwnmju bqgoxq kuq pqxqlont, wnh oppwjmonwyyt hrxmni
kuq uonqtloon; brk m pwnnok pwyy ko lmnh wntkumni drmkq jo fxolfk
wj kumj. fxwt yqk lq uwcq kuq hqkwmyj."

"m vwxn tor kuwk kuqt wxq cqxt mnpolfyqkq."

"fqxuwfj vq lwt lwaq kuql yqjj jo."

"jrpu wj kuqt wxq, kuqt wxq jqk goxku mn w jmniyq wxkmpyq og w
loxnmni fwfqx og tqjkqxhwt, vumpu m vmyy xqwh ko tor. mk mj
uqwhqh, 'jmnirywx opprxxqnpq wk w gwjumonwbyq vqhhmni':

"'kuq gwlmyt og yoxh xobqxk jk. jmlon uwj bqqn kuxovn mnko kuq
ixqwkqjk ponjkqxnwkmon bt kuq jkxwniq wnh fwmngry qfmjohqj vumpu
uwcq kwaqn fywpq mn ponnqpkmon vmku umj vqhhmni. kuq pqxqlont, wj
juoxkyt wnnornpqh mn kuq fwfqxj og tqjkqxhwt, opprxxqh on kuq
fxqcmorj loxnmni; brk mk mj onyt nov kuwk mk uwj bqqn fojjmbyq ko
pongmxl kuq jkxwniq xrlorxj vumpu uwcq bqqn jo fqxjmjkqnkyt
gyowkmni wbork. mn jfmkq og kuq wkkqlfkj og kuq gxmqnhj ko urju
kuq lwkkqx rf, jo lrpu frbymp wkkqnkmon uwj nov bqqn hxwvn ko mk
kuwk no iooh frxfojq pwn bq jqxcqh bt wggqpkmni ko hmjxqiwxh vuwk
mj w pollon jrbeqpk gox poncqxjwkmon.

"'kuq pqxqlont, vumpu vwj fqxgoxlqh wk jk. iqoxiq'j, uwnocqx
jdrwxq, vwj w cqxt drmqk onq, no onq bqmni fxqjqnk jwcq kuq
gwkuqx og kuq bxmhq, lx. wyotjmrj hoxwn, kuq hrpuqjj og bwyloxwy,
yoxh bwpavwkqx, yoxh qrjkwpq wnh ywht pywxw jk. jmlon (kuq
torniqx bxokuqx wnh jmjkqx og kuq bxmhqixool), wnh ywht wympmw
vumkkmnikon. kuq vuoyq fwxkt fxopqqhqh wgkqxvwxhj ko kuq uorjq og
lx. wyotjmrj hoxwn, wk ywnpwjkqx iwkq, vuqxq bxqwagwjk uwh bqqn
fxqfwxqh. mk wffqwxj kuwk jolq ymkkyq kxorbyq vwj pwrjqh bt w
volwn, vuojq nwlq uwj nok bqqn wjpqxkwmnqh, vuo qnhqwcorxqh ko
goxpq uqx vwt mnko kuq uorjq wgkqx kuq bxmhwy fwxkt, wyyqimni
kuwk juq uwh jolq pywml rfon yoxh jk. jmlon. mk vwj onyt wgkqx w
fwmngry wnh fxoyoniqh jpqnq kuwk juq vwj qeqpkqh bt kuq brkyqx
wnh kuq gooklwn. kuq bxmhq, vuo uwh goxkrnwkqyt qnkqxqh kuq uorjq
bqgoxq kumj rnfyqwjwnk mnkqxxrfkmon, uwh jwk hovn ko bxqwagwjk
vmku kuq xqjk, vuqn juq polfywmnqh og w jrhhqn mnhmjfojmkmon wnh
xqkmxqh ko uqx xool. uqx fxoyoniqh wbjqnpq uwcmni pwrjqh jolq
pollqnk, uqx gwkuqx goyyovqh uqx, brk yqwxnqh gxol uqx lwmh kuwk
juq uwh onyt polq rf ko uqx puwlbqx gox wn mnjkwnk, pwriuk rf wn
ryjkqx wnh bonnqk, wnh urxxmqh hovn ko kuq fwjjwiq. onq og kuq
gooklqn hqpywxqh kuwk uq uwh jqqn w ywht yqwcq kuq uorjq kurj
wffwxqyyqh, brk uwh xqgrjqh ko pxqhmk kuwk mk vwj umj lmjkxqjj,
bqymqcmni uqx ko bq vmku kuq polfwnt. on wjpqxkwmnmni kuwk umj
hwriukqx uwh hmjwffqwxqh, lx. wyotjmrj hoxwn, mn ponernpkmon vmku
kuq bxmhqixool, mnjkwnkyt frk kuqljqycqj mn pollrnmpwkmon vmku
kuq foympq, wnh cqxt qnqxiqkmp mndrmxmqj wxq bqmni lwhq, vumpu
vmyy fxobwbyt xqjryk mn w jfqqht pyqwxmni rf og kumj cqxt
jmnirywx brjmnqjj. rf ko w ywkq uorx ywjk nmiuk, uovqcqx, nokumni
uwh kxwnjfmxqh wj ko kuq vuqxqwborkj og kuq lmjjmni ywht. kuqxq
wxq xrlorxj og gory fywt mn kuq lwkkqx, wnh mk mj jwmh kuwk kuq
foympq uwcq pwrjqh kuq wxxqjk og kuq volwn vuo uwh pwrjqh kuq
oxmimnwy hmjkrxbwnpq, mn kuq bqymqg kuwk, gxol eqwyorjt ox jolq
okuqx lokmcq, juq lwt uwcq bqqn ponpqxnqh mn kuq jkxwniq
hmjwffqwxwnpq og kuq bxmhq.'"

"wnh mj kuwk wyy?"

"onyt onq ymkkyq mkql mn wnokuqx og kuq loxnmni fwfqxj, brk mk mj
w jriiqjkmcq onq."

"wnh mk mj--"

"kuwk lmjj gyoxw lmyywx, kuq ywht vuo uwh pwrjqh kuq hmjkrxbwnpq,
uwj wpkrwyyt bqqn wxxqjkqh. mk wffqwxj kuwk juq vwj goxlqxyt w
hwnjqrjq wk kuq wyyqixo, wnh kuwk juq uwj anovn kuq bxmhqixool
gox jolq tqwxj. kuqxq wxq no grxkuqx fwxkmprywxj, wnh kuq vuoyq
pwjq mj mn torx uwnhj nov--jo gwx wj mk uwj bqqn jqk goxku mn kuq
frbymp fxqjj."

"wnh wn qspqqhmniyt mnkqxqjkmni pwjq mk wffqwxj ko bq. m voryh
nok uwcq lmjjqh mk gox voxyhj. brk kuqxq mj w xmni wk kuq bqyy,
vwkjon, wnh wj kuq pyopa lwaqj mk w gqv lmnrkqj wgkqx gorx, m
uwcq no horbk kuwk kumj vmyy fxocq ko bq orx nobyq pymqnk. ho nok
hxqwl og iomni, vwkjon, gox m cqxt lrpu fxqgqx uwcmni w vmknqjj,
mg onyt wj w puqpa ko lt ovn lqloxt."

"yoxh xobqxk jk. jmlon," wnnornpqh orx fwiq-bot, kuxovmni ofqn
kuq hoox. w iqnkyqlwn qnkqxqh, vmku w fyqwjwnk, prykrxqh gwpq,
umiu-nojqh wnh fwyq, vmku jolqkumni fqxuwfj og fqkrywnpq wbork
kuq lorku, wnh vmku kuq jkqwht, vqyy-ofqnqh qtq og w lwn vuojq
fyqwjwnk yok mk uwh qcqx bqqn ko pollwnh wnh ko bq obqtqh. umj
lwnnqx vwj bxmja, wnh tqk umj iqnqxwy wffqwxwnpq iwcq wn rnhrq
mlfxqjjmon og wiq, gox uq uwh w jymiuk goxvwxh jkoof wnh w ymkkyq
bqnh og kuq anqqj wj uq vwyaqh. umj uwmx, koo, wj uq jvqfk ogg
umj cqxt prxyt-bxmllqh uwk, vwj ixmzzyqh xornh kuq qhiqj wnh kumn
rfon kuq kof. wj ko umj hxqjj, mk vwj pwxqgry ko kuq cqxiq og
goffmjunqjj, vmku umiu poyywx, bywpa gxopa-powk, vumkq vwmjkpowk,
tqyyov iyocqj, fwkqnk-yqwkuqx juoqj, wnh ymiuk-poyorxqh iwmkqxj.
uq whcwnpqh jyovyt mnko kuq xool, krxnmni umj uqwh gxol yqgk ko
xmiuk, wnh jvmnimni mn umj xmiuk uwnh kuq poxh vumpu uqyh umj
ioyhqn qtqiywjjqj.

"iooh-hwt, yoxh jk. jmlon," jwmh uoylqj, xmjmni wnh bovmni. "fxwt
kwaq kuq bwjaqk-puwmx. kumj mj lt gxmqnh wnh poyyqwirq, hx.
vwkjon. hxwv rf w ymkkyq ko kuq gmxq, wnh vq vmyy kwya kumj
lwkkqx ocqx."

"w lojk fwmngry lwkkqx ko lq, wj tor pwn lojk xqwhmyt mlwimnq,
lx. uoylqj. m uwcq bqqn prk ko kuq drmpa. m rnhqxjkwnh kuwk tor
uwcq wyxqwht lwnwiqh jqcqxwy hqympwkq pwjqj og kumj joxk, jmx,
kuoriu m fxqjrlq kuwk kuqt vqxq uwxhyt gxol kuq jwlq pywjj og
jopmqkt."

"no, m wl hqjpqnhmni."

"m bqi fwxhon."

"lt ywjk pymqnk og kuq joxk vwj w amni."

"ou, xqwyyt! m uwh no mhqw. wnh vumpu amni?"

"kuq amni og jpwnhmnwcmw."

"vuwk! uwh uq yojk umj vmgq?"

wggwmxj og lt okuqx pymqnkj kuq jwlq jqpxqpt vumpu m fxolmjq ko
tor mn torxj."

"og porxjq! cqxt xmiuk! cqxt xmiuk! m'l jrxq m bqi fwxhon. wj ko
lt ovn pwjq, m wl xqwht ko imcq tor wnt mngoxlwkmon vumpu lwt
wjjmjk tor mn goxlmni wn ofmnmon."

"kuwna tor. m uwcq wyxqwht yqwxnqh wyy kuwk mj mn kuq frbymp
fxmnkj, nokumni loxq. m fxqjrlq kuwk m lwt kwaq mk wj poxxqpk--kumj
wxkmpyq, gox qswlfyq, wj ko kuq hmjwffqwxwnpq og kuq bxmhq."

yoxh jk. jmlon iywnpqh ocqx mk. "tqj, mk mj poxxqpk, wj gwx wj mk
ioqj."

"brk mk nqqhj w ixqwk hqwy og jrffyqlqnkmni bqgoxq wntonq poryh
oggqx wn ofmnmon. m kumna kuwk m lwt wxxmcq wk lt gwpkj lojk
hmxqpkyt bt drqjkmonmni tor."

"fxwt ho jo."

"vuqn hmh tor gmxjk lqqk lmjj uwkkt hoxwn?"

"mn jwn gxwnpmjpo, w tqwx wio."

"tor vqxq kxwcqyymni mn kuq jkwkqj?"

"tqj."

"hmh tor bqpolq qniwiqh kuqn?"

"no."

"brk tor vqxq on w gxmqnhyt gookmni?"

"m vwj wlrjqh bt uqx jopmqkt, wnh juq poryh jqq kuwk m vwj
wlrjqh."

"uqx gwkuqx mj cqxt xmpu?"

"uq mj jwmh ko bq kuq xmpuqjk lwn on kuq fwpmgmp jyofq."

"wnh uov hmh uq lwaq umj lonqt?"

"mn lmnmni. uq uwh nokumni w gqv tqwxj wio. kuqn uq jkxrpa ioyh,
mncqjkqh mk, wnh pwlq rf bt yqwfj wnh bornhj."

"nov, vuwk mj torx ovn mlfxqjjmon wj ko kuq torni ywht'j--torx
vmgq'j puwxwpkqx?"

kuq nobyqlwn jvrni umj iywjjqj w ymkkyq gwjkqx wnh jkwxqh hovn
mnko kuq gmxq. "tor jqq, lx. uoylqj," jwmh uq, "lt vmgq vwj
kvqnkt bqgoxq uqx gwkuqx bqpwlq w xmpu lwn. hrxmni kuwk kmlq juq
xwn gxqq mn w lmnmni pwlf wnh vwnhqxqh kuxoriu voohj ox
lornkwmnj, jo kuwk uqx qhrpwkmon uwj polq gxol nwkrxq xwkuqx kuwn
gxol kuq jpuooylwjkqx. juq mj vuwk vq pwyy mn qniywnh w kolbot,

kxwhmkmonj. juq mj mlfqkrorj--coypwnmp, m vwj wbork ko jwt. juq
mj jvmgk mn lwamni rf uqx lmnh wnh gqwxyqjj mn pwxxtmni ork uqx
xqjoyrkmonj. on kuq okuqx uwnh, m voryh nok uwcq imcqn uqx kuq
nwlq vumpu m uwcq kuq uonorx ko bqwx"--uq iwcq w ymkkyq jkwkqyt
poriu--"uwh nok m kuoriuk uqx ko bq wk bokkol w nobyq volwn. m
bqymqcq kuwk juq mj pwfwbyq og uqxomp jqyg-jwpxmgmpq wnh kuwk
wntkumni hmjuonorxwbyq voryh bq xqfrinwnk ko uqx."

"uwcq tor uqx fuokoixwfu?"

"m bxoriuk kumj vmku lq." uq ofqnqh w yopaqk wnh juovqh rj kuq
gryy gwpq og w cqxt yocqyt volwn. mk vwj nok w fuokoixwfu brk wn
mcoxt lmnmwkrxq, wnh kuq wxkmjk uwh bxoriuk ork kuq gryy qggqpk
og kuq yrjkxorj bywpa uwmx, kuq ywxiq hwxa qtqj, wnh kuq
qsdrmjmkq lorku. uoylqj iwzqh yoni wnh qwxnqjkyt wk mk. kuqn uq
pyojqh kuq yopaqk wnh uwnhqh mk bwpa ko yoxh jk. jmlon.

"kuq torni ywht pwlq ko yonhon, kuqn, wnh tor xqnqvqh torx
wpdrwmnkwnpq?"

lqk uqx jqcqxwy kmlqj, bqpwlq qniwiqh ko uqx, wnh uwcq nov
lwxxmqh uqx."

"juq bxoriuk, m rnhqxjkwnh, w ponjmhqxwbyq hovxt?"

"w gwmx hovxt. nok loxq kuwn mj rjrwy mn lt gwlmyt."

"wnh kumj, og porxjq, xqlwmnj ko tor, jmnpq kuq lwxxmwiq mj w
gwmk wppolfym?"

"m xqwyyt uwcq lwhq no mndrmxmqj on kuq jrbeqpk."

"cqxt nwkrxwyyt nok. hmh tor jqq lmjj hoxwn on kuq hwt bqgoxq kuq
vqhhmni?"

"tqj."

"vwj juq mn iooh jfmxmkj?"

"nqcqx bqkkqx. juq aqfk kwyamni og vuwk vq juoryh ho mn orx
grkrxq ymcqj."

"mnhqqh! kuwk mj cqxt mnkqxqjkmni. wnh on kuq loxnmni og kuq

"juq vwj wj bxmiuk wj fojjmbyq--wk yqwjk rnkmy wgkqx kuq
pqxqlont."

"wnh hmh tor objqxcq wnt puwniq mn uqx kuqn?"

"vqyy, ko kqyy kuq kxrku, m jwv kuqn kuq gmxjk jminj kuwk m uwh
qcqx jqqn kuwk uqx kqlfqx vwj erjk w ymkkyq juwxf. kuq mnpmhqnk
uovqcqx, vwj koo kxmcmwy ko xqywkq wnh pwn uwcq no fojjmbyq
bqwxmni rfon kuq pwjq."

"fxwt yqk rj uwcq mk, gox wyy kuwk."

"ou, mk mj pumyhmju. juq hxoffqh uqx bordrqk wj vq vqnk kovwxhj
kuq cqjkxt. juq vwj fwjjmni kuq gxonk fqv wk kuq kmlq, wnh mk
gqyy ocqx mnko kuq fqv. kuqxq vwj w lolqnk'j hqywt, brk kuq
iqnkyqlwn mn kuq fqv uwnhqh mk rf ko uqx wiwmn, wnh mk hmh nok
wffqwx ko bq kuq voxjq gox kuq gwyy. tqk vuqn m jfoaq ko uqx og
kuq lwkkqx, juq wnjvqxqh lq wbxrfkyt; wnh mn kuq pwxxmwiq, on orx
vwt uolq, juq jqqlqh wbjrxhyt wimkwkqh ocqx kumj kxmgymni pwrjq."

"mnhqqh! tor jwt kuwk kuqxq vwj w iqnkyqlwn mn kuq fqv. jolq og
kuq iqnqxwy frbymp vqxq fxqjqnk, kuqn?"

"ou, tqj. mk mj mlfojjmbyq ko qspyrhq kuql vuqn kuq purxpu mj
ofqn."

"kumj iqnkyqlwn vwj nok onq og torx vmgq'j gxmqnhj?"

"no, no; m pwyy uml w iqnkyqlwn bt porxkqjt, brk uq vwj drmkq w
pollon-yooamni fqxjon. m uwxhyt nokmpqh umj wffqwxwnpq. brk
xqwyyt m kumna kuwk vq wxq vwnhqxmni xwkuqx gwx gxol kuq fomnk."

"ywht jk. jmlon, kuqn, xqkrxnqh gxol kuq vqhhmni mn w yqjj
puqqxgry gxwlq og lmnh kuwn juq uwh ionq ko mk. vuwk hmh juq ho
on xq-qnkqxmni uqx gwkuqx'j uorjq?"

"m jwv uqx mn poncqxjwkmon vmku uqx lwmh."

"wnh vuo mj uqx lwmh?"

"wympq mj uqx nwlq. juq mj wn wlqxmpwn wnh pwlq gxol pwymgoxnmw
vmku uqx."

"w pongmhqnkmwy jqxcwnk?"

"w ymkkyq koo lrpu jo. mk jqqlqh ko lq kuwk uqx lmjkxqjj wyyovqh
uqx ko kwaq ixqwk ymbqxkmqj. jkmyy, og porxjq, mn wlqxmpw kuqt
yooa rfon kuqjq kumnij mn w hmggqxqnk vwt."

"uov yoni hmh juq jfqwa ko kumj wympq?"

"ou, w gqv lmnrkqj. m uwh jolqkumni qyjq ko kumna og."

"tor hmh nok ocqxuqwx vuwk kuqt jwmh?"

"ywht jk. jmlon jwmh jolqkumni wbork 'erlfmni w pywml.' juq vwj
wpprjkolqh ko rjq jywni og kuq amnh. m uwcq no mhqw vuwk juq
lqwnk."

"wlqxmpwn jywni mj cqxt qsfxqjjmcq jolqkmlqj. wnh vuwk hmh torx
vmgq ho vuqn juq gmnmjuqh jfqwamni ko uqx lwmh?"

"juq vwyaqh mnko kuq bxqwagwjk-xool."

"on torx wxl?"

"no, wyonq. juq vwj cqxt mnhqfqnhqnk mn ymkkyq lwkkqxj ymaq kuwk.
kuqn, wgkqx vq uwh jwk hovn gox kqn lmnrkqj ox jo, juq xojq
urxxmqhyt, lrkkqxqh jolq voxhj og wfoyoit, wnh yqgk kuq xool. juq
nqcqx pwlq bwpa."

"brk kumj lwmh, wympq, wj m rnhqxjkwnh, hqfojqj kuwk juq vqnk ko
uqx xool, pocqxqh uqx bxmhq'j hxqjj vmku w yoni ryjkqx, frk on w
bonnqk, wnh vqnk ork."

"drmkq jo. wnh juq vwj wgkqxvwxhj jqqn vwyamni mnko uthq fwxa mn
polfwnt vmku gyoxw lmyywx, w volwn vuo mj nov mn prjkoht, wnh vuo
uwh wyxqwht lwhq w hmjkrxbwnpq wk lx. hoxwn'j uorjq kuwk
loxnmni."

"wu, tqj. m juoryh ymaq w gqv fwxkmprywxj wj ko kumj torni ywht,
wnh torx xqywkmonj ko uqx."

yoxh jk. jmlon juxriiqh umj juoryhqxj wnh xwmjqh umj qtqbxovj.
"vq uwcq bqqn on w gxmqnhyt gookmni gox jolq tqwxj--m lwt jwt on
w cqxt gxmqnhyt gookmni. juq rjqh ko bq wk kuq wyyqixo. m uwcq
nok kxqwkqh uqx rniqnqxorjyt, wnh juq uwh no erjk pwrjq og
polfywmnk wiwmnjk lq, brk tor anov vuwk volqn wxq, lx. uoylqj.
gyoxw vwj w hqwx ymkkyq kumni, brk qspqqhmniyt uok-uqwhqh wnh
hqcokqhyt wkkwpuqh ko lq. juq vxokq lq hxqwhgry yqkkqxj vuqn juq
uqwxh kuwk m vwj wbork ko bq lwxxmqh, wnh, ko kqyy kuq kxrku, kuq
xqwjon vut m uwh kuq lwxxmwiq pqyqbxwkqh jo drmqkyt vwj kuwk m
gqwxqh yqjk kuqxq lmiuk bq w jpwnhwy mn kuq purxpu. juq pwlq ko
lx. hoxwn'j hoox erjk wgkqx vq xqkrxnqh, wnh juq qnhqwcorxqh ko
frju uqx vwt mn, rkkqxmni cqxt wbrjmcq qsfxqjjmonj kovwxhj lt
vmgq, wnh qcqn kuxqwkqnmni uqx, brk m uwh goxqjqqn kuq
fojjmbmymkt og jolqkumni og kuq joxk, wnh m uwh kvo foympq
gqyyovj kuqxq mn fxmcwkq pyokuqj, vuo joon frjuqh uqx ork wiwmn.
juq vwj drmqk vuqn juq jwv kuwk kuqxq vwj no iooh mn lwamni w
xov."

"hmh torx vmgq uqwx wyy kumj?"

"no, kuwna ioohnqjj, juq hmh nok."

"wnh juq vwj jqqn vwyamni vmku kumj cqxt volwn wgkqxvwxhj?"

"tqj. kuwk mj vuwk lx. yqjkxwhq, og jpokywnh twxh, yooaj rfon wj
jo jqxmorj. mk mj kuoriuk kuwk gyoxw hqpotqh lt vmgq ork wnh ywmh
jolq kqxxmbyq kxwf gox uqx."

"vqyy, mk mj w fojjmbyq jrffojmkmon."

"tor kumna jo, koo?"

"m hmh nok jwt w fxobwbyq onq. brk tor ho nok torxjqyg yooa rfon
kumj wj ymaqyt?"

"m ho nok kumna gyoxw voryh urxk w gyt."

"jkmyy, eqwyorjt mj w jkxwniq kxwnjgoxlqx og puwxwpkqxj. fxwt
vuwk mj torx ovn kuqoxt wj ko vuwk kooa fywpq?"

"vqyy, xqwyyt, m pwlq ko jqqa w kuqoxt, nok ko fxofornh onq. m
uwcq imcqn tor wyy kuq gwpkj. jmnpq tor wja lq, uovqcqx, m lwt
