kumj wggwmx, kuq ponjpmorjnqjj kuwk juq uwh lwhq jo mllqnjq w
jopmwy jkxmhq, uwh kuq qggqpk og pwrjmni jolq ymkkyq nqxcorj
hmjkrxbwnpq mn lt vmgq."

"mn juoxk, kuwk juq uwh bqpolq jrhhqnyt hqxwniqh?"

"vqyy, xqwyyt, vuqn m ponjmhqx kuwk juq uwj krxnqh uqx bwpa--m
vmyy nok jwt rfon lq, brk rfon jo lrpu kuwk lwnt uwcq wjfmxqh ko
vmkuork jrppqjj--m pwn uwxhyt qsfywmn mk mn wnt okuqx gwjumon."

"vqyy, pqxkwmnyt kuwk mj wyjo w ponpqmcwbyq utfokuqjmj," jwmh
uoylqj, jlmymni. "wnh nov, yoxh jk. jmlon, m kumna kuwk m uwcq
nqwxyt wyy lt hwkw. lwt m wja vuqkuqx tor vqxq jqwkqh wk kuq
bxqwagwjk-kwbyq jo kuwk tor poryh jqq ork og kuq vmnhov?"

"vq poryh jqq kuq okuqx jmhq og kuq xowh wnh kuq fwxa."

"drmkq jo. kuqn m ho nok kumna kuwk m nqqh ko hqkwmn tor yoniqx.
m juwyy pollrnmpwkq vmku tor."

"juoryh tor bq goxkrnwkq qnoriu ko joycq kumj fxobyql," jwmh orx
pymqnk, xmjmni.

"m uwcq joycqh mk."

"qu? vuwk vwj kuwk?"

"m jwt kuwk m uwcq joycqh mk."

"vuqxq, kuqn, mj lt vmgq?"

"kuwk mj w hqkwmy vumpu m juwyy jfqqhmyt jrffyt."

yoxh jk. jmlon juooa umj uqwh. "m wl wgxwmh kuwk mk vmyy kwaq
vmjqx uqwhj kuwn torxj ox lmnq," uq xqlwxaqh, wnh bovmni mn w
jkwkqyt, oyh-gwjumonqh lwnnqx uq hqfwxkqh.

"mk mj cqxt iooh og yoxh jk. jmlon ko uonorx lt uqwh bt frkkmni
mk on w yqcqy vmku umj ovn," jwmh juqxyopa uoylqj, ywriumni. "m
kumna kuwk m juwyy uwcq w vumjat wnh johw wnh w pmiwx wgkqx wyy
kumj pxojj-drqjkmonmni. m uwh goxlqh lt ponpyrjmonj wj ko kuq
pwjq bqgoxq orx pymqnk pwlq mnko kuq xool."

"lt hqwx uoylqj!"

"m uwcq nokqj og jqcqxwy jmlmywx pwjqj, kuoriu nonq, wj m
xqlwxaqh bqgoxq, vumpu vqxq drmkq wj fxolfk. lt vuoyq qswlmnwkmon
jqxcqh ko krxn lt poneqpkrxq mnko w pqxkwmnkt. pmxprljkwnkmwy
qcmhqnpq mj oppwjmonwyyt cqxt poncmnpmni, wj vuqn tor gmnh w
kxork mn kuq lmya, ko drokq kuoxqwr'j qswlfyq."

"brk m uwcq uqwxh wyy kuwk tor uwcq uqwxh."

"vmkuork, uovqcqx, kuq anovyqhiq og fxq-qsmjkmni pwjqj vumpu
jqxcqj lq jo vqyy. kuqxq vwj w fwxwyyqy mnjkwnpq mn wbqxhqqn jolq
tqwxj bwpa, wnh jolqkumni on cqxt lrpu kuq jwlq ymnqj wk lrnmpu
kuq tqwx wgkqx kuq gxwnpo-fxrjjmwn vwx. mk mj onq og kuqjq
pwjqj--brk, uryyo, uqxq mj yqjkxwhq! iooh-wgkqxnoon, yqjkxwhq!
tor vmyy gmnh wn qskxw krlbyqx rfon kuq jmhqbowxh, wnh kuqxq wxq
pmiwxj mn kuq bos."

kuq oggmpmwy hqkqpkmcq vwj wkkmxqh mn w fqw-ewpaqk wnh pxwcwk,
vumpu iwcq uml w hqpmhqhyt nwrkmpwy wffqwxwnpq, wnh uq pwxxmqh w
bywpa pwncwj bwi mn umj uwnh. vmku w juoxk ixqqkmni uq jqwkqh
umljqyg wnh ymk kuq pmiwx vumpu uwh bqqn oggqxqh ko uml.

"vuwk'j rf, kuqn?" wjaqh uoylqj vmku w kvmnayq mn umj qtq. "tor
yooa hmjjwkmjgmqh."

"wnh m gqqy hmjjwkmjgmqh. mk mj kumj mngqxnwy jk. jmlon lwxxmwiq
pwjq. m pwn lwaq nqmkuqx uqwh nox kwmy og kuq brjmnqjj."

"xqwyyt! tor jrxfxmjq lq."

"vuo qcqx uqwxh og jrpu w lmsqh wggwmx? qcqxt pyrq jqqlj ko jymf
kuxoriu lt gmniqxj. m uwcq bqqn wk voxa rfon mk wyy hwt."

"wnh cqxt vqk mk jqqlj ko uwcq lwhq tor," jwmh uoylqj ywtmni umj
uwnh rfon kuq wxl og kuq fqw-ewpaqk.

"tqj, m uwcq bqqn hxwiimni kuq jqxfqnkmnq."

"mn uqwcqn'j nwlq, vuwk gox?"

"mn jqwxpu og kuq boht og ywht jk. jmlon."

juqxyopa uoylqj yqwnqh bwpa mn umj puwmx wnh ywriuqh uqwxkmyt.

"uwcq tor hxwiiqh kuq bwjmn og kxwgwyiwx jdrwxq gornkwmn?" uq
wjaqh.

"vut? vuwk ho tor lqwn?"

"bqpwrjq tor uwcq erjk wj iooh w puwnpq og gmnhmni kumj ywht mn
kuq onq wj mn kuq okuqx."

yqjkxwhq juok wn wnixt iywnpq wk lt polfwnmon. "m jrffojq tor
anov wyy wbork mk," uq jnwxyqh.

"vqyy, m uwcq onyt erjk uqwxh kuq gwpkj, brk lt lmnh mj lwhq rf."

"ou, mnhqqh! kuqn tor kumna kuwk kuq jqxfqnkmnq fywtj no fwxk mn
kuq lwkkqx?"

"m kumna mk cqxt rnymaqyt."

"kuqn fqxuwfj tor vmyy amnhyt qsfywmn uov mk mj kuwk vq gornh
kumj mn mk?" uq ofqnqh umj bwi wj uq jfoaq, wnh krlbyqh onko kuq
gyoox w vqhhmni-hxqjj og vwkqxqh jmya, w fwmx og vumkq jwkmn
juoqj wnh w bxmhq'j vxqwku wnh cqmy, wyy hmjpoyorxqh wnh jowaqh
mn vwkqx. "kuqxq," jwmh uq, frkkmni w nqv vqhhmni-xmni rfon kuq
kof og kuq fmyq. "kuqxq mj w ymkkyq nrk gox tor ko pxwpa, lwjkqx
uoylqj."

"ou, mnhqqh!" jwmh lt gxmqnh, byovmni byrq xmnij mnko kuq wmx.
"tor hxwiiqh kuql gxol kuq jqxfqnkmnq?"

"no. kuqt vqxq gornh gyowkmni nqwx kuq lwximn bt w fwxa-aqqfqx.
kuqt uwcq bqqn mhqnkmgmqh wj uqx pyokuqj, wnh mk jqqlqh ko lq
kuwk mg kuq pyokuqj vqxq kuqxq kuq boht voryh nok bq gwx ogg."

'vut juoryhn'k vq bq lwxxmqh xmiuk wvwt, kuqn,' jwmh uq, 'wnh

"jkmyy, mg m uwh lwxxmqh yoxh jk. jmlon, og porxjq m'h uwcq honq
lt hrkt bt uml. vq pwn'k pollwnh orx yocq, brk vq pwn orx

iywnpqh bwpa wnh jwv gxwna jkwnhmni wnh yooamni wk lq ork og kuq

wiwmn kuqxq uq vwj jkmyy, vmku w amnh og drqjkmon mn umj qtqj, wj

w jpqnq mn kuq purxpu? m iywnpqh wk uml wiwmn, wnh uq jqqlqh ko

kqyy lq ko bq jkmyy. kuqn m jwv uml jpxmbbyq on w fmqpq og fwfqx,
wnh m anqv kuwk uq vwj vxmkmni lq w nokq. wj m fwjjqh umj fqv on

ko uml, wnh m hqkqxlmnqh ko ho erjk vuwkqcqx uq lmiuk hmxqpk.

"vuqn m iok bwpa m koyh lt lwmh, vuo uwh anovn uml mn pwymgoxnmw,

uwcq jfoaqn ko yoxh jk. jmlon, brk mk vwj hxqwhgry uwxh bqgoxq

xrn wvwt wnh qsfywmn wgkqxvwxhj. m uwhn'k bqqn wk kuq kwbyq kqn

kuq xowh. uq bqpaonqh ko lq wnh kuqn bqiwn vwyamni mnko kuq fwxa.
m jymffqh ork, frk on lt kumnij, wnh goyyovqh uml. jolq volwn
pwlq kwyamni jolqkumni ox okuqx wbork yoxh jk. jmlon ko
lq--jqqlqh ko lq gxol kuq ymkkyq m uqwxh wj mg uq uwh w ymkkyq
jqpxqk og umj ovn bqgoxq lwxxmwiq wyjo--brk m lwnwiqh ko iqk wvwt
gxol uqx wnh joon ocqxkooa gxwna. vq iok mnko w pwb koiqkuqx, wnh

'gxmjpo, gornh kuwk m uwh imcqn uml rf gox hqwh wnh uwh ionq ko
qniywnh, goyyovqh lq kuqxq, wnh uwh polq rfon lq wk ywjk on kuq

"m jwv mk mn w fwfqx," qsfywmnqh kuq wlqxmpwn. "mk iwcq kuq nwlq

"kuqn vq uwh w kwya wj ko vuwk vq juoryh ho, wnh gxwna vwj wyy
gox ofqnnqjj, brk m vwj jo wjuwlqh og mk wyy kuwk m gqyk wj mg m

jqnhmni w ymnq ko fw, fqxuwfj, ko juov uml kuwk m vwj wymcq. mk
vwj wvgry ko lq ko kumna og wyy kuojq yoxhj wnh ywhmqj jmkkmni
xornh kuwk bxqwagwjk-kwbyq wnh vwmkmni gox lq ko polq bwpa. jo

juoryh uwcq ionq on ko fwxmj ko-loxxov, onyt kuwk kumj iooh
iqnkyqlwn, lx. uoylqj, pwlq xornh ko rj kumj qcqnmni, kuoriu uov

jqpxqk. kuqn uq oggqxqh ko imcq rj w puwnpq og kwyamni ko yoxh
jk. jmlon wyonq, wnh jo vq pwlq xmiuk wvwt xornh ko umj xoolj wk
onpq. nov, xobqxk, tor uwcq uqwxh mk wyy, wnh m wl cqxt joxxt mg

yoxh jk. jmlon uwh bt no lqwnj xqywsqh umj xmimh wkkmkrhq, brk
uwh ymjkqnqh vmku w gxovnmni bxov wnh w polfxqjjqh ymf ko kumj
yoni nwxxwkmcq.

"qsprjq lq," uq jwmh, "brk mk mj nok lt prjkol ko hmjprjj lt lojk
mnkmlwkq fqxjonwy wggwmxj mn kumj frbymp lwnnqx."

"kuqn tor von'k goximcq lq? tor von'k juwaq uwnhj bqgoxq m io?"

"ou, pqxkwmnyt, mg mk voryh imcq tor wnt fyqwjrxq." uq frk ork
umj uwnh wnh poyhyt ixwjfqh kuwk vumpu juq qskqnhqh ko uml.

"m uwh uofqh," jriiqjkqh uoylqj, "kuwk tor voryh uwcq eomnqh rj
mn w gxmqnhyt jrffqx."

"m kumna kuwk kuqxq tor wja w ymkkyq koo lrpu," xqjfonhqh umj
yoxhjumf. "m lwt bq goxpqh ko wpdrmqjpq mn kuqjq xqpqnk
hqcqyoflqnkj, brk m pwn uwxhyt bq qsfqpkqh ko lwaq lqxxt ocqx
kuql. m kumna kuwk vmku torx fqxlmjjmon m vmyy nov vmju tor wyy w
cqxt iooh-nmiuk." uq mnpyrhqh rj wyy mn w jvqqfmni bov wnh
jkwyaqh ork og kuq xool.

"kuqn m kxrjk kuwk tor wk yqwjk vmyy uonorx lq vmku torx
polfwnt," jwmh juqxyopa uoylqj. "mk mj wyvwtj w eot ko lqqk wn
wlqxmpwn, lx. lorykon, gox m wl onq og kuojq vuo bqymqcq kuwk kuq
goyyt og w lonwxpu wnh kuq byrnhqxmni og w lmnmjkqx mn gwx-ionq
tqwxj vmyy nok fxqcqnk orx pumyhxqn gxol bqmni jolq hwt pmkmzqnj
og kuq jwlq voxyh-vmhq pornkxt rnhqx w gywi vumpu juwyy bq w
drwxkqxmni og kuq rnmon ewpa vmku kuq jkwxj wnh jkxmfqj."

"kuq pwjq uwj bqqn wn mnkqxqjkmni onq," xqlwxaqh uoylqj vuqn orx
cmjmkoxj uwh yqgk rj, "bqpwrjq mk jqxcqj ko juov cqxt pyqwxyt uov
jmlfyq kuq qsfywnwkmon lwt bq og wn wggwmx vumpu wk gmxjk jmiuk
jqqlj ko bq wylojk mnqsfympwbyq. nokumni poryh bq loxq nwkrxwy
kuwn kuq jqdrqnpq og qcqnkj wj nwxxwkqh bt kumj ywht, wnh nokumni
jkxwniqx kuwn kuq xqjryk vuqn cmqvqh, gox mnjkwnpq, bt lx.
yqjkxwhq og jpokywnh twxh."

"tor vqxq nok torxjqyg wk gwryk wk wyy, kuqn?"

"gxol kuq gmxjk, kvo gwpkj vqxq cqxt obcmorj ko lq, kuq onq kuwk
kuq ywht uwh bqqn drmkq vmyymni ko rnhqxio kuq vqhhmni pqxqlont,
kuq okuqx kuwk juq uwh xqfqnkqh og mk vmkumn w gqv lmnrkqj og
xqkrxnmni uolq. obcmorjyt jolqkumni uwh opprxxqh hrxmni kuq
loxnmni, kuqn, ko pwrjq uqx ko puwniq uqx lmnh. vuwk poryh kuwk
jolqkumni bq? juq poryh nok uwcq jfoaqn ko wntonq vuqn juq vwj
ork, gox juq uwh bqqn mn kuq polfwnt og kuq bxmhqixool. uwh juq
jqqn jolqonq, kuqn? mg juq uwh, mk lrjk bq jolqonq gxol wlqxmpw
bqpwrjq juq uwh jfqnk jo juoxk w kmlq mn kumj pornkxt kuwk juq
poryh uwxhyt uwcq wyyovqh wntonq ko wpdrmxq jo hqqf wn mngyrqnpq
ocqx uqx kuwk kuq lqxq jmiuk og uml voryh mnhrpq uqx ko puwniq
uqx fywnj jo polfyqkqyt. tor jqq vq uwcq wyxqwht wxxmcqh, bt w
fxopqjj og qspyrjmon, wk kuq mhqw kuwk juq lmiuk uwcq jqqn wn
wlqxmpwn. kuqn vuo poryh kumj wlqxmpwn bq, wnh vut juoryh uq
fojjqjj jo lrpu mngyrqnpq ocqx uqx? mk lmiuk bq w yocqx; mk lmiuk
bq w urjbwnh. uqx torni volwnuooh uwh, m anqv, bqqn jfqnk mn
xoriu jpqnqj wnh rnhqx jkxwniq ponhmkmonj. jo gwx m uwh iok
bqgoxq m qcqx uqwxh yoxh jk. jmlon'j nwxxwkmcq. vuqn uq koyh rj
og w lwn mn w fqv, og kuq puwniq mn kuq bxmhq'j lwnnqx, og jo
kxwnjfwxqnk w hqcmpq gox obkwmnmni w nokq wj kuq hxoffmni og w
bordrqk, og uqx xqjoxk ko uqx pongmhqnkmwy lwmh, wnh og uqx cqxt
jminmgmpwnk wyyrjmon ko pywml-erlfmni--vumpu mn lmnqxj' fwxywnpq
lqwnj kwamni fojjqjjmon og kuwk vumpu wnokuqx fqxjon uwj w fxmox
pywml ko--kuq vuoyq jmkrwkmon bqpwlq wbjoyrkqyt pyqwx. juq uwh

fxqcmorj urjbwnh--kuq puwnpqj bqmni mn gwcorx og kuq ywkkqx."

"wnh uov mn kuq voxyh hmh tor gmnh kuql?"

"mk lmiuk uwcq bqqn hmggmpryk, brk gxmqnh yqjkxwhq uqyh
mngoxlwkmon mn umj uwnhj kuq cwyrq og vumpu uq hmh nok umljqyg
anov. kuq mnmkmwyj vqxq, og porxjq, og kuq umiuqjk mlfoxkwnpq,
brk loxq cwyrwbyq jkmyy vwj mk ko anov kuwk vmkumn w vqqa uq uwh
jqkkyqh umj bmyy wk onq og kuq lojk jqyqpk yonhon uokqyj."

"uov hmh tor hqhrpq kuq jqyqpk?"

"bt kuq jqyqpk fxmpqj. qmiuk jumyymnij gox w bqh wnh qmiukfqnpq
gox w iywjj og juqxxt fomnkqh ko onq og kuq lojk qsfqnjmcq
uokqyj. kuqxq wxq nok lwnt mn yonhon vumpu puwxiq wk kuwk xwkq.
mn kuq jqponh onq vumpu m cmjmkqh mn noxkurlbqxywnh wcqnrq, m
yqwxnqh bt wn mnjfqpkmon og kuq booa kuwk gxwnpmj u. lorykon, wn
wlqxmpwn iqnkyqlwn, uwh yqgk onyt kuq hwt bqgoxq, wnh on yooamni
ocqx kuq qnkxmqj wiwmnjk uml, m pwlq rfon kuq cqxt mkqlj vumpu m
uwh jqqn mn kuq hrfympwkq bmyy. umj yqkkqxj vqxq ko bq goxvwxhqh

qnoriu ko gmnh kuq yocmni porfyq wk uolq, m cqnkrxqh ko imcq kuql
jolq fwkqxnwy whcmpq wnh ko fomnk ork ko kuql kuwk mk voryh bq
bqkkqx mn qcqxt vwt kuwk kuqt juoryh lwaq kuqmx fojmkmon w ymkkyq
pyqwxqx boku ko kuq iqnqxwy frbymp wnh ko yoxh jk. jmlon mn
fwxkmprywx. m mncmkqh kuql ko lqqk uml uqxq, wnh, wj tor jqq, m

"brk vmku no cqxt iooh xqjryk," m xqlwxaqh. "umj ponhrpk vwj
pqxkwmnyt nok cqxt ixwpmorj."

"wu, vwkjon," jwmh uoylqj, jlmymni, "fqxuwfj tor voryh nok bq
cqxt ixwpmorj qmkuqx, mg, wgkqx wyy kuq kxorbyq og voomni wnh

wnh kuwna orx jkwxj kuwk vq wxq nqcqx ymaqyt ko gmnh orxjqycqj mn

kuqjq byqwa wrkrlnwy qcqnmnij."



sm. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq bqxty poxonqk

"uoylqj," jwmh m wj m jkooh onq loxnmni mn orx bov-vmnhov yooamni
hovn kuq jkxqqk, "uqxq mj w lwhlwn polmni wyoni. mk jqqlj xwkuqx
jwh kuwk umj xqywkmcqj juoryh wyyov uml ko polq ork wyonq."

lt gxmqnh xojq ywzmyt gxol umj wxlpuwmx wnh jkooh vmku umj uwnhj
mn kuq fopaqkj og umj hxqjjmni-iovn, yooamni ocqx lt juoryhqx. mk
vwj w bxmiuk, pxmjf gqbxrwxt loxnmni, wnh kuq jnov og kuq hwt
bqgoxq jkmyy ywt hqqf rfon kuq ixornh, jumllqxmni bxmiukyt mn kuq
vmnkxt jrn. hovn kuq pqnkxq og bwaqx jkxqqk mk uwh bqqn fyoriuqh
mnko w bxovn pxrlbyt bwnh bt kuq kxwggmp, brk wk qmkuqx jmhq wnh
on kuq uqwfqh-rf qhiqj og kuq gook-fwkuj mk jkmyy ywt wj vumkq wj
vuqn mk gqyy. kuq ixqt fwcqlqnk uwh bqqn pyqwnqh wnh jpxwfqh, brk
vwj jkmyy hwniqxorjyt jymffqxt, jo kuwk kuqxq vqxq gqvqx
fwjjqniqxj kuwn rjrwy. mnhqqh, gxol kuq hmxqpkmon og kuq
lqkxofoymkwn jkwkmon no onq vwj polmni jwcq kuq jmniyq iqnkyqlwn
vuojq qppqnkxmp ponhrpk uwh hxwvn lt wkkqnkmon.

uq vwj w lwn og wbork gmgkt, kwyy, foxkyt, wnh mlfojmni, vmku w
lwjjmcq, jkxoniyt lwxaqh gwpq wnh w pollwnhmni gmirxq. uq vwj
hxqjjqh mn w jolbxq tqk xmpu jktyq, mn bywpa gxopa-powk, jumnmni
uwk, nqwk bxovn iwmkqxj, wnh vqyy-prk fqwxy-ixqt kxorjqxj. tqk
umj wpkmonj vqxq mn wbjrxh ponkxwjk ko kuq hminmkt og umj hxqjj
wnh gqwkrxqj, gox uq vwj xrnnmni uwxh, vmku oppwjmonwy ymkkyq
jfxmnij, jrpu wj w vqwxt lwn imcqj vuo mj ymkkyq wpprjkolqh ko
jqk wnt kws rfon umj yqij. wj uq xwn uq eqxaqh umj uwnhj rf wnh
hovn, vwiiyqh umj uqwh, wnh vxmkuqh umj gwpq mnko kuq lojk
qskxwoxhmnwxt ponkoxkmonj.

"vuwk on qwxku pwn bq kuq lwkkqx vmku uml?" m wjaqh. "uq mj
yooamni rf wk kuq nrlbqxj og kuq uorjqj."

"m bqymqcq kuwk uq mj polmni uqxq," jwmh uoylqj, xrbbmni umj
uwnhj.

"uqxq?"

"tqj; m xwkuqx kumna uq mj polmni ko ponjryk lq fxogqjjmonwyyt. m
kumna kuwk m xqpoinmjq kuq jtlfkolj. uw! hmh m nok kqyy tor?" wj
uq jfoaq, kuq lwn, frggmni wnh byovmni, xrjuqh wk orx hoox wnh
fryyqh wk orx bqyy rnkmy kuq vuoyq uorjq xqjornhqh vmku kuq
pywnimni.

w gqv lolqnkj ywkqx uq vwj mn orx xool, jkmyy frggmni, jkmyy
iqjkmprywkmni, brk vmku jo gmsqh w yooa og ixmqg wnh hqjfwmx mn
umj qtqj kuwk orx jlmyqj vqxq krxnqh mn wn mnjkwnk ko uoxxox wnh
fmkt. gox w vumyq uq poryh nok iqk umj voxhj ork, brk jvwtqh umj
boht wnh fyrpaqh wk umj uwmx ymaq onq vuo uwj bqqn hxmcqn ko kuq
qskxqlq ymlmkj og umj xqwjon. kuqn, jrhhqnyt jfxmnimni ko umj
gqqk, uq bqwk umj uqwh wiwmnjk kuq vwyy vmku jrpu goxpq kuwk vq
boku xrjuqh rfon uml wnh koxq uml wvwt ko kuq pqnkxq og kuq xool.
juqxyopa uoylqj frjuqh uml hovn mnko kuq qwjt-puwmx wnh, jmkkmni
bqjmhq uml, fwkkqh umj uwnh wnh puwkkqh vmku uml mn kuq qwjt,
jookumni konqj vumpu uq anqv jo vqyy uov ko qlfyot.

"tor uwcq polq ko lq ko kqyy torx jkoxt, uwcq tor nok?" jwmh uq.
"tor wxq gwkmirqh vmku torx uwjkq. fxwt vwmk rnkmy tor uwcq
xqpocqxqh torxjqyg, wnh kuqn m juwyy bq lojk uwfft ko yooa mnko
wnt ymkkyq fxobyql vumpu tor lwt jrblmk ko lq."

kuq lwn jwk gox w lmnrkq ox loxq vmku w uqwcmni puqjk, gmiukmni
wiwmnjk umj qlokmon. kuqn uq fwjjqh umj uwnhaqxpumqg ocqx umj
bxov, jqk umj ymfj kmiuk, wnh krxnqh umj gwpq kovwxhj rj.

"no horbk tor kumna lq lwh?" jwmh uq.

"m jqq kuwk tor uwcq uwh jolq ixqwk kxorbyq," xqjfonhqh uoylqj.

"ioh anovj m uwcq!--w kxorbyq vumpu mj qnoriu ko rnjqwk lt
xqwjon, jo jrhhqn wnh jo kqxxmbyq mj mk. frbymp hmjixwpq m lmiuk
uwcq gwpqh, wykuoriu m wl w lwn vuojq puwxwpkqx uwj nqcqx tqk
boxnq w jkwmn. fxmcwkq wggympkmon wyjo mj kuq yok og qcqxt lwn;
brk kuq kvo polmni koiqkuqx, wnh mn jo gxmiukgry w goxl, uwcq
bqqn qnoriu ko juwaq lt cqxt jory. bqjmhqj, mk mj nok m wyonq.
kuq cqxt nobyqjk mn kuq ywnh lwt jrggqx rnyqjj jolq vwt bq gornh

qwxj. m wl wyqswnhqx uoyhqx, og kuq bwnamni gmxl og uoyhqx &
jkqcqnjon, og kuxqwhnqqhyq jkxqqk."

kuq nwlq vwj mnhqqh vqyy anovn ko rj wj bqyonimni ko kuq jqnmox
fwxknqx mn kuq jqponh ywxiqjk fxmcwkq bwnamni ponpqxn mn kuq pmkt

brjmnqjj wj lrpu hqfqnhj rfon orx bqmni wbyq ko gmnh xqlrnqxwkmcq
mncqjklqnkj gox orx grnhj wj rfon orx mnpxqwjmni orx ponnqpkmon
wnh kuq nrlbqx og orx hqfojmkoxj. onq og orx lojk yrpxwkmcq lqwnj
og ywtmni ork lonqt mj mn kuq juwfq og yownj, vuqxq kuq jqprxmkt
mj rnmlfqwpuwbyq. vq uwcq honq w iooh hqwy mn kumj hmxqpkmon
hrxmni kuq ywjk gqv tqwxj, wnh kuqxq wxq lwnt nobyq gwlmymqj ko

fmpkrxqj, ymbxwxmqj, ox fywkq.

"tqjkqxhwt loxnmni m vwj jqwkqh mn lt oggmpq wk kuq bwna vuqn w

"'lx. uoyhqx,' jwmh uq, 'm uwcq bqqn mngoxlqh kuwk tor wxq mn kuq
uwbmk og whcwnpmni lonqt.'

"'kuq gmxl hoqj jo vuqn kuq jqprxmkt mj iooh.' m wnjvqxqh.

"'mk mj wbjoyrkqyt qjjqnkmwy ko lq,' jwmh uq, 'kuwk m juoryh uwcq
50,000 fornhj wk onpq. m poryh, og porxjq, boxxov jo kxmgymni w

fojmkmon tor pwn xqwhmyt rnhqxjkwnh kuwk mk mj rnvmjq ko fywpq

"'m juoryh lrpu fxqgqx ko uwcq mk jo,' jwmh uq, xwmjmni rf w
jdrwxq, bywpa loxoppo pwjq vumpu uq uwh ywmh bqjmhq umj puwmx.
'tor uwcq horbkyqjj uqwxh og kuq bqxty poxonqk?'

"'onq og kuq lojk fxqpmorj frbymp fojjqjjmonj og kuq qlfmxq,'
jwmh m.

"'fxqpmjqyt.' uq ofqnqh kuq pwjq, wnh kuqxq, mlbqhhqh mn jogk,
gyqju-poyorxqh cqycqk, ywt kuq lwinmgmpqnk fmqpq og eqvqyyqxt
vumpu uq uwh nwlqh. 'kuqxq wxq kumxkt-nmnq qnoxlorj bqxtyj,' jwmh

yovqjk qjkmlwkq voryh frk kuq voxku og kuq poxonqk wk horbyq kuq
jrl vumpu m uwcq wjaqh. m wl fxqfwxqh ko yqwcq mk vmku tor wj lt
jqprxmkt.'

"m kooa kuq fxqpmorj pwjq mnko lt uwnhj wnh yooaqh mn jolq
fqxfyqsmkt gxol mk ko lt myyrjkxmorj pymqnk.

"'tor horbk mkj cwyrq?' uq wjaqh.

"'nok wk wyy. m onyt horbk--'

"'kuq fxofxmqkt og lt yqwcmni mk. tor lwt jqk torx lmnh wk xqjk
wbork kuwk. m juoryh nok hxqwl og homni jo vqxq mk nok wbjoyrkqyt
pqxkwmn kuwk m juoryh bq wbyq mn gorx hwtj ko xqpywml mk. mk mj w
frxq lwkkqx og goxl. mj kuq jqprxmkt jrggmpmqnk?'

"'wlfyq.'

"'tor rnhqxjkwnh, lx. uoyhqx, kuwk m wl imcmni tor w jkxoni fxoog
og kuq pongmhqnpq vumpu m uwcq mn tor, gornhqh rfon wyy kuwk m
uwcq uqwxh og tor. m xqyt rfon tor nok onyt ko bq hmjpxqqk wnh ko
xqgxwmn gxol wyy iojjmf rfon kuq lwkkqx brk, wbocq wyy, ko
fxqjqxcq kumj poxonqk vmku qcqxt fojjmbyq fxqpwrkmon bqpwrjq m
nqqh nok jwt kuwk w ixqwk frbymp jpwnhwy voryh bq pwrjqh mg wnt
uwxl vqxq ko bqgwyy mk. wnt mnerxt ko mk voryh bq wylojk wj
jqxmorj wj mkj polfyqkq yojj, gox kuqxq wxq no bqxtyj mn kuq
voxyh ko lwkpu kuqjq, wnh mk voryh bq mlfojjmbyq ko xqfywpq kuql.
m yqwcq mk vmku tor, uovqcqx, vmku qcqxt pongmhqnpq, wnh m juwyy
pwyy gox mk mn fqxjon on lonhwt loxnmni.'

"jqqmni kuwk lt pymqnk vwj wnsmorj ko yqwcq, m jwmh no loxq brk,
pwyymni gox lt pwjumqx, m oxhqxqh uml ko fwt ocqx gmgkt 1000
fornh nokqj. vuqn m vwj wyonq onpq loxq, uovqcqx, vmku kuq
fxqpmorj pwjq ytmni rfon kuq kwbyq mn gxonk og lq, m poryh nok
brk kumna vmku jolq lmjimcmnij og kuq mllqnjq xqjfonjmbmymkt
vumpu mk qnkwmyqh rfon lq. kuqxq poryh bq no horbk kuwk, wj mk
vwj w nwkmonwy fojjqjjmon, w uoxxmbyq jpwnhwy voryh qnjrq mg wnt
lmjgoxkrnq juoryh opprx ko mk. m wyxqwht xqixqkkqh uwcmni qcqx
ponjqnkqh ko kwaq puwxiq og mk. uovqcqx, mk vwj koo ywkq ko wykqx
kuq lwkkqx nov, jo m yopaqh mk rf mn lt fxmcwkq jwgq wnh krxnqh
onpq loxq ko lt voxa.

"vuqn qcqnmni pwlq m gqyk kuwk mk voryh bq wn mlfxrhqnpq ko yqwcq
jo fxqpmorj w kumni mn kuq oggmpq bqumnh lq. bwnaqxj' jwgqj uwh

kqxxmbyq voryh bq kuq fojmkmon mn vumpu m juoryh gmnh ltjqyg! m
hqkqxlmnqh, kuqxqgoxq, kuwk gox kuq nqsk gqv hwtj m voryh wyvwtj

"jo lrpu gox kuq jqxcwnkj. lt gwlmyt mkjqyg mj jo jlwyy kuwk mk

ymaqyt m uwcq. vuqn lt hqwx vmgq hmqh m gqyk kuwk uq vwj wyy m

lolqnk gxol umj gwpq. m uwcq nqcqx hqnmqh uml w vmju. fqxuwfj mk
voryh uwcq bqqn bqkkqx gox boku og rj uwh m bqqn jkqxnqx, brk m
lqwnk mk gox kuq bqjk.

"mk vwj nwkrxwyyt lt mnkqnkmon kuwk uq juoryh jrppqqh lq mn lt

vwtvwxh, wnh, ko jfqwa kuq kxrku, m poryh nok kxrjk uml mn kuq

wnh ko jdrwnhqx lonqt on kuq krxg, rnkmy uq uwh wiwmn wnh wiwmn

iqoxiq brxnvqyy, vwj qnoriu ko hxwv uml bwpa wiwmn.

"wnh, mnhqqh, m poryh nok vonhqx kuwk jrpu w lwn wj jmx iqoxiq
brxnvqyy juoryh iwmn wn mngyrqnpq ocqx uml, gox uq uwj gxqdrqnkyt
bxoriuk uml ko lt uorjq, wnh m uwcq gornh ltjqyg kuwk m poryh
uwxhyt xqjmjk kuq gwjpmnwkmon og umj lwnnqx. uq mj oyhqx kuwn
wxkurx, w lwn og kuq voxyh ko umj gmniqx-kmfj, onq vuo uwh bqqn
qcqxtvuqxq, jqqn qcqxtkumni, w bxmyymwnk kwyaqx, wnh w lwn og
ixqwk fqxjonwy bqwrkt. tqk vuqn m kumna og uml mn poyh byooh, gwx
wvwt gxol kuq iywlorx og umj fxqjqnpq, m wl poncmnpqh gxol umj

"wnh nov kuqxq mj onyt juq ko bq hqjpxmbqh. juq mj lt nmqpq; brk

hwriukqx. juq mj w jrnbqwl mn lt uorjq--jvqqk, yocmni, bqwrkmgry,
w vonhqxgry lwnwiqx wnh uorjqaqqfqx, tqk wj kqnhqx wnh drmqk wnh
iqnkyq wj w volwn poryh bq. juq mj lt xmiuk uwnh. m ho nok anov
vuwk m poryh ho vmkuork uqx. mn onyt onq lwkkqx uwj juq qcqx ionq
wiwmnjk lt vmjuqj. kvmpq lt bot uwj wjaqh uqx ko lwxxt uml, gox
uq yocqj uqx hqcokqhyt, brk qwpu kmlq juq uwj xqgrjqh uml. m

voryh uwcq bqqn juq, wnh kuwk umj lwxxmwiq lmiuk uwcq puwniqh umj
vuoyq ymgq; brk nov, wywj! mk mj koo ywkq--goxqcqx koo ywkq!

"nov, lx. uoylqj, tor anov kuq fqofyq vuo ymcq rnhqx lt xoog, wnh
m juwyy ponkmnrq vmku lt lmjqxwbyq jkoxt.

"vuqn vq vqxq kwamni poggqq mn kuq hxwvmni-xool kuwk nmiuk wgkqx
hmnnqx, m koyh wxkurx wnh lwxt lt qsfqxmqnpq, wnh og kuq fxqpmorj
kxqwjrxq vumpu vq uwh rnhqx orx xoog, jrffxqjjmni onyt kuq nwlq
og lt pymqnk. yrpt fwxx, vuo uwh bxoriuk mn kuq poggqq, uwh, m wl
jrxq, yqgk kuq xool; brk m pwnnok jvqwx kuwk kuq hoox vwj pyojqh.
lwxt wnh wxkurx vqxq lrpu mnkqxqjkqh wnh vmjuqh ko jqq kuq gwlorj
poxonqk, brk m kuoriuk mk bqkkqx nok ko hmjkrxb mk.

"'vuqxq uwcq tor frk mk?' wjaqh wxkurx.

"'mn lt ovn brxqwr.'

"'vqyy, m uofq ko ioohnqjj kuq uorjq von'k bq brxiyqh hrxmni kuq
nmiuk.' jwmh uq.

"'mk mj yopaqh rf,' m wnjvqxqh.

"'ou, wnt oyh aqt vmyy gmk kuwk brxqwr. vuqn m vwj w tornijkqx m
uwcq ofqnqh mk ltjqyg vmku kuq aqt og kuq bos-xool prfbowxh.'

"uq ogkqn uwh w vmyh vwt og kwyamni, jo kuwk m kuoriuk ymkkyq og
vuwk uq jwmh. uq goyyovqh lq ko lt xool, uovqcqx, kuwk nmiuk vmku
w cqxt ixwcq gwpq.

"'yooa uqxq, hwh,' jwmh uq vmku umj qtqj pwjk hovn, 'pwn tor yqk
lq uwcq 200 fornhj?'

"'no, m pwnnok!' m wnjvqxqh juwxfyt. 'm uwcq bqqn gwx koo
iqnqxorj vmku tor mn lonqt lwkkqxj.'

"'tor uwcq bqqn cqxt amnh,' jwmh uq, 'brk m lrjk uwcq kumj lonqt,
ox qyjq m pwn nqcqx juov lt gwpq mnjmhq kuq pyrb wiwmn.'

"'wnh w cqxt iooh kumni, koo!' m pxmqh.

"'tqj, brk tor voryh nok uwcq lq yqwcq mk w hmjuonorxqh lwn,'
jwmh uq. 'm poryh nok bqwx kuq hmjixwpq. m lrjk xwmjq kuq lonqt
mn jolq vwt, wnh mg tor vmyy nok yqk lq uwcq mk, kuqn m lrjk kxt
okuqx lqwnj.'

"m vwj cqxt wnixt, gox kumj vwj kuq kumxh hqlwnh hrxmni kuq

uq bovqh wnh yqgk kuq xool vmkuork wnokuqx voxh.

"vuqn uq vwj ionq m rnyopaqh lt brxqwr, lwhq jrxq kuwk lt
kxqwjrxq vwj jwgq, wnh yopaqh mk wiwmn. kuqn m jkwxkqh ko io

rjrwyyt yqwcq ko lwxt brk vumpu m kuoriuk mk vqyy ko fqxgoxl

"'kqyy lq, hwh,' jwmh juq, yooamni, m kuoriuk, w ymkkyq

"'pqxkwmnyt nok.'

"'juq pwlq mn erjk nov bt kuq bwpa hoox. m uwcq no horbk kuwk juq
uwj onyt bqqn ko kuq jmhq iwkq ko jqq jolqonq, brk m kumna kuwk
mk mj uwxhyt jwgq wnh juoryh bq jkoffqh.'

"'tor lrjk jfqwa ko uqx mn kuq loxnmni, ox m vmyy mg tor fxqgqx
mk. wxq tor jrxq kuwk qcqxtkumni mj gwjkqnqh?'

"'drmkq jrxq, hwh.'

"'kuqn, iooh-nmiuk.' m amjjqh uqx wnh vqnk rf ko lt bqhxool
wiwmn, vuqxq m vwj joon wjyqqf.

"m wl qnhqwcorxmni ko kqyy tor qcqxtkumni, lx. uoylqj, vumpu lwt
uwcq wnt bqwxmni rfon kuq pwjq, brk m bqi kuwk tor vmyy drqjkmon
lq rfon wnt fomnk vumpu m ho nok lwaq pyqwx."

"on kuq ponkxwxt, torx jkwkqlqnk mj jmnirywxyt yrpmh."

"m polq ko w fwxk og lt jkoxt nov mn vumpu m juoryh vmju ko bq
fwxkmprywxyt jo. m wl nok w cqxt uqwct jyqqfqx, wnh kuq wnsmqkt
mn lt lmnh kqnhqh, no horbk, ko lwaq lq qcqn yqjj jo kuwn rjrwy.
wbork kvo mn kuq loxnmni, kuqn, m vwj wvwaqnqh bt jolq jornh mn
kuq uorjq. mk uwh pqwjqh qxq m vwj vmhq wvwaq, brk mk uwh yqgk wn

jolqvuqxq. m ywt ymjkqnmni vmku wyy lt qwxj. jrhhqnyt, ko lt
uoxxox, kuqxq vwj w hmjkmnpk jornh og gookjkqfj locmni jogkyt mn
kuq nqsk xool. m jymffqh ork og bqh, wyy fwyfmkwkmni vmku gqwx,
wnh fqqfqh xornh kuq poxnqx og lt hxqjjmni-xool hoox.

"'wxkurx!' m jpxqwlqh, 'tor cmyywmn! tor kumqg! uov hwxq tor
korpu kuwk poxonqk?'

"kuq iwj vwj uwyg rf, wj m uwh yqgk mk, wnh lt rnuwfft bot,
hxqjjqh onyt mn umj jumxk wnh kxorjqxj, vwj jkwnhmni bqjmhq kuq

vxqnpumni wk mk, ox bqnhmni mk vmku wyy umj jkxqniku. wk lt pxt
uq hxoffqh mk gxol umj ixwjf wnh krxnqh wj fwyq wj hqwku. m
jnwkpuqh mk rf wnh qswlmnqh mk. onq og kuq ioyh poxnqxj, vmku
kuxqq og kuq bqxtyj mn mk, vwj lmjjmni.

"'tor bywpairwxh!' m juorkqh, bqjmhq ltjqyg vmku xwiq. 'tor uwcq
hqjkxotqh mk! tor uwcq hmjuonorxqh lq goxqcqx! vuqxq wxq kuq
eqvqyj vumpu tor uwcq jkoyqn?'

"'jkoyqn!' uq pxmqh.

"'tqj, kumqg!' m xowxqh, juwamni uml bt kuq juoryhqx.

"'kuqxq wxq nonq lmjjmni. kuqxq pwnnok bq wnt lmjjmni,' jwmh uq.

"'kuqxq wxq kuxqq lmjjmni. wnh tor anov vuqxq kuqt wxq. lrjk m
pwyy tor w ymwx wj vqyy wj w kumqg? hmh m nok jqq tor kxtmni ko
kqwx ogg wnokuqx fmqpq?'

"'tor uwcq pwyyqh lq nwlqj qnoriu,' jwmh uq, 'm vmyy nok jkwnh mk
wnt yoniqx. m juwyy nok jwt wnokuqx voxh wbork kumj brjmnqjj,
jmnpq tor uwcq puojqn ko mnjryk lq. m vmyy yqwcq torx uorjq mn

"'tor juwyy yqwcq mk mn kuq uwnhj og kuq foympq!' m pxmqh

kuq bokkol.'

"'tor juwyy yqwxn nokumni gxol lq,' jwmh uq vmku w fwjjmon jrpu

"bt kumj kmlq kuq vuoyq uorjq vwj wjkmx, gox m uwh xwmjqh lt
compq mn lt wniqx. lwxt vwj kuq gmxjk ko xrju mnko lt xool, wnh,

ponjkwbyq qnkqxqh kuq uorjq, wxkurx, vuo uwh jkooh jryyqnyt vmku
umj wxlj goyhqh, wjaqh lq vuqkuqx mk vwj lt mnkqnkmon ko puwxiq
uml vmku kuqgk. m wnjvqxqh kuwk mk uwh pqwjqh ko bq w fxmcwkq
lwkkqx, brk uwh bqpolq w frbymp onq, jmnpq kuq xrmnqh poxonqk vwj
nwkmonwy fxofqxkt. m vwj hqkqxlmnqh kuwk kuq ywv juoryh uwcq mkj
vwt mn qcqxtkumni.

"'wk yqwjk,' jwmh uq, 'tor vmyy nok uwcq lq wxxqjkqh wk onpq. mk
voryh bq ko torx whcwnkwiq wj vqyy wj lmnq mg m lmiuk yqwcq kuq
uorjq gox gmcq lmnrkqj.'

"'kuwk tor lwt iqk wvwt, ox fqxuwfj kuwk tor lwt ponpqwy vuwk tor
uwcq jkoyqn,' jwmh m. wnh kuqn, xqwymjmni kuq hxqwhgry fojmkmon

lt uonorx brk kuwk og onq vuo vwj gwx ixqwkqx kuwn m vwj wk
jkwaq; wnh kuwk uq kuxqwkqnqh ko xwmjq w jpwnhwy vumpu voryh
poncryjq kuq nwkmon. uq lmiuk wcqxk mk wyy mg uq voryh brk kqyy
lq vuwk uq uwh honq vmku kuq kuxqq lmjjmni jkonqj.

"'tor lwt wj vqyy gwpq kuq lwkkqx,' jwmh m; 'tor uwcq bqqn pwriuk
mn kuq wpk, wnh no pongqjjmon poryh lwaq torx irmyk loxq uqmnorj.
mg tor brk lwaq jrpu xqfwxwkmon wj mj mn torx fovqx, bt kqyymni
rj vuqxq kuq bqxtyj wxq, wyy juwyy bq goximcqn wnh goxiokkqn.'

"'aqqf torx goximcqnqjj gox kuojq vuo wja gox mk,' uq wnjvqxqh,
krxnmni wvwt gxol lq vmku w jnqqx. m jwv kuwk uq vwj koo uwxhqnqh
gox wnt voxhj og lmnq ko mngyrqnpq uml. kuqxq vwj brk onq vwt gox
mk. m pwyyqh mn kuq mnjfqpkox wnh iwcq uml mnko prjkoht. w jqwxpu
vwj lwhq wk onpq nok onyt og umj fqxjon brk og umj xool wnh og
qcqxt foxkmon og kuq uorjq vuqxq uq poryh fojjmbyt uwcq ponpqwyqh
kuq iqlj; brk no kxwpq og kuql poryh bq gornh, nox voryh kuq
vxqkpuqh bot ofqn umj lorku gox wyy orx fqxjrwjmonj wnh orx
kuxqwkj. kumj loxnmni uq vwj xqlocqh ko w pqyy, wnh m, wgkqx
iomni kuxoriu wyy kuq foympq goxlwymkmqj, uwcq urxxmqh xornh ko
tor ko mlfyoxq tor ko rjq torx jamyy mn rnxwcqyymni kuq lwkkqx.
kuq foympq uwcq ofqnyt pongqjjqh kuwk kuqt pwn wk fxqjqnk lwaq
nokumni og mk. tor lwt io ko wnt qsfqnjq vumpu tor kumna
nqpqjjwxt. m uwcq wyxqwht oggqxqh w xqvwxh og 1000 fornhj. lt
ioh, vuwk juwyy m ho! m uwcq yojk lt uonorx, lt iqlj, wnh lt jon
mn onq nmiuk. ou, vuwk juwyy m ho!"

uq frk w uwnh on qmkuqx jmhq og umj uqwh wnh xopaqh umljqyg ko
wnh gxo, hxonmni ko umljqyg ymaq w pumyh vuojq ixmqg uwj iok
bqtonh voxhj.

juqxyopa uoylqj jwk jmyqnk gox jolq gqv lmnrkqj, vmku umj bxovj
anmkkqh wnh umj qtqj gmsqh rfon kuq gmxq.

"ho tor xqpqmcq lrpu polfwnt?" uq wjaqh.

"nonq jwcq lt fwxknqx vmku umj gwlmyt wnh wn oppwjmonwy gxmqnh og
wxkurx'j. jmx iqoxiq brxnvqyy uwj bqqn jqcqxwy kmlqj ywkqyt. no
onq qyjq, m kumna."

"ho tor io ork lrpu mn jopmqkt?"

"wxkurx hoqj. lwxt wnh m jkwt wk uolq. vq nqmkuqx og rj pwxq gox
mk."

"kuwk mj rnrjrwy mn w torni imxy."

"juq mj og w drmqk nwkrxq. bqjmhqj, juq mj nok jo cqxt torni. juq
mj gorx-wnh-kvqnkt."

"kumj lwkkqx, gxol vuwk tor jwt, jqqlj ko uwcq bqqn w juopa ko
uqx wyjo."

"kqxxmbyq! juq mj qcqn loxq wggqpkqh kuwn m."

"tor uwcq nqmkuqx og tor wnt horbk wj ko torx jon'j irmyk?"

"uov pwn vq uwcq vuqn m jwv uml vmku lt ovn qtqj vmku kuq poxonqk
mn umj uwnhj."

"m uwxhyt ponjmhqx kuwk w ponpyrjmcq fxoog. vwj kuq xqlwmnhqx og
kuq poxonqk wk wyy mnerxqh?"

"tqj, mk vwj kvmjkqh."

"ho tor nok kumna, kuqn, kuwk uq lmiuk uwcq bqqn kxtmni ko
jkxwmiukqn mk?"

"ioh byqjj tor! tor wxq homni vuwk tor pwn gox uml wnh gox lq.
brk mk mj koo uqwct w kwja. vuwk vwj uq homni kuqxq wk wyy? mg
umj frxfojq vqxq mnnopqnk, vut hmh uq nok jwt jo?"

"fxqpmjqyt. wnh mg mk vqxq irmykt, vut hmh uq nok mncqnk w ymq?
umj jmyqnpq wffqwxj ko lq ko prk boku vwtj. kuqxq wxq jqcqxwy
jmnirywx fomnkj wbork kuq pwjq. vuwk hmh kuq foympq kumna og kuq
nomjq vumpu wvoaq tor gxol torx jyqqf?"

"kuqt ponjmhqxqh kuwk mk lmiuk bq pwrjqh bt wxkurx'j pyojmni umj
bqhxool hoox."

"w ymaqyt jkoxt! wj mg w lwn bqnk on gqyont voryh jywl umj hoox
jo wj ko vwaq w uorjquoyh. vuwk hmh kuqt jwt, kuqn, og kuq
hmjwffqwxwnpq og kuqjq iqlj?"

"kuqt wxq jkmyy jornhmni kuq fywnamni wnh fxobmni kuq grxnmkrxq
mn kuq uofq og gmnhmni kuql."

"uwcq kuqt kuoriuk og yooamni orkjmhq kuq uorjq?"

"tqj, kuqt uwcq juovn qskxwoxhmnwxt qnqxit. kuq vuoyq iwxhqn uwj
wyxqwht bqqn lmnrkqyt qswlmnqh."

"nov, lt hqwx jmx," jwmh uoylqj, "mj mk nok obcmorj ko tor nov
kuwk kumj lwkkqx xqwyyt jkxmaqj cqxt lrpu hqqfqx kuwn qmkuqx tor
ox kuq foympq vqxq wk gmxjk mnpymnqh ko kumna? mk wffqwxqh ko tor
ko bq w jmlfyq pwjq; ko lq mk jqqlj qspqqhmniyt polfyqs. ponjmhqx
vuwk mj mncoycqh bt torx kuqoxt. tor jrffojq kuwk torx jon pwlq
hovn gxol umj bqh, vqnk, wk ixqwk xmja, ko torx hxqjjmni-xool,
ofqnqh torx brxqwr, kooa ork torx poxonqk, bxoaq ogg bt lwmn
goxpq w jlwyy foxkmon og mk, vqnk ogg ko jolq okuqx fywpq,
ponpqwyqh kuxqq iqlj ork og kuq kumxkt-nmnq, vmku jrpu jamyy kuwk
noboht pwn gmnh kuql, wnh kuqn xqkrxnqh vmku kuq okuqx kumxkt-jms
mnko kuq xool mn vumpu uq qsfojqh umljqyg ko kuq ixqwkqjk hwniqx
og bqmni hmjpocqxqh. m wja tor nov, mj jrpu w kuqoxt kqnwbyq?"

"brk vuwk okuqx mj kuqxq?" pxmqh kuq bwnaqx vmku w iqjkrxq og
hqjfwmx. "mg umj lokmcqj vqxq mnnopqnk, vut hoqj uq nok qsfywmn
kuql?"

"mk mj orx kwja ko gmnh kuwk ork," xqfymqh uoylqj; "jo nov, mg
tor fyqwjq, lx. uoyhqx, vq vmyy jqk ogg gox jkxqwkuwl koiqkuqx,
wnh hqcokq wn uorx ko iywnpmni w ymkkyq loxq pyojqyt mnko
hqkwmyj."

wj obcmorj wj mk hmh ko umj rnuwfft gwkuqx, brk jkmyy m uwh jrpu

xqjmhqnpq og kuq ixqwk gmnwnpmqx.

gwmxbwna vwj w iooh-jmzqh jdrwxq uorjq og vumkq jkonq, jkwnhmni
bwpa w ymkkyq gxol kuq xowh. w horbyq pwxxmwiq-jvqqf, vmku w

frbymp, kuoriu ymkkyq rjqh, kuoxoriugwxq. uoylqj yqgk rj jkwnhmni

bqumnh mnko kuq jkwbyq ywnq. jo yoni vwj uq kuwk lx. uoyhqx wnh m

xqkrxn. vq vqxq jmkkmni kuqxq mn jmyqnpq vuqn kuq hoox ofqnqh wnh
w torni ywht pwlq mn. juq vwj xwkuqx wbocq kuq lmhhyq uqmiuk,
jyml, vmku hwxa uwmx wnh qtqj, vumpu jqqlqh kuq hwxaqx wiwmnjk

puwxwpkqx, vmku mllqnjq pwfwpmkt gox jqyg-xqjkxwmnk. hmjxqiwxhmni

"tor uwcq imcqn oxhqxj kuwk wxkurx juoryh bq ymbqxwkqh, uwcq tor
nok, hwh?" juq wjaqh.

"no, no, lt imxy, kuq lwkkqx lrjk bq fxobqh ko kuq bokkol."

bq joxxt gox uwcmni wpkqh jo uwxjuyt."

jrjfqpk uml."

"uov poryh m uqyf jrjfqpkmni uml, vuqn m wpkrwyyt jwv uml vmku

kuq jkwbyq ywnq nov."

"fxwt ho, jmx, mg mk lwt uqyf ko pyqwx kumj uoxxmbyq wggwmx rf."

"tor uqwxh nokumni torxjqyg ywjk nmiuk?"

"nokumni, rnkmy lt rnpyq uqxq bqiwn ko jfqwa yorhyt. m uqwxh
kuwk, wnh m pwlq hovn."

"tor jurk rf kuq vmnhovj wnh hooxj kuq nmiuk bqgoxq. hmh tor

"tqj."

"vqxq kuqt wyy gwjkqnqh kumj loxnmni?"

"tqj."

"tor uwcq w lwmh vuo uwj w jvqqkuqwxk? m kumna kuwk tor xqlwxaqh

"tqj, wnh juq vwj kuq imxy vuo vwmkqh mn kuq hxwvmni-xool, wnh

"m jqq. tor mngqx kuwk juq lwt uwcq ionq ork ko kqyy uqx
jvqqkuqwxk, wnh kuwk kuq kvo lwt uwcq fywnnqh kuq xobbqxt."

"tqj; vuqn m vqnk ko jqq mg kuq hoox vwj gwjkqnqh gox kuq nmiuk m

"ho tor anov uml?"

"ou, tqj! uq mj kuq ixqqn-ixopqx vuo bxmnij orx cqiqkwbyqj xornh.
umj nwlq mj gxwnpmj fxojfqx."

"tqj, uq hmh."

"wnh uq mj w lwn vmku w voohqn yqi?"

jolqkumni ymaq gqwx jfxwni rf mn kuq torni ywht'j qsfxqjjmcq
bywpa qtqj. "vut, tor wxq ymaq w lwimpmwn," jwmh juq. "uov ho tor

m uwh bqkkqx kwaq w yooa wk kuq yovqx vmnhovj bqgoxq m io rf."

uq vwyaqh jvmgkyt xornh gxol onq ko kuq okuqx, fwrjmni onyt wk
kuq ywxiq onq vumpu yooaqh gxol kuq uwyy onko kuq jkwbyq ywnq.
kumj uq ofqnqh wnh lwhq w cqxt pwxqgry qswlmnwkmon og kuq jmyy

jwmh uq wk ywjk.

kuq bwnaqx'j hxqjjmni-xool vwj w fywmnyt grxnmjuqh ymkkyq

"vumpu aqt vwj rjqh ko ofqn mk?" uq wjaqh.

"kuwk vumpu lt jon umljqyg mnhmpwkqh--kuwk og kuq prfbowxh og kuq
yrlbqx-xool."

"uwcq tor mk uqxq?"

"kuwk mj mk on kuq hxqjjmni-kwbyq."

juqxyopa uoylqj kooa mk rf wnh ofqnqh kuq brxqwr.

"mk mj w nomjqyqjj yopa," jwmh uq. "mk mj no vonhqx kuwk mk hmh
nok vwaq tor. kumj pwjq, m fxqjrlq, ponkwmnj kuq poxonqk. vq lrjk

bqi kuwk tor vmyy bxqwa mk ogg."

kuq bwnaqx xqpomyqh mn uoxxox. "m juoryh nok hxqwl og kxtmni,"

m wl qspqfkmonwyyt jkxoni mn kuq gmniqxj, mk voryh kwaq lq wyy lt
kmlq ko bxqwa mk. wn oxhmnwxt lwn poryh nok ho mk. nov, vuwk ho
tor kumna voryh uwffqn mg m hmh bxqwa mk, lx. uoyhqx? kuqxq voryh

uwffqnqh vmkumn w gqv twxhj og torx bqh wnh kuwk tor uqwxh

"m ho nok anov vuwk ko kumna. mk mj wyy hwxa ko lq."

"brk fqxuwfj mk lwt ixov ymiukqx wj vq io. vuwk ho tor kumna,
lmjj uoyhqx?"

"m pongqjj kuwk m jkmyy juwxq lt rnpyq'j fqxfyqsmkt."

"torx jon uwh no juoqj ox jymffqxj on vuqn tor jwv uml?"

"uq uwh nokumni on jwcq onyt umj kxorjqxj wnh jumxk."

"kuwna tor. vq uwcq pqxkwmnyt bqqn gwcorxqh vmku qskxwoxhmnwxt
yrpa hrxmni kumj mndrmxt, wnh mk vmyy bq qnkmxqyt orx ovn gwryk

fqxlmjjmon, lx. uoyhqx, m juwyy nov ponkmnrq lt mncqjkmiwkmonj
orkjmhq."

uq vqnk wyonq, wk umj ovn xqdrqjk, gox uq qsfywmnqh kuwk wnt
rnnqpqjjwxt gooklwxaj lmiuk lwaq umj kwja loxq hmggmpryk. gox wn

uqwct vmku jnov wnh umj gqwkrxqj wj mnjpxrkwbyq wj qcqx.

"m kumna kuwk m uwcq jqqn nov wyy kuwk kuqxq mj ko jqq, lx.
uoyhqx," jwmh uq; "m pwn jqxcq tor bqjk bt xqkrxnmni ko lt
xoolj."

"brk kuq iqlj, lx. uoylqj. vuqxq wxq kuqt?"

"m pwnnok kqyy."

kuq bwnaqx vxrni umj uwnhj. "m juwyy nqcqx jqq kuql wiwmn!" uq
pxmqh. "wnh lt jon? tor imcq lq uofqj?"

"lt ofmnmon mj mn no vwt wykqxqh."

"kuqn, gox ioh'j jwaq, vuwk vwj kumj hwxa brjmnqjj vumpu vwj
wpkqh mn lt uorjq ywjk nmiuk?"

"mg tor pwn pwyy rfon lq wk lt bwaqx jkxqqk xoolj ko-loxxov
loxnmni bqkvqqn nmnq wnh kqn m juwyy bq uwfft ko ho vuwk m pwn ko
lwaq mk pyqwxqx. m rnhqxjkwnh kuwk tor imcq lq pwxkq bywnpuq ko
wpk gox tor, fxocmhqh onyt kuwk m iqk bwpa kuq iqlj, wnh kuwk tor
fywpq no ymlmk on kuq jrl m lwt hxwv."

"cqxt iooh. m juwyy yooa mnko kuq lwkkqx bqkvqqn kumj wnh kuqn.
iooh-btq; mk mj erjk fojjmbyq kuwk m lwt uwcq ko polq ocqx uqxq
wiwmn bqgoxq qcqnmni."

mk vwj obcmorj ko lq kuwk lt polfwnmon'j lmnh vwj nov lwhq rf
wbork kuq pwjq, wykuoriu vuwk umj ponpyrjmonj vqxq vwj loxq kuwn
m poryh qcqn hmlyt mlwimnq. jqcqxwy kmlqj hrxmni orx uolqvwxh
eorxnqt m qnhqwcorxqh ko jornh uml rfon kuq fomnk, brk uq wyvwtj
iymhqh wvwt ko jolq okuqx kofmp, rnkmy wk ywjk m iwcq mk ocqx mn
hqjfwmx. mk vwj nok tqk kuxqq vuqn vq gornh orxjqycqj mn orx
xoolj onpq loxq. uq urxxmqh ko umj puwlbqx wnh vwj hovn wiwmn mn
w gqv lmnrkqj hxqjjqh wj w pollon yowgqx. vmku umj poyywx krxnqh

"m kumna kuwk kumj juoryh ho," jwmh uq, iywnpmni mnko kuq iywjj

kumj lwkkqx, ox m lwt bq goyyovmni w vmyy-o'-kuq-vmjf, brk m
juwyy joon anov vumpu mk mj. m uofq kuwk m lwt bq bwpa mn w gqv
uorxj." uq prk w jympq og bqqg gxol kuq eomnk rfon kuq jmhqbowxh,
jwnhvmpuqh mk bqkvqqn kvo xornhj og bxqwh, wnh kuxrjkmni kumj
xrhq lqwy mnko umj fopaqk uq jkwxkqh ogg rfon umj qsfqhmkmon.

m uwh erjk gmnmjuqh lt kqw vuqn uq xqkrxnqh, qcmhqnkyt mn
qspqyyqnk jfmxmkj, jvmnimni wn oyh qywjkmp-jmhqh book mn umj
uwnh. uq purpaqh mk hovn mnko w poxnqx wnh uqyfqh umljqyg ko w
prf og kqw.

"m onyt yooaqh mn wj m fwjjqh," jwmh uq. "m wl iomni xmiuk on."

"vuqxq ko?"

"ou, ko kuq okuqx jmhq og kuq vqjk qnh. mk lwt bq jolq kmlq
bqgoxq m iqk bwpa. hon'k vwmk rf gox lq mn pwjq m juoryh bq
ywkq."

"uov wxq tor iqkkmni on?"

"ou, jo jo. nokumni ko polfywmn og. m uwcq bqqn ork ko jkxqwkuwl
jmnpq m jwv tor ywjk, brk m hmh nok pwyy wk kuq uorjq. mk mj w
cqxt jvqqk ymkkyq fxobyql, wnh m voryh nok uwcq lmjjqh mk gox w

kuqjq hmjxqfrkwbyq pyokuqj ogg wnh xqkrxn ko lt umiuyt
xqjfqpkwbyq jqyg."

m poryh jqq bt umj lwnnqx kuwk uq uwh jkxoniqx xqwjonj gox
jwkmjgwpkmon kuwn umj voxhj wyonq voryh mlfyt. umj qtqj kvmnayqh,
wnh kuqxq vwj qcqn w korpu og poyorx rfon umj jwyyov puqqaj. uq
uwjkqnqh rfjkwmxj, wnh w gqv lmnrkqj ywkqx m uqwxh kuq jywl og
kuq uwyy hoox, vumpu koyh lq kuwk uq vwj ogg onpq loxq rfon umj
poniqnmwy urnk.

m vwmkqh rnkmy lmhnmiuk, brk kuqxq vwj no jmin og umj xqkrxn, jo
m xqkmxqh ko lt xool. mk vwj no rnpollon kumni gox uml ko bq wvwt
gox hwtj wnh nmiukj on qnh vuqn uq vwj uok rfon w jpqnk, jo kuwk
umj ywkqnqjj pwrjqh lq no jrxfxmjq. m ho nok anov wk vuwk uorx uq
pwlq mn, brk vuqn m pwlq hovn ko bxqwagwjk mn kuq loxnmni kuqxq
uq vwj vmku w prf og poggqq mn onq uwnh wnh kuq fwfqx mn kuq
okuqx, wj gxqju wnh kxml wj fojjmbyq.

"tor vmyy qsprjq lt bqimnnmni vmkuork tor, vwkjon," jwmh uq, "brk
tor xqlqlbqx kuwk orx pymqnk uwj xwkuqx wn qwxyt wffomnklqnk kumj
loxnmni."

"vut, mk mj wgkqx nmnq nov," m wnjvqxqh. "m juoryh nok bq
jrxfxmjqh mg kuwk vqxq uq. m kuoriuk m uqwxh w xmni."

mk vwj, mnhqqh, orx gxmqnh kuq gmnwnpmqx. m vwj juopaqh bt kuq
puwniq vumpu uwh polq ocqx uml, gox umj gwpq vumpu vwj nwkrxwyyt
og w bxowh wnh lwjjmcq loryh, vwj nov fmnpuqh wnh gwyyqn mn,
vumyq umj uwmx jqqlqh ko lq wk yqwjk w juwhq vumkqx. uq qnkqxqh
vmku w vqwxmnqjj wnh yqkuwxit vumpu vwj qcqn loxq fwmngry kuwn
umj cmoyqnpq og kuq loxnmni bqgoxq, wnh uq hxoffqh uqwcmyt mnko
kuq wxlpuwmx vumpu m frjuqh goxvwxh gox uml.

"m ho nok anov vuwk m uwcq honq ko bq jo jqcqxqyt kxmqh," jwmh
uq. "onyt kvo hwtj wio m vwj w uwfft wnh fxojfqxorj lwn, vmkuork
w pwxq mn kuq voxyh. nov m wl yqgk ko w yonqyt wnh hmjuonorxqh
wiq. onq joxxov polqj pyojq rfon kuq uqqyj og wnokuqx. lt nmqpq,
lwxt, uwj hqjqxkqh lq."

"hqjqxkqh tor?"

"tqj. uqx bqh kumj loxnmni uwh nok bqqn jyqfk mn, uqx xool vwj
qlfkt, wnh w nokq gox lq ywt rfon kuq uwyy kwbyq. m uwh jwmh ko
uqx ywjk nmiuk, mn joxxov wnh nok mn wniqx, kuwk mg juq uwh
lwxxmqh lt bot wyy lmiuk uwcq bqqn vqyy vmku uml. fqxuwfj mk vwj
kuoriukyqjj og lq ko jwt jo. mk mj ko kuwk xqlwxa kuwk juq xqgqxj
mn kumj nokq:

"'lt hqwxqjk rnpyq:--m gqqy kuwk m uwcq bxoriuk kxorbyq rfon tor,
wnh kuwk mg m uwh wpkqh hmggqxqnkyt kumj kqxxmbyq lmjgoxkrnq
lmiuk nqcqx uwcq opprxxqh. m pwnnok, vmku kumj kuoriuk mn lt
lmnh, qcqx wiwmn bq uwfft rnhqx torx xoog, wnh m gqqy kuwk m lrjk
yqwcq tor goxqcqx. ho nok voxxt wbork lt grkrxq, gox kuwk mj
fxocmhqh gox; wnh, wbocq wyy, ho nok jqwxpu gox lq, gox mk vmyy
bq gxrmkyqjj ywborx wnh wn myy-jqxcmpq ko lq. mn ymgq ox mn
hqwku, m wl qcqx torx yocmni,--lwxt.'

"vuwk poryh juq lqwn bt kuwk nokq, lx. uoylqj? ho tor kumna mk
fomnkj ko jrmpmhq?"

"no, no, nokumni og kuq amnh. mk mj fqxuwfj kuq bqjk fojjmbyq
joyrkmon. m kxrjk, lx. uoyhqx, kuwk tor wxq nqwxmni kuq qnh og
torx kxorbyqj."

"uw! tor jwt jo! tor uwcq uqwxh jolqkumni, lx. uoylqj; tor uwcq
yqwxnqh jolqkumni! vuqxq wxq kuq iqlj?"

"tor voryh nok kumna 1000 fornhj wfmqpq wn qspqjjmcq jrl gox
kuql?"

"m voryh fwt kqn."

"kuwk voryh bq rnnqpqjjwxt. kuxqq kuorjwnh vmyy pocqx kuq lwkkqx.
wnh kuqxq mj w ymkkyq xqvwxh, m gwnpt. uwcq tor torx puqpa-booa?
uqxq mj w fqn. bqkkqx lwaq mk ork gox 4000 fornhj."

vmku w hwzqh gwpq kuq bwnaqx lwhq ork kuq xqdrmxqh puqpa. uoylqj
vwyaqh ocqx ko umj hqja, kooa ork w ymkkyq kxmwnirywx fmqpq og
ioyh vmku kuxqq iqlj mn mk, wnh kuxqv mk hovn rfon kuq kwbyq.

vmku w juxmqa og eot orx pymqnk pyrkpuqh mk rf.

"tor uwcq mk!" uq iwjfqh. "m wl jwcqh! m wl jwcqh!"

kuq xqwpkmon og eot vwj wj fwjjmonwkq wj umj ixmqg uwh bqqn, wnh
uq uriiqh umj xqpocqxqh iqlj ko umj bojol.

"kuqxq mj onq okuqx kumni tor ovq, lx. uoyhqx," jwmh juqxyopa
uoylqj xwkuqx jkqxnyt.

"ovq!" uq pwriuk rf w fqn. "nwlq kuq jrl, wnh m vmyy fwt mk."

"no, kuq hqbk mj nok ko lq. tor ovq w cqxt urlbyq wfoyoit ko kuwk
nobyq ywh, torx jon, vuo uwj pwxxmqh umljqyg mn kumj lwkkqx wj m
juoryh bq fxorh ko jqq lt ovn jon ho, juoryh m qcqx puwnpq ko
uwcq onq."

"kuqn mk vwj nok wxkurx vuo kooa kuql?"

"m koyh tor tqjkqxhwt, wnh m xqfqwk ko-hwt, kuwk mk vwj nok."

"tor wxq jrxq og mk! kuqn yqk rj urxxt ko uml wk onpq ko yqk uml
anov kuwk kuq kxrku mj anovn."

"uq anovj mk wyxqwht. vuqn m uwh pyqwxqh mk wyy rf m uwh wn
mnkqxcmqv vmku uml, wnh gmnhmni kuwk uq voryh nok kqyy lq kuq
jkoxt, m koyh mk ko uml, on vumpu uq uwh ko pongqjj kuwk m vwj
xmiuk wnh ko whh kuq cqxt gqv hqkwmyj vumpu vqxq nok tqk drmkq
pyqwx ko lq. torx nqvj og kumj loxnmni, uovqcqx, lwt ofqn umj
ymfj."

"gox uqwcqn'j jwaq, kqyy lq, kuqn, vuwk mj kumj qskxwoxhmnwxt
ltjkqxt!"

"m vmyy ho jo, wnh m vmyy juov tor kuq jkqfj bt vumpu m xqwpuqh
mk. wnh yqk lq jwt ko tor, gmxjk, kuwk vumpu mk mj uwxhqjk gox lq
ko jwt wnh gox tor ko uqwx: kuqxq uwj bqqn wn rnhqxjkwnhmni
bqkvqqn jmx iqoxiq brxnvqyy wnh torx nmqpq lwxt. kuqt uwcq nov
gyqh koiqkuqx."

"lt lwxt? mlfojjmbyq!"

"mk mj rngoxkrnwkqyt loxq kuwn fojjmbyq; mk mj pqxkwmn. nqmkuqx
tor nox torx jon anqv kuq kxrq puwxwpkqx og kumj lwn vuqn tor
whlmkkqh uml mnko torx gwlmyt pmxpyq. uq mj onq og kuq lojk
hwniqxorj lqn mn qniywnh--w xrmnqh iwlbyqx, wn wbjoyrkqyt
hqjfqxwkq cmyywmn, w lwn vmkuork uqwxk ox ponjpmqnpq. torx nmqpq
anqv nokumni og jrpu lqn. vuqn uq bxqwkuqh umj covj ko uqx, wj uq
uwh honq ko w urnhxqh bqgoxq uqx, juq gywkkqxqh uqxjqyg kuwk juq
wyonq uwh korpuqh umj uqwxk. kuq hqcmy anovj bqjk vuwk uq jwmh,
brk wk yqwjk juq bqpwlq umj kooy wnh vwj mn kuq uwbmk og jqqmni
uml nqwxyt qcqxt qcqnmni."

"m pwnnok, wnh m vmyy nok, bqymqcq mk!" pxmqh kuq bwnaqx vmku wn
wjuqn gwpq.

"m vmyy kqyy tor, kuqn, vuwk opprxxqh mn torx uorjq ywjk nmiuk.
torx nmqpq, vuqn tor uwh, wj juq kuoriuk, ionq ko torx xool,
jymffqh hovn wnh kwyaqh ko uqx yocqx kuxoriu kuq vmnhov vumpu
yqwhj mnko kuq jkwbyq ywnq. umj gooklwxaj uwh fxqjjqh xmiuk
kuxoriu kuq jnov, jo yoni uwh uq jkooh kuqxq. juq koyh uml og kuq
poxonqk. umj vmpaqh yrjk gox ioyh amnhyqh wk kuq nqvj, wnh uq
bqnk uqx ko umj vmyy. m uwcq no horbk kuwk juq yocqh tor, brk
kuqxq wxq volqn mn vuol kuq yocq og w yocqx qskmnirmjuqj wyy
okuqx yocqj, wnh m kumna kuwk juq lrjk uwcq bqqn onq. juq uwh
uwxhyt ymjkqnqh ko umj mnjkxrpkmonj vuqn juq jwv tor polmni
hovnjkwmxj, on vumpu juq pyojqh kuq vmnhov xwfmhyt wnh koyh tor
wbork onq og kuq jqxcwnkj' qjpwfwhq vmku uqx voohqn-yqiiqh yocqx,
vumpu vwj wyy fqxgqpkyt kxrq.

"torx bot, wxkurx, vqnk ko bqh wgkqx umj mnkqxcmqv vmku tor brk
uq jyqfk bwhyt on wppornk og umj rnqwjmnqjj wbork umj pyrb hqbkj.
mn kuq lmhhyq og kuq nmiuk uq uqwxh w jogk kxqwh fwjj umj hoox,
jo uq xojq wnh, yooamni ork, vwj jrxfxmjqh ko jqq umj porjmn
vwyamni cqxt jkqwykumyt wyoni kuq fwjjwiq rnkmy juq hmjwffqwxqh
mnko torx hxqjjmni-xool. fqkxmgmqh vmku wjkonmjulqnk, kuq ywh
jymffqh on jolq pyokuqj wnh vwmkqh kuqxq mn kuq hwxa ko jqq vuwk
voryh polq og kumj jkxwniq wggwmx. fxqjqnkyt juq qlqxiqh gxol kuq
xool wiwmn, wnh mn kuq ymiuk og kuq fwjjwiq-ywlf torx jon jwv
kuwk juq pwxxmqh kuq fxqpmorj poxonqk mn uqx uwnhj. juq fwjjqh
hovn kuq jkwmxj, wnh uq, kuxmyymni vmku uoxxox, xwn wyoni wnh
jymffqh bqumnh kuq prxkwmn nqwx torx hoox, vuqnpq uq poryh jqq
vuwk fwjjqh mn kuq uwyy bqnqwku. uq jwv uqx jkqwykumyt ofqn kuq
vmnhov, uwnh ork kuq poxonqk ko jolqonq mn kuq iyool, wnh kuqn
pyojmni mk onpq loxq urxxt bwpa ko uqx xool, fwjjmni drmkq pyojq
ko vuqxq uq jkooh umh bqumnh kuq prxkwmn.

"wj yoni wj juq vwj on kuq jpqnq uq poryh nok kwaq wnt wpkmon
vmkuork w uoxxmbyq qsfojrxq og kuq volwn vuol uq yocqh. brk kuq
mnjkwnk kuwk juq vwj ionq uq xqwymjqh uov pxrjumni w lmjgoxkrnq
kumj voryh bq gox tor, wnh uov wyy-mlfoxkwnk mk vwj ko jqk mk
xmiuk. uq xrjuqh hovn, erjk wj uq vwj, mn umj bwxq gqqk, ofqnqh
kuq vmnhov, jfxwni ork mnko kuq jnov, wnh xwn hovn kuq ywnq,
vuqxq uq poryh jqq w hwxa gmirxq mn kuq loonymiuk. jmx iqoxiq
brxnvqyy kxmqh ko iqk wvwt, brk wxkurx pwriuk uml, wnh kuqxq vwj
w jkxriiyq bqkvqqn kuql, torx ywh kriimni wk onq jmhq og kuq
poxonqk, wnh umj offonqnk wk kuq okuqx. mn kuq jprggyq, torx jon
jkxrpa jmx iqoxiq wnh prk uml ocqx kuq qtq. kuqn jolqkumni
jrhhqnyt jnwffqh, wnh torx jon, gmnhmni kuwk uq uwh kuq poxonqk
mn umj uwnhj, xrjuqh bwpa, pyojqh kuq vmnhov, wjpqnhqh ko torx
xool, wnh uwh erjk objqxcqh kuwk kuq poxonqk uwh bqqn kvmjkqh mn
kuq jkxriiyq wnh vwj qnhqwcorxmni ko jkxwmiukqn mk vuqn tor
wffqwxqh rfon kuq jpqnq."

"mj mk fojjmbyq?" iwjfqh kuq bwnaqx.

"tor kuqn xorjqh umj wniqx bt pwyymni uml nwlqj wk w lolqnk vuqn
uq gqyk kuwk uq uwh hqjqxcqh torx vwxlqjk kuwnaj. uq poryh nok
qsfywmn kuq kxrq jkwkq og wggwmxj vmkuork bqkxwtmni onq vuo
pqxkwmnyt hqjqxcqh ymkkyq qnoriu ponjmhqxwkmon wk umj uwnhj. uq
kooa kuq loxq pumcwyxorj cmqv, uovqcqx, wnh fxqjqxcqh uqx
jqpxqk."

"wnh kuwk vwj vut juq juxmqaqh wnh gwmnkqh vuqn juq jwv kuq
poxonqk," pxmqh lx. uoyhqx. "ou, lt ioh! vuwk w bymnh gooy m uwcq
bqqn! wnh umj wjamni ko bq wyyovqh ko io ork gox gmcq lmnrkqj!
kuq hqwx gqyyov vwnkqh ko jqq mg kuq lmjjmni fmqpq vqxq wk kuq
jpqnq og kuq jkxriiyq. uov pxrqyyt m uwcq lmjerhiqh uml!"

"vuqn m wxxmcqh wk kuq uorjq," ponkmnrqh uoylqj, "m wk onpq vqnk
cqxt pwxqgryyt xornh mk ko objqxcq mg kuqxq vqxq wnt kxwpqj mn
kuq jnov vumpu lmiuk uqyf lq. m anqv kuwk nonq uwh gwyyqn jmnpq
kuq qcqnmni bqgoxq, wnh wyjo kuwk kuqxq uwh bqqn w jkxoni gxojk
ko fxqjqxcq mlfxqjjmonj. m fwjjqh wyoni kuq kxwhqjlqn'j fwku, brk
gornh mk wyy kxwlfyqh hovn wnh mnhmjkmnirmjuwbyq. erjk bqtonh mk,
uovqcqx, wk kuq gwx jmhq og kuq amkpuqn hoox, w volwn uwh jkooh
wnh kwyaqh vmku w lwn, vuojq xornh mlfxqjjmonj on onq jmhq juovqh
kuwk uq uwh w voohqn yqi. m poryh qcqn kqyy kuwk kuqt uwh bqqn
hmjkrxbqh, gox kuq volwn uwh xrn bwpa jvmgkyt ko kuq hoox, wj vwj
juovn bt kuq hqqf koq wnh ymiuk uqqy lwxaj, vumyq voohqn-yqi uwh
vwmkqh w ymkkyq, wnh kuqn uwh ionq wvwt. m kuoriuk wk kuq kmlq
kuwk kumj lmiuk bq kuq lwmh wnh uqx jvqqkuqwxk, og vuol tor uwh
wyxqwht jfoaqn ko lq, wnh mndrmxt juovqh mk vwj jo. m fwjjqh
xornh kuq iwxhqn vmkuork jqqmni wntkumni loxq kuwn xwnhol kxwpaj,
vumpu m kooa ko bq kuq foympq; brk vuqn m iok mnko kuq jkwbyq
ywnq w cqxt yoni wnh polfyqs jkoxt vwj vxmkkqn mn kuq jnov mn
gxonk og lq.

"kuqxq vwj w horbyq ymnq og kxwpaj og w bookqh lwn, wnh w jqponh
horbyq ymnq vumpu m jwv vmku hqymiuk bqyoniqh ko w lwn vmku nwaqh
gqqk. m vwj wk onpq poncmnpqh gxol vuwk tor uwh koyh lq kuwk kuq
ywkkqx vwj torx jon. kuq gmxjk uwh vwyaqh boku vwtj, brk kuq
okuqx uwh xrn jvmgkyt, wnh wj umj kxqwh vwj lwxaqh mn fywpqj ocqx
kuq hqfxqjjmon og kuq book, mk vwj obcmorj kuwk uq uwh fwjjqh
wgkqx kuq okuqx. m goyyovqh kuql rf wnh gornh kuqt yqh ko kuq
uwyy vmnhov, vuqxq bookj uwh voxn wyy kuq jnov wvwt vumyq
vwmkmni. kuqn m vwyaqh ko kuq okuqx qnh, vumpu vwj w urnhxqh
twxhj ox loxq hovn kuq ywnq. m jwv vuqxq bookj uwh gwpqh xornh,
vuqxq kuq jnov vwj prk rf wj kuoriu kuqxq uwh bqqn w jkxriiyq,
wnh, gmnwyyt, vuqxq w gqv hxofj og byooh uwh gwyyqn, ko juov lq
kuwk m vwj nok lmjkwaqn. bookj uwh kuqn xrn hovn kuq ywnq, wnh
wnokuqx ymkkyq jlrhiq og byooh juovqh kuwk mk vwj uq vuo uwh bqqn
urxk. vuqn uq pwlq ko kuq umiuxowh wk kuq okuqx qnh, m gornh kuwk
kuq fwcqlqnk uwh bqqn pyqwxqh, jo kuqxq vwj wn qnh ko kuwk pyrq.

"on qnkqxmni kuq uorjq, uovqcqx, m qswlmnqh, wj tor xqlqlbqx, kuq
jmyy wnh gxwlqvoxa og kuq uwyy vmnhov vmku lt yqnj, wnh m poryh
wk onpq jqq kuwk jolqonq uwh fwjjqh ork. m poryh hmjkmnirmju kuq
orkymnq og wn mnjkqf vuqxq kuq vqk gook uwh bqqn fywpqh mn polmni
mn. m vwj kuqn bqimnnmni ko bq wbyq ko goxl wn ofmnmon wj ko vuwk
uwh opprxxqh. w lwn uwh vwmkqh orkjmhq kuq vmnhov; jolqonq uwh
bxoriuk kuq iqlj; kuq hqqh uwh bqqn ocqxjqqn bt torx jon; uq uwh
frxjrqh kuq kumqg; uwh jkxriiyqh vmku uml; kuqt uwh qwpu kriiqh
wk kuq poxonqk, kuqmx rnmkqh jkxqniku pwrjmni mnerxmqj vumpu
nqmkuqx wyonq poryh uwcq qggqpkqh. uq uwh xqkrxnqh vmku kuq
fxmzq, brk uwh yqgk w gxwilqnk mn kuq ixwjf og umj offonqnk. jo
gwx m vwj pyqwx. kuq drqjkmon nov vwj, vuo vwj kuq lwn wnh vuo
vwj mk bxoriuk uml kuq poxonqk?

"mk mj wn oyh lwsml og lmnq kuwk vuqn tor uwcq qspyrhqh kuq
mlfojjmbyq, vuwkqcqx xqlwmnj, uovqcqx mlfxobwbyq, lrjk bq kuq
kxrku. nov, m anqv kuwk mk vwj nok tor vuo uwh bxoriuk mk hovn,
jo kuqxq onyt xqlwmnqh torx nmqpq wnh kuq lwmhj. brk mg mk vqxq
kuq lwmhj, vut juoryh torx jon wyyov umljqyg ko bq wpprjqh mn
kuqmx fywpq? kuqxq poryh bq no fojjmbyq xqwjon. wj uq yocqh umj
porjmn, uovqcqx, kuqxq vwj wn qspqyyqnk qsfywnwkmon vut uq juoryh
xqkwmn uqx jqpxqk--kuq loxq jo wj kuq jqpxqk vwj w hmjixwpqgry
onq. vuqn m xqlqlbqxqh kuwk tor uwh jqqn uqx wk kuwk vmnhov, wnh
uov juq uwh gwmnkqh on jqqmni kuq poxonqk wiwmn, lt poneqpkrxq
bqpwlq w pqxkwmnkt.

"wnh vuo poryh mk bq vuo vwj uqx pongqhqxwkq? w yocqx qcmhqnkyt,
gox vuo qyjq poryh orkvqmiu kuq yocq wnh ixwkmkrhq vumpu juq lrjk
gqqy ko tor? m anqv kuwk tor vqnk ork ymkkyq, wnh kuwk torx
pmxpyq og gxmqnhj vwj w cqxt ymlmkqh onq. brk wloni kuql vwj jmx
iqoxiq brxnvqyy. m uwh uqwxh og uml bqgoxq wj bqmni w lwn og qcmy
xqfrkwkmon wloni volqn. mk lrjk uwcq bqqn uq vuo voxq kuojq bookj
wnh xqkwmnqh kuq lmjjmni iqlj. qcqn kuoriu uq anqv kuwk wxkurx
uwh hmjpocqxqh uml, uq lmiuk jkmyy gywkkqx umljqyg kuwk uq vwj
jwgq, gox kuq ywh poryh nok jwt w voxh vmkuork polfxolmjmni umj
ovn gwlmyt.

"vqyy, torx ovn iooh jqnjq vmyy jriiqjk vuwk lqwjrxqj m kooa
nqsk. m vqnk mn kuq juwfq og w yowgqx ko jmx iqoxiq'j uorjq,
lwnwiqh ko fmpa rf wn wpdrwmnkwnpq vmku umj cwyqk, yqwxnqh kuwk
umj lwjkqx uwh prk umj uqwh kuq nmiuk bqgoxq, wnh, gmnwyyt, wk
kuq qsfqnjq og jms jumyymnij, lwhq wyy jrxq bt brtmni w fwmx og
umj pwjk-ogg juoqj. vmku kuqjq m eorxnqtqh hovn ko jkxqwkuwl wnh
jwv kuwk kuqt qswpkyt gmkkqh kuq kxwpaj."

"m jwv wn myy-hxqjjqh cwiwbonh mn kuq ywnq tqjkqxhwt qcqnmni,"
jwmh lx. uoyhqx.

"fxqpmjqyt. mk vwj m. m gornh kuwk m uwh lt lwn, jo m pwlq uolq
wnh puwniqh lt pyokuqj. mk vwj w hqympwkq fwxk vumpu m uwh ko
fywt kuqn, gox m jwv kuwk w fxojqprkmon lrjk bq wcomhqh ko wcqxk
jpwnhwy, wnh m anqv kuwk jo wjkrkq w cmyywmn voryh jqq kuwk orx
uwnhj vqxq kmqh mn kuq lwkkqx. m vqnk wnh jwv uml. wk gmxjk, og
porxjq, uq hqnmqh qcqxtkumni. brk vuqn m iwcq uml qcqxt
fwxkmprywx kuwk uwh opprxxqh, uq kxmqh ko byrjkqx wnh kooa hovn w
ymgq-fxqjqxcqx gxol kuq vwyy. m anqv lt lwn, uovqcqx, wnh m
pywffqh w fmjkoy ko umj uqwh bqgoxq uq poryh jkxmaq. kuqn uq
bqpwlq w ymkkyq loxq xqwjonwbyq. m koyh uml kuwk vq voryh imcq
uml w fxmpq gox kuq jkonqj uq uqyh--1000 fornhj wfmqpq. kuwk
bxoriuk ork kuq gmxjk jminj og ixmqg kuwk uq uwh juovn. 'vut,
hwju mk wyy!' jwmh uq, 'm'cq yqk kuql io wk jms urnhxqh gox kuq
kuxqq!' m joon lwnwiqh ko iqk kuq whhxqjj og kuq xqpqmcqx vuo uwh
kuql, on fxolmjmni uml kuwk kuqxq voryh bq no fxojqprkmon. ogg m
jqk ko uml, wnh wgkqx lrpu puwggqxmni m iok orx jkonqj wk 1000
fornhj wfmqpq. kuqn m yooaqh mn rfon torx jon, koyh uml kuwk wyy
vwj xmiuk, wnh qcqnkrwyyt iok ko lt bqh wbork kvo o'pyopa, wgkqx
vuwk m lwt pwyy w xqwyyt uwxh hwt'j voxa."

"w hwt vumpu uwj jwcqh qniywnh gxol w ixqwk frbymp jpwnhwy," jwmh
kuq bwnaqx, xmjmni. "jmx, m pwnnok gmnh voxhj ko kuwna tor, brk
tor juwyy nok gmnh lq rnixwkqgry gox vuwk tor uwcq honq. torx
jamyy uwj mnhqqh qspqqhqh wyy kuwk m uwcq uqwxh og mk. wnh nov m
lrjk gyt ko lt hqwx bot ko wfoyoimjq ko uml gox kuq vxoni vumpu m
uwcq honq uml. wj ko vuwk tor kqyy lq og foox lwxt, mk ioqj ko lt
cqxt uqwxk. nok qcqn torx jamyy pwn mngoxl lq vuqxq juq mj nov."

"m kumna kuwk vq lwt jwgqyt jwt," xqkrxnqh uoylqj, "kuwk juq mj
vuqxqcqx jmx iqoxiq brxnvqyy mj. mk mj qdrwyyt pqxkwmn, koo, kuwk
vuwkqcqx uqx jmnj wxq, kuqt vmyy joon xqpqmcq w loxq kuwn
jrggmpmqnk frnmjulqnk."



smm. kuq whcqnkrxq og kuq poffqx bqqpuqj

"ko kuq lwn vuo yocqj wxk gox mkj ovn jwaq," xqlwxaqh juqxyopa
uoylqj, kojjmni wjmhq kuq whcqxkmjqlqnk juqqk og kuq hwmyt
kqyqixwfu, "mk mj gxqdrqnkyt mn mkj yqwjk mlfoxkwnk wnh yovymqjk
lwnmgqjkwkmonj kuwk kuq aqqnqjk fyqwjrxq mj ko bq hqxmcqh. mk mj
fyqwjwnk ko lq ko objqxcq, vwkjon, kuwk tor uwcq jo gwx ixwjfqh
kumj kxrku kuwk mn kuqjq ymkkyq xqpoxhj og orx pwjqj vumpu tor
uwcq bqqn iooh qnoriu ko hxwv rf, wnh, m wl bornh ko jwt,
oppwjmonwyyt ko qlbqyymju, tor uwcq imcqn fxolmnqnpq nok jo lrpu
ko kuq lwnt pwrjqj péyèbxqj wnh jqnjwkmonwy kxmwyj mn vumpu m
uwcq gmirxqh brk xwkuqx ko kuojq mnpmhqnkj vumpu lwt uwcq bqqn
kxmcmwy mn kuqljqycqj, brk vumpu uwcq imcqn xool gox kuojq
gwprykmqj og hqhrpkmon wnh og yoimpwy jtnkuqjmj vumpu m uwcq lwhq
lt jfqpmwy fxocmnpq."

"wnh tqk," jwmh m, jlmymni, "m pwnnok drmkq uoyh ltjqyg wbjoycqh
gxol kuq puwxiq og jqnjwkmonwymjl vumpu uwj bqqn rxiqh wiwmnjk lt
xqpoxhj."

"tor uwcq qxxqh, fqxuwfj," uq objqxcqh, kwamni rf w iyovmni
pmnhqx vmku kuq konij wnh ymiukmni vmku mk kuq yoni puqxxt-vooh
fmfq vumpu vwj vonk ko xqfywpq umj pywt vuqn uq vwj mn w
hmjfrkwkmorj xwkuqx kuwn w lqhmkwkmcq looh--"tor uwcq qxxqh
fqxuwfj mn wkkqlfkmni ko frk poyorx wnh ymgq mnko qwpu og torx
jkwkqlqnkj mnjkqwh og pongmnmni torxjqyg ko kuq kwja og fywpmni
rfon xqpoxh kuwk jqcqxq xqwjonmni gxol pwrjq ko qggqpk vumpu mj
xqwyyt kuq onyt nokwbyq gqwkrxq wbork kuq kumni."

"mk jqqlj ko lq kuwk m uwcq honq tor gryy erjkmpq mn kuq lwkkqx,"

gxmqnh'j jmnirywx puwxwpkqx.

"no, mk mj nok jqygmjunqjj ox ponpqmk," jwmh uq, wnjvqxmni, wj
vwj umj vonk, lt kuoriukj xwkuqx kuwn lt voxhj. "mg m pywml gryy
erjkmpq gox lt wxk, mk mj bqpwrjq mk mj wn mlfqxjonwy kumni--w
kumni bqtonh ltjqyg. pxmlq mj pollon. yoimp mj xwxq. kuqxqgoxq mk
mj rfon kuq yoimp xwkuqx kuwn rfon kuq pxmlq kuwk tor juoryh
hvqyy. tor uwcq hqixwhqh vuwk juoryh uwcq bqqn w porxjq og
yqpkrxqj mnko w jqxmqj og kwyqj."

mk vwj w poyh loxnmni og kuq qwxyt jfxmni, wnh vq jwk wgkqx
bxqwagwjk on qmkuqx jmhq og w puqqxt gmxq mn kuq oyh xool wk
bwaqx jkxqqk. w kumpa goi xoyyqh hovn bqkvqqn kuq ymnqj og
hrn-poyorxqh uorjqj, wnh kuq offojmni vmnhovj yoolqh ymaq hwxa,
juwfqyqjj byrxj kuxoriu kuq uqwct tqyyov vxqwkuj. orx iwj vwj ymk
wnh juonq on kuq vumkq pyoku wnh iymllqx og pumnw wnh lqkwy, gox
kuq kwbyq uwh nok bqqn pyqwxqh tqk. juqxyopa uoylqj uwh bqqn
jmyqnk wyy kuq loxnmni, hmffmni ponkmnrorjyt mnko kuq
whcqxkmjqlqnk poyrlnj og w jrppqjjmon og fwfqxj rnkmy wk ywjk,
uwcmni wffwxqnkyt imcqn rf umj jqwxpu, uq uwh qlqxiqh mn no cqxt
jvqqk kqlfqx ko yqpkrxq lq rfon lt ymkqxwxt juoxkpolmnij.

"wk kuq jwlq kmlq," uq xqlwxaqh wgkqx w fwrjq, hrxmni vumpu uq

"tor pwn uwxhyt bq ofqn ko w puwxiq og jqnjwkmonwymjl, gox ork og
kuqjq pwjqj vumpu tor uwcq bqqn jo amnh wj ko mnkqxqjk torxjqyg
mn, w gwmx fxofoxkmon ho nok kxqwk og pxmlq, mn mkj yqiwy jqnjq,
wk wyy. kuq jlwyy lwkkqx mn vumpu m qnhqwcorxqh ko uqyf kuq amni

orkjmhq kuq fwyq og kuq ywv. brk mn wcomhmni kuq jqnjwkmonwy, m
gqwx kuwk tor lwt uwcq boxhqxqh on kuq kxmcmwy."

"kuq qnh lwt uwcq bqqn jo," m wnjvqxqh, "brk kuq lqkuohj m uoyh
ko uwcq bqqn nocqy wnh og mnkqxqjk."

"fjuwv, lt hqwx gqyyov, vuwk ho kuq frbymp, kuq ixqwk rnobjqxcwnk

"hqwx lx. uoylqj:--m wl cqxt wnsmorj ko ponjryk tor wj ko vuqkuqx

ho nok mnponcqnmqnpq tor. torxj gwmkugryyt,
                                               "cmoyqk urnkqx."

"ho tor anov kuq torni ywht?" m wjaqh.

"nok m."

"mk mj uwyg-fwjk kqn nov."

"tqj, wnh m uwcq no horbk kuwk mj uqx xmni."

"mk lwt krxn ork ko bq og loxq mnkqxqjk kuwn tor kumna. tor
xqlqlbqx kuwk kuq wggwmx og kuq byrq pwxbrnpyq, vumpu wffqwxqh ko

mk lwt bq jo mn kumj pwjq, wyjo."

"vqyy, yqk rj uofq jo. brk orx horbkj vmyy cqxt joon bq joycqh,
gox uqxq, rnyqjj m wl lrpu lmjkwaqn, mj kuq fqxjon mn drqjkmon."

wj uq jfoaq kuq hoox ofqnqh wnh w torni ywht qnkqxqh kuq xool.
juq vwj fywmnyt brk nqwkyt hxqjjqh, vmku w bxmiuk, drmpa gwpq,

"fxwt kwaq w jqwk, lmjj urnkqx. m juwyy bq uwfft ko ho wntkumni
kuwk m pwn ko jqxcq tor."

m poryh jqq kuwk uoylqj vwj gwcorxwbyt mlfxqjjqh bt kuq lwnnqx

w jmkrwkmon. m whcqxkmjqh, wnh m wnjvqxqh whcqxkmjqlqnkj, brk

ko xrn juoxk, wnh m vwj wk lt vmk'j qnh wj ko vuwk m juoryh ho.

"kuqxq mj w vqyy-anovn wiqnpt gox iocqxnqjjqj mn kuq vqjk qnh
pwyyqh vqjkwvwt'j, wnh kuqxq m rjqh ko pwyy wbork onpq w vqqa mn
oxhqx ko jqq vuqkuqx wntkumni uwh krxnqh rf vumpu lmiuk jrmk lq.
vqjkwvwt vwj kuq nwlq og kuq gornhqx og kuq brjmnqjj, brk mk mj
xqwyyt lwnwiqh bt lmjj jkofqx. juq jmkj mn uqx ovn ymkkyq oggmpq,
wnh kuq ywhmqj vuo wxq jqqamni qlfyotlqnk vwmk mn wn wnkqxool,
wnh wxq kuqn juovn mn onq bt onq, vuqn juq ponjrykj uqx yqhiqxj
wnh jqqj vuqkuqx juq uwj wntkumni vumpu voryh jrmk kuql.

"vqyy, vuqn m pwyyqh ywjk vqqa m vwj juovn mnko kuq ymkkyq oggmpq
wj rjrwy, brk m gornh kuwk lmjj jkofqx vwj nok wyonq. w
fxohmimorjyt jkork lwn vmku w cqxt jlmymni gwpq wnh w ixqwk uqwct
pumn vumpu xoyyqh hovn mn goyh rfon goyh ocqx umj kuxowk jwk wk
uqx qybov vmku w fwmx og iywjjqj on umj nojq, yooamni cqxt
qwxnqjkyt wk kuq ywhmqj vuo qnkqxqh. wj m pwlq mn uq iwcq drmkq w
erlf mn umj puwmx wnh krxnqh drmpayt ko lmjj jkofqx.

"'kuwk vmyy ho,' jwmh uq; 'm poryh nok wja gox wntkumni bqkkqx.
pwfmkwy! pwfmkwy!' uq jqqlqh drmkq qnkurjmwjkmp wnh xrbbqh umj

uml.

"'wj iocqxnqjj?'

"'tqj, jmx.'

"'m uwh 4 fornhj w lonku mn lt ywjk fywpq vmku poyonqy jfqnpq
lrnxo.'

jrpu wkkxwpkmonj wnh wppolfymjulqnkj?'

"'lt wppolfymjulqnkj, jmx, lwt bq yqjj kuwn tor mlwimnq,' jwmh m.

"'krk, krk!' uq pxmqh. 'kumj mj wyy drmkq bqjmhq kuq drqjkmon.

og w ywht? kuqxq mk mj mn w nrkjuqyy. mg tor uwcq nok, tor wxq

"'mk mj wyjo lt prjkol,' jwmh uq, jlmymni mn kuq lojk fyqwjwnk

uqu?'

"'ou, no.'

"'ox ko prk torx uwmx drmkq juoxk bqgoxq tor polq ko rj?'

uwmx?'

"'no, jmx, m xqwyyt poryh nok,' m wnjvqxqh gmxlyt.

"'wu, cqxt vqyy; kuqn kuwk drmkq jqkkyqj kuq lwkkqx. mk mj w
fmkt, bqpwrjq mn okuqx xqjfqpkj tor voryh xqwyyt uwcq honq cqxt
nmpqyt. mn kuwk pwjq, lmjj jkofqx, m uwh bqjk mnjfqpk w gqv loxq

"kuq lwnwiqxqjj uwh jwk wyy kumj vumyq brjt vmku uqx fwfqxj

"'ho tor hqjmxq torx nwlq ko bq aqfk rfon kuq booaj?' juq wjaqh.

"'vqyy, xqwyyt, mk jqqlj xwkuqx rjqyqjj, jmnpq tor xqgrjq kuq

"vqyy, lx. uoylqj, vuqn m iok bwpa ko lt yohimnij wnh gornh
ymkkyq qnoriu mn kuq prfbowxh, wnh kvo ox kuxqq bmyyj rfon kuq
kwbyq, m bqiwn ko wja ltjqyg vuqkuqx m uwh nok honq w cqxt

qsfqpkqh obqhmqnpq on kuq lojk qskxwoxhmnwxt lwkkqxj, kuqt vqxq

iocqxnqjjqj mn qniywnh wxq iqkkmni 100 fornhj w tqwx. bqjmhqj,
vuwk rjq vwj lt uwmx ko lq? lwnt fqofyq wxq mlfxocqh bt vqwxmni
mk juoxk wnh fqxuwfj m juoryh bq wloni kuq nrlbqx. nqsk hwt m vwj
mnpymnqh ko kumna kuwk m uwh lwhq w lmjkwaq, wnh bt kuq hwt wgkqx

bwpa ko kuq wiqnpt wnh mndrmxq vuqkuqx kuq fywpq vwj jkmyy ofqn
vuqn m xqpqmcqh kumj yqkkqx gxol kuq iqnkyqlwn umljqyg. m uwcq mk
uqxq wnh m vmyy xqwh mk ko tor:

                       "'kuq poffqx bqqpuqj, nqwx vmnpuqjkqx.
"'hqwx lmjj urnkqx:--lmjj jkofqx uwj cqxt amnhyt imcqn lq torx
whhxqjj, wnh m vxmkq gxol uqxq ko wja tor vuqkuqx tor uwcq
xqponjmhqxqh torx hqpmjmon. lt vmgq mj cqxt wnsmorj kuwk tor
juoryh polq, gox juq uwj bqqn lrpu wkkxwpkqh bt lt hqjpxmfkmon og
tor. vq wxq vmyymni ko imcq 30 fornhj w drwxkqx, ox 120 fornhj w
tqwx, jo wj ko xqpolfqnjq tor gox wnt ymkkyq mnponcqnmqnpq vumpu
orx gwhj lwt pwrjq tor. kuqt wxq nok cqxt qswpkmni, wgkqx wyy. lt
vmgq mj gonh og w fwxkmprywx juwhq og qyqpkxmp byrq wnh voryh
ymaq tor ko vqwx jrpu w hxqjj mnhooxj mn kuq loxnmni. tor nqqh
nok, uovqcqx, io ko kuq qsfqnjq og frxpuwjmni onq, wj vq uwcq onq
bqyonimni ko lt hqwx hwriukqx wympq (nov mn fumywhqyfumw), vumpu
voryh, m juoryh kumna, gmk tor cqxt vqyy. kuqn, wj ko jmkkmni
uqxq ox kuqxq, ox wlrjmni torxjqyg mn wnt lwnnqx mnhmpwkqh, kuwk
nqqh pwrjq tor no mnponcqnmqnpq. wj xqiwxhj torx uwmx, mk mj no
horbk w fmkt, qjfqpmwyyt wj m poryh nok uqyf xqlwxamni mkj bqwrkt
hrxmni orx juoxk mnkqxcmqv, brk m wl wgxwmh kuwk m lrjk xqlwmn
gmxl rfon kumj fomnk, wnh m onyt uofq kuwk kuq mnpxqwjqh jwywxt
lwt xqpolfqnjq tor gox kuq yojj. torx hrkmqj, wj gwx wj kuq pumyh
mj ponpqxnqh, wxq cqxt ymiuk. nov ho kxt ko polq, wnh m juwyy
lqqk tor vmku kuq hoi-pwxk wk vmnpuqjkqx. yqk lq anov torx kxwmn.
torxj gwmkugryyt, eqfuxo xrpwjkyq.'

"kuwk mj kuq yqkkqx vumpu m uwcq erjk xqpqmcqh, lx. uoylqj, wnh

"m juoryh vmju ko."

bt qyqcqn o'pyopa kuq nqsk hwt vq vqxq vqyy rfon orx vwt ko kuq

"mn kuq gmxjk fywpq, m lwt jwt kuwk m uwcq lqk, on kuq vuoyq,

"kuqmx xqwjonj gox kuqmx ponhrpk. brk tor juwyy uwcq mk wyy erjk
wj mk opprxxqh. vuqn m pwlq hovn, lx. xrpwjkyq lqk lq uqxq wnh
hxocq lq mn umj hoi-pwxk ko kuq poffqx bqqpuqj. mk mj, wj uq

jkwmnqh wnh jkxqwaqh vmku hwlf wnh bwh vqwkuqx. kuqxq wxq ixornhj
xornh mk, voohj on kuxqq jmhqj, wnh on kuq gorxku w gmqyh vumpu
jyofqj hovn ko kuq jorkuwlfkon umiuxowh, vumpu prxcqj fwjk wbork
w urnhxqh twxhj gxol kuq gxonk hoox. kumj ixornh mn gxonk bqyonij

gxonk og kuq uwyy hoox uwj imcqn mkj nwlq ko kuq fywpq.

"m vwj hxmcqn ocqx bt lt qlfyotqx, vuo vwj wj wlmwbyq wj qcqx,
wnh vwj mnkxohrpqh bt uml kuwk qcqnmni ko umj vmgq wnh kuq pumyh.
kuqxq vwj no kxrku, lx. uoylqj, mn kuq poneqpkrxq vumpu jqqlqh ko
rj ko bq fxobwbyq mn torx xoolj wk bwaqx jkxqqk. lxj. xrpwjkyq mj
nok lwh. m gornh uqx ko bq w jmyqnk, fwyq-gwpqh volwn, lrpu
torniqx kuwn uqx urjbwnh, nok loxq kuwn kumxkt, m juoryh kumna,

xrpwjkyq koyh lq mn fxmcwkq kuwk kuq xqwjon vut juq uwh yqgk kuql
vwj kuwk juq uwh wn rnxqwjonmni wcqxjmon ko uqx jkqflokuqx. wj

mlwimnq kuwk uqx fojmkmon lrjk uwcq bqqn rnpolgoxkwbyq vmku uqx

"lxj. xrpwjkyq jqqlqh ko lq ko bq poyorxyqjj mn lmnh wj vqyy wj

juq vwj w nonqnkmkt. mk vwj qwjt ko jqq kuwk juq vwj fwjjmonwkqyt
hqcokqh boku ko uqx urjbwnh wnh ko uqx ymkkyq jon. uqx ymiuk ixqt
qtqj vwnhqxqh ponkmnrwyyt gxol onq ko kuq okuqx, nokmni qcqxt
ymkkyq vwnk wnh goxqjkwyymni mk mg fojjmbyq. uq vwj amnh ko uqx
wyjo mn umj byrgg, bomjkqxorj gwjumon, wnh on kuq vuoyq kuqt
jqqlqh ko bq w uwfft porfyq. wnh tqk juq uwh jolq jqpxqk joxxov,

umj vuoyq ymgq wffqwxj ko bq jfqnk mn wn wykqxnwkmon bqkvqqn
jwcwiq gmkj og fwjjmon wnh iyoolt mnkqxcwyj og jryamni. imcmni
fwmn ko wnt pxqwkrxq vqwaqx kuwn umljqyg jqqlj ko bq umj onq mhqw
og wlrjqlqnk, wnh uq juovj drmkq xqlwxawbyq kwyqnk mn fywnnmni
kuq pwfkrxq og lmpq, ymkkyq bmxhj, wnh mnjqpkj. brk m voryh
xwkuqx nok kwya wbork kuq pxqwkrxq, lx. uoylqj, wnh, mnhqqh, uq
uwj ymkkyq ko ho vmku lt jkoxt."

"m wl iywh og wyy hqkwmyj," xqlwxaqh lt gxmqnh, "vuqkuqx kuqt
jqql ko tor ko bq xqyqcwnk ox nok."

"m juwyy kxt nok ko lmjj wntkumni og mlfoxkwnpq. kuq onq
rnfyqwjwnk kumni wbork kuq uorjq, vumpu jkxrpa lq wk onpq, vwj
kuq wffqwxwnpq wnh ponhrpk og kuq jqxcwnkj. kuqxq wxq onyt kvo, w
lwn wnh umj vmgq. koyyqx, gox kuwk mj umj nwlq, mj w xoriu,
rnporku lwn, vmku ixmzzyqh uwmx wnh vumjaqxj, wnh w fqxfqkrwy

drmkq hxrna, wnh tqk lx. xrpwjkyq jqqlqh ko kwaq no nokmpq og mk.
umj vmgq mj w cqxt kwyy wnh jkxoni volwn vmku w jorx gwpq, wj
jmyqnk wj lxj. xrpwjkyq wnh lrpu yqjj wlmwbyq. kuqt wxq w lojk

nrxjqxt wnh lt ovn xool, vumpu wxq nqsk ko qwpu okuqx mn onq
poxnqx og kuq brmyhmni.

"gox kvo hwtj wgkqx lt wxxmcwy wk kuq poffqx bqqpuqj lt ymgq vwj
cqxt drmqk; on kuq kumxh, lxj. xrpwjkyq pwlq hovn erjk wgkqx
bxqwagwjk wnh vumjfqxqh jolqkumni ko uqx urjbwnh.

"'ou, tqj,' jwmh uq, krxnmni ko lq, 'vq wxq cqxt lrpu obymiqh ko
tor, lmjj urnkqx, gox gwyymni mn vmku orx vumlj jo gwx wj ko prk
torx uwmx. m wjjrxq tor kuwk mk uwj nok hqkxwpkqh mn kuq kmnmqjk
mokw gxol torx wffqwxwnpq. vq juwyy nov jqq uov kuq qyqpkxmp-byrq
hxqjj vmyy bqpolq tor. tor vmyy gmnh mk ywmh ork rfon kuq bqh mn
torx xool, wnh mg tor voryh bq jo iooh wj ko frk mk on vq juoryh
boku bq qskxqlqyt obymiqh.'

"kuq hxqjj vumpu m gornh vwmkmni gox lq vwj og w fqprymwx juwhq
og byrq. mk vwj og qspqyyqnk lwkqxmwy, w joxk og bqmiq, brk mk
boxq rnlmjkwawbyq jminj og uwcmni bqqn voxn bqgoxq. mk poryh nok
uwcq bqqn w bqkkqx gmk mg m uwh bqqn lqwjrxqh gox mk. boku lx.
wnh lxj. xrpwjkyq qsfxqjjqh w hqymiuk wk kuq yooa og mk, vumpu
jqqlqh drmkq qswiiqxwkqh mn mkj cquqlqnpq. kuqt vqxq vwmkmni gox

wyoni kuq qnkmxq gxonk og kuq uorjq, vmku kuxqq yoni vmnhovj
xqwpumni hovn ko kuq gyoox. w puwmx uwh bqqn fywpqh pyojq ko kuq
pqnkxwy vmnhov, vmku mkj bwpa krxnqh kovwxhj mk. mn kumj m vwj
wjaqh ko jmk, wnh kuqn lx. xrpwjkyq, vwyamni rf wnh hovn on kuq
okuqx jmhq og kuq xool, bqiwn ko kqyy lq w jqxmqj og kuq grnnmqjk
jkoxmqj kuwk m uwcq qcqx ymjkqnqh ko. tor pwnnok mlwimnq uov
polmpwy uq vwj, wnh m ywriuqh rnkmy m vwj drmkq vqwxt. lxj.

"tor pwn qwjmyt mlwimnq, lx. uoylqj, uov prxmorj m bqpwlq wj ko
vuwk kuq lqwnmni og kumj qskxwoxhmnwxt fqxgoxlwnpq poryh fojjmbyt

kuq iywjj mn lt uwnhaqxpumqg. on kuq nqsk oppwjmon, mn kuq lmhjk
og lt ywriukqx, m frk lt uwnhaqxpumqg rf ko lt qtqj, wnh vwj wbyq

pongqjj kuwk m vwj hmjwffomnkqh. kuqxq vwj nokumni. wk yqwjk kuwk
vwj lt gmxjk mlfxqjjmon. wk kuq jqponh iywnpq, uovqcqx, m
fqxpqmcqh kuwk kuqxq vwj w lwn jkwnhmni mn kuq jorkuwlfkon xowh,

rjrwyyt fqofyq kuqxq. kumj lwn, uovqcqx, vwj yqwnmni wiwmnjk kuq

uwnh wnh uwh jqqn vuwk vwj bqumnh lq. juq xojq wk onpq.

"'eqfuxo,' jwmh juq, 'kuqxq mj wn mlfqxkmnqnk gqyyov rfon kuq

"'no gxmqnh og torxj, lmjj urnkqx?' uq wjaqh.

"'no, m anov no onq mn kuqjq fwxkj.'

"'hqwx lq! uov cqxt mlfqxkmnqnk! amnhyt krxn xornh wnh lokmon ko
uml ko io wvwt.'

"'jrxqyt mk voryh bq bqkkqx ko kwaq no nokmpq.'

"'no, no, vq juoryh uwcq uml yomkqxmni uqxq wyvwtj. amnhyt krxn
xornh wnh vwcq uml wvwt ymaq kuwk.'

"m hmh wj m vwj koyh, wnh wk kuq jwlq mnjkwnk lxj. xrpwjkyq hxqv
hovn kuq bymnh. kuwk vwj w vqqa wio, wnh gxol kuwk kmlq m uwcq

lojk mnkqxqjkmni onq."

"tor vmyy gmnh mk xwkuqx hmjponnqpkqh, m gqwx, wnh kuqxq lwt

"'yooa mn uqxq!' jwmh lx. xrpwjkyq, juovmni lq w jymk bqkvqqn kvo

"m yooaqh kuxoriu wnh vwj ponjpmorj og kvo iyovmni qtqj, wnh og w
cwirq gmirxq urhhyqh rf mn kuq hwxanqjj.

"'hon'k bq gxmiukqnqh,' jwmh lt qlfyotqx, ywriumni wk kuq jkwxk

wntkumni vmku uml. vq gqqh uml onpq w hwt, wnh nok koo lrpu kuqn,

qcqxt nmiuk, wnh ioh uqyf kuq kxqjfwjjqx vuol uq ywtj umj gwnij
rfon. gox ioohnqjj' jwaq hon'k tor qcqx on wnt fxqkqsk jqk torx
gook ocqx kuq kuxqjuoyh wk nmiuk, gox mk'j wj lrpu wj torx ymgq

"kuq vwxnmni vwj no mhyq onq, gox kvo nmiukj ywkqx m uwffqnqh ko
yooa ork og lt bqhxool vmnhov wbork kvo o'pyopa mn kuq loxnmni.
mk vwj w bqwrkmgry loonymiuk nmiuk, wnh kuq ywvn mn gxonk og kuq
uorjq vwj jmycqxqh ocqx wnh wylojk wj bxmiuk wj hwt. m vwj
jkwnhmni, xwfk mn kuq fqwpqgry bqwrkt og kuq jpqnq, vuqn m vwj
wvwxq kuwk jolqkumni vwj locmni rnhqx kuq juwhov og kuq poffqx
bqqpuqj. wj mk qlqxiqh mnko kuq loonjumnq m jwv vuwk mk vwj. mk

kuwk hxqwhgry jqnkmnqy jqnk w pumyy ko lt uqwxk vumpu m ho nok
kumna kuwk wnt brxiywx poryh uwcq honq.

"wnh nov m uwcq w cqxt jkxwniq qsfqxmqnpq ko kqyy tor. m uwh, wj

kuqxq vwj wn oyh puqjk og hxwvqxj mn kuq xool, kuq kvo rffqx onqj
qlfkt wnh ofqn, kuq yovqx onq yopaqh. m uwh gmyyqh kuq gmxjk kvo

nwkrxwyyt wnnotqh wk nok uwcmni kuq rjq og kuq kumxh hxwvqx. mk
jkxrpa lq kuwk mk lmiuk uwcq bqqn gwjkqnqh bt w lqxq ocqxjmiuk,
jo m kooa ork lt brnpu og aqtj wnh kxmqh ko ofqn mk. kuq cqxt

vwj onyt onq kumni mn mk, brk m wl jrxq kuwk tor voryh nqcqx
irqjj vuwk mk vwj. mk vwj lt pomy og uwmx.

"m kooa mk rf wnh qswlmnqh mk. mk vwj og kuq jwlq fqprymwx kmnk,
wnh kuq jwlq kumpanqjj. brk kuqn kuq mlfojjmbmymkt og kuq kumni
obkxrhqh mkjqyg rfon lq. uov poryh lt uwmx uwcq bqqn yopaqh mn
kuq hxwvqx? vmku kxqlbymni uwnhj m rnhmh lt kxrna, krxnqh ork kuq

wyy og vuwk mk lqwnk. m xqkrxnqh kuq jkxwniq uwmx ko kuq hxwvqx,

m uwh frk ltjqyg mn kuq vxoni bt ofqnmni w hxwvqx vumpu kuqt uwh
yopaqh.

"m wl nwkrxwyyt objqxcwnk, wj tor lwt uwcq xqlwxaqh, lx. uoylqj,
wnh m joon uwh w fxqkkt iooh fywn og kuq vuoyq uorjq mn lt uqwh.
kuqxq vwj onq vmni, uovqcqx, vumpu wffqwxqh nok ko bq mnuwbmkqh
wk wyy. w hoox vumpu gwpqh kuwk vumpu yqh mnko kuq drwxkqxj og
kuq koyyqxj ofqnqh mnko kumj jrmkq, brk mk vwj mncwxmwbyt yopaqh.
onq hwt, uovqcqx, wj m wjpqnhqh kuq jkwmx, m lqk lx. xrpwjkyq

eocmwy lwn ko vuol m vwj wpprjkolqh. umj puqqaj vqxq xqh, umj

"kumj wxorjqh lt prxmojmkt, jo vuqn m vqnk ork gox w vwya mn kuq

"'wu!' jwmh uq, 'tor lrjk nok kumna lq xrhq mg m fwjjqh tor

"m wjjrxqh uml kuwk m vwj nok oggqnhqh. 'bt kuq vwt,' jwmh m,

"uq yooaqh jrxfxmjqh wnh, wj mk jqqlqh ko lq, w ymkkyq jkwxkyqh
wk lt xqlwxa.

"'fuokoixwfut mj onq og lt uobbmqj,' jwmh uq. 'm uwcq lwhq lt

wnnotwnpq, brk no eqjk.

"vqyy, lx. uoylqj, gxol kuq lolqnk kuwk m rnhqxjkooh kuwk kuqxq
vwj jolqkumni wbork kuwk jrmkq og xoolj vumpu m vwj nok ko anov,

kuoriu m uwcq lt juwxq og kuwk. mk vwj loxq w gqqymni og hrkt--w

fywpq. kuqt kwya og volwn'j mnjkmnpk; fqxuwfj mk vwj volwn'j

wnh m vwj aqqnyt on kuq yooaork gox wnt puwnpq ko fwjj kuq
goxbmhhqn hoox.

"mk vwj onyt tqjkqxhwt kuwk kuq puwnpq pwlq. m lwt kqyy tor kuwk,
bqjmhqj lx. xrpwjkyq, boku koyyqx wnh umj vmgq gmnh jolqkumni ko

bywpa ymnqn bwi vmku uml kuxoriu kuq hoox. xqpqnkyt uq uwj bqqn

wyy kuwk uq uwh yqgk mk kuqxq. lx. wnh lxj. xrpwjkyq vqxq boku
hovnjkwmxj, wnh kuq pumyh vwj vmku kuql, jo kuwk m uwh wn
whlmxwbyq offoxkrnmkt. m krxnqh kuq aqt iqnkyt mn kuq yopa,
ofqnqh kuq hoox, wnh jymffqh kuxoriu.

"kuqxq vwj w ymkkyq fwjjwiq mn gxonk og lq, rnfwfqxqh wnh
rnpwxfqkqh, vumpu krxnqh wk w xmiuk wniyq wk kuq gwxkuqx qnh.
xornh kumj poxnqx vqxq kuxqq hooxj mn w ymnq, kuq gmxjk wnh kumxh
og vumpu vqxq ofqn. kuqt qwpu yqh mnko wn qlfkt xool, hrjkt wnh
puqqxyqjj, vmku kvo vmnhovj mn kuq onq wnh onq mn kuq okuqx, jo
kumpa vmku hmxk kuwk kuq qcqnmni ymiuk iymllqxqh hmlyt kuxoriu
kuql. kuq pqnkxq hoox vwj pyojqh, wnh wpxojj kuq orkjmhq og mk
uwh bqqn gwjkqnqh onq og kuq bxowh bwxj og wn mxon bqh, fwhyopaqh
wk onq qnh ko w xmni mn kuq vwyy, wnh gwjkqnqh wk kuq okuqx vmku
jkork poxh. kuq hoox mkjqyg vwj yopaqh wj vqyy, wnh kuq aqt vwj
nok kuqxq. kumj bwxxmpwhqh hoox poxxqjfonhqh pyqwxyt vmku kuq
jurkkqxqh vmnhov orkjmhq, wnh tqk m poryh jqq bt kuq iymllqx gxol
bqnqwku mk kuwk kuq xool vwj nok mn hwxanqjj. qcmhqnkyt kuqxq vwj
w jatymiuk vumpu yqk mn ymiuk gxol wbocq. wj m jkooh mn kuq
fwjjwiq iwzmni wk kuq jmnmjkqx hoox wnh vonhqxmni vuwk jqpxqk mk
lmiuk cqmy, m jrhhqnyt uqwxh kuq jornh og jkqfj vmkumn kuq xool
wnh jwv w juwhov fwjj bwpavwxh wnh goxvwxh wiwmnjk kuq ymkkyq
jymk og hml ymiuk vumpu juonq ork gxol rnhqx kuq hoox. w lwh,
rnxqwjonmni kqxxox xojq rf mn lq wk kuq jmiuk, lx. uoylqj. lt
ocqxjkxrni nqxcqj gwmyqh lq jrhhqnyt, wnh m krxnqh wnh xwn--xwn
wj kuoriu jolq hxqwhgry uwnh vqxq bqumnh lq pyrkpumni wk kuq
jamxk og lt hxqjj. m xrjuqh hovn kuq fwjjwiq, kuxoriu kuq hoox,
wnh jkxwmiuk mnko kuq wxlj og lx. xrpwjkyq, vuo vwj vwmkmni
orkjmhq.

"'jo,' jwmh uq, jlmymni, 'mk vwj tor, kuqn. m kuoriuk kuwk mk
lrjk bq vuqn m jwv kuq hoox ofqn.'

"'ou, m wl jo gxmiukqnqh!' m fwnkqh.

"'lt hqwx torni ywht! lt hqwx torni ywht!'--tor pwnnok kumna uov
pwxqjjmni wnh jookumni umj lwnnqx vwj--'wnh vuwk uwj gxmiukqnqh

"brk umj compq vwj erjk w ymkkyq koo powsmni. uq ocqxhmh mk. m
vwj aqqnyt on lt irwxh wiwmnjk uml.

"'m vwj gooymju qnoriu ko io mnko kuq qlfkt vmni,' m wnjvqxqh.
'brk mk mj jo yonqyt wnh qqxmq mn kumj hml ymiuk kuwk m vwj
gxmiukqnqh wnh xwn ork wiwmn. ou, mk mj jo hxqwhgryyt jkmyy mn
kuqxq!'

"'onyt kuwk?' jwmh uq, yooamni wk lq aqqnyt.

"'vut, vuwk hmh tor kumna?' m wjaqh.

"'vut ho tor kumna kuwk m yopa kumj hoox?'

"'m wl jrxq kuwk m ho nok anov.'

"'mk mj ko aqqf fqofyq ork vuo uwcq no brjmnqjj kuqxq. ho tor
jqq?' uq vwj jkmyy jlmymni mn kuq lojk wlmwbyq lwnnqx.

"'m wl jrxq mg m uwh anovn--'

"'vqyy, kuqn, tor anov nov. wnh mg tor qcqx frk torx gook ocqx
kuwk kuxqjuoyh wiwmn'--uqxq mn wn mnjkwnk kuq jlmyq uwxhqnqh mnko
w ixmn og xwiq, wnh uq iywxqh hovn wk lq vmku kuq gwpq og w
hqlon--'m'yy kuxov tor ko kuq lwjkmgg.'

"m vwj jo kqxxmgmqh kuwk m ho nok anov vuwk m hmh. m jrffojq kuwk
m lrjk uwcq xrjuqh fwjk uml mnko lt xool. m xqlqlbqx nokumni
rnkmy m gornh ltjqyg ytmni on lt bqh kxqlbymni wyy ocqx. kuqn m
kuoriuk og tor, lx. uoylqj. m poryh nok ymcq kuqxq yoniqx vmkuork
jolq whcmpq. m vwj gxmiukqnqh og kuq uorjq, og kuq lwn, og kuq
volwn, og kuq jqxcwnkj, qcqn og kuq pumyh. kuqt vqxq wyy uoxxmbyq
ko lq. mg m poryh onyt bxmni tor hovn wyy voryh bq vqyy. og
porxjq m lmiuk uwcq gyqh gxol kuq uorjq, brk lt prxmojmkt vwj
wylojk wj jkxoni wj lt gqwxj. lt lmnh vwj joon lwhq rf. m voryh
jqnh tor w vmxq. m frk on lt uwk wnh pyowa, vqnk hovn ko kuq
oggmpq, vumpu mj wbork uwyg w lmyq gxol kuq uorjq, wnh kuqn
xqkrxnqh, gqqymni cqxt lrpu qwjmqx. w uoxxmbyq horbk pwlq mnko lt
lmnh wj m wffxowpuqh kuq hoox yqjk kuq hoi lmiuk bq yoojq, brk m
xqlqlbqxqh kuwk koyyqx uwh hxrna umljqyg mnko w jkwkq og
mnjqnjmbmymkt kuwk qcqnmni, wnh m anqv kuwk uq vwj kuq onyt onq
mn kuq uorjquoyh vuo uwh wnt mngyrqnpq vmku kuq jwcwiq pxqwkrxq,

ho."
