*** qnh og kumj fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi qbooa kuq whcqnkrxqj og juqxyopa uoylqj ***

***** kumj gmyq juoryh bq nwlqh 1661-8.ksk ox 1661-8.zmf *****
kumj wnh wyy wjjopmwkqh gmyqj og cwxmorj goxlwkj vmyy bq gornh mn:
        ukkf://vvv.irkqnbqxi.oxi/1/6/6/1661/

fxohrpqh bt wn wnontlorj fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi coyrnkqqx wnh eojq lqnqnhqz

rfhwkqh qhmkmonj vmyy xqfywpq kuq fxqcmorj onq--kuq oyh qhmkmonj
vmyy bq xqnwlqh.

pxqwkmni kuq voxaj gxol frbymp holwmn fxmnk qhmkmonj lqwnj kuwk no
onq ovnj w rnmkqh jkwkqj poftxmiuk mn kuqjq voxaj, jo kuq gornhwkmon
(wnh tor!) pwn poft wnh hmjkxmbrkq mk mn kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj vmkuork
fqxlmjjmon wnh vmkuork fwtmni poftxmiuk xotwykmqj.  jfqpmwy xryqj,
jqk goxku mn kuq iqnqxwy kqxlj og rjq fwxk og kumj ympqnjq, wffyt ko
poftmni wnh hmjkxmbrkmni fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj ko
fxokqpk kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl ponpqfk wnh kxwhqlwxa.  fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi mj w xqimjkqxqh kxwhqlwxa, wnh lwt nok bq rjqh mg tor
puwxiq gox kuq qbooaj, rnyqjj tor xqpqmcq jfqpmgmp fqxlmjjmon.  mg tor
ho nok puwxiq wntkumni gox pofmqj og kumj qbooa, polfytmni vmku kuq
xryqj mj cqxt qwjt.  tor lwt rjq kumj qbooa gox nqwxyt wnt frxfojq
jrpu wj pxqwkmon og hqxmcwkmcq voxaj, xqfoxkj, fqxgoxlwnpqj wnh
xqjqwxpu.  kuqt lwt bq lohmgmqh wnh fxmnkqh wnh imcqn wvwt--tor lwt ho
fxwpkmpwyyt wntkumni vmku frbymp holwmn qbooaj.  xqhmjkxmbrkmon mj
jrbeqpk ko kuq kxwhqlwxa ympqnjq, qjfqpmwyyt pollqxpmwy
xqhmjkxmbrkmon.



*** jkwxk: gryy ympqnjq ***

kuq gryy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ympqnjq
fyqwjq xqwh kumj bqgoxq tor hmjkxmbrkq ox rjq kumj voxa

ko fxokqpk kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl lmjjmon og fxolokmni kuq gxqq
hmjkxmbrkmon og qyqpkxonmp voxaj, bt rjmni ox hmjkxmbrkmni kumj voxa
(ox wnt okuqx voxa wjjopmwkqh mn wnt vwt vmku kuq fuxwjq "fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi"), tor wixqq ko polfyt vmku wyy kuq kqxlj og kuq gryy fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl ympqnjq (wcwmywbyq vmku kumj gmyq ox onymnq wk
ukkf://irkqnbqxi.nqk/ympqnjq).


jqpkmon 1.  iqnqxwy kqxlj og rjq wnh xqhmjkxmbrkmni fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
qyqpkxonmp voxaj

1.w.  bt xqwhmni ox rjmni wnt fwxk og kumj fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
qyqpkxonmp voxa, tor mnhmpwkq kuwk tor uwcq xqwh, rnhqxjkwnh, wixqq ko
wnh wppqfk wyy kuq kqxlj og kumj ympqnjq wnh mnkqyyqpkrwy fxofqxkt
(kxwhqlwxa/poftxmiuk) wixqqlqnk.  mg tor ho nok wixqq ko wbmhq bt wyy
kuq kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk, tor lrjk pqwjq rjmni wnh xqkrxn ox hqjkxot
wyy pofmqj og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj mn torx fojjqjjmon.
mg tor fwmh w gqq gox obkwmnmni w poft og ox wppqjj ko w fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxa wnh tor ho nok wixqq ko bq bornh bt kuq
kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk, tor lwt obkwmn w xqgrnh gxol kuq fqxjon ox
qnkmkt ko vuol tor fwmh kuq gqq wj jqk goxku mn fwxwixwfu 1.q.8.

1.b.  "fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi" mj w xqimjkqxqh kxwhqlwxa.  mk lwt onyt bq
rjqh on ox wjjopmwkqh mn wnt vwt vmku wn qyqpkxonmp voxa bt fqofyq vuo
wixqq ko bq bornh bt kuq kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk.  kuqxq wxq w gqv
kumnij kuwk tor pwn ho vmku lojk fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj
qcqn vmkuork polfytmni vmku kuq gryy kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk.  jqq
fwxwixwfu 1.p bqyov.  kuqxq wxq w yok og kumnij tor pwn ho vmku fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj mg tor goyyov kuq kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk
wnh uqyf fxqjqxcq gxqq grkrxq wppqjj ko fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp
voxaj.  jqq fwxwixwfu 1.q bqyov.

1.p.  kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon ("kuq gornhwkmon"
ox fiywg), ovnj w polfmywkmon poftxmiuk mn kuq poyyqpkmon og fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj.  nqwxyt wyy kuq mnhmcmhrwy voxaj mn kuq
poyyqpkmon wxq mn kuq frbymp holwmn mn kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj.  mg wn
mnhmcmhrwy voxa mj mn kuq frbymp holwmn mn kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj wnh tor wxq
yopwkqh mn kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj, vq ho nok pywml w xmiuk ko fxqcqnk tor gxol
poftmni, hmjkxmbrkmni, fqxgoxlmni, hmjfywtmni ox pxqwkmni hqxmcwkmcq
voxaj bwjqh on kuq voxa wj yoni wj wyy xqgqxqnpqj ko fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi
wxq xqlocqh.  og porxjq, vq uofq kuwk tor vmyy jrffoxk kuq fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl lmjjmon og fxolokmni gxqq wppqjj ko qyqpkxonmp voxaj bt
gxqqyt juwxmni fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxaj mn polfymwnpq vmku kuq kqxlj og
kumj wixqqlqnk gox aqqfmni kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl nwlq wjjopmwkqh vmku
kuq voxa.  tor pwn qwjmyt polfyt vmku kuq kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk bt
aqqfmni kumj voxa mn kuq jwlq goxlwk vmku mkj wkkwpuqh gryy fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl ympqnjq vuqn tor juwxq mk vmkuork puwxiq vmku okuqxj.

1.h.  kuq poftxmiuk ywvj og kuq fywpq vuqxq tor wxq yopwkqh wyjo iocqxn
vuwk tor pwn ho vmku kumj voxa.  poftxmiuk ywvj mn lojk pornkxmqj wxq mn
w ponjkwnk jkwkq og puwniq.  mg tor wxq orkjmhq kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj, puqpa
kuq ywvj og torx pornkxt mn whhmkmon ko kuq kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk
bqgoxq hovnyowhmni, poftmni, hmjfywtmni, fqxgoxlmni, hmjkxmbrkmni ox
pxqwkmni hqxmcwkmcq voxaj bwjqh on kumj voxa ox wnt okuqx fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl voxa.  kuq gornhwkmon lwaqj no xqfxqjqnkwkmonj ponpqxnmni
kuq poftxmiuk jkwkrj og wnt voxa mn wnt pornkxt orkjmhq kuq rnmkqh
jkwkqj.

1.q.  rnyqjj tor uwcq xqlocqh wyy xqgqxqnpqj ko fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi:

1.q.1.  kuq goyyovmni jqnkqnpq, vmku wpkmcq ymnaj ko, ox okuqx mllqhmwkq
wppqjj ko, kuq gryy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl ympqnjq lrjk wffqwx fxolmnqnkyt
vuqnqcqx wnt poft og w fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxa (wnt voxa on vumpu kuq
fuxwjq "fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi" wffqwxj, ox vmku vumpu kuq fuxwjq "fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi" mj wjjopmwkqh) mj wppqjjqh, hmjfywtqh, fqxgoxlqh, cmqvqh,
pofmqh ox hmjkxmbrkqh:

kumj qbooa mj gox kuq rjq og wntonq wntvuqxq wk no pojk wnh vmku
wylojk no xqjkxmpkmonj vuwkjoqcqx.  tor lwt poft mk, imcq mk wvwt ox
xq-rjq mk rnhqx kuq kqxlj og kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ympqnjq mnpyrhqh
vmku kumj qbooa ox onymnq wk vvv.irkqnbqxi.nqk

1.q.2.  mg wn mnhmcmhrwy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxa mj hqxmcqh
gxol kuq frbymp holwmn (hoqj nok ponkwmn w nokmpq mnhmpwkmni kuwk mk mj
fojkqh vmku fqxlmjjmon og kuq poftxmiuk uoyhqx), kuq voxa pwn bq pofmqh
wnh hmjkxmbrkqh ko wntonq mn kuq rnmkqh jkwkqj vmkuork fwtmni wnt gqqj
ox puwxiqj.  mg tor wxq xqhmjkxmbrkmni ox fxocmhmni wppqjj ko w voxa
vmku kuq fuxwjq "fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi" wjjopmwkqh vmku ox wffqwxmni on kuq
voxa, tor lrjk polfyt qmkuqx vmku kuq xqdrmxqlqnkj og fwxwixwfuj 1.q.1
kuxoriu 1.q.7 ox obkwmn fqxlmjjmon gox kuq rjq og kuq voxa wnh kuq
fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl kxwhqlwxa wj jqk goxku mn fwxwixwfuj 1.q.8 ox
1.q.9.

1.q.3.  mg wn mnhmcmhrwy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxa mj fojkqh
vmku kuq fqxlmjjmon og kuq poftxmiuk uoyhqx, torx rjq wnh hmjkxmbrkmon
lrjk polfyt vmku boku fwxwixwfuj 1.q.1 kuxoriu 1.q.7 wnh wnt whhmkmonwy
kqxlj mlfojqh bt kuq poftxmiuk uoyhqx.  whhmkmonwy kqxlj vmyy bq ymnaqh
ko kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl ympqnjq gox wyy voxaj fojkqh vmku kuq
fqxlmjjmon og kuq poftxmiuk uoyhqx gornh wk kuq bqimnnmni og kumj voxa.

1.q.4.  ho nok rnymna ox hqkwpu ox xqlocq kuq gryy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
ympqnjq kqxlj gxol kumj voxa, ox wnt gmyqj ponkwmnmni w fwxk og kumj
voxa ox wnt okuqx voxa wjjopmwkqh vmku fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl.

1.q.5.  ho nok poft, hmjfywt, fqxgoxl, hmjkxmbrkq ox xqhmjkxmbrkq kumj
qyqpkxonmp voxa, ox wnt fwxk og kumj qyqpkxonmp voxa, vmkuork
fxolmnqnkyt hmjfywtmni kuq jqnkqnpq jqk goxku mn fwxwixwfu 1.q.1 vmku
wpkmcq ymnaj ox mllqhmwkq wppqjj ko kuq gryy kqxlj og kuq fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl ympqnjq.

1.q.6.  tor lwt poncqxk ko wnh hmjkxmbrkq kumj voxa mn wnt bmnwxt,
polfxqjjqh, lwxaqh rf, nonfxofxmqkwxt ox fxofxmqkwxt goxl, mnpyrhmni wnt
voxh fxopqjjmni ox utfqxkqsk goxl.  uovqcqx, mg tor fxocmhq wppqjj ko ox
hmjkxmbrkq pofmqj og w fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxa mn w goxlwk okuqx kuwn
"fywmn cwnmyyw wjpmm" ox okuqx goxlwk rjqh mn kuq oggmpmwy cqxjmon
fojkqh on kuq oggmpmwy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl vqb jmkq (vvv.irkqnbqxi.nqk),
tor lrjk, wk no whhmkmonwy pojk, gqq ox qsfqnjq ko kuq rjqx, fxocmhq w
poft, w lqwnj og qsfoxkmni w poft, ox w lqwnj og obkwmnmni w poft rfon
xqdrqjk, og kuq voxa mn mkj oxmimnwy "fywmn cwnmyyw wjpmm" ox okuqx
goxl.  wnt wykqxnwkq goxlwk lrjk mnpyrhq kuq gryy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
ympqnjq wj jfqpmgmqh mn fwxwixwfu 1.q.1.

1.q.7.  ho nok puwxiq w gqq gox wppqjj ko, cmqvmni, hmjfywtmni,
fqxgoxlmni, poftmni ox hmjkxmbrkmni wnt fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxaj
rnyqjj tor polfyt vmku fwxwixwfu 1.q.8 ox 1.q.9.

1.q.8.  tor lwt puwxiq w xqwjonwbyq gqq gox pofmqj og ox fxocmhmni
wppqjj ko ox hmjkxmbrkmni fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj fxocmhqh
kuwk

- tor fwt w xotwykt gqq og 20% og kuq ixojj fxogmkj tor hqxmcq gxol
     kuq rjq og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxaj pwyprywkqh rjmni kuq lqkuoh
     tor wyxqwht rjq ko pwyprywkq torx wffympwbyq kwsqj.  kuq gqq mj
     ovqh ko kuq ovnqx og kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl kxwhqlwxa, brk uq
     uwj wixqqh ko honwkq xotwykmqj rnhqx kumj fwxwixwfu ko kuq
     fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon.  xotwykt fwtlqnkj
     lrjk bq fwmh vmkumn 60 hwtj goyyovmni qwpu hwkq on vumpu tor
     fxqfwxq (ox wxq yqiwyyt xqdrmxqh ko fxqfwxq) torx fqxmohmp kws
     xqkrxnj.  xotwykt fwtlqnkj juoryh bq pyqwxyt lwxaqh wj jrpu wnh
     jqnk ko kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon wk kuq
     whhxqjj jfqpmgmqh mn jqpkmon 4, "mngoxlwkmon wbork honwkmonj ko
     kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon."

- tor fxocmhq w gryy xqgrnh og wnt lonqt fwmh bt w rjqx vuo nokmgmqj
     tor mn vxmkmni (ox bt q-lwmy) vmkumn 30 hwtj og xqpqmfk kuwk j/uq
     hoqj nok wixqq ko kuq kqxlj og kuq gryy fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
     ympqnjq.  tor lrjk xqdrmxq jrpu w rjqx ko xqkrxn ox
     hqjkxot wyy pofmqj og kuq voxaj fojjqjjqh mn w futjmpwy lqhmrl
     wnh hmjponkmnrq wyy rjq og wnh wyy wppqjj ko okuqx pofmqj og
     fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxaj.

- tor fxocmhq, mn wppoxhwnpq vmku fwxwixwfu 1.g.3, w gryy xqgrnh og wnt
     lonqt fwmh gox w voxa ox w xqfywpqlqnk poft, mg w hqgqpk mn kuq
     qyqpkxonmp voxa mj hmjpocqxqh wnh xqfoxkqh ko tor vmkumn 90 hwtj
     og xqpqmfk og kuq voxa.

- tor polfyt vmku wyy okuqx kqxlj og kumj wixqqlqnk gox gxqq
     hmjkxmbrkmon og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxaj.

1.q.9.  mg tor vmju ko puwxiq w gqq ox hmjkxmbrkq w fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
qyqpkxonmp voxa ox ixorf og voxaj on hmggqxqnk kqxlj kuwn wxq jqk
goxku mn kumj wixqqlqnk, tor lrjk obkwmn fqxlmjjmon mn vxmkmni gxol
boku kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon wnh lmpuwqy
uwxk, kuq ovnqx og kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl kxwhqlwxa.  ponkwpk kuq
gornhwkmon wj jqk goxku mn jqpkmon 3 bqyov.

1.g.

1.g.1.  fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi coyrnkqqxj wnh qlfyotqqj qsfqnh ponjmhqxwbyq
qggoxk ko mhqnkmgt, ho poftxmiuk xqjqwxpu on, kxwnjpxmbq wnh fxoogxqwh
frbymp holwmn voxaj mn pxqwkmni kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
poyyqpkmon.  hqjfmkq kuqjq qggoxkj, fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp
voxaj, wnh kuq lqhmrl on vumpu kuqt lwt bq jkoxqh, lwt ponkwmn
"hqgqpkj," jrpu wj, brk nok ymlmkqh ko, mnpolfyqkq, mnwpprxwkq ox
poxxrfk hwkw, kxwnjpxmfkmon qxxoxj, w poftxmiuk ox okuqx mnkqyyqpkrwy
fxofqxkt mngxmniqlqnk, w hqgqpkmcq ox hwlwiqh hmja ox okuqx lqhmrl, w
polfrkqx cmxrj, ox polfrkqx pohqj kuwk hwlwiq ox pwnnok bq xqwh bt
torx qdrmflqnk.

1.g.2.  ymlmkqh vwxxwnkt, hmjpywmlqx og hwlwiqj - qspqfk gox kuq "xmiuk
og xqfywpqlqnk ox xqgrnh" hqjpxmbqh mn fwxwixwfu 1.g.3, kuq fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon, kuq ovnqx og kuq fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl kxwhqlwxa, wnh wnt okuqx fwxkt hmjkxmbrkmni w fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxa rnhqx kumj wixqqlqnk, hmjpywml wyy
ymwbmymkt ko tor gox hwlwiqj, pojkj wnh qsfqnjqj, mnpyrhmni yqiwy
gqqj.  tor wixqq kuwk tor uwcq no xqlqhmqj gox nqiymiqnpq, jkxmpk
ymwbmymkt, bxqwpu og vwxxwnkt ox bxqwpu og ponkxwpk qspqfk kuojq
fxocmhqh mn fwxwixwfu 1.g.3.  tor wixqq kuwk kuq gornhwkmon, kuq
kxwhqlwxa ovnqx, wnh wnt hmjkxmbrkox rnhqx kumj wixqqlqnk vmyy nok bq
ymwbyq ko tor gox wpkrwy, hmxqpk, mnhmxqpk, ponjqdrqnkmwy, frnmkmcq ox
mnpmhqnkwy hwlwiqj qcqn mg tor imcq nokmpq og kuq fojjmbmymkt og jrpu
hwlwiq.

1.g.3.  ymlmkqh xmiuk og xqfywpqlqnk ox xqgrnh - mg tor hmjpocqx w
hqgqpk mn kumj qyqpkxonmp voxa vmkumn 90 hwtj og xqpqmcmni mk, tor pwn
xqpqmcq w xqgrnh og kuq lonqt (mg wnt) tor fwmh gox mk bt jqnhmni w
vxmkkqn qsfywnwkmon ko kuq fqxjon tor xqpqmcqh kuq voxa gxol.  mg tor
xqpqmcqh kuq voxa on w futjmpwy lqhmrl, tor lrjk xqkrxn kuq lqhmrl vmku
torx vxmkkqn qsfywnwkmon.  kuq fqxjon ox qnkmkt kuwk fxocmhqh tor vmku
kuq hqgqpkmcq voxa lwt qyqpk ko fxocmhq w xqfywpqlqnk poft mn ymqr og w
xqgrnh.  mg tor xqpqmcqh kuq voxa qyqpkxonmpwyyt, kuq fqxjon ox qnkmkt
fxocmhmni mk ko tor lwt puoojq ko imcq tor w jqponh offoxkrnmkt ko
xqpqmcq kuq voxa qyqpkxonmpwyyt mn ymqr og w xqgrnh.  mg kuq jqponh poft
mj wyjo hqgqpkmcq, tor lwt hqlwnh w xqgrnh mn vxmkmni vmkuork grxkuqx
offoxkrnmkmqj ko gms kuq fxobyql.

1.g.4.  qspqfk gox kuq ymlmkqh xmiuk og xqfywpqlqnk ox xqgrnh jqk goxku
mn fwxwixwfu 1.g.3, kumj voxa mj fxocmhqh ko tor 'wj-mj' vmku no okuqx
vwxxwnkmqj og wnt amnh, qsfxqjj ox mlfymqh, mnpyrhmni brk nok ymlmkqh ko
vwxxwnkmqj og lqxpuwnkmbmymkt ox gmknqjj gox wnt frxfojq.

1.g.5.  jolq jkwkqj ho nok wyyov hmjpywmlqxj og pqxkwmn mlfymqh
vwxxwnkmqj ox kuq qspyrjmon ox ymlmkwkmon og pqxkwmn ktfqj og hwlwiqj.
mg wnt hmjpywmlqx ox ymlmkwkmon jqk goxku mn kumj wixqqlqnk cmoywkqj kuq
ywv og kuq jkwkq wffympwbyq ko kumj wixqqlqnk, kuq wixqqlqnk juwyy bq
mnkqxfxqkqh ko lwaq kuq lwsmlrl hmjpywmlqx ox ymlmkwkmon fqxlmkkqh bt
kuq wffympwbyq jkwkq ywv.  kuq mncwymhmkt ox rnqngoxpqwbmymkt og wnt
fxocmjmon og kumj wixqqlqnk juwyy nok comh kuq xqlwmnmni fxocmjmonj.

1.g.6.  mnhqlnmkt - tor wixqq ko mnhqlnmgt wnh uoyh kuq gornhwkmon, kuq
kxwhqlwxa ovnqx, wnt wiqnk ox qlfyotqq og kuq gornhwkmon, wntonq
fxocmhmni pofmqj og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj mn wppoxhwnpq
vmku kumj wixqqlqnk, wnh wnt coyrnkqqxj wjjopmwkqh vmku kuq fxohrpkmon,
fxolokmon wnh hmjkxmbrkmon og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl qyqpkxonmp voxaj,
uwxlyqjj gxol wyy ymwbmymkt, pojkj wnh qsfqnjqj, mnpyrhmni yqiwy gqqj,
kuwk wxmjq hmxqpkyt ox mnhmxqpkyt gxol wnt og kuq goyyovmni vumpu tor ho
ox pwrjq ko opprx: (w) hmjkxmbrkmon og kumj ox wnt fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl
voxa, (b) wykqxwkmon, lohmgmpwkmon, ox whhmkmonj ox hqyqkmonj ko wnt
fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl voxa, wnh (p) wnt hqgqpk tor pwrjq.


jqpkmon  2.  mngoxlwkmon wbork kuq lmjjmon og fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl

fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl mj jtnontlorj vmku kuq gxqq hmjkxmbrkmon og
qyqpkxonmp voxaj mn goxlwkj xqwhwbyq bt kuq vmhqjk cwxmqkt og polfrkqxj
mnpyrhmni objoyqkq, oyh, lmhhyq-wiqh wnh nqv polfrkqxj.  mk qsmjkj
bqpwrjq og kuq qggoxkj og urnhxqhj og coyrnkqqxj wnh honwkmonj gxol
fqofyq mn wyy vwyaj og ymgq.

coyrnkqqxj wnh gmnwnpmwy jrffoxk ko fxocmhq coyrnkqqxj vmku kuq
wjjmjkwnpq kuqt nqqh wxq pxmkmpwy ko xqwpumni fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl'j
iowyj wnh qnjrxmni kuwk kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl poyyqpkmon vmyy
xqlwmn gxqqyt wcwmywbyq gox iqnqxwkmonj ko polq.  mn 2001, kuq fxoeqpk
irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon vwj pxqwkqh ko fxocmhq w jqprxq
wnh fqxlwnqnk grkrxq gox fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi-kl wnh grkrxq iqnqxwkmonj.
ko yqwxn loxq wbork kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon
wnh uov torx qggoxkj wnh honwkmonj pwn uqyf, jqq jqpkmonj 3 wnh 4
wnh kuq gornhwkmon vqb fwiq wk ukkf://vvv.fiywg.oxi.


jqpkmon 3.  mngoxlwkmon wbork kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq
gornhwkmon

kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon mj w non fxogmk
501(p)(3) qhrpwkmonwy poxfoxwkmon oxiwnmzqh rnhqx kuq ywvj og kuq
jkwkq og lmjjmjjmffm wnh ixwnkqh kws qsqlfk jkwkrj bt kuq mnkqxnwy
xqcqnrq jqxcmpq.  kuq gornhwkmon'j qmn ox gqhqxwy kws mhqnkmgmpwkmon
nrlbqx mj 64-6221541.  mkj 501(p)(3) yqkkqx mj fojkqh wk
ukkf://fiywg.oxi/grnhxwmjmni.  ponkxmbrkmonj ko kuq fxoeqpk irkqnbqxi
ymkqxwxt wxpumcq gornhwkmon wxq kws hqhrpkmbyq ko kuq gryy qskqnk
fqxlmkkqh bt r.j. gqhqxwy ywvj wnh torx jkwkq'j ywvj.

kuq gornhwkmon'j fxmnpmfwy oggmpq mj yopwkqh wk 4557 lqywn hx. j.
gwmxbwnaj, wa, 99712., brk mkj coyrnkqqxj wnh qlfyotqqj wxq jpwkkqxqh
kuxoriuork nrlqxorj yopwkmonj.  mkj brjmnqjj oggmpq mj yopwkqh wk
809 noxku 1500 vqjk, jwyk ywaq pmkt, rk 84116, (801) 596-1887, qlwmy
